<p><b>"Point me!"</b>
</p>
This article is about <b>the headmaster of Hogwarts during Harry Potter's tenure at the school</b>. You may be looking for <b>Harry Potter's son <a href="/wiki/Albus_Potter" title="Albus Potter">Albus Potter</a> who was named after him, his <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore_family" title="Dumbledore family">family</a>, or <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore_(Chocolate_Frog_Card)" title="Albus Dumbledore (Chocolate Frog Card)">a specific Chocolate Frog Card</a></b>.</div>

<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>Albus Dumbledore was never proud or vain; he could find something to value in anyone, however apparently insignificant or wretched, and I believe that his early losses endowed him with great humanity and sympathy. I shall miss his friendship more than I can say, but my loss is as nothing compared to the Wizarding world’s. That he was the most inspiring and the best loved of all Hogwarts headmasters cannot be in question. He died as he lived: working always for the greater good and, to his last hour, as willing to stretch out a hand to a small boy with dragon pox as he was on the day that I met him.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Albus Dumbledore's obituary<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p><b>Professor Albus Percival Wulfric Brian Dumbledore</b>, <span class="template-c"><a href="/wiki/Order_of_Merlin" title="Order of Merlin">O.M. (First Class)</a></span>, <small>Grand Sorc.</small>, <small>D. Wiz.</small>, <small>X.J. (sorc.)</small>, <small>S. of Mag.Q.</small><sup id="cite_ref-HPFW_21-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HPFW-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> (c. Summer<sup id="cite_ref-birthday_1-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-birthday-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/1881" class="mw-redirect" title="1881">1881</a><sup id="cite_ref-PottermoreFactFile_3-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PottermoreFactFile-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> – <a href="/wiki/30_June" title="30 June">30 June</a>, <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a><sup id="cite_ref-PottermoreFactFile_3-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PottermoreFactFile-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup>) was an <a href="/wiki/England" title="England">English</a> <a href="/wiki/Half-blood" title="Half-blood">half-blood</a> <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">wizard</a>, who was the <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> <a href="/wiki/Professor" title="Professor">Professor</a>, later the <a href="/wiki/Transfiguration_(class)" title="Transfiguration (class)">Transfiguration</a> Professor, and later the <a href="/wiki/Headmaster" title="Headmaster">Headmaster</a> of <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a>. Professor Dumbledore also served as <a href="/wiki/Supreme_Mugwump" title="Supreme Mugwump">Supreme Mugwump</a> of the <a href="/wiki/International_Confederation_of_Wizards" title="International Confederation of Wizards">International Confederation of Wizards</a> <span class="template-c">(?–1995)</span> and <a href="/wiki/Chief_Warlock" title="Chief Warlock">Chief Warlock</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Wizengamot" title="Wizengamot">Wizengamot</a> <span class="template-c">(?–1995; 1996–1997)</span>. He was a <a href="/wiki/Half-blood" title="Half-blood">half-blood</a>, <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggle</a>-supporting <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">wizard</a> considered to have been the greatest wizard of modern times, perhaps of all time. The son of <a href="/wiki/Percival_Dumbledore" title="Percival Dumbledore">Percival</a> and <a href="/wiki/Kendra_Dumbledore" title="Kendra Dumbledore">Kendra Dumbledore</a>, and the elder brother of <a href="/wiki/Aberforth_Dumbledore" title="Aberforth Dumbledore">Aberforth</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ariana_Dumbledore" title="Ariana Dumbledore">Ariana</a>. His father died in <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a> when Dumbledore was young, while his mother and sister were later accidentally killed. His early losses greatly affected him early on, even at his death, but, in turn, made him a better person. 
</p><p>While initially unable to directly act against <a href="/wiki/Gellert_Grindelwald" title="Gellert Grindelwald">Gellert Grindelwald</a>, due to their past <a href="/wiki/Blood_pact" title="Blood pact">Blood pact</a>, the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry</a>'s surveillance of him, his lingering feelings of love toward Grindelwald, and his lingering guilt over <a href="/wiki/Ariana_Dumbledore" title="Ariana Dumbledore">Ariana</a>'s death, Dumbledore sent <a href="/wiki/Newton_Scamander" title="Newton Scamander">Newt Scamander</a> to <a href="/wiki/New_York" title="New York">New York</a> to release the <a href="/wiki/Thunderbird" title="Thunderbird">Thunderbird</a> <a href="/wiki/Frank" title="Frank">Frank</a>, and later sent Newt to <a href="/wiki/Paris" title="Paris">Paris</a> to rescue <a href="/wiki/Credence_Barebone" title="Credence Barebone">Credence Barebone</a>. After the tragic death of <a href="/wiki/Leta_Lestrange" title="Leta Lestrange">Leta Lestrange</a> in Paris, Dumbledore became determined to contribute helpful advice to the resistance against Grindelwald, notably <a href="/wiki/Newton_Scamander" title="Newton Scamander">Newt</a>, <a href="/wiki/Theseus_Scamander" title="Theseus Scamander">Theseus</a>, <a href="/wiki/Porpentina_Goldstein" title="Porpentina Goldstein">Tina</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jacob_Kowalski" title="Jacob Kowalski">Jacob</a>, <a href="/wiki/Yusuf_Kama" title="Yusuf Kama">Yusuf</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Nagini" title="Nagini">Nagini</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Global_wizarding_war" title="Global wizarding war">Global wizarding war</a>. Initially unbeknownst to Dumbledore however, Grindelwald intended to use the former's alleged <a href="/wiki/Obscurial" title="Obscurial">Obscurial</a> relative, <a href="/wiki/Credence_Barebone" title="Credence Barebone">Aurelius Dumbledore</a>, as a weapon against him.
</p><p>Following the <a href="/wiki/Global_wizarding_war" title="Global wizarding war">Global wizarding war</a> and the end of the <i><a href="/wiki/For_the_Greater_Good" title="For the Greater Good">For the Greater Good</a></i> revolution, regardless of Aurelius Dumbledore's fate, Dumbledore became most famous for <a href="/wiki/Duel_between_Albus_Dumbledore_and_Gellert_Grindelwald" title="Duel between Albus Dumbledore and Gellert Grindelwald">defeating</a> Grindelwald in arguably the most epic duel of all time. Dumbledore also gained much more recognition with his involvement in the discovery of the twelve uses of <a href="/wiki/Dragon_blood" title="Dragon blood">dragon's blood</a> and his work on <a href="/wiki/Alchemy" title="Alchemy">alchemy</a> with <a href="/wiki/Nicolas_Flamel" title="Nicolas Flamel">Nicolas Flamel</a>. 
</p><p>It was through Dumbledore that resistance to the rise of <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> was formed, as it was he who founded and lead the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> against Voldemort during the <a href="/wiki/First_Wizarding_War" title="First Wizarding War">First Wizarding War</a>. Following Voldemort's sudden return and the start of the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a> after the resignation of <a href="/wiki/Cornelius_Fudge" title="Cornelius Fudge">Cornelius Fudge</a>, Dumbledore swiftly formed and lead the second Order of the Phoenix. He would also support <a href="/wiki/Jacob%27s_sibling" title="Jacob&#39;s sibling">Jacob's sibling</a> in the latter's quest for the <a href="/wiki/Cursed_Vaults" title="Cursed Vaults">Cursed Vaults</a>, and consistently aid the trio of <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione</a> during their first six years at Hogwarts, thus leading them to name <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a> after him.
</p><p>Due to the fact that he had a keen mind and legendary power, Dumbledore became the only <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">wizard</a> that Voldemort ever feared. He was the wielder and the master of the <a href="/wiki/Elder_Wand" title="Elder Wand">Elder Wand</a> from <a href="/wiki/1945" title="1945">1945</a> until <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a> and considered by many as the greatest <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Headmaster" title="Hogwarts Headmaster">Hogwarts Headmaster</a>. As he was about to die by a <a href="/wiki/Marvolo_Gaunt%27s_Ring" title="Marvolo Gaunt&#39;s Ring">cursed ring</a>, Dumbledore planned his own <a href="/wiki/Death" title="Death">death</a> with <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>. Per the plan, Dumbledore was killed by <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Snape</a> during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a>.
</p><p>Though he was no longer alive at the time, it was through Dumbledore's manipulations that Lord Voldemort was ultimately defeated and lasting peace finally restored to the <a href="/wiki/Wizarding_world" title="Wizarding world">wizarding world</a>. Dumbledore is the only Headmaster that was <a href="/wiki/White_Tomb" title="White Tomb">laid to rest</a> at Hogwarts. <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore%27s_portrait" title="Albus Dumbledore&#39;s portrait">A portrait</a> of him still remains at Hogwarts. <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> later named his second son <a href="/wiki/Albus_Potter" title="Albus Potter">Albus Severus Potter</a> after him.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Biography">Biography</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=1" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Biography">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Biography"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span id="Early_life_(1881–1892)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_life_.281881.E2.80.931892.29">Early life <span class="template-c">(1881–1892)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=2" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Early life (1881–1892)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Early life (1881–1892)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>You know the secret of my sister’s ill-health, what those Muggles did, what she became. You know how my poor father sought revenge, and paid the price, died in Azkaban. You know how my mother gave up her own life to care for Ariana. </i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Dumbledore retells his early years to Harry<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>Albus Percival Wulfric Brian Dumbledore was born to <a href="/wiki/Kendra_Dumbledore" title="Kendra Dumbledore">Kendra</a> and <a href="/wiki/Percival_Dumbledore" title="Percival Dumbledore">Percival Dumbledore</a> in the summer<sup id="cite_ref-birthday_1-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-birthday-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> of <a href="/wiki/1881" class="mw-redirect" title="1881">1881</a>, in the mainly wizarding village of <a href="/wiki/Mould-on-the-Wold" title="Mould-on-the-Wold">Mould-on-the-Wold</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-HPLE_4-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HPLE-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> The early years of Dumbledore's life were marked by tragedy when his younger sister, <a href="/wiki/Ariana_Dumbledore" title="Ariana Dumbledore">Ariana Dumbledore</a>, was attacked by a group of <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggle</a> <a href="/wiki/Unidentified_Mould-on-the-Wold_boys" title="Unidentified Mould-on-the-Wold boys">boys</a>, who saw her performing magic and were frightened by what they saw.
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Ariana_Dumbledore" title="Ariana Dumbledore">Ariana</a> was left mentally and emotionally scarred by the event and her <a href="/wiki/Magic" title="Magic">magical</a> powers were left severely altered and would manifest themselves on rare occasions usually in random or destructive ways. Albus' father, <a href="/wiki/Percival_Dumbledore" title="Percival Dumbledore">Percival Dumbledore</a>, was heartbroken and set out in search of his own brand of justice. He located the Muggle boys and attacked them, as they had his daughter. For this, Percival was sentenced to <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a> where he later <a href="/wiki/Azkaban_burial_ground" title="Azkaban burial ground">died</a>, choosing the sentence over explaining why he had attacked the boys as it would have meant Ariana being taken away.
</p><p>To escape the accusing eyes of the local community, <a href="/wiki/Kendra_Dumbledore" title="Kendra Dumbledore">Kendra Dumbledore</a> moved her young family to the village of <a href="/wiki/Godric%27s_Hollow" title="Godric&#39;s Hollow">Godric's Hollow</a> which, like Mould-on-the-Wold, was a part-wizarding village. Fearing - like her husband - that the ousting of her daughter's inability to control her magical ability would see her confined indefinitely to <a href="/wiki/St_Mungo%27s_Hospital_for_Magical_Maladies_and_Injuries" title="St Mungo&#39;s Hospital for Magical Maladies and Injuries">St Mungo's Hospital for Magical Maladies and Injuries</a>, Kendra rebuffed all her neighbours, with the eventual exception of <a href="/wiki/Bathilda_Bagshot" title="Bathilda Bagshot">Bathilda Bagshot</a>, preferring to be left alone: and Albus learned not to mention his <a href="/wiki/Ariana_Dumbledore" title="Ariana Dumbledore">sister</a> or <a href="/wiki/Percival_Dumbledore" title="Percival Dumbledore">father</a> in public.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_22-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="Hogwarts_years_(1892–1899)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Hogwarts_years_.281892.E2.80.931899.29">Hogwarts years <span class="template-c">(1892–1899)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=3" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Hogwarts years (1892–1899)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Hogwarts years (1892–1899)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>By the end of his first year, he would never again be known as the son of a Muggle-hater, but as nothing more or less than the most brilliant student ever seen at the school.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Dumbledore's years as a Hogwarts student<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/11/Hogwarts_Castle_%E2%80%93_HPatPS.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20130514141001" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="141" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hogwarts Castle – HPatPS.jpg" data-image-key="Hogwarts_Castle_–_HPatPS.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/11/Hogwarts_Castle_%E2%80%93_HPatPS.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130514141001" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/11/Hogwarts_Castle_%E2%80%93_HPatPS.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20130514141001" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/11/Hogwarts_Castle_%E2%80%93_HPatPS.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130514141001" decoding="async" width="250" height="141" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hogwarts Castle – HPatPS.jpg" data-image-key="Hogwarts_Castle_–_HPatPS.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/11/Hogwarts_Castle_%E2%80%93_HPatPS.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130514141001" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hogwarts_Castle_%E2%80%93_HPatPS.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Dumbledore began attending <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a> in the autumn of <a href="/wiki/1892" class="mw-redirect" title="1892">1892</a> and was <a href="/wiki/Sorting_ceremony" title="Sorting ceremony">Sorted</a> into <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a> house. Dumbledore's first year was met with much whispering about his father's crime. Many of Albus' fellow students mistakenly believed that, like father like son, Albus too hated <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggles</a>. Some praised his <a href="/wiki/Percival_Dumbledore" title="Percival Dumbledore">father</a>'s actions, hoping to gain his trust, but they would not find favour with the young Dumbledore this way. Though later in his young life, under the influence of his love for <a href="/wiki/Gellert_Grindelwald" title="Gellert Grindelwald">Gellert Grindelwald</a>, some anti-<a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggle</a> prejudice did develop, but he soon saw the error of his intent.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_22-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He befriended a young <a href="/wiki/Elphias_Doge" title="Elphias Doge">Elphias Doge</a> on his first day at Hogwarts; <a href="/wiki/Elphias_Doge" title="Elphias Doge">Doge</a> was suffering from the aftermath of <a href="/wiki/Dragon_Pox" title="Dragon Pox">Dragon Pox</a> at the time (greenish skin and pockmarks), which discouraged most from approaching him. Dumbledore, however, demonstrated his uncommon kindness and willingness to look past the surface and find inner beauty in people. Dumbledore also became very well-connected during his Hogwarts years, making notable friends such as <a href="/wiki/Nicolas_Flamel" title="Nicolas Flamel">Nicolas Flamel</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bathilda_Bagshot" title="Bathilda Bagshot">Bathilda Bagshot</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Griselda_Marchbanks" title="Griselda Marchbanks">Griselda Marchbanks</a>, who marked him in his <a href="/wiki/Nastily_Exhausting_Wizarding_Test" title="Nastily Exhausting Wizarding Test">N.E.W.T.s</a> for <a href="/wiki/Charms_(class)" title="Charms (class)">Charms</a> and <a href="/wiki/Transfiguration_(class)" title="Transfiguration (class)">Transfiguration</a> and later recalled that he did things with a wand that she had never seen before. He also had several of his papers published during his studies and exchanged letters with theoretician <a href="/wiki/Adalbert_Waffling" title="Adalbert Waffling">Adalbert Waffling</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH2_23-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH2-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</a> later shared these letters with members of the <a href="/wiki/Statute_of_Secrecy_Task_Force" title="Statute of Secrecy Task Force">Statute of Secrecy Task Force</a> who pursued a <a href="/wiki/Professor" title="Professor">Professorship</a> profession to help improve their skills in addressing the <a href="/wiki/Calamity" title="Calamity">Calamity</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-WU_24-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WU-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In his third year, Dumbledore presumably took <a href="/wiki/Study_of_Ancient_Runes" title="Study of Ancient Runes">Study of Ancient Runes</a> and at least one other subject, which was known not to be <a href="/wiki/Divination_(class)" title="Divination (class)">Divination</a>.
</p><p>During his fourth year, Dumbledore "accidentally" set the bed-curtains in his dormitory on <a href="/wiki/Fire" title="Fire">fire</a> (although he admitted that he had never liked them anyway).
</p><p>Albus was made a <a href="/wiki/Prefect" title="Prefect">prefect</a> during his fifth year and was made <a href="/wiki/Head_Boy_or_Girl" title="Head Boy or Girl">Head Boy</a> in his <a href="/wiki/Seventh_year" title="Seventh year">seventh year</a>. At some point over the course of his school career, Dumbledore also won the <a href="/wiki/Barnabus_Finkley_Prize_for_Exceptional_Spell-Casting" title="Barnabus Finkley Prize for Exceptional Spell-Casting">Barnabus Finkley Prize for Exceptional Spell-Casting</a>, became the <a href="/wiki/British_Youth_Representative_to_the_Wizengamot" title="British Youth Representative to the Wizengamot">British Youth Representative to the Wizengamot</a>, and received the <a href="/wiki/Gold_Medal_for_Ground-Breaking_Contribution_to_the_International_Alchemical_Conference" title="Gold Medal for Ground-Breaking Contribution to the International Alchemical Conference">Gold Medal for Ground-Breaking Contribution to the International Alchemical Conference</a> in <a href="/wiki/Cairo" title="Cairo">Cairo</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-DH_22-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> not to mention the recognition of having been arguably the most brilliant student to have ever attended the school.
</p>
<h3><span id="Tragedy_and_romance_(1899)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Tragedy_and_romance_.281899.29">Tragedy and romance <span class="template-c">(1899)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=4" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Tragedy and romance (1899)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Tragedy and romance (1899)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>So that, when my mother died, and I was left the responsibility of a damaged sister and a wayward brother, I returned to my village in anger and bitterness. Trapped and wasted, I thought! And then, of course, he came.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Dumbledore discussing his harsh past<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/28/Albus_Dumbledore_and_Gellert_Grindelwald.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190801183310" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="321" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Albus Dumbledore and Gellert Grindelwald.jpg" data-image-key="Albus_Dumbledore_and_Gellert_Grindelwald.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/28/Albus_Dumbledore_and_Gellert_Grindelwald.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190801183310" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/28/Albus_Dumbledore_and_Gellert_Grindelwald.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190801183310" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/28/Albus_Dumbledore_and_Gellert_Grindelwald.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190801183310" decoding="async" width="250" height="321" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Albus Dumbledore and Gellert Grindelwald.jpg" data-image-key="Albus_Dumbledore_and_Gellert_Grindelwald.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/28/Albus_Dumbledore_and_Gellert_Grindelwald.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190801183310" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Albus_Dumbledore_and_Gellert_Grindelwald.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Albus with his best friend and lover <a href="/wiki/Gellert_Grindelwald" title="Gellert Grindelwald">Gellert Grindelwald</a> in <a href="/wiki/1899" class="mw-redirect" title="1899">1899</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After graduating from <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a> in <a href="/wiki/June" title="June">June</a> <a href="/wiki/1899" class="mw-redirect" title="1899">1899</a>, Dumbledore planned to take the traditional "Grand Tour" of the world with his friend Doge. However, tragedy ensued on the eve of the departure when <a href="/wiki/Kendra_Dumbledore" title="Kendra Dumbledore">Kendra Dumbledore</a> was killed by an <a href="/wiki/Backfiring_Jinx" title="Backfiring Jinx">outburst</a> of <a href="/wiki/Ariana_Dumbledore" title="Ariana Dumbledore">Ariana</a>'s uncontrollable magic, leaving Albus the head of his own broken family and now in charge of his younger siblings. Albus returned to <a href="/wiki/Godric%27s_Hollow" title="Godric&#39;s Hollow">Godric's Hollow</a> full of bitter resentment at his situation, feeling trapped and wasted, although he refused to let Aberfoth quit school and insisted he complete his education first before taking care of Ariana. Fortune finally appeared to shine on Dumbledore, however, when a foreigner arrived at their little village, by the name of <a href="/wiki/Gellert_Grindelwald" title="Gellert Grindelwald">Gellert Grindelwald</a>. A young man around Albus's age, he lived for the next two months with his great-aunt, the celebrated magical historian and family friend of the Dumbledores, <a href="/wiki/Bathilda_Bagshot" title="Bathilda Bagshot">Bathilda Bagshot</a>, who introduced the two soon after Grindelwald crossed her doorstep. Thrilled to realise that the newcomer was every bit as brilliant as himself, the two young men took to each other right away and quickly struck up a close friendship, unified by the revelation of Grindelwald's research into the existence and whereabouts of the fabled <a href="/wiki/Deathly_Hallows" title="Deathly Hallows">Deathly Hallows</a>. Dumbledore also quickly became fascinated by Grindelwald's ideas of wizarding domination, obviously considering Grindelwald an unexpected new chance to show his own brilliance and come out of the local misery. Over the course of the two months Grindelwald stayed in Godric's Hollow, the two young men’s friendship became romantic, with Albus ignoring any misgivings he had about Gellert's dark intents by convincing himself the <a href="/wiki/Global_wizarding_war" title="Global wizarding war">revolution</a> they were planning to embark on was truly <a href="/wiki/For_the_Greater_Good" title="For the Greater Good">For the Greater Good</a>, and that any harm caused would be repaid a thousandfold after its conclusion.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_22-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Albus's brother <a href="/wiki/Aberforth_Dumbledore" title="Aberforth Dumbledore">Aberforth</a>, however, was disgusted with Albus for his plans and concerned over the fact that he and Ariana would have to be dragged along for the ride. Aberforth angrily confronted Albus over his neglect of <a href="/wiki/Ariana_Dumbledore" title="Ariana Dumbledore">Ariana</a> over the past few weeks, bluntly telling him that he couldn't carry out his plans with Grindelwald, as he would have to take her with him. This brought Albus back to reality despite not wanting to hear the truth of the words his younger brother shouted at him. Grindelwald, however, was furious with Aberforth's intervention, and used the <a href="/wiki/Cruciatus_Curse" title="Cruciatus Curse">Cruciatus Curse</a> on him in a fit of anger. Albus moved to defend his brother and a <a href="/wiki/Duel_at_Godric%27s_Hollow" title="Duel at Godric&#39;s Hollow">violent duel</a> erupted between the three teenage boys. Ariana herself tried to intervene in the fight, but couldn't due to her erratic abilities, and in the ensuing chaos was hit by a stray curse and died. No one knew whose curse it was that killed her, but Grindelwald fled immediately, as he already had a bad record back home, leaving the devastated Albus and Aberforth behind. Aberforth resented Albus and they had a strained relationship, with Aberforth <a href="/wiki/Muggle_duelling" title="Muggle duelling">punching</a> Albus and breaking his nose at Ariana's funeral. Aberforth never knew of the great guilt and regret Albus would feel for the rest of his life about his part in Ariana's death.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_22-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="Early_career_at_Hogwarts_(1910s–1925)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_career_at_Hogwarts_.281910s.E2.80.931925.29">Early career at Hogwarts <span class="template-c">(1910s–1925)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=5" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Early career at Hogwarts (1910s–1925)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Early career at Hogwarts (1910s–1925)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows"><b>Dumbledore</b>: "<i>I had proven, as a very young man, that power was my weakness and temptation. I was safer at Hogwarts. I think I was a good teacher.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>You were the best.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; A discussion in <a href="/wiki/Limbo" title="Limbo">limbo</a> regarding power and leadership<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div><p>Shortly thereafter, Albus, who had been exchanging owls with the famous researcher as far back when he had been a student at Hogwarts, travelled to <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">France</a> and spent "some time"<sup id="cite_ref-HM_Beauxbatons_25-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HM_Beauxbatons-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> in <a href="/wiki/Paris" title="Paris">Paris</a> studying the ancient art and science of <a href="/wiki/Alchemy" title="Alchemy">alchemy</a> under the tutelage of <a href="/wiki/Nicolas_Flamel" title="Nicolas Flamel">Nicholas Flamel</a>. He presumably did so in order to both give his brother some space, as well as to get away for a bit and spend his time grieving more productively than he otherwise would have done simply wallowing in his own misery. It is unknown when exactly he returned to <a href="/wiki/Great_Britain" title="Great Britain">Britain</a>, but around the time he did, Albus had become intrigued with the study of <a href="/wiki/Dragon%27s_blood" class="mw-redirect" title="Dragon&#39;s blood">dragon's blood</a>, and was ultimately credited with the discovery of no less than twelve new uses for it,<sup id="cite_ref-PS6_26-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS6-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> even though a wizard by the name of <a href="/wiki/Ivor_Dillonsby" title="Ivor Dillonsby">Ivor Dillonsby</a> would later claim that he had already discovered eight of them when Dumbledore "borrowed" his notes.<sup id="cite_ref-DH2_23-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH2-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> This accomplishment nevertheless earned him widespread fame and recognition, and played no small role in the subsequent offer of employment that he received from <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> Having always felt drawn towards teaching himself, even as a student, Albus was happy to accept.
</p><figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/15/Dumbledore_teaching_DADA.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190325024211" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dumbledore teaching DADA.gif" data-image-key="Dumbledore_teaching_DADA.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/15/Dumbledore_teaching_DADA.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190325024211" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/15/Dumbledore_teaching_DADA.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190325024211" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/15/Dumbledore_teaching_DADA.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190325024211" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dumbledore teaching DADA.gif" data-image-key="Dumbledore_teaching_DADA.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/15/Dumbledore_teaching_DADA.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190325024211" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dumbledore_teaching_DADA.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore teaching Defence Against The Dark Arts</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>And so it was that Albus Dumbledore returned to Hogwarts Castle, which was now under the stewardship of <a href="/wiki/Professor" title="Professor">Professor</a> <a href="/wiki/Phineas_Nigellus_Black" title="Phineas Nigellus Black">Phineas Nigellus Black</a>, not to learn this time, but to teach. Burdened by the secret knowledge of Grindelwald's imminent <a href="/wiki/Global_wizarding_war" title="Global wizarding war">rise to power</a> and wanting to rectify past mistakes, it was natural, perhaps, that he felt drawn towards the job of <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> instructor, a position in which he could most easily prepare his charges for the dangers he knew one day would come.<sup id="cite_ref-COG_28-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COG-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> Albus, who would henceforth come to be known to successive generations of students as ‘Professor Dumbledore’, was granted <a href="/wiki/Classroom_3C" title="Classroom 3C">Classroom 3C</a> located off of the <a href="/wiki/Serpentine_Corridor" title="Serpentine Corridor">Serpentine Corridor</a> on the third-floor and an office.
</p><p>Even though the freshly hired instructor would henceforth largely busy himself with the training of young witches and wizards, Albus would continue to keep in touch with Nicolas Flamel, alongside whom he would eventually achieve a number of advancements in the field of alchemy over the years as their relationship blossomed from that of student-and-mentor, to that of an equal partnership and near life-long friendship.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_7-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> At some point after this, Albus would visit his old friend and pose for a photograph in Flamel's <a href="/wiki/Flamel_House" title="Flamel House">workshop</a> alongside his celebrated tutor, with many of his alchemical tools and equipment being visible in the background, as well as <a href="/wiki/Nicolas_Flamel%27s_crystal_ball" title="Nicolas Flamel&#39;s crystal ball">crystal ball</a> and a <a href="/wiki/Nicolas_Flamel%27s_phoenix-embossed_book" title="Nicolas Flamel&#39;s phoenix-embossed book">book with a phoenix on the cover</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-HM_Beauxbatons_25-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HM_Beauxbatons-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In the <a href="/wiki/1910s" title="1910s">1910s</a>, Dumbledore taught <a href="/wiki/Hufflepuff" title="Hufflepuff">Hufflepuff</a> <a href="/wiki/Newton_Scamander" title="Newton Scamander">Newton Scamander</a> and <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin</a> <a href="/wiki/Leta_Lestrange" title="Leta Lestrange">Leta Lestrange</a>. One of his lessons involved confronting a <a href="/wiki/Boggart" title="Boggart">Boggart</a> and learning the <a href="/wiki/Boggart-Banishing_Spell" title="Boggart-Banishing Spell">spell</a> to banish it. When Newt's Boggart turned into a desk, Dumbledore commented on its unexpected nature and kindly inquired why it took this form: Newt confessed that his greatest fear was being stuck working in an office. After Newt successfully dispatched the Boggart, Dumbledore encouraged Leta to take her turn, reassuring her that being afraid of something wasn't shameful; everyone was afraid of something. The form of Leta's Boggart surprised both Dumbledore and the entire class: a white sheet containing an undistinguishable, slight <a href="/wiki/Corvus_Lestrange_(V)" title="Corvus Lestrange (V)">form</a> floating through a dark blue glow. The event badly shook Leta.<sup id="cite_ref-COG_28-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COG-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/26/NewtRiddikulus.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190224141731" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="NewtRiddikulus.gif" data-image-key="NewtRiddikulus.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/26/NewtRiddikulus.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190224141731" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/26/NewtRiddikulus.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190224141731" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/26/NewtRiddikulus.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190224141731" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="NewtRiddikulus.gif" data-image-key="NewtRiddikulus.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/26/NewtRiddikulus.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190224141731" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:NewtRiddikulus.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore teaching Newt Scamander, Leta Lestrange and other students the <a href="/wiki/Boggart-Banishing_Spell" title="Boggart-Banishing Spell">Boggart-Banishing Spell</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/1913" title="1913">1913</a>, one of Leta's experiments with a <a href="/wiki/Jarvey" title="Jarvey">Jarvey</a> went too far endangering the life of another student. Newt decided to take the blame and was sentenced to expulsion by Headmaster <a href="/wiki/Phineas_Nigellus_Black" title="Phineas Nigellus Black">Phineas Nigellus Black</a>. Dumbledore, however, argued strongly on his behalf. Whether Newt's expulsion was enforced or not is unknown but Dumbledore succeeded in at least allowing Newt to keep his wand.<sup id="cite_ref-FBS_29-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FBS-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>During his time at Hogwarts, Dumbledore also developed close relationships and friendships with wizards and witches throughout the world. Among these friends, he counted the French <a href="/wiki/Alchemy" title="Alchemy">alchemist</a> <a href="/wiki/Nicolas_Flamel" title="Nicolas Flamel">Nicolas Flamel</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ilvermorny_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Ilvermorny School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Ilvermorny</a> <a href="/wiki/Charm" title="Charm">Charms</a> Professor <a href="/wiki/Eulalie_Hicks" title="Eulalie Hicks">Eulalie Hicks</a>. He maintained close contact with these friends in the form of <a href="/wiki/Nicolas_Flamel%27s_phoenix-embossed_book" title="Nicolas Flamel&#39;s phoenix-embossed book">enchanted books</a> they all possessed which allowed them to speak despite the distance. The <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">British Ministry of Magic</a>, which was already suspicious of Dumbledore because of his past connection to Grindelwald, was wary of these relationships, believing that he used these contacts as spies to allow him to act as an independent authority to theirs, and maintained a close watch on Dumbledore and his allies. Chief among Dumbledore's rivals within the Ministry was <a href="/wiki/Torquil_Travers" title="Torquil Travers">Torquil Travers</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Department_of_Magical_Law_Enforcement" title="Department of Magical Law Enforcement">Head of the Department of Magical Law Enforcement</a>, who never tried to hide his dislike for the Hogwarts teacher.<sup id="cite_ref-COG_28-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COG-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="Global_Wizarding_War_(1926–1945)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Global_Wizarding_War_.281926.E2.80.931945.29">Global Wizarding War <span class="template-c">(1926–1945)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=6" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Global Wizarding War (1926–1945)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Global Wizarding War (1926–1945)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span id="Newt_Scamander's_visit_to_New_York"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Newt_Scamander.27s_visit_to_New_York">Newt Scamander's visit to New York</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=7" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Newt Scamander&#039;s visit to New York">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Newt Scamander&#039;s visit to New York"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/1926" title="1926">1926</a>, Dumbledore received word that strange events were occurring in New York, events that had also caught the attention of the <a href="/wiki/International_Confederation_of_Wizards" title="International Confederation of Wizards">International Confederation of Wizards</a>. These events came as the European wizarding communities had been suffering a <a href="/wiki/Grindelwald_Attacks" title="Grindelwald Attacks">series of attacks</a> conducted by Grindelwald and his <a href="/wiki/Gellert_Grindelwald%27s_acolytes" title="Gellert Grindelwald&#39;s acolytes">cadre of followers</a>. Dumbledore, suspecting other circumstances that might nevertheless interest his old friend, wanted to arrange for his plans to be thwarted.<sup id="cite_ref-COG_28-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COG-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He contacted his old student, Newt Scamander, who had become a <a href="/wiki/Magizoologist" title="Magizoologist">Magizoologist</a> in the employment of the <a href="/wiki/Department_for_the_Regulation_and_Control_of_Magical_Creatures" title="Department for the Regulation and Control of Magical Creatures">Department for the Regulation and Control of Magical Creatures</a> at the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a> in London and had been travelling throughout the world, locating and rescuing magical creatures from wizard hunters who believed that these creatures represented a threat to their secrecy. Dumbledore told Newt of <a href="/wiki/Frank" title="Frank">a</a> <a href="/wiki/Thunderbird" title="Thunderbird">Thunderbird</a> that was being held captive in <a href="/wiki/Egypt" title="Egypt">Egypt</a>, knowing he would not stand for such an injustice and would not only rescue him but also return him to his native <a href="/wiki/Arizona" title="Arizona">Arizona</a>. To accomplish this, Newt would have to pass through the Muggle customs in <a href="/wiki/New_York" title="New York">New York</a>. Newt's visit to New York resulted not only in the discovery of <a href="/wiki/Credence_Barebone" title="Credence Barebone">Credence Barebone</a>, the most powerful <a href="/wiki/Obscurus" title="Obscurus">Obscurus</a> ever recorded (the only one to survive into adulthood), but also in the capture of Grindelwald, who had been disguised as a high-ranking official at <a href="/wiki/Magical_Congress_of_the_United_States_of_America" title="Magical Congress of the United States of America">MACUSA</a> by the name of <a href="/wiki/Percival_Graves" title="Percival Graves">Percival Graves</a> to find the Obscurus. While there, however, Newt got in <a href="/wiki/Newton_Scamander%27s_Grade_One_Infraction_of_the_International_Statute_of_Wizarding_Secrecy" title="Newton Scamander&#39;s Grade One Infraction of the International Statute of Wizarding Secrecy">trouble</a> when a number of the magical creatures his case escaped and ran loose in areas of the city inhabited mainly by <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Non-magical people</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-FBS_29-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FBS-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-COG_28-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COG-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/03/TransfigurationToday.png/revision/latest?cb=20161205200722" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="371" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="TransfigurationToday.png" data-image-key="TransfigurationToday.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/03/TransfigurationToday.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161205200722" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/03/TransfigurationToday.png/revision/latest?cb=20161205200722" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/03/TransfigurationToday.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161205200722" decoding="async" width="250" height="371" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="TransfigurationToday.png" data-image-key="TransfigurationToday.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/03/TransfigurationToday.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161205200722" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:TransfigurationToday.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore mentioned in Transfiguration Today magazine</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>For his role in the incident in New York, as well as his reluctance and evasiveness in providing his superiors at the Ministry details about why he had been in New York in the first place, Newt was banned from travelling internationally by the Ministry, a ban they offered to lift if he confessed that Dumbledore had been the one to send him to New York. Although he realised that Dumbledore had covertly sent him to New York, Newt remained loyal to his old teacher and refused to confess his role in the affair.<sup id="cite_ref-COG_28-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COG-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> Even in later years, when the rumours were published by <a href="/wiki/Rita_Skeeter" title="Rita Skeeter">Rita Skeeter</a> in a biography of Newt called <i><a href="/wiki/Man_or_Monster%3F_The_TRUTH_about_Newt_Scamander" title="Man or Monster? The TRUTH about Newt Scamander">Man or Monster? The TRUTH about Newt Scamander</a></i>, he continued to deny that Dumbledore was responsible for his trip to New York in the foreword of a new edition of <i><a href="/wiki/Fantastic_Beasts_and_Where_to_Find_Them" title="Fantastic Beasts and Where to Find Them">Fantastic Beasts and Where to Find Them</a></i>.
</p><p>In the same year Dumbledore became a regular columnist for <i><a href="/wiki/Transfiguration_Today" title="Transfiguration Today">Transfiguration Today</a></i>, with the <i><a href="/wiki/Daily_Prophet" title="Daily Prophet">Daily Prophet</a></i> quoting him as saying he was "enraptured!" to be writing for the magazine.<sup id="cite_ref-FBF-prophet_18-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FBF-prophet-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Moving_against_Gellert_Grindelwald">Moving against Gellert Grindelwald</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=8" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Moving against Gellert Grindelwald">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Moving against Gellert Grindelwald"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8d/Albus_with_Newt.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190325014948" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="102" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Albus with Newt.jpg" data-image-key="Albus_with_Newt.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8d/Albus_with_Newt.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190325014948" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8d/Albus_with_Newt.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190325014948" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8d/Albus_with_Newt.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190325014948" decoding="async" width="250" height="102" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Albus with Newt.jpg" data-image-key="Albus_with_Newt.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8d/Albus_with_Newt.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190325014948" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Albus_with_Newt.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore asking <a href="/wiki/Newton_Scamander" title="Newton Scamander">Newt Scamander</a> for help in <a href="/wiki/London" title="London">London</a>, <a href="/wiki/1927" title="1927">1927</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/1927" title="1927">1927</a>, when Grindelwald had escaped, Dumbledore, feeling that he would not be able to fight him, met with Newt in <a href="/wiki/London" title="London">London</a> to ask him for help. He sent his former student to <a href="/wiki/Paris" title="Paris">Paris</a> to find <a href="/wiki/Credence_Barebone" title="Credence Barebone">Credence Barebone</a>, who survived battle in New York, and rescue him from Grindelwald. He also gave Scamander the address for a '<a href="/wiki/Nicolas_Flamel%27s_house" class="mw-redirect" title="Nicolas Flamel&#39;s house">safe house</a>' where he can go if he needs to hide for a time.<sup id="cite_ref-COG_28-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COG-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup>   
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ac/Travers_Admonitors.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190325025112" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Travers Admonitors.gif" data-image-key="Travers_Admonitors.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ac/Travers_Admonitors.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190325025112" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ac/Travers_Admonitors.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190325025112" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ac/Travers_Admonitors.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190325025112" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Travers Admonitors.gif" data-image-key="Travers_Admonitors.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ac/Travers_Admonitors.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190325025112" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Travers_Admonitors.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Travers puting Dumbledore into Admonitors during interrogation</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The rumours of Newt's potential travel to <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">France</a> reached the British Ministry of Magic, and a delegation of <a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">Aurors</a>, including Newt's brother <a href="/wiki/Theseus_Scamander" title="Theseus Scamander">Theseus Scamander</a> and <a href="/wiki/Torquil_Travers" title="Torquil Travers">Torquil Travers</a>, was sent to Hogwarts Castle to question Dumbledore. Travers demanded that Dumbledore fight Grindelwald for him, but Albus refused, which angered Travers to the point that he cuffed Dumbledore into <a href="/wiki/Admonitor" title="Admonitor">Admonitors</a>, and forbade him from ever teaching Defence Against the Dark Arts again. Dumbledore turned to Theseus, who was last in leaving the classroom, and warned him that if he'd ever trusted him, he should not let Travers send him to <a href="/wiki/Gellert_Grindelwald%27s_Paris_rally" title="Gellert Grindelwald&#39;s Paris rally">Grindelwald's rally</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-COG_28-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COG-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup>  
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ec/Leta_talking_with_Dumbledore.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190122230319" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="123" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Leta talking with Dumbledore.jpg" data-image-key="Leta_talking_with_Dumbledore.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ec/Leta_talking_with_Dumbledore.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190122230319" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ec/Leta_talking_with_Dumbledore.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190122230319" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ec/Leta_talking_with_Dumbledore.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190122230319" decoding="async" width="250" height="123" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Leta talking with Dumbledore.jpg" data-image-key="Leta_talking_with_Dumbledore.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ec/Leta_talking_with_Dumbledore.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190122230319" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Leta_talking_with_Dumbledore.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore talking with Leta Lestrange about her past</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Moments later, in one of the classrooms, he met Leta Lestrange, who was also in the delegation, but had separated herself from the group of Aurors. Leta accused Albus of being the only one who did not consider her bad in her youth and stated that he was wrong about this. Dumbledore mentioned that rumours about her brother Corvus Lestrange, who was now believed to be Credence Barebone, must have been painful for her, which angered the witch, who interrupted his statement and added that he could not understand her, because he did not lose his brother. Dumbledore only replied that years ago he lost his sister, <a href="/wiki/Ariana_Dumbledore" title="Ariana Dumbledore">Ariana</a>. Ending the conversation, Albus advised her to get rid of regret because it was his inseparable companion since the death of his sister.<sup id="cite_ref-COG_28-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COG-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup>   
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a2/Dumbledore_Mirror_of_Erised.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190209142936" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="138" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dumbledore Mirror of Erised.gif" data-image-key="Dumbledore_Mirror_of_Erised.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a2/Dumbledore_Mirror_of_Erised.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190209142936" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a2/Dumbledore_Mirror_of_Erised.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190209142936" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a2/Dumbledore_Mirror_of_Erised.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190209142936" decoding="async" width="250" height="138" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dumbledore Mirror of Erised.gif" data-image-key="Dumbledore_Mirror_of_Erised.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a2/Dumbledore_Mirror_of_Erised.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190209142936" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dumbledore_Mirror_of_Erised.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore standing in front of the Mirror of Erised and seeing Gellert Grindelwald</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>One night, Dumbledore went to the <a href="/wiki/Room_of_Requirement" title="Room of Requirement">Room of Requirement</a>, where the <a href="/wiki/Mirror_of_Erised" title="Mirror of Erised">Mirror of Erised</a> was stored. At first, to his joy, he saw an old memory he still valued of himself and Grindelwald from the time when their friendship was at its peak that led to them sealing their bond with a blood pact in a barn, swearing to never fight each other. Dumbledore also saw Grindelwald himself from the present. Albus was longing for this meeting, while at the same time being very afraid of it, because he knew that he was the only person who could stop Grindelwald, and he could face the truth about who Ariana's killer was.<sup id="cite_ref-COG_28-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COG-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> 
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e9/Newt_and_Dumbledore_talking_at_Hogwarts.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190324230849" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Newt and Dumbledore talking at Hogwarts.jpg" data-image-key="Newt_and_Dumbledore_talking_at_Hogwarts.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e9/Newt_and_Dumbledore_talking_at_Hogwarts.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190324230849" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e9/Newt_and_Dumbledore_talking_at_Hogwarts.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190324230849" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e9/Newt_and_Dumbledore_talking_at_Hogwarts.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190324230849" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Newt and Dumbledore talking at Hogwarts.jpg" data-image-key="Newt_and_Dumbledore_talking_at_Hogwarts.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e9/Newt_and_Dumbledore_talking_at_Hogwarts.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190324230849" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Newt_and_Dumbledore_talking_at_Hogwarts.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Newt giving Dumbledore a blood pact pendant at Hogwarts</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After the <a href="/wiki/Gellert_Grindelwald%27s_Paris_rally" title="Gellert Grindelwald&#39;s Paris rally">Battle of the</a> <a href="/wiki/Lestrange_Mausoleum" title="Lestrange Mausoleum">Lestrange family Mausoleum</a>, Dumbledore was waiting for Newt at Hogwarts. Albus expressed his sadness over Leta's death at Grindelwald's hands. Then, the magizoologist gave him an object stolen by Newt's <a href="/wiki/Niffler" title="Niffler">Niffler</a>. It was the <a href="/wiki/Gellert_Grindelwald%27s_pendant" title="Gellert Grindelwald&#39;s pendant">pendant</a> of his former teacher's blood pact with Grindelwald, giving Albus the chance to destroy it, which would allow him to finally participate in the war and defeat the Dark wizard once and for all.<sup id="cite_ref-COG_28-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COG-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Meeting_Tom_Riddle">Meeting Tom Riddle</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=9" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Meeting Tom Riddle">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Meeting Tom Riddle"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/48/Young_voldie.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180720151022" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Young voldie.jpg" data-image-key="Young_voldie.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/48/Young_voldie.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180720151022" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/48/Young_voldie.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180720151022" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/48/Young_voldie.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180720151022" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Young voldie.jpg" data-image-key="Young_voldie.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/48/Young_voldie.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180720151022" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Young_voldie.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore meets Tom Riddle for the first time, 1938</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure><p>Dumbledore also served in recruiting students for Hogwarts. Most prominent among the students he recruited was <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Tom Riddle</a>, whom he found in <a href="/wiki/Wool%27s_Orphanage" title="Wool&#39;s Orphanage">Wool's Orphanage</a> in <a href="/wiki/1938" title="1938">1938</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_30-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> Alone of all the professors at Hogwarts, Dumbledore was not charmed by the natural charisma and cunning of Tom Riddle. In their first encounter, Dumbledore became immediately suspicious of his "<i>obvious instincts for cruelty, secrecy and domination</i>"<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_30-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> and resolved to keep a close eye on him during his studies at the school. As Dumbledore was not so easily taken in by his charming façade, Riddle came to despise and fear him.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_30-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> At some point after this, Dumbledore partook of <a href="/wiki/Bertie_Bott%27s_Every_Flavour_Beans" title="Bertie Bott&#39;s Every Flavour Beans">Bertie Bott's Every Flavour Beans</a>, at which point he had the unfortunate experience of tasting one flavoured like vomit. Ever since then, he lost his liking for them.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_7-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Professor_of_Transfiguration">Professor of Transfiguration</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=10" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Professor of Transfiguration">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Professor of Transfiguration"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets"><b>Albus Dumbledore</b>: "<i>What are you doing, wandering around this late, Tom?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Tom Riddle</b>: "<i>I had to see the headmaster, sir.</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Albus Dumbledore</b>: "<i>Well, hurry off to bed. Best not to roam the corridors these days. Not since…</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Dumbledore speaking to a young Tom Riddle at Hogwarts<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a6/Dumbledore_watching_Tom_Riddle.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180122221958" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="107" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dumbledore watching Tom Riddle.jpg" data-image-key="Dumbledore_watching_Tom_Riddle.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a6/Dumbledore_watching_Tom_Riddle.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180122221958" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a6/Dumbledore_watching_Tom_Riddle.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180122221958" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a6/Dumbledore_watching_Tom_Riddle.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180122221958" decoding="async" width="250" height="107" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dumbledore watching Tom Riddle.jpg" data-image-key="Dumbledore_watching_Tom_Riddle.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a6/Dumbledore_watching_Tom_Riddle.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180122221958" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dumbledore_watching_Tom_Riddle.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Professor Dumbledore talking with Tom Riddle during the first opening of the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a>, <a href="/wiki/1943" title="1943">1943</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>At an unknown point in or before <a href="/wiki/1943" title="1943">1943</a>, Dumbledore became the Professor of <a href="/wiki/Transfiguration_(class)" title="Transfiguration (class)">Transfiguration</a>. In 1943, several Muggle-born students were mysteriously <a href="/wiki/Petrification" title="Petrification">petrified</a> by a beast rumoured to have been released by the <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Heir of Slytherin</a> from the mythical Chamber of Secrets. Indeed, the final victim of the beast, <a href="/wiki/Myrtle_Warren" title="Myrtle Warren">Myrtle Warren</a>, was actually killed; this act seemed likely to ensure the permanent closure of the school, forcing Riddle to go back to the orphanage. While Dumbledore rightly suspected Riddle was behind the attacks, the aspiring Dark Wizard expertly framed Gryffindor student <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Rubeus Hagrid</a> as the perpetrator.<sup id="cite_ref-COS_31-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COS-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Riddle was able to pass off Hagrid's tamed <a href="/wiki/Acromantula" title="Acromantula">Acromantula</a>, <a href="/wiki/Aragog" title="Aragog">Aragog</a>, as the beast attacking students, resulting in Hagrid's expulsion and ensuring that Hogwarts remained open. Dumbledore was never able to uncover hard evidence implicating Riddle, however, he nonetheless kept a very close watch over Riddle, preventing him from opening the Chamber of Secrets again during his remaining years at Hogwarts. He was also able to convince the Headmaster to allow Hagrid to remain at the school as the groundskeeper-in-training.<sup id="cite_ref-COS_31-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COS-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Defeat_of_Gellert_Grindelwald"><a href="/wiki/Duel_between_Albus_Dumbledore_and_Gellert_Grindelwald" title="Duel between Albus Dumbledore and Gellert Grindelwald">Defeat of Gellert Grindelwald</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=11" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Defeat of Gellert Grindelwald">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Defeat of Gellert Grindelwald"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>Dumbledore is particularly famous for his defeat of the Dark Wizard Grindelwald in 1945.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Info on Dumbledore's <a href="/wiki/Chocolate_Frog_Card" title="Chocolate Frog Card">Chocolate Frog Card</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div><p>As Dumbledore was educating young wizards and witches, <a href="/wiki/Gellert_Grindelwald" title="Gellert Grindelwald">Gellert Grindelwald</a> was still at large in <a href="/wiki/Europe" title="Europe">Europe</a>, building up his army, and had already found one of the <a href="/wiki/Deathly_Hallows" title="Deathly Hallows">Deathly Hallows</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Elder_Wand" title="Elder Wand">Elder Wand</a>, which he used to continue terrorising the continent. Initially prevented from opposing Grindelwald directly because of the <a href="/wiki/Blood_pact" title="Blood pact">Blood pact</a> they once made, even once that was destroyed, Dumbledore still felt conflicted about going after his old friend. In spite of himself, he still felt a lingering love for the man Grindelwald had been, or rather, the man he had once convinced himself Grindelwald was and/or could be. More than anything, however, Dumbledore feared facing Grindelwald. While secure in his ability to defeat him in battle if it came to it, more than anything, Dumbledore was afraid Grindelwald could reveal to him that it had in fact been he himself who had cast the curse that killed Ariana. Having delayed pursuing him as long as he could, however, at the height of Grindelwald's power, in <a href="/wiki/1945" title="1945">1945</a>, Albus could no longer in good conscience turn a blind eye to the many atrocities of Grindelwald and his followers, and so he finally tracked his old friend down. Upon finding Grindelwald, Dumbledore engaged him in what would later be widely considered the greatest duel ever fought between two wizards. Dumbledore defeated Grindelwald and then brought him before the authorities of the magical world, and Grindelwald was imprisoned in the uppermost cell at <a href="/wiki/Nurmengard_Castle" title="Nurmengard Castle">Nurmengard</a>, while Dumbledore kept the Elder Wand for himself.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_22-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> Celebrated worldwide as the hero who put to rest the <a href="/wiki/Global_wizarding_war" title="Global wizarding war">Global wizarding war</a>, and ended Grindelwald's <i><a href="/wiki/For_the_Greater_Good" title="For the Greater Good">For the Greater Good</a></i> revolution of wizarding dominance over Muggles, Dumbledore was awarded the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_Merlin" title="Order of Merlin">Order of Merlin (First Class</a>), by <a href="/wiki/Leonard_Spencer-Moon" title="Leonard Spencer-Moon">Leonard Spencer-Moon</a>'s administration.<sup id="cite_ref-PMordermerlin_32-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PMordermerlin-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup>
</p><h3><span id="Aftermath_(1946–1969)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Aftermath_.281946.E2.80.931969.29">Aftermath <span class="template-c">(1946–1969)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=12" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Aftermath (1946–1969)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Aftermath (1946–1969)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Turning_down_power">Turning down power</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=13" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Turning down power">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Turning down power"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Resuming his career following this legendary event, Dumbledore taught several other students over the years, some of whom would become staunchly loyal to him and what he stood for, whereas others would become enemies, allying themselves with <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> in the latter's rise to power. Among these students were future <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> members <a href="/wiki/Arthur_Weasley" title="Arthur Weasley">Arthur Weasley</a> and <a href="/wiki/Molly_Weasley" title="Molly Weasley">Molly Prewett</a>, <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>-to-be <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Black</a> and <a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy" title="Lucius Malfoy">Lucius Malfoy</a>, as well as neutral parties, such as the one-day world-famous <a href="/wiki/Curse-Breaker" title="Curse-Breaker">Curse-Breaker</a> <a href="/wiki/Patricia_Rakepick" title="Patricia Rakepick">Patricia Rakepick</a>. During this time, he was offered the position of <a href="/wiki/Minister_for_Magic" title="Minister for Magic">Minister for Magic</a> several times, but he turned down the offer every time, remembering how his quest for power had been his weakness in the past.
