It was around this time that he encountered a <a href="/wiki/House-elf" title="House-elf">house-elf</a> named <a href="/wiki/Hokey" title="Hokey">Hokey</a>. Before she died, he took a memory from her, in which <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Tom Riddle</a> showed his interest towards the magical antiques of a recently deceased <a href="/wiki/Hepzibah_Smith" title="Hepzibah Smith">Hepzibah Smith</a>. This memory was not sufficient evidence to show Hokey's innocence, as it only proved that Riddle was aware of the artefacts' existence.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_30-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Becoming_Headmaster_of_Hogwarts">Becoming Headmaster of Hogwarts</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=14" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Becoming Headmaster of Hogwarts">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Becoming Headmaster of Hogwarts"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/10/Screenshot_2290.png/revision/latest?cb=20150627222611" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="195" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Screenshot 2290.png" data-image-key="Screenshot_2290.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/10/Screenshot_2290.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150627222611" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/10/Screenshot_2290.png/revision/latest?cb=20150627222611" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/10/Screenshot_2290.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150627222611" decoding="async" width="250" height="195" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Screenshot 2290.png" data-image-key="Screenshot_2290.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/10/Screenshot_2290.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150627222611" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Screenshot_2290.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Headmaster Dumbledore welcoming students to the new school term</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>By the mid-<a href="/wiki/1960s" title="1960s">1960s</a>, the amount of Dark magical activity across the country was growing steadily, and while few knew what was behind the mounting attacks and sightings, this was but the precursor to <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>'s first rise to power. Aware that it was only a matter of time before his former student made his presence and intent known to the wizarding community as a whole, and already <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">preparing to oppose</a> him, by the time the <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> began recruiting Dark creatures to help them overthrow the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-PM2_33-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PM2-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> Dumbledore already had spies in their midst reporting to him. It was through these contacts that Dumbledore first learned of the attack on a young boy by the name of <a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin" title="Remus Lupin">Remus Lupin</a>, who had been infected with <a href="/wiki/Lycanthropy" title="Lycanthropy">lycanthropy</a> by a <a href="/wiki/Fenrir_Greyback" title="Fenrir Greyback">Fenrir Greyback</a>. Rather than trying to manage his condition, however, the attacker had instead made it his mission in life to infect as many people as possible and was harbouring grand plans of raising an army of werewolves big enough to take over the wizarding world; having even earned notoriety for targeting children with the intent of raising them away from other witches and wizards and teaching them to despise regular humans for that very reason. Knowing how this would have had to have impacted the <a href="/wiki/Lupin_family" title="Lupin family">Lupin family</a>, the old Transfiguration teacher could not help but be sympathetic to their predicament. As fortune would have it, however, a blessing in disguise presented itself when the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Board_of_Governors" title="Hogwarts Board of Governors">Hogwarts Board of Governors</a> was faced with the decision of finding a suitable candidate to succeed <a href="/wiki/Armando_Dippet" title="Armando Dippet">Armando Dippet</a> in the post of <a href="/wiki/Headmaster" title="Headmaster">Headmaster</a> and judged Professor Dumbledore to be the best man for the job;<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> which in turn granted him the authority to properly accommodate the Lupins when the time came for Remus to attend school.
</p><p>Shortly after Dumbledore assumed the position, by which time he had already relocated to the <a href="/wiki/Headmaster%27s_Tower" title="Headmaster&#39;s Tower">Headmaster's Tower</a> and filled his new <a href="/wiki/Headmaster%27s_Office" title="Headmaster&#39;s Office">study</a> with a number of curious magical instruments that had formerly been housed in his old classroom, Tom Riddle, now known exclusively as Lord Voldemort, approached him with the same request he had proposed to Dippet before him, to be allowed to return to Hogwarts as a teacher. Dumbledore, who knew of Voldemort's illicit activities since he left <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a> and suspected that he might have meant to use the position as means of recruiting more <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">followers</a>, turned down his application. This led Voldemort to angrily <a href="/wiki/Jinx_on_the_post_of_Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts_teacher" title="Jinx on the post of Defence Against the Dark Arts teacher">jinx</a> the position of <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> instructor, preventing anyone from holding the position for more than a single school year. What was more; while being entrusted the stewardship of the school was, in and of itself, an honour and a privilege, it also meant that he was henceforth expected to shoulder the responsibility of making all the difficult decisions that came with leadership. On such occasions, Dumbledore would step out into the <a href="/wiki/Clock_Tower_Courtyard" title="Clock Tower Courtyard">Clock Tower Courtyard</a>, where he found the quiet night and crisp air helpful in regard to putting one's troubles in perspective,<sup id="cite_ref-HMy1ch6_35-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HMy1ch6-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> and developed a habit of pacing around his new office a lot, especially in times when the security of the castle was breached.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_36-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-POAF_37-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POAF-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> On occasion, he would also see students in his office, be it because of a misdemeanour that had to be addressed, or because one of the pupils sought redress during conflicts with their peers, such as <a href="/wiki/Bertha_Jorkins" title="Bertha Jorkins">Bertha Jorkins</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_38-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> At some point following his appointment, Professor Dumbledore began to offer to <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore_Homework_Help" title="Albus Dumbledore Homework Help">help students with their homework</a>, whom he would meet every Friday in <a href="/wiki/Classroom_E-13" title="Classroom E-13">Classroom E-13</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-HPPS_39-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HPPS-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> Fond of festivities in general, he would also sometimes stand for the entertainment during the annual <a href="/wiki/Hallowe%27en_Feast" title="Hallowe&#39;en Feast">Hallowe'en Feast</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Great_Hall" title="Great Hall">Great Hall</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-HM_y1_Hallowe.27en_40-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HM_y1_Hallowe.27en-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>As the day neared when young <a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin" title="Remus Lupin">Remus Lupin</a> would be of an eligible age to begin his magical education, Dumbledore wasted little time in making the necessary preparations for the young man's arrival: To this end, Dumbledore arranged for a <a href="/wiki/Shrieking_Shack" title="Shrieking Shack">house</a> to be built a little way above the rest of the nearby <a href="/wiki/Hogsmeade" title="Hogsmeade">Hogsmeade</a>; perched atop a hill overlooking the village. Once finished, the Headmaster applied the appropriate spells to provide Remus with a safe and secure place for his transformations that could contain even a fully grown werewolf, if necessary. Next, he arranged for an underground passage <a href="/wiki/Gouging_Spell" title="Gouging Spell">to be made</a> on the school grounds to give Remus an easy and discreet way of accessing the building when necessary, and had a <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Whomping_Willow" title="Hogwarts Whomping Willow">Whomping Willow</a> planted over the opening; both to hide it from view, and as a security measure to stop anyone from coming across the future pupil whilst he was dangerous. Shortly before <a href="/wiki/10_March" title="10 March">10 March</a> <a href="/wiki/1971" title="1971">1971</a>, Dumbledore showed up unannounced at the doorstep of <a href="/wiki/Lyall_Lupin" title="Lyall Lupin">Lyall</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hope_Howell" title="Hope Howell">Hope Lupin</a> to invite their son to attend school. Well aware that their initial reaction, namely to try and keep him from entering their home, stemmed from fear more than anything else, the Headmaster took the liberty of finding his own way into the house. Five minutes later, Dumbledore was sitting on their living room floor by the fireplace, eating crumpets and playing <a href="/wiki/Gobstones" title="Gobstones">Gobstones</a> with Remus.
</p><p>After explaining to the three of them that he was aware of their situation and, more importantly, that as far as he was concerned, there was no reason why Remus should not be able to attend Hogwarts, as long as special precautions were taken to ensure the safety of both Remus and the other students, a mutual understanding was reached, and it was eventually agreed that young Mr Lupin would indeed present himself at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Castle" title="Hogwarts Castle">Hogwarts Castle</a> for the <a href="/wiki/Start-of-Term_Feast" title="Start-of-Term Feast">Start-of-Term</a>. This would forever earn Dumbledore Remus' gratitude, as most others would simply have forbidden the boy from even setting foot in the school. When <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a> found out Remus' secret, Dumbledore forbade him from repeating it to anyone.
</p>
<h3><span id="First_Wizarding_War_(1970–1981)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="First_Wizarding_War_.281970.E2.80.931981.29">First Wizarding War <span class="template-c">(1970–1981)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=15" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: First Wizarding War (1970–1981)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: First Wizarding War (1970–1981)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows"><b>Severus Snape</b>: "<i>Hide them all, then. Keep her — them — safe. Please.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Dumbledore</b>: "<i>And what will you give me in return, Severus?</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Severus Snape</b>: "<i>In — in return? Anything.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Snape pleading with Dumbledore to protect <a href="/wiki/Lily_Potter" title="Lily Potter">Lily Potter</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ad/The_Marauders_in_Order_of_the_Pheonix_image.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180720155740" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="The Marauders in Order of the Pheonix image.jpg" data-image-key="The_Marauders_in_Order_of_the_Pheonix_image.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ad/The_Marauders_in_Order_of_the_Pheonix_image.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180720155740" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ad/The_Marauders_in_Order_of_the_Pheonix_image.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180720155740" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ad/The_Marauders_in_Order_of_the_Pheonix_image.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180720155740" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="The Marauders in Order of the Pheonix image.jpg" data-image-key="The_Marauders_in_Order_of_the_Pheonix_image.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ad/The_Marauders_in_Order_of_the_Pheonix_image.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180720155740" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:The_Marauders_in_Order_of_the_Pheonix_image.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Some of the members of the original Order of the Phoenix</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> started his first rise to power in 1970, Dumbledore founded the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a>, a secret organisation of witches and wizards willing to risk their lives to fight Voldemort and his <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>. As the only wizard Voldemort was ever truly afraid of, Dumbledore was the perfect leader of the organisation and was a significant contributor to the war effort.
</p><p>Later on in the war, Dumbledore was approached by another person who also wanted a job at Hogwarts: <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney" title="Sybill Trelawney">Sybill Trelawney</a>, who applied to become the new <a href="/wiki/Professor" title="Professor">professor</a> of <a href="/wiki/Divination_(class)" title="Divination (class)">Divination</a>, a subject Dumbledore disliked and barely considered a part of necessary education for young wizards and witches. Dumbledore gave her a chance because she was the great-great-granddaughter of the celebrated <a href="/wiki/Seer" title="Seer">Seer</a> <a href="/wiki/Cassandra_Trelawney" title="Cassandra Trelawney">Cassandra Trelawney</a>. To his disappointment, when he was interviewing Sybill at the <a href="/wiki/Hog%27s_Head" class="mw-redirect" title="Hog&#39;s Head">Hog's Head</a>, he came to the conclusion that she was not a real Seer. However, as Dumbledore was about to leave, Trelawney fell into a real trance and made a<a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney%27s_first_prophecy" title="Sybill Trelawney&#39;s first prophecy"> prophecy</a> about the birth of the one that would have the power to vanquish the Dark Lord, who would be born to those "who have thrice defied him, born as the seventh month dies".<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_41-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> This astonished Dumbledore, but as it turned out, the Death Eater <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a> had overheard most of the prophecy but had been caught in the act of spying and ejected from the tavern by <a href="/wiki/Aberforth_Dumbledore" title="Aberforth Dumbledore">Aberforth Dumbledore</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_30-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> Dumbledore hired Trelawney in order to protect her from the Death Eaters.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="The_Cursed_Vaults">The Cursed Vaults</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=16" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: The Cursed Vaults">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: The Cursed Vaults"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>While his presence at Hogwarts effectively ensured that the Dark Lord and his followers never strayed too close to the school, Dumbledore was still unable to prevent the security of the castle from being breached when <a href="/wiki/Jacob_(Hogwarts_student)" title="Jacob (Hogwarts student)">one of his students</a> embarked on a foolhardy quest to uncover the secrets of the fabled <a href="/wiki/Cursed_Vaults" title="Cursed Vaults">Cursed Vaults</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-HMy1ch1_42-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HMy1ch1-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> presumably in order to get his hands on the gold, prophecies and various other powerful magical artefacts myth would have it had been sealed within them.<sup id="cite_ref-HMy1ch6_35-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HMy1ch6-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> Not alone in this endeavour, however, assisting him in this search were two of his friends, <a href="/wiki/Duncan_Ashe" title="Duncan Ashe">Duncan Ashe</a> and <a href="/wiki/Olivia_Green" title="Olivia Green">Olivia Green</a>, who were in <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ravenclaw" title="Ravenclaw">Ravenclaw House</a>, respectively.<sup id="cite_ref-HMy5ch3_43-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HMy5ch3-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> This was not the first time that a student was known to have looked for the vaults, the last one being the former <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a> student, <a href="/wiki/Patricia_Rakepick" title="Patricia Rakepick">Patricia Rakepick</a>, who likewise was a firm believer in the existence of the vaults and had previously tried to warn the staff about them, but whose claims were dismissed due to a lack of evidence.<sup id="cite_ref-HMy4ch1_44-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HMy4ch1-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> In the case of the pupil in question, however, it would seem like there was some merit to the old tales. Admittedly intrigued by their soon-to-be notorious ringleader, who was, after all, judged to be thoughtful and considerate by some,<sup id="cite_ref-HMy3ch1_45-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HMy3ch1-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> while simultaneously being one of the most talented and rebellious students of his time at the school,<sup id="cite_ref-HMy1ch2_46-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HMy1ch2-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> the Headmaster took a personal interest in young <a href="/wiki/Jacob_(Hogwarts_student)" title="Jacob (Hogwarts student)">Jacob</a>, and even decided to help him nurture his gift upon discovering that Jacob was a born <a href="/wiki/Legilimency" title="Legilimency">Legilimens</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-HMy5ch19_47-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HMy5ch19-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>As time passed, however, Dumbledore could not help but notice how Jacob became increasingly obsessive in his search for the vaults and, he sensed, changed because of it. The boy become ever more impulsive and reckless, leading to the violation of "all sorts of school rules" and endangerment of both himself and others in the process. Eventually, Dumbledore began to grow concerned that this fixation might even drive him to madness. Unable to overlook their pursuit for the vaults for these reasons, he was known to have reprimanded both Jacob and Mr Ashe for their many indiscretions on at least one occasion.<sup id="cite_ref-HMy5ch19_47-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HMy5ch19-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> This did not dissuade the adventurous youths, however, who continued their search despite Dumbledore's firm words of caution. Some time later, the Headmaster became aware that Jacob had even snapped his own wand in two over the course of this quest, which greatly shocked him.<sup id="cite_ref-HMy1ch9_48-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HMy1ch9-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> Unaware at the time that he had only done so in order to pay the price required to break the curse on the <a href="/wiki/Vault_of_Fear" title="Vault of Fear">Vault of Fear</a>, this was a contributing factor to his eventual decision to terminate Jacob's attendance, seeing as how it stood to reason that a wizard desperate enough to break his own wand would be willing to do anything to get what he wanted.
</p><p>In the end, their hunt for the vaults ended in tragedy when Duncan was killed while attempting to brew a particularly potent <a href="/wiki/Erumpent_Potion" title="Erumpent Potion">Erumpent Potion</a> in an effort to get past one of the obstacles standing between them and one of the Cursed Vaults.<sup id="cite_ref-HMy5ch7_49-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HMy5ch7-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> No longer able to turn a blind eye to the magnitude of what had just transpired, Dumbledore notified the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a> about Duncan's untimely demise, which sent two <a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">Aurors</a> to bring Jacob in for questioning about the incident. Having found him at the <a href="/wiki/Three_Broomsticks_Inn" title="Three Broomsticks Inn">Three Broomsticks Inn</a> in <a href="/wiki/Hogsmeade" title="Hogsmeade">Hogsmeade</a> village, they apprehended him and took him away.<sup id="cite_ref-HMy3ch3_50-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HMy3ch3-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> During the interrogation, Jacob falsely admitted to having pressured his friend into making the potion as part of their bid for the vaults.<sup id="cite_ref-HMy5ch7_49-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HMy5ch7-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> In light of Jacob's confession, Dumbledore had no other choice but to <a href="/wiki/Discipline_at_Hogwarts#Expulsion" title="Discipline at Hogwarts">expel</a> him.<sup id="cite_ref-HMy1ch1_42-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HMy1ch1-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> Duncan Ashe was not the first casualty in their foolhardy quest, unfortunately, nor was he the last. Olivia Green met a similar fate, and every time one of the vaults were disturbed, another curse was triggered and unleashed upon the school.
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Cursed_ice" title="Cursed ice">Cursed ice</a> began to appear and spread throughout the castle, turning whole rooms into crystalline prisons and threatened to encase the whole school,<sup id="cite_ref-HMy2ch1_51-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HMy2ch1-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> severely injuring several of the students. A <a href="/wiki/Sleepwalking_curse" title="Sleepwalking curse">Sleepwalking curse</a> was also triggered, placing students in a deep slumber and causing them to mindlessly wander off into the <a href="/wiki/Forbidden_Forest" title="Forbidden Forest">Forbidden Forest</a> in the direction of <a href="/wiki/Forest_Vault" title="Forest Vault">one of the vaults</a>, where those whom the staff failed to stop were, due to their condition and inability to defend themselves, ravaged and some even outright devoured by the dangerous creatures within. Others, <a href="/wiki/Poppy_Pomfrey" title="Poppy Pomfrey">Madam Pomfrey</a> observed, simply never woke up again.<sup id="cite_ref-HMy4ch1_44-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HMy4ch1-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> There were also a curse that was rather unique in that it trapped the castle's residents <a href="/wiki/Portrait_curse" title="Portrait curse">inside portraits</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> Although Dumbledore and the rest of the staff ultimately managed to contain the curses and got the situation under control, the faculty nevertheless denied any knowledge that the vaults actually existed, quite possibly hoping to dissuade other students from pursuing the vaults as well, by quieting down the attention around them after Jacob's removal from the school was so prominently covered at the time in the <i><a href="/wiki/Daily_Prophet" title="Daily Prophet">Daily Prophet</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>At some point after all of this took place, however, Dumbledore became aware of the existence of a secretive cabal known simply by the initial '<a href="/wiki/R" title="R">R</a>', which had become active in the <a href="/wiki/Wizarding_world" title="Wizarding world">wizarding world</a> some time prior. A dissenting group of dangerous <a href="/wiki/Dark_Wizard" title="Dark Wizard">Dark Wizards</a> about which very little was known, yet whose ruthless pursuit of 'enlightenment and <a href="/wiki/Immortality" title="Immortality">immortality</a>'<sup id="cite_ref-HMy5ch7_49-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HMy5ch7-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> had given rise to various clandestine operations around the world<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> and ultimately led them to turn their attention towards Hogwarts. Their involvement in the disturbance of the Cursed Vaults had been a covert one, however. Unbeknownst to Dumbledore and the rest of the staff at the time, this group had made both Jacob and Duncan unwitting pawns in their bid for the vaults,<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> until finally in the fullness of time they had made their presence known to the students involved. From that point on, coercion had been a driving force behind Jacob's obsession with the vaults, by threatening to make those Jacob cared about '<a href="/wiki/Death" title="Death">disappear</a>' if he failed to cooperate, while simultaneously hanging a superficial promise of future membership over his head. It had in fact been 'R' that pressured Duncan Ashe into making the potion that cost him his life, and Jacob had simply taken the blame out of fear that they would make good on their threats had he exposed them.<sup id="cite_ref-HMy5ch7_49-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HMy5ch7-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Thus, any decision the Headmaster might have meant to make about revoking Jacob's expulsion upon said discovery, however, was rendered inconsequential when, a few months later, Jacob ran away from home and rumours began to circulate that he had earned quite a bit of notoriety in the figurative underworld of wizarding Britain, with former teachers even describing him as the "most feared wizard in <a href="/wiki/Knockturn_Alley" title="Knockturn Alley">Knockturn Alley</a>."<sup id="cite_ref-HMy5ch7_49-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HMy5ch7-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> Realising that <a href="/wiki/Jacob_(Hogwarts_student)" title="Jacob (Hogwarts student)">Jacob</a> must have continued to pursue the vaults for 'R' as a means of keeping his loved ones safe;<sup id="cite_ref-HMy5ch3_43-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HMy5ch3-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> even though the Headmaster immediately recognised the rumour that he had even become a <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a> under <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a>'s command for the empty hearsay it was,<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup> anything he could have done to help him likewise became rather inappreciable when Jacob subsequently went mysteriously missing without a trace.<sup id="cite_ref-HMy1ch1_42-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HMy1ch1-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>With Jacob gone and thus unable to protect <a href="/wiki/Jacob%27s_family" title="Jacob&#39;s family">his kin</a>, and given the possibility that the Cabal, whose members were still unknown and very much at large, might make good on their threats had he moved against them, Dumbledore initially kept his findings to himself. As such, there were only three people who knew the full story once the dust had settled: <a href="/wiki/Jacob_(Hogwarts_student)" title="Jacob (Hogwarts student)">Jacob</a>, <a href="/wiki/Duncan_Ashe" title="Duncan Ashe">Duncan Ashe</a>, who had returned as a <a href="/wiki/Ghost" title="Ghost">ghost</a>, and the Headmaster himself.<sup id="cite_ref-HMy5ch7_49-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HMy5ch7-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> Which was not to say, however, that Dumbledore did not have every intention of probing the situation as closely as he could under the circumstances. Having prudently decided that the best way to proceed in order to prevent this new enemy from knowing that he was onto them was with much care and caution, Dumbledore tasked his old friend, veteran <a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">Auror</a> and brother-in-arms in the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a>, <a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">Alastor Moody</a>, with investigating 'R',<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup> who henceforth monitored their activities off-the-books.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="Between_the_wars_(1981–1995)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Between_the_wars_.281981.E2.80.931995.29">Between the wars <span class="template-c">(1981–1995)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=17" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Between the wars (1981–1995)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Between the wars (1981–1995)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Fall_of_the_Dark_Lord">Fall of the Dark Lord</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=18" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Fall of the Dark Lord">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Fall of the Dark Lord"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-12498.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180104174538" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="106" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-12498.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-12498.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-12498.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180104174538" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-12498.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180104174538" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-12498.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180104174538" decoding="async" width="250" height="106" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-12498.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-12498.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-12498.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180104174538" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-12498.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Albus Dumbledore in 1981, at age 100, during the trial of <a href="/wiki/Igor_Karkaroff" title="Igor Karkaroff">Igor Karkaroff</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Still, the wizarding war raged beyond the walls of Hogwarts: Shortly before the Potters' deaths, Dumbledore discovered that James's <a href="/wiki/Cloak_of_Invisibility" title="Cloak of Invisibility">Cloak of Invisibility</a> was, in fact, one of the <a href="/wiki/Deathly_Hallows" title="Deathly Hallows">Deathly Hallows</a>. Although Dumbledore had long given up his desire to unite the Hallows and become Master of Death, he could not resist the thought of studying the Cloak. To that end, he borrowed it from James while James and Lilly were in hiding. Later, Severus Snape approached Dumbledore, having already told Voldemort about the Prophecy. Snape was shocked by the fact that Voldemort had concluded that the prophecy was about <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, the son of <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_I" title="James Potter I">James Potter</a>, and Snape's own beloved childhood friend, Lily Evans. Dumbledore agreed, on the basis that Snape worked as a double agent for the Order. Dumbledore made arrangements to ensure the safety of the three; he advised them to stay hidden in their house in <a href="/wiki/Godric%27s_Hollow" title="Godric&#39;s Hollow">Godric's Hollow</a>, which was protected by a <a href="/wiki/Fidelius_Charm" title="Fidelius Charm">Fidelius Charm</a>. However, their <a href="/wiki/Secret-Keeper" class="mw-redirect" title="Secret-Keeper">Secret-Keeper</a> (believed by Dumbledore and everyone else to be <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a>, but was in truth <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Peter Pettigrew</a>) betrayed them, resulting in James and Lily's deaths at Voldemort's hands. However, as Voldemort attempted to murder Harry the curse backfired due to the protection provided by Lily Potter's love for her son and destroyed his body. This unfortunate occurrence provided Dumbledore with ownership of two of the Hallows, having already confirmed James' old cloak was indeed the one of legend.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4a/BumbleboreMcGeegeeHARRY.PNG/revision/latest?cb=20161127213858" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="163" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="BumbleboreMcGeegeeHARRY.PNG" data-image-key="BumbleboreMcGeegeeHARRY.PNG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4a/BumbleboreMcGeegeeHARRY.PNG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161127213858" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4a/BumbleboreMcGeegeeHARRY.PNG/revision/latest?cb=20161127213858" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4a/BumbleboreMcGeegeeHARRY.PNG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161127213858" decoding="async" width="250" height="163" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="BumbleboreMcGeegeeHARRY.PNG" data-image-key="BumbleboreMcGeegeeHARRY.PNG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4a/BumbleboreMcGeegeeHARRY.PNG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161127213858" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:BumbleboreMcGeegeeHARRY.PNG" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Albus Dumbledore delivering <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> with Minerva McGonagall</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Presumably well aware that Lord Voldemort wasn't truly vanquished, Dumbledore made sure that Harry would be kept safe with his family, the <a href="/wiki/Dursley_family" title="Dursley family">Dursleys</a>, despite them not being selected as his guardians in the event of James and Lily's death, as his spells ensured that Voldemort could not harm Harry there as long as he could have a home with those with whom he was related by blood. He convinced Snape to help him protect Harry, although years later Dumbledore secretly planned to allow Voldemort to kill Harry in the end, which would destroy the piece of Voldemort's <a href="/wiki/Soul" title="Soul">soul</a> inside Harry. However, he also hoped to influence Harry into such a person who would willingly sacrifice his life for the greater good, allowing him the chance to choose between life and death in the end, guessing correctly the significance of such an act. Shortly thereafter, Dumbledore gave Snape employment at Hogwarts as the <a href="/wiki/Potions_(class)" title="Potions (class)">Potions</a> master, and later defended Snape against the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a>, who were rounding up and arresting remaining Death Eaters. Dumbledore attended many <a href="/wiki/Council_of_Magical_Law" title="Council of Magical Law">Death Eater trials</a>, including that of the <a href="/wiki/Lestrange_family" title="Lestrange family">Lestranges</a> and <a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">Barty Crouch, Jnr</a>. He was also a witness to Igor Karkaroff's testimony which secured his release from Azkaban in return for the names of fellow Death Eaters. With Harry safe and <a href="/wiki/Arabella_Figg" title="Arabella Figg">certain</a> <a href="/wiki/Dedalus_Diggle" title="Dedalus Diggle">members</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> and <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">allies of their cause</a> keeping watch over him and reporting back to Dumbledore, he continued his work as the brilliant if eccentric Headmaster of his beloved school.
</p>
<h4><span id="1984–1985"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="1984.E2.80.931985">1984–1985</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=19" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: 1984–1985">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: 1984–1985"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Start-of-Term">Start-of-Term</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=20" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Start-of-Term">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Start-of-Term"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/1984_sorting.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200403034410" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="141" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="1984 sorting.jpg" data-image-key="1984_sorting.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/1984_sorting.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200403034410" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/1984_sorting.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200403034410" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/1984_sorting.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200403034410" decoding="async" width="250" height="141" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="1984 sorting.jpg" data-image-key="1984_sorting.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/1984_sorting.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200403034410" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:1984_sorting.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore at the Sorting ceremony of 1984</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>At the <a href="/wiki/Start-of-Term_Feast" title="Start-of-Term Feast">Start-of-Term Feast</a> during the <a href="/wiki/1984%E2%80%931985_school_year" title="1984–1985 school year">1984–1985 school year</a>, Professor Dumbledore was seated in the magnificent golden chair at the centre of the <a href="/wiki/High_Table" title="High Table">High Table</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Great_Hall" title="Great Hall">Great Hall</a>, looking on with interest as Professor McGonagall presided over the annual <a href="/wiki/Sorting_ceremony" title="Sorting ceremony">sorting ceremony</a> and the most recent addition to the student body, as they were placed in their allotted houses. Among the newcomers, he observed, was the <a href="/wiki/Charles_Weasley" title="Charles Weasley">second oldest son</a> of <a href="/wiki/Arthur_Weasley" title="Arthur Weasley">Arthur</a> and <a href="/wiki/Molly_Weasley" title="Molly Weasley">Molly Weasley</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Nymphadora_Tonks" title="Nymphadora Tonks">daughter</a> of <a href="/wiki/Andromeda_Tonks" title="Andromeda Tonks">Andromeda Black</a> and her <a href="/wiki/Muggle-borns" class="mw-redirect" title="Muggle-borns">Muggle-borns</a> husband <a href="/wiki/Edward_Tonks" title="Edward Tonks">Edward Tonks</a>. The former, to no one's surprise, was placed in <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor House</a>, whereas the latter defied her mother's long history of notoriously <a href="/wiki/Pure-blood_supremacy" title="Pure-blood supremacy">pro-</a><a href="/wiki/Pure-blood" title="Pure-blood">pure-blood</a> fanatics by being sorted into <a href="/wiki/Hufflepuff" title="Hufflepuff">Hufflepuff</a>. The new batch also included <a href="/wiki/Tulip_Karasu" title="Tulip Karasu">Tulip Karasu</a>, the young daughter of two members of the <a href="/wiki/Department_of_Magical_Law_Enforcement" title="Department of Magical Law Enforcement">Department of Magical Law Enforcement</a> at <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Magic" title="Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a>, whom Dumbledore presumably would be familiar with given his ties to said institution and affiliation with the <a href="/wiki/Wizengamot" title="Wizengamot">Wizengamot</a>. <a href="/wiki/Merula_Snyde" title="Merula Snyde">Merula Snyde</a> and <a href="/wiki/Barnaby_Lee" title="Barnaby Lee">Barnaby Lee</a>, both of whom had parents who had earned notoriety as <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> during the wizarding war and been sent to <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a> for their many atrocities, found their way to <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin House</a>. <a href="/wiki/Rowan_Khanna" title="Rowan Khanna">Rowan Khanna</a>, the scion of a wizarding family that owned a rather <a href="/wiki/Khanna_Farms" title="Khanna Farms">well-known tree farm</a> famous for supplying various high-quality wood for the manufacture of <a href="/wiki/Wand" title="Wand">wands</a> and <a href="/wiki/Broomstick" title="Broomstick">broomsticks</a>. Perhaps most notably, however, <a href="/wiki/Jacob_(disambiguation)" title="Jacob (disambiguation)">Jacob</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Jacob%27s_sibling" title="Jacob&#39;s sibling">younger sibling</a> was sorted this year, whose arrival was met with much muttering of their brother's disappearance by staff and fellow students alike.<sup id="cite_ref-HMy1ch2_46-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HMy1ch2-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After this time-honoured tradition had ran its course, Dumbledore rose from his seat and took place at the <a href="/wiki/Owl_Lecturn" title="Owl Lecturn">Owl Lecturn</a> and held the customary welcoming speech, explained how the <a href="/wiki/House_points" title="House points">house point system</a> worked and encouraged them all to do their utmost to be a credit to the new house. It did not take long, however, before he was approached by <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Professor Snape</a>, who informed him that he and the <a href="/wiki/Charms_Master" title="Charms Master">Charms Master</a>, <a href="/wiki/Filius_Flitwick" title="Filius Flitwick">Professor Flitwick</a>, had caught the <a href="/wiki/Jacob%27s_sibling" title="Jacob&#39;s sibling">younger sibling</a> and one of the other <a href="/wiki/First_year" title="First year">first-years</a>, <a href="/wiki/Merula_Snyde" title="Merula Snyde">Merula Snyde</a>, <a href="/wiki/Duelling" title="Duelling">duelling</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Clock_Tower_Courtyard" title="Clock Tower Courtyard">Clocktower Courtyard</a>. And though Snape was of the opinion that the latter pupil should be expelled for this misdemeanour, the Headmaster on the other hand, was as always inclined to exercise a modicum of patience with students that broke the school rules without any sort of malicious intent behind it. Quick to reject his suggestion as a punishment that did not to fit the crime, Dumbledore limited the <a href="/wiki/Potions_Master" title="Potions Master">Potions Master</a> to mete out more conventional methods of discipline. Almost immediately afterwards, however, Snape returned with some most disconcerting news. The <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Caretaker" title="Hogwarts Caretaker">Caretaker</a>, had found <a href="/wiki/Cursed_ice" title="Cursed ice">Cursed ice</a> in a room one of the farthest <a href="/wiki/Upstairs_Corridor" title="Upstairs Corridor">corridor</a> on the east end of the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Castle#Fifth_Floor" title="Hogwarts Castle">fifth floor</a>;<sup id="cite_ref-HMy1ch6_35-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HMy1ch6-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> a sign that someone had been tampering with <a href="/wiki/Vault_of_Ice" title="Vault of Ice">one of</a> the Cursed Vaults.
</p><p>In the aftermath of this discovery, the faculty successfully managed to keep it from spreading any further and securely sealed up the room afterwards, and placed it under guard by <a href="/wiki/Argus_Filch" title="Argus Filch">Mr Filch</a><sup id="cite_ref-HMy1ch6_35-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HMy1ch6-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Mrs_Norris" title="Mrs Norris">Mrs Norris</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-HMy1ch9_48-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HMy1ch9-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> Acknowledging that his own knowledge on the vaults and whatever horrors they contained both fell rather short of enabling him to adequately address the threat that they posed to the security of the other denizens of the castle, however, the Headmaster soon reached out to a <a href="/wiki/Patricia_Rakepick" title="Patricia Rakepick">former student</a> of his, who had since become a renowned <a href="/wiki/Curse-Breaker" title="Curse-Breaker">expert</a> on the <a href="/wiki/Curse-Breaker" title="Curse-Breaker">subject</a>, and whose extensive research into the Cursed Vaults in her youth would hopefully be of some help to the staff in bringing the matter to a quick and decisive conclusion.<sup id="cite_ref-HMy1ch9_48-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HMy1ch9-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h5><span id="The_Howling_Hallowe'en"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="The_Howling_Hallowe.27en">The Howling Hallowe'en</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=21" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: The Howling Hallowe&#039;en">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: The Howling Hallowe&#039;en"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/43/Dumbledore_with_Jacob%27s_sibling_Hallowe%27en_Decorations_HM.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200601004621" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="152" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dumbledore with Jacob&#39;s sibling Hallowe&#39;en Decorations HM.jpg" data-image-key="Dumbledore_with_Jacob&#39;s_sibling_Hallowe&#39;en_Decorations_HM.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/43/Dumbledore_with_Jacob%27s_sibling_Hallowe%27en_Decorations_HM.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200601004621" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/43/Dumbledore_with_Jacob%27s_sibling_Hallowe%27en_Decorations_HM.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200601004621" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/43/Dumbledore_with_Jacob%27s_sibling_Hallowe%27en_Decorations_HM.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200601004621" decoding="async" width="250" height="152" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dumbledore with Jacob&#39;s sibling Hallowe&#39;en Decorations HM.jpg" data-image-key="Dumbledore_with_Jacob&#39;s_sibling_Hallowe&#39;en_Decorations_HM.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/43/Dumbledore_with_Jacob%27s_sibling_Hallowe%27en_Decorations_HM.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200601004621" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dumbledore_with_Jacob%27s_sibling_Hallowe%27en_Decorations_HM.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore discussing Hallowe'en decorations with Jacob's sibling</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As the always much-anticipated <a href="/wiki/Hallowe%27en_Feast" title="Hallowe&#39;en Feast">Hallowe'en Feast</a> drew ever closer and the faculty prepared the castle for the annual festivities, Dumbledore decided to make that year's celebration one with "more of a personal touch" than usual. To this end, the Headmaster requested several students to meet him in the <a href="/wiki/Great_Hall" title="Great Hall">Great Hall</a>, where he proceeded to ask whether or not any of them might be persuaded to lend him and the teachers a hand in the decoration process. Delighted to find that a number of volunteers from the student body was willing to take time off their busy schedules to help out, he immediately put them to work, tasking them with among other things the carving of jack-o'-lanterns from pumpkins from <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Hagrid</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid%27s_pumpkin_patch" title="Rubeus Hagrid&#39;s pumpkin patch">pumpkin patch</a> and crafting hats for a <a href="/wiki/Troupe_of_dancing_skeletons" title="Troupe of dancing skeletons">troupe of skeletons</a> that he revealed he would be <a href="/wiki/Dancing_Feet_Spell" title="Dancing Feet Spell">bewitching to dance</a> at the feast, going as far as saying he believed it was going to be "a treat" for both himself as well as the students, seeing as he had never made skeletons dance before.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup> Unfortunately, the Headmaster would not be able to fully appreciate the improvements that had been made upon the time-honoured tradition that year: Near the end of the feast, when the Headmaster would usually have announced the evening's entertainment, Dumbledore was nowhere to be found; having realised that there was something amiss on the school grounds and left to investigate.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8c/Dumbledore_and_Jacob%27s_sibling_Howling_Hallowe%27en_1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200524032644" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="98" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dumbledore and Jacob&#39;s sibling Howling Hallowe&#39;en 1.jpg" data-image-key="Dumbledore_and_Jacob&#39;s_sibling_Howling_Hallowe&#39;en_1.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8c/Dumbledore_and_Jacob%27s_sibling_Howling_Hallowe%27en_1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200524032644" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8c/Dumbledore_and_Jacob%27s_sibling_Howling_Hallowe%27en_1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200524032644" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8c/Dumbledore_and_Jacob%27s_sibling_Howling_Hallowe%27en_1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200524032644" decoding="async" width="250" height="98" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dumbledore and Jacob&#39;s sibling Howling Hallowe&#39;en 1.jpg" data-image-key="Dumbledore_and_Jacob&#39;s_sibling_Howling_Hallowe&#39;en_1.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8c/Dumbledore_and_Jacob%27s_sibling_Howling_Hallowe%27en_1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200524032644" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dumbledore_and_Jacob%27s_sibling_Howling_Hallowe%27en_1.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore checking up on Jacob's sibling</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>There, he found that the school had come <a href="/wiki/Fenrir_Greyback%27s_attack_on_Hogwarts" title="Fenrir Greyback&#39;s attack on Hogwarts">under attack</a> by a <a href="/wiki/Fenrir_Greyback%27s_werewolf_pack" class="mw-redirect" title="Fenrir Greyback&#39;s werewolf pack">pack of werewolves</a>, and, with no time to alert the rest of the staff, set out into the night to repel the <a href="/wiki/Lycanthropy" title="Lycanthropy">cursed</a> canines himself; successfully removing five of them that had almost overran <a href="/wiki/Hagrid%27s_Hut" title="Hagrid&#39;s Hut">Hagrid's Hut</a> before returning to the castle, where he arrived just in time to save <a href="/wiki/Jacob%27s_sibling" title="Jacob&#39;s sibling">Jacob's sibling</a> from three more, who had tried to take advantage of his absence to attack a couple of students that had stepped outside, only for Greyback and the remaining members of his pack to hastily retreat into the <a href="/wiki/Forbidden_Forest" title="Forbidden Forest">Forbidden Forest</a> once they caught the scent of him. After making sure that the aforementioned pupil was unharmed, he noticed someone lying on the ground nearby, unconscious. Immediately recognising the victim as another student; a young witch in <a href="/wiki/Hufflepuff" title="Hufflepuff">Hufflepuff House</a> by the name of <a href="/wiki/Chiara_Lobosca" title="Chiara Lobosca">Chiara Lobosca</a>, the Headmaster briefly examined her injuries and, concluding that she did not appear to have been bitten, instructed Jacob's sibling to return to their dormitory while he took care of their classmate. Following the attack, Dumbledore informed the Ministry of Magic about the incident and requested that they send someone to the school that could look into the matter and hopefully rounded up the werewolves before anyone else was hurt.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/98/DancingSkeletonsHallowe%27en.gif/revision/latest?cb=20181020144537" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="148" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="DancingSkeletonsHallowe&#39;en.gif" data-image-key="DancingSkeletonsHallowe&#39;en.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/98/DancingSkeletonsHallowe%27en.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20181020144537" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/98/DancingSkeletonsHallowe%27en.gif/revision/latest?cb=20181020144537" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/98/DancingSkeletonsHallowe%27en.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20181020144537" decoding="async" width="250" height="148" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="DancingSkeletonsHallowe&#39;en.gif" data-image-key="DancingSkeletonsHallowe&#39;en.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/98/DancingSkeletonsHallowe%27en.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20181020144537" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:DancingSkeletonsHallowe%27en.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore animating skeletons</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In response, they sent <a href="/wiki/Cecil_Lee" title="Cecil Lee">Cecil Lee</a> from the <a href="/wiki/Werewolf_Capture_Unit" title="Werewolf Capture Unit">Werewolf Capture Unit</a> to track the werewolves down, whom the Headmaster gave permission to conduct an investigation and question the students and staff if necessary. It would take another month before Mr Lee's involvement brought results, however, when Mr Lee showed up at his office and reported that he had, with some good help from Jacob's sibling, successfully captured Greyback and most of his pack. Whilst he had left Greyback and the rest of the werewolves he had been able to catch safely tied up on the <a href="/wiki/Training_Grounds" title="Training Grounds">Training Grounds</a> for his colleagues to find, there was one werewolf that had stood out among the rest; a female werewolf with white fur that Jacob's sibling had called "a friend", and whom the Ministry official had decided to bring to Dumbledore instead of to the Ministry.<sup id="cite_ref-HM_y1_Hallowe.27en_40-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HM_y1_Hallowe.27en-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> Upon learning that the <a href="/wiki/Werewolf" title="Werewolf">Lycanthrope</a> in question was, in fact, Chiara Lobosca, who it turned out was also a werewolf herself, having been bitten as a young child and thus being counted among Greyback's many victims in addition to the prejudice around werewolves that was still very much widespread in the wizarding world, Dumbledore resolved to extend her the same offer he did <a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin" title="Remus Lupin">Remus Lupin</a> years before; a continued place at Hogwarts in exchange for her consent to certain precautions relating to the management of her condition, and a limitless supply of the recently invented <a href="/wiki/Wolfsbane_Potion" title="Wolfsbane Potion">Wolfsbane Potion</a>, courtesy of Professor Snape.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup> Once the issue of the werewolf attacks were taken care of, Dumbledore resolved to host a second feast as neither he, nor the student body, had been able to fully appreciate the first on account of Greyback's involvement.
</p>
<h5><span id="Hagrid's_birthday"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Hagrid.27s_birthday">Hagrid's birthday</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=22" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Hagrid&#039;s birthday">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Hagrid&#039;s birthday"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b3/HM_-_Hagrid_Birthday_Planning.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200507161640" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="140" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="HM - Hagrid Birthday Planning.jpg" data-image-key="HM_-_Hagrid_Birthday_Planning.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b3/HM_-_Hagrid_Birthday_Planning.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200507161640" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b3/HM_-_Hagrid_Birthday_Planning.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200507161640" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b3/HM_-_Hagrid_Birthday_Planning.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200507161640" decoding="async" width="250" height="140" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="HM - Hagrid Birthday Planning.jpg" data-image-key="HM_-_Hagrid_Birthday_Planning.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b3/HM_-_Hagrid_Birthday_Planning.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200507161640" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:HM_-_Hagrid_Birthday_Planning.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore planning with the students</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Sometime after this, their trusty <a href="/wiki/Keeper_of_Keys_and_Grounds" title="Keeper of Keys and Grounds">Keeper of Keys and Grounds</a> lost one of his <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid%27s_pets" title="Rubeus Hagrid&#39;s pets">favourite pets</a>, after which he was known to have been decidedly more sombre for quite a while, which eventually prompted the Headmaster to look for a way to lift his spirits. Sometime during early <a href="/wiki/December" title="December">December</a>, Dumbledore, having grown quite impressed by their enthusiasm and creativity where helping their friends and fellow classmates were concerned, not to mention well aware that Hagrid had grown quite fond of them, sent an owl to <a href="/wiki/Jacob%27s_sibling" title="Jacob&#39;s sibling">Jacob's sibling</a> and asked that they came to the <a href="/wiki/Clock_Tower_Courtyard" title="Clock Tower Courtyard">Clocktower Courtyard</a> to discuss a matter of great importance. Once the pupil in question presented themselves, however, the Headmaster revealed that he had nothing worse in store for them than wanting to solicit their assistance in organising a surprise party for their trusty Groundskeeper; a task, he was delighted to find, they gladly accepted. Soon, other pupils in the courtyard wanted to participate in their discussion about the right way to give their mutual friend the best party possible. Thereafter, Albus and his young co-conspirator parted ways; Jacob's sibling went to ask their best friend <a href="/wiki/Rowan_Khanna" title="Rowan Khanna">Rowan Khanna</a> for advice on party planning, whereas the Headmaster left to call in a favour with an "old friend" of his in the employment of the <a href="/wiki/Department_for_the_Regulation_and_Control_of_Magical_Creatures" title="Department for the Regulation and Control of Magical Creatures">Department for the Regulation and Control of Magical Creatures</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-HM_Party_Planner_63-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HM_Party_Planner-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bb/Hagrid%27s_birthday.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180929211342" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="95" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hagrid&#39;s birthday.jpg" data-image-key="Hagrid&#39;s_birthday.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bb/Hagrid%27s_birthday.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180929211342" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bb/Hagrid%27s_birthday.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180929211342" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bb/Hagrid%27s_birthday.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180929211342" decoding="async" width="250" height="95" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hagrid&#39;s birthday.jpg" data-image-key="Hagrid&#39;s_birthday.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bb/Hagrid%27s_birthday.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180929211342" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hagrid%27s_birthday.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore attending Hagrid's birthday celebration</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The Headmaster later bumped into Professor McGonagall and confided how he had just spoken to <a href="/wiki/Amos_Diggory" title="Amos Diggory">Amos Diggory</a>, who had agreed to drop by the castle with a selection of magical creatures for them to pick from as a birthday gift, but told her to keep it a secret, and to instruct his fellow party-planner if she saw them issue an invitation to Mr Filch while they were at it. In order to distract their unwitting guest of honour so the rest of the involved parties could make the necessary preparations, Dumbledore asked Hagrid to meet him at the at the <a href="/wiki/Training_Grounds" title="Training Grounds">Training Grounds</a>, explaining that there was "urgent business" in <a href="/wiki/Hogsmeade" title="Hogsmeade">Hogsmeade</a> that he had to take care of, and requested that he accompanied him. In the meantime, he told <a href="/wiki/Jacob%27s_sibling" title="Jacob&#39;s sibling">Jacob's sibling</a> to stay behind and babysit <a href="/wiki/Fang" title="Fang">Fang</a> while he and Hagrid completed their "tasks". When they both returned a short while later, he proceeded to discreetly instruct the pupil to invite Professor Snape next, and even advised them to bribe him with a gift if that was what it took to win him over. At the scheduled time, Dumbledore and the rest of Hagrid's party guests met up in the <a href="/wiki/Great_Hall" title="Great Hall">Great Hall</a>, where their surprise party for Hagrid would ultimately be a <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid%27s_birthday_celebration" title="Rubeus Hagrid&#39;s birthday celebration">massive success</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-HM_Party_Planner_63-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HM_Party_Planner-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Around <a href="/wiki/Christmas" title="Christmas">Christmas</a> that year, Dumbledore requested students that stayed behind at the school during the holidays to get involved in the decoration process, seeing as how well they did decorating for <a href="/wiki/Hallowe%27en" title="Hallowe&#39;en">Hallowe'en</a>: Student participation during Hallowe'en and Christmas both eventually became something of a time-honoured tradition.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="End-of-Term">End-of-Term</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=23" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: End-of-Term">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: End-of-Term"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/87/Dumbledore_talks_with_Jacob%27s_sibling_Courtyard_HM.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200601004301" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="177" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dumbledore talks with Jacob&#39;s sibling Courtyard HM.jpg" data-image-key="Dumbledore_talks_with_Jacob&#39;s_sibling_Courtyard_HM.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/87/Dumbledore_talks_with_Jacob%27s_sibling_Courtyard_HM.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200601004301" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/87/Dumbledore_talks_with_Jacob%27s_sibling_Courtyard_HM.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200601004301" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/87/Dumbledore_talks_with_Jacob%27s_sibling_Courtyard_HM.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200601004301" decoding="async" width="250" height="177" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dumbledore talks with Jacob&#39;s sibling Courtyard HM.jpg" data-image-key="Dumbledore_talks_with_Jacob&#39;s_sibling_Courtyard_HM.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/87/Dumbledore_talks_with_Jacob%27s_sibling_Courtyard_HM.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200601004301" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dumbledore_talks_with_Jacob%27s_sibling_Courtyard_HM.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore talking with Jacob's sibling in the Clocktower Courtyard</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Their efforts to keep their charges safe from the aforementioned cursed ice, however, was ultimately unsuccessful, as it was later discovered that a group of students had broken into the locked room it was located. The following evening, Dumbledore stepped outside into the <a href="/wiki/Clock_Tower_Courtyard" title="Clock Tower Courtyard">Clocktower Courtyard</a> to consider the events that had taken place at Hogwarts since the sorting of <a href="/wiki/Jacob%27s_sibling" title="Jacob&#39;s sibling">Jacob's sibling</a>, and upon realising that their trespassing of the room they had been sealed off had nothing at all to do with some selfish quest for glory and riches by uncovering the content of the <a href="/wiki/Cursed_Vaults" title="Cursed Vaults">Cursed Vaults</a>, and everything to do with a desperate search to find <a href="/wiki/Jacob_(Hogwarts_student)" title="Jacob (Hogwarts student)">the older sibling</a> who had gone missing, Dumbledore sent for the student in question to meet him there. When the pupil arrived, however, it quickly occurred to him that whilst it looked like they expected a lecture, there was nevertheless something they wanted to ask him; and hence, he decided to allow them to do so. Wishing to shield and protect them from <a href="/wiki/R" title="R">the truth</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> Dumbledore was still reluctant to reveal too much about the circumstances surrounding Jacob's expulsion, only denoting it as a long and complicated story and otherwise reminded them that the school held many mysteries, advising them to limit their exploration to those that were not life-threatening in the future. Rather than punishing their latest transgression, however, the Headmaster instead went on to commend them for their display of courage, compassion, and resourcefulness throughout the year, for which he awarded them 100 <a href="/wiki/House_points" title="House points">house points</a> and assured them that they would talk more after the summer holidays.<sup id="cite_ref-HMy1ch9_48-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HMy1ch9-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>During the <a href="/wiki/End-of-Term_Feast" title="End-of-Term Feast">End-of-Term Feast</a> that year, Dumbledore announced the winner of the <a href="/wiki/House_Cup" title="House Cup">House Cup</a>, expressed his hope that the students had learned as much from the teachers that year as he himself had learned from them, and wished them all a good <a href="/wiki/Summer_holidays" title="Summer holidays">summer holidays</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="1985–1986"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="1985.E2.80.931986">1985–1986</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=24" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: 1985–1986">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: 1985–1986"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Looking_for_answers">Looking for answers</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=25" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Looking for answers">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Looking for answers"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bb/HM_Staff_Convene.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200507164940" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="250" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="HM Staff Convene.jpg" data-image-key="HM_Staff_Convene.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bb/HM_Staff_Convene.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200507164940" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bb/HM_Staff_Convene.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200507164940" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bb/HM_Staff_Convene.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200507164940" decoding="async" width="250" height="250" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="HM Staff Convene.jpg" data-image-key="HM_Staff_Convene.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bb/HM_Staff_Convene.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200507164940" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:HM_Staff_Convene.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore and McGonagall discussing the security of the school in view of the Cursed Vault</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Although the room with the cursed ice had been duly secured following the meddling misadventure of <a href="/wiki/Jacob%27s_sibling" title="Jacob&#39;s sibling">Jacob's sibling</a> and their peers near the end of the previous term, the staff was still unable to fully determine what the repercussions of said incident would be, and what it might mean for the immediate future of the school. As such, when Dumbledore took the podium at the <a href="/wiki/Start-of-Term_Feast" title="Start-of-Term Feast">Start-of-Term Feast</a> to welcome students new and old for another year of learning, he also offered a word of caution to his usual speech; instructing them all to be extra careful as they journeyed through the castle that year, and to immediately inform one of their teachers if they saw anything out of the ordinary. Upon returning to his seat, it was discovered that one of the <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a> students were unaccounted for; a <a href="/wiki/Second_year" title="Second year">second-year</a> by the name of <a href="/wiki/Ben_Copper" title="Ben Copper">Ben Copper</a>, whose curious absence puzzled his classmates as much as it did the staff.
