After the feast, it was decided that the staff would search for him. At some point the next day, Dumbledore was paid a visit by <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Professor McGonagall</a>, who informed him that she had met with <a href="/wiki/Jacob%27s_sibling" title="Jacob&#39;s sibling">Jacob's sibling</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Clock_Tower_Courtyard" title="Clock Tower Courtyard">Clocktower Courtyard</a> to discuss the matter of Mr Copper's disappearance and the visit to the locked room, from whom she learned that there had been a secret message that may have hinted at threats beyond the room itself.<sup id="cite_ref-HMy2ch1_51-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HMy2ch1-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Having taken the cryptic warning about an '<a href="/wiki/Ice_Knight" title="Ice Knight">Ice Knight</a>' and '<a href="/wiki/Vanished_Stairs" title="Vanished Stairs">Vanished Stairs</a>' under advisement, it was nevertheless the case that the sudden reappearance of cursed ice inside the castle the previous term had given rise to a number of difficult questions. Having come to suspect that there might be answers to be found somewhere outside of it, especially in light of his failed attempt at getting hold of <a href="/wiki/Patricia_Rakepick" title="Patricia Rakepick">Patricia Rakepick</a>. Professor Dumbledore left Hogwarts shortly afterwards,<sup id="cite_ref-HMy2ch3_68-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HMy2ch3-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup> but not before tasking <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Hagrid</a> with doing some research into <a href="/wiki/Winged_horse" title="Winged horse">winged horses</a> in <a href="/wiki/Scotland" title="Scotland">Scotland</a>;<sup id="cite_ref-HMy2ch9_69-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HMy2ch9-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup> specifically, on <a href="/wiki/Abraxan" title="Abraxan">Abraxans</a>, as this information would go a long way in helping to prepare the school for an impending visit from the equally prestigious counterpart in <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">France</a>, with whom Hogwarts had always maintained a cordial relationship. To this end, he advised Hagrid to solicit the assistance of <a href="/wiki/Jacob%27s_sibling" title="Jacob&#39;s sibling">Jacob's sibling</a>, who he had learned attended to one such magnificent beast in the <a href="/wiki/Magical_Creatures_Reserve" title="Magical Creatures Reserve">Magical Creatures Reserve</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup> No sooner had he left the school, however, before he received an owl from <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Professor Snape</a> with some rather concerning news: '<a href="/wiki/R" title="R">R</a>' was back, and resumed their bid for the <a href="/wiki/Cursed_Vaults" title="Cursed Vaults">Cursed Vaults</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-HMy2ch3_68-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HMy2ch3-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/03/Screenshot_20180311-145702.png/revision/latest?cb=20180407012436" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="141" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Screenshot 20180311-145702.png" data-image-key="Screenshot_20180311-145702.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/03/Screenshot_20180311-145702.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180407012436" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/03/Screenshot_20180311-145702.png/revision/latest?cb=20180407012436" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/03/Screenshot_20180311-145702.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180407012436" decoding="async" width="250" height="141" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Screenshot 20180311-145702.png" data-image-key="Screenshot_20180311-145702.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/03/Screenshot_20180311-145702.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180407012436" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Screenshot_20180311-145702.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The professors handling the spread of cursed ice</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The Cabal had unwittingly showed their hand when <a href="/wiki/Jacob%27s_sibling" title="Jacob&#39;s sibling">Jacob's sibling</a> and <a href="/wiki/Rowan_Khanna" title="Rowan Khanna">Rowan Khanna</a> stumbled upon a message from them addressed to Ben Copper while assisting the teachers with looking for their friend, who had apparently been forced to embark on a scavenger hunt throughout the castle, the objective of which was to find a series of written instructions hidden throughout the castle by one of more members of 'R', threatening Ben with 'severe punishment' if he failed to meet their demands.<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup> This, his trusty <a href="/wiki/Potions_Master" title="Potions Master">Potions Master</a> had discovered when he caught the aforementioned pair exiting the <a href="/wiki/Common_Room" class="mw-redirect" title="Common Room">Common Room</a> of another House, and, upon questioning them, they had admitted to be re-tracing Ben's steps by following the directions given on one such message.<sup id="cite_ref-HMy2ch3_68-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HMy2ch3-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup> Not too long after this, their missing student was finally recovered, having been found in the farthest corridor on the east side of the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Castle#Fifth_Floor" title="Hogwarts Castle">fifth floor</a> of the castle; trapped by cursed ice; which had now began to spread throughout the corridor outside the locked room that had been intruded upon during the previous term. Due to his prolonged exposure to the cursed ice, however, which was known to have strange effects on those that came in contact with it, the young pupil was suffering from a sort of delirium that left his <a href="/wiki/Memory" title="Memory">memory</a> erratic, and hence in no condition to provide further insight into whatever plans the Cabal were making behind the scenes.<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Return_to_Hogwarts">Return to Hogwarts</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=26" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Return to Hogwarts">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Return to Hogwarts"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>Painfully aware that the cursed ice would only continue to spread and inflict ever more of the castle's inhabitants, the need to find a solution to their current predicament became increasingly urgent, prompting Dumbledore to spend the remainder of the school year travelling the world in an attempt to track down "an expert <a href="/wiki/Curse-Breaker" title="Curse-Breaker">Curse-Breaker</a>" whom he thought could be of great assistance in helping him and the rest of the staff with the task of locating the rest of the vaults, and hopefully break the curses placed on each of them before they claimed any more victims in the student body.<sup id="cite_ref-HMy2ch9_69-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HMy2ch9-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup> Upon his eventual return to the school, however, it did not take long before the cursed ice suddenly vanished without a trace; a clear sign that someone had successfully opened the door to <a href="/wiki/Vault_of_Ice" title="Vault of Ice">the vault</a> that the <a href="/wiki/Curse" title="Curse">curse</a> of the cursed ice had been tethered to.<sup id="cite_ref-HMy2ch10_73-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HMy2ch10-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup> Upon realising this, Dumbledore went to the fifth floor corridor to investigate the place where the cursed ice had first appeared for himself, where he discovered <a href="/wiki/Vanished_Stairs" title="Vanished Stairs">the hidden entrance</a> leading up to the <a href="/wiki/Vault_of_Ice" title="Vault of Ice">Vault of Ice</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-HMy5ch7_49-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HMy5ch7-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> Upon examining the wintry entrance hall, the Headmaster was able to determine that 'a terrible amount of work' had gone into its construction, not to mention 'complex and dangerous magic,'<sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup> and realised that the door leading into the heart of the vault had recently been opened, and even more importantly, he was able to determine that the <a href="/wiki/Cursed_ice" title="Cursed ice">ice curse</a> that had been unleashed upon the school had indeed broken. This did not bring Dumbledore any closer to uncover the identity of the person who had tampered with the vault this time.<sup id="cite_ref-HMy2ch10_73-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HMy2ch10-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/54/DumbledoreHMYear2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200403230649" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="250" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="DumbledoreHMYear2.jpg" data-image-key="DumbledoreHMYear2.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/54/DumbledoreHMYear2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200403230649" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/54/DumbledoreHMYear2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200403230649" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/54/DumbledoreHMYear2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200403230649" decoding="async" width="250" height="250" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="DumbledoreHMYear2.jpg" data-image-key="DumbledoreHMYear2.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/54/DumbledoreHMYear2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200403230649" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:DumbledoreHMYear2.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore discusses recent events with <a href="/wiki/Jacob%27s_sibling" title="Jacob&#39;s sibling">Jacob's sibling</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Upon returning from this venture, he shared his findings with the rest of the staff, before he returned to the <a href="/wiki/Headmaster%27s_Tower" title="Headmaster&#39;s Tower">Headmaster's Tower</a>. Shortly thereafter, he asked <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Professor McGonagall</a> to summon <a href="/wiki/Jacob%27s_sibling" title="Jacob&#39;s sibling">Jacob's sibling</a> and send them up to his office, having guessed correctly that it was this pupil who had ventured up to the Ice Vault and broken the curse and, in doing so, saved the school from a terrible fate, just like their brother before them. When the student in question presented themselves in his study, however, he gave them the run of his office while he finished scribbling down some notes on all that he had learned. When he was done, however, he gave his young visitor his full attention. Upon hearing that his guest had appeared to have been beckoned to the Ice Vault by the disembodied voice of <a href="/wiki/Jacob_(disambiguation)" title="Jacob (disambiguation)">Jacob</a>, which they believed to be some sort of <a href="/wiki/Vision" title="Vision">vision</a>, Professor Dumbledore gently dismissed the idea, theorising instead that there might be another, more likely <a href="/wiki/Legilimency" title="Legilimency">explanation</a>. That said, however, Dumbledore still asked the pupil to explain themselves. And although the Headmaster readily admitted that there was still much to be learned about the origins and the purpose of the Cursed Vaults, and that with any luck, the person he had attempted to locate would be able to shed some light on the matter once he finally got hold of her. He also commended them for their heroism in breaking the curse, yet also prudently pointed out how they and their friends had to needlessly endanger themselves, and asked that they henceforth left the search for the remaining vaults and their brother to him, but not before awarding them with 50 House points and subsequently sending them on their way.<sup id="cite_ref-HMy2ch10_73-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HMy2ch10-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h5><span id="Hosting_Aurélie_Dumont"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Hosting_Aur.C3.A9lie_Dumont">Hosting Aurélie Dumont</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=27" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Hosting Aurélie Dumont">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Hosting Aurélie Dumont"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>Although the report he had received from Hagrid earlier that year was undoubtedly put to good use with the arrival of <a href="/wiki/Professor" title="Professor">Professor</a> <a href="/wiki/Olympe_Maxime" title="Olympe Maxime">Olympe Maxime</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Headmaster" title="Headmaster">Headmistress</a> of <a href="/wiki/Beauxbatons_Academy_of_Magic" title="Beauxbatons Academy of Magic">Beauxbatons Academy of Magic</a>, Dumbledore still still fell a little short in terms of offering her the appropriate accommodations. When <a href="/wiki/Beauxbatons_Carriage" title="Beauxbatons Carriage">her carriage</a> landed at the school, Hagrid was away on official Hogwarts business at the time, and their <a href="/wiki/Care_of_Magical_Creatures" title="Care of Magical Creatures">Care of Magical Creatures</a> was "predisposed with an ornery <a href="/wiki/Streeler" title="Streeler">Streeler</a>", meaning that he could not provide her with an attendant to care for the dozen <a href="/wiki/Abraxan" title="Abraxan">Abraxans</a> that had flown her there all the way from France. Hence, Dumbledore found a place for them on the <a href="/wiki/Training_Grounds" title="Training Grounds">Training Grounds</a>, where they were well supplied with several big barrels of <a href="/wiki/Single_malt_whiskey" title="Single malt whiskey">single malt whiskey</a> to drink. Although she had initially come in so that she and Dumbledore could "discuss some school matters", she had also taken the opportunity to bring along one of her own students, <a href="/wiki/Aur%C3%A9lie_Dumont" title="Aurélie Dumont">Aurélie Dumont</a>, for a visit to Hogwarts to meet with her penfriend, <a href="/wiki/Penny_Haywood" title="Penny Haywood">Penny Haywood</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-HM_Beauxbatons_25-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HM_Beauxbatons-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> Over the duration of their stay, however, it came to Dumbledore's attention that the youngest of their two guests had ulterior motives for being there. Rather than considering a transfer and wishing to simply accept a guided tour of the castle by two of the residents like she claimed, it quickly became apparent that she had spent her time looking for something. Upon realising this, he asked Professor Maxime to find Miss Dumont and <a href="/wiki/Jacob%27s_sibling" title="Jacob&#39;s sibling">Jacob's sibling</a> and send them to his office.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4c/DumbledoreHM2_%282%29.png/revision/latest?cb=20200406052037" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="137" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="DumbledoreHM2 (2).png" data-image-key="DumbledoreHM2_(2).png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4c/DumbledoreHM2_%282%29.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200406052037" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4c/DumbledoreHM2_%282%29.png/revision/latest?cb=20200406052037" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4c/DumbledoreHM2_%282%29.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200406052037" decoding="async" width="250" height="137" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="DumbledoreHM2 (2).png" data-image-key="DumbledoreHM2_(2).png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4c/DumbledoreHM2_%282%29.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200406052037" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:DumbledoreHM2_(2).png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore talking to <a href="/wiki/Aur%C3%A9lie_Dumont" title="Aurélie Dumont">Aurélie Dumont</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When they arrived, he expressed his appreciation for how the latter had gone to the trouble of showing their visitor around, but that he was still curious as to why she had not come to him directly, given his connection to <a href="/wiki/Nicolas_Flamel" title="Nicolas Flamel">Nicolas Flamel</a> and given her search for something related to alchemy. After confirming that he was indeed the young man on the old photography that they found posing with the famous alchemist, Dumbledore humoured them for a bit by telling them both a little about the man himself. Upon hearing from Miss Dumont that there was a rumour circulating in France about a treasure hidden in a protected vault at Hogwarts believed to house a chalice that once belonged to Flamel; an ancient alchemical artefact that would make whoever possessed it into a great alchemist as well, the Headmaster was quick to assure them that while he could not say if any such object existed, he was certain that it was not anywhere at Hogwarts. Upon seeing how disheartened she was by learning this, however, and hearing her express the fear that without it, her dreams of getting out from under her prodigiously gifted <a href="/wiki/Davet_Dumont" title="Davet Dumont">brother</a>'s shadow and becoming a great alchemist seemed virtually unattainable, the Headmaster resolutely encouraged her not to give up on them, informing her that she could very well reach these worthy goals once she stopped comparing herself to him and learned to truly appreciate her own talents; which was a lesson he felt that Jacob's sibling would do well to learn too.<sup id="cite_ref-HM_Beauxbatons_25-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HM_Beauxbatons-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Following this, Dumbledore was present at the <a href="/wiki/End-of-Term_Feast" title="End-of-Term Feast">End-of-Term Feast</a>, where he praised the student body for their bravery in the face of adversity that year in facing the cursed ice, before finally announcing the <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">winner</a> of the <a href="/wiki/House_Cup" title="House Cup">House Cup</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="1986–1987"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="1986.E2.80.931987">1986–1987</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=28" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: 1986–1987">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: 1986–1987"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Start-of-Term_2">Start-of-Term</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=29" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Start-of-Term">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Start-of-Term"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1b/DumbledoreHMY3.png/revision/latest?cb=20200409044257" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="92" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="DumbledoreHMY3.png" data-image-key="DumbledoreHMY3.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1b/DumbledoreHMY3.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200409044257" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1b/DumbledoreHMY3.png/revision/latest?cb=20200409044257" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1b/DumbledoreHMY3.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200409044257" decoding="async" width="250" height="92" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="DumbledoreHMY3.png" data-image-key="DumbledoreHMY3.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1b/DumbledoreHMY3.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200409044257" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:DumbledoreHMY3.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore greeting the students</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Present as always in the <a href="/wiki/Great_Hall" title="Great Hall">Great Hall</a> alongside the rest of the staff to welcome the students for the <a href="/wiki/1986%E2%80%931987_school_year" title="1986–1987 school year">1986–1987 school year</a>, once the traditional <a href="/wiki/Sorting_ceremony" title="Sorting ceremony">Sorting ceremony</a> was at an end and everyone had found their way back to their seats, Dumbledore positioned himself at the <a href="/wiki/Owl_Lecturn" title="Owl Lecturn">Owl Lecturn</a> to deliver his usual words of welcome. Among these, however, was also instructions relating to student conducts where the <a href="/wiki/Cursed_Vaults" title="Cursed Vaults">Cursed Vaults</a> were concerned. Having already decided that they were entitled to an explanation in light of the dark events that had put so many of them in such grave danger during the past school term, the Headmaster finally confirmed that the existence of the <a href="/wiki/Cursed_Vaults" title="Cursed Vaults">Cursed Vaults</a>, as well as that the rumours that had been circulating claiming that a group of students had found their way into <a href="/wiki/Vault_of_Ice" title="Vault of Ice">one such vault</a> and broken the <a href="/wiki/Curse" title="Curse">curse</a> placed on it were indeed true, but that he would still be amiss if he did not point out how they had nevertheless placed both themselves and others at great risk in doing so. For this reason, he imposed a blanket ban on all future attempts to look for, not to mention entering any of the Cursed Vaults by any students, as each one would be likely to unleash another curse on the school if tampered with. Assuring them that the faculty would deal with the situation and do whatever they could to keep them all safe, he invited them all to enjoy the rest of the <a href="/wiki/Start-of-Term_Feast" title="Start-of-Term Feast">Start-of-Term Feast</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-HMy3ch1_45-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HMy3ch1-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Around the same time, Dumbledore also met with <a href="/wiki/Jacob%27s_sibling" title="Jacob&#39;s sibling">Jacob's sibling</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Head_of_House" title="Head of House">Head of House</a>: Having correctly anticipated their non-compliance with his instructions to stay away from the vaults in view of the fact that bringing Jacob home safe and sound was at the heart of their fixation with them, the Headmaster resolved to provide the well-intentioned inciter with some overdue incentive to turn their focus away from their dangerous quest and onto their schoolwork by disallowing them to leave the school to partake in the always popular <a href="/wiki/Hogsmeade_weekend_trips" title="Hogsmeade weekend trips">weekend trips</a> to <a href="/wiki/Hogsmeade" title="Hogsmeade">Hogsmeade</a> village, even with the required <a href="/wiki/Hogsmeade_permission_form" title="Hogsmeade permission form">permission slip</a>. Not entirely unreasonable, however, he would permit them to earn back the privilege of visiting the village, and gave the <a href="/wiki/Professor" title="Professor">Professor</a> charged with their care permission to lift the ban if they deemed their diligence where their academics was concerned sufficient to warrant it.<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup> His efforts would eventually turn out to be futile, however, as said pupil would immediately proceed to question the landlady of the <a href="/wiki/Three_Broomsticks_Inn" title="Three Broomsticks Inn">Three Broomsticks Inn</a>, and used what they learned from <a href="/wiki/Rosmerta" title="Rosmerta">Madam Rosmerta</a> to further facilitate their search for the Cursed Vaults and their brother.<sup id="cite_ref-HMy3ch3_50-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HMy3ch3-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Within days after the Welcoming Feat, however, Dumbledore was approached by the school's <a href="/wiki/Head_of_Herbology" title="Head of Herbology">Head of Herbology</a>, <a href="/wiki/Pomona_Sprout" title="Pomona Sprout">Professor Sprout</a>, who notified him that one of her <a href="/wiki/Third_year" title="Third year">third year</a> classes had been disrupted by the sudden appearance of a <a href="/wiki/Boggart" title="Boggart">Boggart</a> in <a href="/wiki/Greenhouse_Three" title="Greenhouse Three">Greenhouse Three</a>, which had assumed the form of a <a href="/wiki/Werewolf" title="Werewolf">werewolf</a> and terrified one of her <a href="/wiki/Hufflepuff" title="Hufflepuff">Hufflepuff</a> students, <a href="/wiki/Penny_Haywood" title="Penny Haywood">Penny Haywood</a>. An odd occurrence, seeing as how Boggarts were usually found in dark, enclosed spaces,<sup id="cite_ref-POA_36-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> not big, airy, sunlit greenhouses.<sup id="cite_ref-HMy3ch1_45-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HMy3ch1-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> Given this discovery, the staff came to suspect that the reason behind its odd behaviour was that it had been influenced by a <a href="/wiki/Curse" title="Curse">curse</a>, and that someone had disturbed yet another one of the vaults. <a href="/wiki/Vault_of_Fear" title="Vault of Fear">One that fed on the fears</a> of those around it. He would later receive an <a href="/wiki/Owl_Postal_Service" title="Owl Postal Service">owl</a> from <a href="/wiki/Rosmerta" title="Rosmerta">Madam Rosmerta</a>, informing him that <a href="/wiki/Jacob%27s_sibling" title="Jacob&#39;s sibling">Jacob's sibling</a> had helped her make a new, extra-sweet <a href="/wiki/Butterbeer" title="Butterbeer">Butterbeer</a> and proposed that he awarded them some <a href="/wiki/House_points" title="House points">House points</a> for their troubles.<sup id="cite_ref-HMy3ch3_50-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HMy3ch3-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Lies_and_deception">Lies and deception</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=30" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Lies and deception">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Lies and deception"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2c/Dumbledore_and_Snape_evaluating_potion_HM.jpeg/revision/latest?cb=20200601003513" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="141" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dumbledore and Snape evaluating potion HM.jpeg" data-image-key="Dumbledore_and_Snape_evaluating_potion_HM.jpeg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2c/Dumbledore_and_Snape_evaluating_potion_HM.jpeg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200601003513" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2c/Dumbledore_and_Snape_evaluating_potion_HM.jpeg/revision/latest?cb=20200601003513" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2c/Dumbledore_and_Snape_evaluating_potion_HM.jpeg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200601003513" decoding="async" width="250" height="141" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dumbledore and Snape evaluating potion HM.jpeg" data-image-key="Dumbledore_and_Snape_evaluating_potion_HM.jpeg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2c/Dumbledore_and_Snape_evaluating_potion_HM.jpeg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200601003513" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dumbledore_and_Snape_evaluating_potion_HM.jpeg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore and Snape evaluating Merula Snyde's Wit-Sharpening Potion</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Later still, the Headmaster found himself enjoying some <a href="/wiki/Pumpkin_juice" class="mw-redirect" title="Pumpkin juice">pumpkin juice</a> with the other teachers in the <a href="/wiki/Great_Hall" title="Great Hall">Great Hall</a> around lunch time, when <a href="/wiki/Merula_Snyde" title="Merula Snyde">Merula Snyde</a> made her way up to them to show them a <a href="/wiki/Wit-Sharpening_Potion" title="Wit-Sharpening Potion">Wit-Sharpening Potion</a> that she had been working on. Judged by their very own <a href="/wiki/Potions_Master" title="Potions Master">Potions Master</a> to be the single best sample he had seen a student brew in the years he had spent teaching the subject, Dumbledore found himself heartily agreeing with him when he was invited to examine it for himself; and shared his fellow professor's sentiment that Miss Snyde deserved special recognition for demonstrating such an impressive dedication and technique. As it turned out, however, it would take no less than a month's worth of relentless preparation and dedication by two of Miss Snyde's retaliating peers, and, perhaps most of all, an admirable amount of cheek before Dumbledore actually realised that he had been hoodwinked.<sup id="cite_ref-HM_Polyjuice_Potion_77-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HM_Polyjuice_Potion-77">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f5/Dumbledore_talking_to_Fake_Snape_HM.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200601003830" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="117" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dumbledore talking to Fake Snape HM.jpg" data-image-key="Dumbledore_talking_to_Fake_Snape_HM.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f5/Dumbledore_talking_to_Fake_Snape_HM.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200601003830" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f5/Dumbledore_talking_to_Fake_Snape_HM.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200601003830" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f5/Dumbledore_talking_to_Fake_Snape_HM.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200601003830" decoding="async" width="250" height="117" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dumbledore talking to Fake Snape HM.jpg" data-image-key="Dumbledore_talking_to_Fake_Snape_HM.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f5/Dumbledore_talking_to_Fake_Snape_HM.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200601003830" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dumbledore_talking_to_Fake_Snape_HM.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore talking with "Professor Snape"</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>On that particular occasion, the good professor had been seated at the <a href="/wiki/High_Table" title="High Table">High Table</a> and busily discussing <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> with <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Professor McGonagall</a> when he noticed someone that looked for all the world like Professor Snape come to a halt right in front of them and invited him to join the conversation; and asked that he took a seat so they could discuss the <a href="/wiki/Potions_(class)" title="Potions (class)">Potions</a> curriculum. Over the course of this dialogue, Dumbledore also included a bit of socialising, such as mentioning how <a href="/wiki/Filius_Flitwick" title="Filius Flitwick">the resident</a> <a href="/wiki/Charms_Master" title="Charms Master">Charms Master</a> had been "bragging about the remarkable batch of <a href="/wiki/Ravenclaw" title="Ravenclaw">Ravenclaws</a>" they had gotten that term, jokingly asking him whether he was "up for the challenge" of handling five more of the <a href="/wiki/Weasley_family" title="Weasley family">Weasley</a> children that would be attending the school in a few years, and commenting on the academic prowess of <a href="/wiki/Rowan_Khanna" title="Rowan Khanna">Rowan Khanna</a>, a pupil whom he found to be "exceptionally bright."
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b9/Dumbledore_and_%22Snape%22_talking.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200524033333" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="88" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dumbledore and &quot;Snape&quot; talking.jpg" data-image-key="Dumbledore_and_&quot;Snape&quot;_talking.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b9/Dumbledore_and_%22Snape%22_talking.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200524033333" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b9/Dumbledore_and_%22Snape%22_talking.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200524033333" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b9/Dumbledore_and_%22Snape%22_talking.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200524033333" decoding="async" width="250" height="88" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dumbledore and &quot;Snape&quot; talking.jpg" data-image-key="Dumbledore_and_&quot;Snape&quot;_talking.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b9/Dumbledore_and_%22Snape%22_talking.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200524033333" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dumbledore_and_%22Snape%22_talking.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore conversing with "Professor Snape"</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>On the flip side, however, he also took the opportunity to address some of the more disconcerting news of recent past, such as asking the <a href="/wiki/Head_of_Slytherin_House" title="Head of Slytherin House">Head of Slytherin House</a> if there was any truth to the rumour he had heard that some of the <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin</a> students had been writing letters to <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a> lately, and indirectly revealing the identity of the <a href="/wiki/Curse-Breaker" title="Curse-Breaker">Curse-Breaker</a> he had been trying to find during the previous term by casually mentioning a fellow pupil from Snape's days as a schoolboy who had aspired to said profession; still unaware that the individual next to him was in fact someone other than the faculty member he thought that it was. That was not to say, however, that Dumbledore was completely in the dark about the fact that there was something amiss. Indeed; neither the Headmaster, nor its <a href="/wiki/Deputy_Headmaster" title="Deputy Headmaster">Deputy</a> could help but notice that their co-worker was acting rather odd.<sup id="cite_ref-HM_Polyjuice_Potion_77-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HM_Polyjuice_Potion-77">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8c/DumbledoreHMPolyjuiceSQ.png/revision/latest?cb=20200421092526" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="97" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="DumbledoreHMPolyjuiceSQ.png" data-image-key="DumbledoreHMPolyjuiceSQ.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8c/DumbledoreHMPolyjuiceSQ.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200421092526" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8c/DumbledoreHMPolyjuiceSQ.png/revision/latest?cb=20200421092526" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8c/DumbledoreHMPolyjuiceSQ.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200421092526" decoding="async" width="250" height="97" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="DumbledoreHMPolyjuiceSQ.png" data-image-key="DumbledoreHMPolyjuiceSQ.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8c/DumbledoreHMPolyjuiceSQ.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200421092526" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:DumbledoreHMPolyjuiceSQ.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Professor Dumbledore rectifying the mistake</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>How it all fit together first dawned on him once "Professor Snape" called Merula Snyde to them and unexpectedly demanded that she confessed to a wrongdoing that, up until that point, there had been no evidence to suggest that she had committed. Though the young pupil initially feigned ignorance, she finally gave in under pressure and admitted that she had in fact stolen the Wit-Sharpening Potion she had showed them from one of her own classmates, who it was quickly decided would receive the overdue recognition she deserved. Raising to his feet, Dumbledore called for everyone's attention and invited <a href="/wiki/Penny_Haywood" title="Penny Haywood">Penny Haywood</a> up to join him on the podium; where he rectified the mistake done by publicly commending her skill at potion-making and assuring her that she would be adequately rewarded. Once Miss Haywood found her way back to her seat, however, the Headmaster turned his attention to <a href="/wiki/Jacob%27s_sibling" title="Jacob&#39;s sibling">Jacob's sibling</a>, who he had correctly deduced was the one he had been speaking to for the past few minutes, and cheerfully advised them to exit the hall before the <a href="/wiki/Polyjuice_Potion" title="Polyjuice Potion">Polyjuice Potion</a> they had taken to assume Professor Snape's likeness wore off; but not before rewarding them with ten house points for having displayed such loyalty and gone to such lengths to right a wrong.<sup id="cite_ref-HM_Polyjuice_Potion_77-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HM_Polyjuice_Potion-77">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Dark_Horses">Dark Horses</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=31" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Dark Horses">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Dark Horses"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>Over <a href="/wiki/1986%E2%80%931987_school_year" title="1986–1987 school year">the same period</a>, the <a href="/wiki/International_Confederation_of_Wizards" title="International Confederation of Wizards">International Confederation of Wizards</a> was due to convene for a conference somewhere in <a href="/wiki/Great_Britain" title="Great Britain">Great Britain</a>, to which he invited the school's trusty <a href="/wiki/Keeper_of_Keys_and_Grounds" title="Keeper of Keys and Grounds">Groundskeeper</a> to give a demonstration on <a href="/wiki/Thestral" title="Thestral">thestrals</a> to clear up the misconceptions that so many of its delegates had come to have about them over the years; specifically by showing that even a thestral that has had limited exposure to strangers could be comfortable working with several of them. To help him prepare his speech, the Headmaster advised him to solicit the assistance of not only <a href="/wiki/Jacob%27s_sibling" title="Jacob&#39;s sibling">Jacob's sibling</a>, who had proved time and time again to have a way with magical creatures, but also <a href="/wiki/Merula_Snyde" title="Merula Snyde">Merula Snyde</a>: Well <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">acquainted</a> with her <a href="/wiki/Snyde_family" title="Snyde family">family</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">history</a>, and hence privy to the fact that not only was the strife-torn young <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin</a> able to see thestrals, but that she had also tried hard to bury and forget the <a href="/wiki/Memory" title="Memory">memory</a> of the incident that enabled her to do so; the brutal murder of an <a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">Auror</a> from the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a> at the hands of her own <a href="/wiki/Merula_Snyde%27s_mother" title="Merula Snyde&#39;s mother">mother</a> at an early age, it had been for the purposes of filling two needs with one deed that Dumbledore had asked Hagrid to bring her along; hoping that by having Merula work with a thestral, a gentle and intelligent creature that could only be seen by those who had seen <a href="/wiki/Death" title="Death">death</a>, she might come to realise that something wonderful could come from even the most unpleasant of circumstances, and, in doing so, finally confront her past in earnest and be able to truly move on.<sup id="cite_ref-HM_Dark_Horses_78-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HM_Dark_Horses-78">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4d/Dumbledore_HM_Dark_Horses.png/revision/latest?cb=20200422082532" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="145" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dumbledore HM Dark Horses.png" data-image-key="Dumbledore_HM_Dark_Horses.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4d/Dumbledore_HM_Dark_Horses.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200422082532" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4d/Dumbledore_HM_Dark_Horses.png/revision/latest?cb=20200422082532" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4d/Dumbledore_HM_Dark_Horses.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200422082532" decoding="async" width="250" height="145" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dumbledore HM Dark Horses.png" data-image-key="Dumbledore_HM_Dark_Horses.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4d/Dumbledore_HM_Dark_Horses.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200422082532" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dumbledore_HM_Dark_Horses.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The Headmaster revealing his plan</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Once he had given Hagrid adequate time to get ready and time came for them to depart for the meeting, Dumbledore went to the <a href="/wiki/Training_Grounds" title="Training Grounds">Training Grounds</a> to collect him, and was delighted to find that his attempt to help the troubled pupil had been a success; meaning she had gained something more valuable than the <a href="/wiki/House_points" title="House points">house points</a> she had hoped to earn from the experience. Moreover, during the aforementioned assembly, not only was the thestral, in Hagrid's own words; "practically perfect," but his passionate lecture on the dark horse that he had brought along with him was so touching that even wizards in attendance that were not able to see it had been moved, and prompted several to volunteer to fly on it as part of the demonstration and even considering taking up training thestrals themselves, thus successfully inspiring many in the crowd to start treating the "dark horses" with kindness and respect rather than fear and disgust.<sup id="cite_ref-HM_Dark_Horses_78-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HM_Dark_Horses-78">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Searching_for_Rakepick">Searching for Rakepick</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=32" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Searching for Rakepick">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Searching for Rakepick"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>At some point prior to his second departure from the school in as many years, Dumbledore gave <a href="/wiki/Rita_Skeeter" title="Rita Skeeter">Rita Skeeter</a> 'periodical permission' to visit <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Castle" title="Hogwarts Castle">Hogwarts Castle</a> to observe the students, and to invite them to partake in a "friendly competition" where the winner would receive a first-page article in the <a href="/wiki/Daily_Prophet" title="Daily Prophet">Daily Prophet</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup> By the time she first arrived at the school to announce the reason behind her visit and those that had yet to come, however, the Headmaster had already left to resume his search for <a href="/wiki/Patricia_Rakepick" title="Patricia Rakepick">Patricia Rakepick</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup> Although it would take almost the remainder school term for him to return to the school, Dumbledore's latest attempt to get hold of the adventurous banker would eventually yield significantly more results than the previous two, and he was finally able to track her down. Curious, however, as to what motive one of his former pupil might have to go to such great lengths to elude him, the Headmaster spent quite some time tracking her movements, having found her "here and there", in places where he had not expected to find her; which in of itself had raised its own set of questions.<sup id="cite_ref-HMy3ch10_81-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HMy3ch10-81">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup> Concluding, however, that in view of the fact that he had not found her to be guilty of any actual wrongdoing, he would be doing her a disservice if he did not give her the benefit of the doubt, the Headmaster hence decided to trust her.<sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup> Having followed her as far as to <a href="/wiki/South_America" title="South America">South America</a> before he made his presence known to her, he finally approached her as she began investigating some ancient ruins that had recently been discovered beneath the <a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazilian</a> wizarding school of <a href="/wiki/Castelobruxo" title="Castelobruxo">Castelobruxo</a>, situated in the heart of the <a href="/wiki/Amazon_rainforest" title="Amazon rainforest">Amazon rainforest</a>. Unable to leave <a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazil</a> until her work there was finished, an arrangement was made where she would instead come to Hogwarts at the beginning of the next term.<sup id="cite_ref-HMy3ch10_81-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HMy3ch10-81">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Back_at_Hogwarts">Back at Hogwarts</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=33" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Back at Hogwarts">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Back at Hogwarts"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e4/DumbledoreHM.png/revision/latest?cb=20200401230617" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="141" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="DumbledoreHM.png" data-image-key="DumbledoreHM.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e4/DumbledoreHM.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200401230617" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e4/DumbledoreHM.png/revision/latest?cb=20200401230617" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e4/DumbledoreHM.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200401230617" decoding="async" width="250" height="141" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="DumbledoreHM.png" data-image-key="DumbledoreHM.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e4/DumbledoreHM.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200401230617" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:DumbledoreHM.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore back at Hogwarts</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Having convened with the rest of the faculty upon his return to the castle, more noteworthy than the numerous encounters that members of the student body had had with their worst fears in his absence, however, was a nearly instantaneous drop in <a href="/wiki/Boggart" title="Boggart">Boggart</a>-related incidents that had just taken place; an improvement that coincided suspiciously well with what <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Professor Snape</a> had only just been told by two of his <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin</a> students; <a href="/wiki/Merula_Snyde" title="Merula Snyde">Merula Snyde</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ismelda_Murk" title="Ismelda Murk">Ismelda Murk</a>. Specifically, they had informed him that they had seen that <a href="/wiki/Jacob%27s_sibling" title="Jacob&#39;s sibling">Jacob's sibling</a> and four other co-conspirators had trespassed into the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_library" class="mw-redirect" title="Hogwarts library">school library</a> after it had closed for the night and successfully made their way into the <a href="/wiki/Restricted_Section" title="Restricted Section">Restricted Section</a>; where they had been able to locate a <a href="/wiki/Vault_of_Fear" title="Vault of Fear">second vault</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup> While naturally pleased to hear of the improving conditions, Dumbledore still concurred with <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Professor McGonagall</a>'s instruction for <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Rubeus Hagrid</a> to keep this new development to himself, as announcing it too soon after it happened could only serve to dilute the reprehension that the culprits were due for breaking the school rules. Shortly afterwards, the good Professor went to look for <a href="/wiki/Jacob%27s_sibling" title="Jacob&#39;s sibling">Jacob's sibling</a>, and eventually found them in the middle of a big victory celebration alongside their many accomplices at the <a href="/wiki/Three_Broomsticks_Inn" title="Three Broomsticks Inn">Three Broomsticks Inn</a> in <a href="/wiki/Hogsmeade" title="Hogsmeade">Hogsmeade</a>. Once there, he asked them to see him in his study later that day, during which he wanted to discuss both the pupil's "unprecedented heroics" in once again breaking a curse that threatened the whole school, and to hear everything that they could possibly tell him about the vault that they had entered. He also, however, took the opportunity to address their "egregious misbehaviour." Having finally started to run out of excuses for them, the Headmaster solemnly warned them that the next time they broke the rules, he could no longer spare them the rod. Ultimately, however, he still gave them a hundred <a href="/wiki/House_points" title="House points">house points</a> as an award for saving the school, before giving them leave to go.
</p><p>Following this, Dumbledore briefly left the school again, this time in search for someone else; an individual that he would later admit that he hoped never to find Even so, he was back in time to see the students off for the summer, and presented the the <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">winner</a> of that year <a href="/wiki/House_Cup" title="House Cup">House Cup</a> with their just award.<sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="1987–1988"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="1987.E2.80.931988">1987–1988</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=34" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: 1987–1988">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: 1987–1988"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Start-of-Term_3">Start-of-Term</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=35" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Start-of-Term">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: Start-of-Term"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c3/Rakepick_and_Dumbledore.png/revision/latest?cb=20180825012919" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="232" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Rakepick and Dumbledore.png" data-image-key="Rakepick_and_Dumbledore.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c3/Rakepick_and_Dumbledore.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180825012919" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c3/Rakepick_and_Dumbledore.png/revision/latest?cb=20180825012919" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c3/Rakepick_and_Dumbledore.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180825012919" decoding="async" width="250" height="232" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Rakepick and Dumbledore.png" data-image-key="Rakepick_and_Dumbledore.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c3/Rakepick_and_Dumbledore.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180825012919" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Rakepick_and_Dumbledore.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore consulting Rakepick</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Anxious to finally put the annual breach of the castle's security to rest, and, by his own admission, concerned about the effect that their growing obsession with the cursed vaults might have on <a href="/wiki/Jacob%27s_sibling" title="Jacob&#39;s sibling">Jacob's sibling</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-HMy5ch19_47-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HMy5ch19-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> Dumbledore was quick to invite <a href="/wiki/Patricia_Rakepick" title="Patricia Rakepick">Madam Rakepick</a> to join him up at the <a href="/wiki/High_Table" title="High Table">High Table</a> upon her eventual arrival in the <a href="/wiki/Great_Hall" title="Great Hall">Great Hall</a> alongside the student body on <a href="/wiki/1_September" title="1 September">September 1</a>, <a href="/wiki/1987" title="1987">1987</a>. Curious to hear her opinion on not only the vaults, but also on the aforementioned student,<sup id="cite_ref-HMy3ch10_81-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HMy3ch10-81">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup> the Headmaster spent the what little time he had left between the students entering the hall and finding their seats and when he was scheduled to make the usual start-of-the-term announcements filling her in on the events that had taken place over past three school terms and put her in charge of attending to all matters related to the <a href="/wiki/Cursed_Vaults" title="Cursed Vaults">Cursed Vaults</a>, and even bestowed upon her a place on the faculty; making her a member of the non-teaching staff as means of granting her both the run of the castle for the remainder of her stay, as well as some disciplinary powers over the students, such as giving and docking <a href="/wiki/House_points" title="House points">house points</a>. During his customary welcoming speech, he included a quick introduction wherein he clarified to the students who she was and why he had invited her, before letting her take his place at the podium so that she could address the students.<sup id="cite_ref-HMy4ch1_44-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HMy4ch1-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> It would seem history repeated itself, however, when, as had been the case during the previous term, another student failed to meet up for the <a href="/wiki/Welcoming_Feast" title="Welcoming Feast">Welcoming Feast</a>.
</p><p>This time, it were one of young Mr Copper's classmates; a <a href="/wiki/Ravenclaw" title="Ravenclaw">Ravenclaw</a> student by the name of <a href="/wiki/Tulip_Karasu" title="Tulip Karasu">Tulip Karasu</a>. Having dozed off on her way to the school at the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Express" title="Hogwarts Express">Hogwarts Express</a> and woken up in the <a href="/wiki/Black_Forest" title="Black Forest">Black Forest</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Rubeus Hagrid</a> had found Miss Karasu wandering the grounds on his way to the feast, apparently sleepwalking. And though she had reached the dark woods to the east of the castle by the time he caught up with her, fortunately, Miss Karasu had hit her head on a low-hanging branch as he tried to enter, allowing their trusty <a href="/wiki/Keeper_of_Keys_and_Grounds" title="Keeper of Keys and Grounds">Groundskeeper</a> to bring her to the <a href="/wiki/Clock_Tower_Courtyard" title="Clock Tower Courtyard">Clocktower Courtyard</a>. Once there, he was finally able to wake her up. After a brief two of <a href="/wiki/Jacob%27s_sibling" title="Jacob&#39;s sibling">her</a> <a href="/wiki/Ben_Copper" title="Ben Copper">peers</a>, not to mention some efficient use of a <a href="/wiki/Episkey" title="Episkey">healing spell</a> by one of them to relieve her of a headache, Hagrid was finally able to convince her to let him take her up to the <a href="/wiki/Hospital_Wing" title="Hospital Wing">Hospital Wing</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-HMy4ch1_44-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HMy4ch1-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup>​​ Upon learning about this incident, the Headmaster quickly deduced that someone had already disturbed one of the other vaults and unleashed a new curse upon the school and its denizens, and informed the teaching staff; telling them to watch the perimeters around the Forbidden Forest to prevent a repeat of this incident.<sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="The_Celestial_Ball">The Celestial Ball</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=36" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: The Celestial Ball">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: The Celestial Ball"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c8/Dumbledore%2C_Snape_and_Rakepick.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200722125817" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="250" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dumbledore, Snape and Rakepick.jpg" data-image-key="Dumbledore,_Snape_and_Rakepick.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c8/Dumbledore%2C_Snape_and_Rakepick.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200722125817" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c8/Dumbledore%2C_Snape_and_Rakepick.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200722125817" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c8/Dumbledore%2C_Snape_and_Rakepick.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200722125817" decoding="async" width="250" height="250" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dumbledore, Snape and Rakepick.jpg" data-image-key="Dumbledore,_Snape_and_Rakepick.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c8/Dumbledore%2C_Snape_and_Rakepick.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200722125817" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dumbledore,_Snape_and_Rakepick.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore, alongside members of faculty, helping to decorate for the Celestial Ball</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Even though the number of students that succumbed to the <a href="/wiki/Sleepwalking_curse" title="Sleepwalking curse">Sleepwalking curse</a> only continued to grow steadily in the time that followed, and while there was no denying that there were still those among the castle's residents that remained suspicious of <a href="/wiki/Patricia_Rakepick" title="Patricia Rakepick">their visitor</a>, even on the staff, the fact that they now had a tried-and-tested expert looking into the matter nevertheless took some of the pressure off of the rest of the faculty, to the point where Dumbledore decided that it was past time that the denizens of <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Castle" title="Hogwarts Castle">Hogwarts Castle</a> all got a much needed distraction from the trying times that was now behind them, not to mention a happy memory to look back on given the dark times that still laid ahead. After discussing the matter among themselves, the staff finally agreed to arrange an <a href="/wiki/Astronomy_(class)" title="Astronomy (class)">Astronomy</a>-themed social gathering for the students in the <a href="/wiki/Great_Hall" title="Great Hall">Great Hall</a> known as the <a href="/wiki/Celestial_Ball" title="Celestial Ball">Celestial Ball</a>. In order to further involve the students in the festivities, the Headmaster was able to persuade <a href="/wiki/Irma_Pince" title="Irma Pince">Madam Pince</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Librarian" title="Hogwarts Librarian">school librarian</a>, to allow the election for the head of a student committee that would be in charge of the decorations to take place in the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Library" title="Hogwarts Library">library</a>. Thereafter, he summoned the students to the Great Hall in order to to announce the event, explaining that there would be music, refreshments and dancing, with the dress code being "<a href="/wiki/Dress_robes" title="Dress robes">formal</a>." He also invited the students to partake in the election for the <a href="/wiki/Celestial_Ball_decorating_committee" title="Celestial Ball decorating committee">decorating committee</a>, which would be overseen by Madam Pince, before giving the pupils leave to return to class.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/46/CelestialBall2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20191130224620" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="121" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="CelestialBall2.jpg" data-image-key="CelestialBall2.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/46/CelestialBall2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20191130224620" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/46/CelestialBall2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20191130224620" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/46/CelestialBall2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20191130224620" decoding="async" width="250" height="121" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="CelestialBall2.jpg" data-image-key="CelestialBall2.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/46/CelestialBall2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20191130224620" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:CelestialBall2.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The faculty chaperoning the Celestial Ball</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Following <a href="/wiki/Penny_Haywood" title="Penny Haywood">Penny Haywood</a>'s victory over <a href="/wiki/Emily_Tyler" title="Emily Tyler">Emily Tyler</a> in the student election, their trusty <a href="/wiki/Charms_Master" title="Charms Master">Charms Master</a> was kind enough to lend the decorating committee the use of <a href="/wiki/Charms_Classroom" title="Charms Classroom">his classroom</a> for the creation of the decor, some of which was made without magic and in line with their leader's "stellar vision" for the end result: Aside from a big banner reading "Celestial Ball", the centre of the hall was dominated by a large, glowing model of the moon; the four house tables were gone, and in their place, six circular ones with matching chairs where students could mingle had been situated along the walls nearest the entrance; flanking a magnificent carpet that ran across the length of most of the floor. At the far-end of the the hall, in front of the <a href="/wiki/High_Table" title="High Table">High Table</a>, the floor was covered by a large, glass-like dance floor with a bluish tint to it that was blank-polished and reflected the starry evening sky from the <a href="/wiki/Enchanted_Ceiling" title="Enchanted Ceiling">Enchanted Ceiling</a> above. On the eve of said event, the Headmaster chaperoned the festivities alongside the four <a href="/wiki/Head_of_House" title="Head of House">Heads of Houses</a>, <a href="/wiki/Professor" title="Professor">Professors</a> <a href="/wiki/Cuthbert_Binns" title="Cuthbert Binns">Binns</a> and <a href="/wiki/Silvanus_Kettleburn" title="Silvanus Kettleburn">Kettleburn</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Rubeus Hagrid</a>. At the start of the event, Dumbledore stood by the doors, greeting the students as they entered the hall, among them <a href="/wiki/Jacob%27s_sibling" title="Jacob&#39;s sibling">Jacob's sibling</a>, and later held a short speech wherein he commended Penny Heywood and the committee's success. During the event, he was seen socialising with <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Professor McGonagall</a>, and later watched the pupils enjoy themselves alongside <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Professor Snape</a>, beaming as Rubeus Hagrid and <a href="/wiki/Filius_Flitwick" title="Filius Flitwick">Professor Flitwick</a> eventually opted to join the students on the dance floor, and over a job well done in spite of everything.<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">&#91;86&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="1988–1989"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="1988.E2.80.931989">1988–1989</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=37" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: 1988–1989">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: 1988–1989"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Dumbledore's decision to appoint Rakepick proved a costly one as Rakepick turned out to be one of R's members and nearly managed to kill Jacob's sibling and their friends before being defeated by a Garroting Gas and forced to flee but left Merula Snyde traumatised with the betrayal and use of the Cruciatus Curse when they went to the Cursed Vault. Dumbledore was away at the time and unable to stop it and was left responsible with what had happened, admitting regret for being outside to deal with threats and promising to prioritise capturing Rakepick.
</p>
<h4><span id="1989–1990"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="1989.E2.80.931990">1989–1990</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=38" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: 1989–1990">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: 1989–1990"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>The next year was by no means any less troublesome than the previous year, with Jacob's sibling and their friends more determined than ever to stopping R and finding the last Cursed Vault, despite Dumbledore's attempts to make them focus on their studies. He was even more disturbed with how Ben Cooper and Merula Snyde had became different due to the events of last year and that an Azkaban escapee who turned out to be an expelled student of Mahoutokoro School of Magic was working with R. When Rowan Khanna was killed by Rakepick, Dumbledore lead a huge memorial to their noble sacrifice.
</p>
<h4><span id="1991–1992"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="1991.E2.80.931992">1991–1992</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=39" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: 1991–1992">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=39" title="Edit section: 1991–1992"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone"><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>But why couldn't Quirrell touch me?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Albus Dumbledore</b>: "<i>Your mother died to save you. If there is one thing Voldemort cannot understand, it is love. He didn't realise that love as powerful as your mother's for you leaves its own mark. Not a scar, no visible sign... to have been loved so deeply, even though the person who loved us is gone, will give us some protection forever. It is in your very skin. Quirrell, full of hatred, greed, and ambition, sharing his soul with Voldemort, could not touch you for this reason. It was agony to touch a person marked by something so good.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; <strong class="mw-selflink selflink">Dumbledore</strong> and <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a> discussing the power of <a href="/wiki/Love" title="Love">love</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div><p>Ten years after Dumbledore left Harry Potter with his uncle and aunt, the <a href="/wiki/Dursley_family" title="Dursley family">Dursleys</a>, Harry started attending <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>, not as happy as Dumbledore might have hoped, considering the neglect he had faced at the hands of his intolerant aunt and uncle, but alive and well. That year, <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> formulated a plan to regain human form. Dumbledore and his friend <a href="/wiki/Nicolas_Flamel" title="Nicolas Flamel">Nicolas Flamel</a> (the only known maker of the <a href="/wiki/Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Philosopher&#39;s Stone">Philosopher's Stone</a>) began to suspect that the disembodied Dark Lord was plotting to steal the invaluable object, which would be capable of restoring him to full power. Dumbledore had the stone moved to a medium security vault at <a href="/wiki/Gringotts_Wizarding_Bank" title="Gringotts Wizarding Bank">Gringotts Wizarding Bank</a>, but later had it moved to Hogwarts itself; coincidentally, on the same day that an attempted break-in was made upon the vault. It was retrieved by Hagrid, who was also taking Harry to buy his school supplies.
</p><figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/69/Dumbledore_speech.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180607064715" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dumbledore speech.jpg" data-image-key="Dumbledore_speech.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/69/Dumbledore_speech.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180607064715" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/69/Dumbledore_speech.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180607064715" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/69/Dumbledore_speech.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180607064715" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dumbledore speech.jpg" data-image-key="Dumbledore_speech.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/69/Dumbledore_speech.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180607064715" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dumbledore_speech.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore giving his customary school speech</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
