<p>Dumbledore and several teachers (<a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">McGonagall</a>, <a href="/wiki/Filius_Flitwick" title="Filius Flitwick">Flitwick</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sprout_(disambiguation)" title="Sprout (disambiguation)">Sprout</a>, <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Snape</a> and, dubiously, <a href="/wiki/Quirinus_Quirrell" title="Quirinus Quirrell">Quirrell</a>) at Hogwarts planted magical security methods to protect the stone. Dumbledore was behind the final, and most powerful protection placed upon the stone. He enchanted the Mirror of Erised to contain the Philosopher's Stone, only to be removed by someone who did not intend to use or possess it, but only to keep it from the hands of evil. Dumbledore suspected that the <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> Professor Quirinus Quirrell was behind the plot to steal the Philosopher's Stone, while working for the weakened Lord Voldemort, and as such he asked Snape to keep an eye on him. He also anonymously returned James's <a href="/wiki/Cloak_of_Invisibility" title="Cloak of Invisibility">Cloak of Invisibility</a> to Harry as a Christmas present.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_7-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a1/Dumbledore_talking_to_Harry_about_the_Mirror_of_Erised.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170524232937" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="106" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dumbledore talking to Harry about the Mirror of Erised.jpg" data-image-key="Dumbledore_talking_to_Harry_about_the_Mirror_of_Erised.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a1/Dumbledore_talking_to_Harry_about_the_Mirror_of_Erised.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170524232937" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a1/Dumbledore_talking_to_Harry_about_the_Mirror_of_Erised.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170524232937" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a1/Dumbledore_talking_to_Harry_about_the_Mirror_of_Erised.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170524232937" decoding="async" width="250" height="106" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dumbledore talking to Harry about the Mirror of Erised.jpg" data-image-key="Dumbledore_talking_to_Harry_about_the_Mirror_of_Erised.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a1/Dumbledore_talking_to_Harry_about_the_Mirror_of_Erised.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170524232937" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dumbledore_talking_to_Harry_about_the_Mirror_of_Erised.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore advising Harry from seeking out the Mirror of Erised again</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Over a series of nights, Harry Potter proceeded to visit the <a href="/wiki/Mirror_of_Erised" title="Mirror of Erised">Mirror of Erised</a> as often as he could to see <a href="/wiki/James_and_Lily_Potter" title="James and Lily Potter">his parents</a>' faces. Dumbledore found Harry visiting the mirror one night, and after explaining to Harry what the mirror was all about, told him that the mirror was to be moved and requested that Harry not go looking for it. Before heading back to bed, Harry asked Dumbledore what he saw when he looked into the mirror. Dumbledore claimed to see himself holding a pair of thick, woollen socks, telling Harry that "<i>one can never have enough socks.</i>"<sup id="cite_ref-PS_7-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> However, Dumbledore was joking — the matter being a very personal one. At first, still yearning for Grindelwald’s love, Albus saw himself with his former lover in the Mirror. However, after Grindelwald’s defeat and having come to terms with his past guilt over his sister’s death, later in his life Dumbledore would see <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore_family" title="Dumbledore family">his family</a> whole and intact, free of any pain or suffering.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_22-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> It is unknown if Grindelwald, as a redeemed man, was included in these later reflections.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ef/Dumbledore_comforting_Harry_in_the_Hospital_Wing.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150724143933" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="121" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dumbledore comforting Harry in the Hospital Wing.jpg" data-image-key="Dumbledore_comforting_Harry_in_the_Hospital_Wing.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ef/Dumbledore_comforting_Harry_in_the_Hospital_Wing.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150724143933" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ef/Dumbledore_comforting_Harry_in_the_Hospital_Wing.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150724143933" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ef/Dumbledore_comforting_Harry_in_the_Hospital_Wing.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150724143933" decoding="async" width="250" height="121" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dumbledore comforting Harry in the Hospital Wing.jpg" data-image-key="Dumbledore_comforting_Harry_in_the_Hospital_Wing.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ef/Dumbledore_comforting_Harry_in_the_Hospital_Wing.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150724143933" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dumbledore_comforting_Harry_in_the_Hospital_Wing.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore visits Harry Potter in the <a href="/wiki/Hospital_Wing" title="Hospital Wing">Hospital Wing</a> after the latter protects the Philosopher's Stone from Voldemort</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In the end it was Harry who protected the Philosopher's Stone from Quirrell and Voldemort. Voldemort failed for the same reasons he had failed to murder Harry previously: due to <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily Potter</a>'s love for Harry. When Voldemort, who had possessed the body of Quirrell, ordered his servant to attack the young boy, the <a href="/wiki/Sacrificial_protection" title="Sacrificial protection">sacrificial protection</a> instilled within him at the point of his mother's death killed him and forced the Dark Lord's spirit to flee. When Harry recovered from the ordeal in the hospital wing, he questioned Dumbledore about why Voldemort had tried to murder him as a baby.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_7-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> Dumbledore did not believe that Harry was ready to know the truth about the <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney%27s_first_prophecy" title="Sybill Trelawney&#39;s first prophecy">Prophecy</a> <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney" title="Sybill Trelawney">Sybill Trelawney</a> had made, and told him he would know when he was older (although this would actually later turn out to be a mistake).<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_41-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>At the end-of-year feast, Dumbledore awarded an extra 170 house points to <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a> students, Harry Potter (60), Ron Weasley (50), Hermione Granger (50) and <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a> (10), respectively for bravery and logical skills, prompting Gryffindor to win the <a href="/wiki/House_Cup" title="House Cup">House Cup</a>, ruining Slytherin’s chance of the cup for the seventh year in a row. This may have shown an amount of bias towards Gryffindor to announce their win in such unusual circumstances.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_7-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Sometime before the next year began, Dumbledore, having never been fooled by <a href="/wiki/Gilderoy_Lockhart" title="Gilderoy Lockhart">Gilderoy Lockhart</a>'s tall tales, figured out the truth soon when Lockhart erased the memories of two wizards that Dumbledore personally knew. He realised that Lockhart had gone too far in his desire for fame and decided to track him down and make him pay for his crimes. Having the position of the <a href="/wiki/Professor" title="Professor">Professor</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> vacant proved to be useful for Dumbledore, as he offered Lockhart the job and although Lockhart was reluctant as his career as an author was progressing very well, successfully convinced him by slyly hinting that <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> was a second-year student in <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>, causing Lockhart to accept.<sup id="cite_ref-lockhart_87-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-lockhart-87">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Having intended for Lockhart to show his ineptitude and fraudulence to the students and thus expose him to the public secretly, Dumbledore's decision was shocking to take by the other staff members as they never forgot Lockhart as the obnoxious attention seeker back then despite his achievements, with <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">McGonagall</a> saying what the students could possibly learn under a man as vain and celebrity-hungry man as Lockhart. Dumbledore, however, skilfully talked himself out by pointing out that Lockhart was the only one who was willing to take it and also saying that there was a lot to learn from even a bad teacher: what not to do, how not to be.<sup id="cite_ref-lockhart_87-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-lockhart-87">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="1992–1993"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="1992.E2.80.931993">1992–1993</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=40" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: 1992–1993">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=40" title="Edit section: 1992–1993"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">"<i>It is our choices Harry, that show what we truly are, far more than our abilities.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Dumbledore's advice to Harry Potter<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div><figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Harry-potter2-professors.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161129042803" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="107" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry-potter2-professors.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter2-professors.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Harry-potter2-professors.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161129042803" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Harry-potter2-professors.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161129042803" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Harry-potter2-professors.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161129042803" decoding="async" width="250" height="107" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry-potter2-professors.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter2-professors.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Harry-potter2-professors.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161129042803" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter2-professors.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Albus Dumbledore and colleagues discovering a blood-written message on the wall</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Shortly into the school year of 1992, students again fell under attack from a beast allegedly released from the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a>. Under the influence of <a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy" title="Lucius Malfoy">Lucius Malfoy</a>, the Hogwarts board of governors voted to remove Dumbledore from his position as Headmaster when he proved unable to uncover the culprit; <a href="/wiki/Minister_for_Magic" title="Minister for Magic">Minister for Magic</a> <a href="/wiki/Cornelius_Fudge" title="Cornelius Fudge">Cornelius Fudge</a> also had the groundskeeper <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Rubeus Hagrid</a> taken to Azkaban, acting under the theory that it had been he who opened the Chamber in 1943.<sup id="cite_ref-COS_31-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COS-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>It was later revealed that first year student, <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny Weasley</a>, had come into possession of <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle%27s_Diary" class="mw-redirect" title="Tom Riddle&#39;s Diary">Tom Riddle's Diary</a>, a bewitched object capable of interacting with whoever wrote in it. The diary slowly drained the life force from Ginny, and when the memory it contained was nearly strong enough to take physical form, it had her journey into the heart of the Chamber. However, <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> was able to find the Chamber himself, and there, defeated the beast that dwelt within; <a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin" title="Salazar Slytherin">Salazar Slytherin</a>'s basilisk. He also destroyed the diary with one of the basilisk's fangs, saving Ginny and defeating the nearly fully formed memory of Riddle. Harry was only able to achieve these feats by displaying an extreme amount of loyalty to Dumbledore; for only someone truly loyal to the Headmaster would be capable of summoning his pet <a href="/wiki/Phoenix" title="Phoenix">phoenix</a> <a href="/wiki/Fawkes" title="Fawkes">Fawkes</a>, who provided the tools needed for Potter to defeat Riddle and the basilisk.<sup id="cite_ref-COS_31-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COS-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/B2C18M1_Sword_of_Gryffindor_engraving.png/revision/latest?cb=20161210035910" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="95" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="B2C18M1 Sword of Gryffindor engraving.png" data-image-key="B2C18M1_Sword_of_Gryffindor_engraving.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/B2C18M1_Sword_of_Gryffindor_engraving.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161210035910" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/B2C18M1_Sword_of_Gryffindor_engraving.png/revision/latest?cb=20161210035910" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/B2C18M1_Sword_of_Gryffindor_engraving.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161210035910" decoding="async" width="250" height="95" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="B2C18M1 Sword of Gryffindor engraving.png" data-image-key="B2C18M1_Sword_of_Gryffindor_engraving.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/B2C18M1_Sword_of_Gryffindor_engraving.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161210035910" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:B2C18M1_Sword_of_Gryffindor_engraving.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Harry and Dumbledore talk after Harry slayed the <a href="/wiki/Basilisk" title="Basilisk">Basilisk</a> in the chamber</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Dumbledore mysteriously returned to his position as <a href="/wiki/Headmaster" title="Headmaster">Headmaster</a> after the memory of Riddle was revealed as being behind the attacks. He commended both Harry and Ron for solving the mystery with the <a href="/wiki/Special_Award_for_Services_to_the_School" title="Special Award for Services to the School">Special Award for Services to the School</a> and two hundred points each for them. This secured Gryffindor for the House Cup for the second year running and again ruining Slytherin's chances, fuelling the hatred and rivalry between the two houses. He also secured Hagrid's release from <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a> by having Ron deliver his release papers via owl and cancelled exams as a special treat, much to the delight of the students and the dismay of Hermione Granger. <a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy" title="Lucius Malfoy">Lucius Malfoy</a> was also sacked from his position as a governor of Hogwarts, much to Draco's dismay and Harry's satisfaction.<sup id="cite_ref-COS_31-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COS-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f8/Dumbledore_diary.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161012000239" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dumbledore diary.jpg" data-image-key="Dumbledore_diary.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f8/Dumbledore_diary.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161012000239" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f8/Dumbledore_diary.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161012000239" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f8/Dumbledore_diary.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161012000239" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dumbledore diary.jpg" data-image-key="Dumbledore_diary.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f8/Dumbledore_diary.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161012000239" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dumbledore_diary.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore contemplating Tom Riddle's diary</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>However, Dumbledore was privately concerned by the phenomena that Harry described; a mere memory capable of taking physical form was unheard of. Dumbledore then began to suspect that Riddle's diary was in fact a <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcrux</a>, and furthermore, considering the lack of care the Dark Lord had taken in protecting the diary, that he had created more than one.<sup id="cite_ref-COS_31-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COS-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>During his final talk with Harry in his office, Dumbledore came close to telling Harry about his connection with Voldemort but refrained from doing so as he felt that twelve years old was still too young to learn the truth and he wanted Harry to enjoy this night of triumph.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_41-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="1993–1994"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="1993.E2.80.931994">1993–1994</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=41" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: 1993–1994">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=41" title="Edit section: 1993–1994"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">"<i>Now, pay attention. Sirius is locked in Professor Flitwick's office on the seventh floor. Thirteenth window from the right of the West Tower. If all goes well, you will be able to save more than one innocent life tonight. But remember this, both of you: you must not be seen. Miss Granger, you know the law — you know what is at stake... I am going to lock you in. It is — five minutes to midnight. Miss Granger, three turns should do it. Good luck.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Dumbledore giving instructions to save Sirius<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div><p>The year after, the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a> took it upon itself to increase security around <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>. Sirius Black, who had been sentenced to life in <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a> for murdering <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Peter Pettigrew</a> and twelve <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggles</a> with a single curse, had escaped from the wizarding prison. The Ministry, afraid that he was going after <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, placed a large number of <a href="/wiki/Dementor" title="Dementor">Dementors</a> at Hogwarts to try to recapture him. Dumbledore reluctantly tolerated the Dementors on school grounds, but refused to allow them within the school itself.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_36-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>However, the Dementors violated Dumbledore's decree when they entered the <a href="/wiki/Quidditch" title="Quidditch">Quidditch</a> match between <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hufflepuff" title="Hufflepuff">Hufflepuff</a>, causing Harry to fall unconscious and fall from the sky. Dumbledore was able to prevent Harry from hitting the ground and repelled the Dementors with a Patronus.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_36-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d2/Dumbledore_Bedside_Manner_POA.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170106042250" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="164" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dumbledore Bedside Manner POA.jpg" data-image-key="Dumbledore_Bedside_Manner_POA.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d2/Dumbledore_Bedside_Manner_POA.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170106042250" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d2/Dumbledore_Bedside_Manner_POA.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170106042250" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d2/Dumbledore_Bedside_Manner_POA.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170106042250" decoding="async" width="250" height="164" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dumbledore Bedside Manner POA.jpg" data-image-key="Dumbledore_Bedside_Manner_POA.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d2/Dumbledore_Bedside_Manner_POA.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170106042250" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dumbledore_Bedside_Manner_POA.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore hinting that Harry and Hermione should travel back in time</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As the school year drew to its close, it became clear to Harry and his friends that <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a> had been framed for his crimes, commuted by Pettigrew, who has been disguised as Scabbers for twelve years. But Sirius was captured, locked in the highest tower, and sentenced to the <a href="/wiki/Dementor%27s_Kiss" title="Dementor&#39;s Kiss">Dementor's Kiss</a>. Dumbledore instantly believed Harry and his friends about Sirius's innocence, but the Minister did not. Dumbledore was incapable of over-ruling the Ministry's decision despite him being <a href="/wiki/Chief_Warlock" title="Chief Warlock">Chief Warlock</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Wizengamot" title="Wizengamot">Wizengamot</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_36-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Instead, Dumbledore told <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a> to use her <a href="/wiki/Time-Turner" title="Time-Turner">Time-Turner</a> to save Sirius and in the process Buckbeak as well. Harry and Hermione's rescue mission was a success, Sirius escaped on <a href="/wiki/Buckbeak" title="Buckbeak">Buckbeak</a>. The Dementors were removed from the grounds for their attack on Harry and the attempted removal of his soul. During the rescue Harry also conjured a powerful corporal <a href="/wiki/Patronus_Charm" title="Patronus Charm">Patronus</a> , that Dumbledore later commented on.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_36-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9b/B3C22M1_Lupin_leaving_his_office_and_teaching_post.png/revision/latest?cb=20180420201420" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="91" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="B3C22M1 Lupin leaving his office and teaching post.png" data-image-key="B3C22M1_Lupin_leaving_his_office_and_teaching_post.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9b/B3C22M1_Lupin_leaving_his_office_and_teaching_post.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180420201420" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9b/B3C22M1_Lupin_leaving_his_office_and_teaching_post.png/revision/latest?cb=20180420201420" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9b/B3C22M1_Lupin_leaving_his_office_and_teaching_post.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180420201420" decoding="async" width="250" height="91" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="B3C22M1 Lupin leaving his office and teaching post.png" data-image-key="B3C22M1_Lupin_leaving_his_office_and_teaching_post.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9b/B3C22M1_Lupin_leaving_his_office_and_teaching_post.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180420201420" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:B3C22M1_Lupin_leaving_his_office_and_teaching_post.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Harry Potter and Dumbledore seeing <a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin" title="Remus Lupin">Remus Lupin</a> off</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Dumbledore saw Remus Lupin (the new <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> teacher) off after Snape leaked his identity as a werewolf to the school. Harry was also seeing Lupin off too and Dumbledore could tell that Harry was troubled. Harry explained how guilty he felt allowing Pettigrew, the real culprit who had framed Sirius, to escape, which coincides with a prediction <a href="/wiki/Trelawney_family" title="Trelawney family">Trelawney</a> made. Therefore, he feared that he may have indirectly given Voldemort a servant to return him to power. Dumbledore assured Harry that he did a noble thing in saving Pettigrew's life, forging a deep, magical bond between them, and he promised Harry that one day he'd be glad he spared Pettigrew.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_36-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>At the end of the year Dumbledore began to feel uneasy about concealing the truth of <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney%27s_first_prophecy" title="Sybill Trelawney&#39;s first prophecy">Sybill Trelawney's prophecy</a> because even though Harry was still young, he had proven himself to be exceptional, and he would have to be told soon.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_41-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="1994–1995"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="1994.E2.80.931995">1994–1995</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=42" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: 1994–1995">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=42" title="Edit section: 1994–1995"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">"<i>It is my belief — and never have I so hoped that I am mistaken — that we are all facing dark and difficult times. Some of you in this Hall have already suffered directly at the hands of <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>... A week ago, a student was taken from our midst. Remember Cedric. Remember, if the time should come when you have to make a choice between what is right and what is easy, remember what happened to a boy who was good, and kind, and brave, because he strayed across the path of Lord Voldemort. Remember Cedric Diggory.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Dumbledore giving respect to Cedric Diggory<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div><p>Before the beginning of the new school year, the first <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a> activity in years broke out at the <a href="/wiki/Quidditch_World_Cup" title="Quidditch World Cup">Quidditch World Cup</a>, causing Dumbledore to suspect that the second rise of Lord Voldemort was near. Later, Hogwarts played host to the first <a href="/wiki/Triwizard_Tournament" title="Triwizard Tournament">Triwizard Tournament</a> since 1792. It was decided that only students of age would be allowed to enter their names to the Goblet of Fire, because of the dangers the tournament represented and its high death toll. Dumbledore personally drew an <a href="/wiki/Age_Line" title="Age Line">Age Line</a> around the magical artefact to ensure that this rule would be impossible to break. During this year, Dumbledore employed his old friend, <a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">Alastor Moody</a>, an ex-<a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">Auror</a>, as the new <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> Professor. Moody took this position only as a personal favour to Dumbledore.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_38-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup>
</p><figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b3/B4C16M1_Champions_chosen_v1.png/revision/latest?cb=20190326015217" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="91" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="B4C16M1 Champions chosen v1.png" data-image-key="B4C16M1_Champions_chosen_v1.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b3/B4C16M1_Champions_chosen_v1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190326015217" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b3/B4C16M1_Champions_chosen_v1.png/revision/latest?cb=20190326015217" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b3/B4C16M1_Champions_chosen_v1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190326015217" decoding="async" width="250" height="91" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="B4C16M1 Champions chosen v1.png" data-image-key="B4C16M1_Champions_chosen_v1.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b3/B4C16M1_Champions_chosen_v1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190326015217" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:B4C16M1_Champions_chosen_v1.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Albus Dumbledore withdrawing Harry's name from the <a href="/wiki/Goblet_of_Fire" title="Goblet of Fire">Goblet of Fire</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>However, unknown to anybody, a day before Moody was set to arrive at Hogwarts, he was overpowered by Death Eaters <a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">Barty Crouch, Jnr</a> and <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Peter Pettigrew</a>. On the orders of Voldemort, Crouch brewed <a href="/wiki/Polyjuice_Potion" title="Polyjuice Potion">Polyjuice Potion</a>, which he used to impersonate Moody and take his place at Hogwarts. Crouch, in the guise of Moody, successfully fooled the Goblet of Fire and ensured that <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> was chosen as the fourth champion of the Triwizard Tournament. Crouch secretly aided Potter throughout the tournament, so that in the final task it would be him to touch the Triwizard trophy first; which he had bewitched to become a <a href="/wiki/Portkey" title="Portkey">Portkey</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_38-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When Harry and fellow champion <a href="/wiki/Cedric_Diggory" title="Cedric Diggory">Cedric Diggory</a> touched the trophy at the same time they were transported to the graveyard of <a href="/wiki/Little_Hangleton" title="Little Hangleton">Little Hangleton</a>. There, Diggory was killed on the orders of Lord Voldemort, and Harry's blood was taken as the final ingredient in a potion the Dark Lord used to return to full power. Using the Portkey, Harry was able to escape Voldemort and return to Hogwarts.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_38-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4a/BartyCrouchJnr_PM.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160608173854" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="98" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="BartyCrouchJnr PM.jpg" data-image-key="BartyCrouchJnr_PM.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4a/BartyCrouchJnr_PM.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160608173854" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4a/BartyCrouchJnr_PM.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160608173854" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4a/BartyCrouchJnr_PM.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160608173854" decoding="async" width="250" height="98" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="BartyCrouchJnr PM.jpg" data-image-key="BartyCrouchJnr_PM.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4a/BartyCrouchJnr_PM.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160608173854" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:BartyCrouchJnr_PM.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore and Harry discover the location of the real Alastor Moody</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>It was when Crouch, still in the guise of Moody, took Harry from out of Dumbledore's presence (something the real Moody never would have done in such a traumatic situation) that the headmaster realised that it was not Moody who had been at the school the whole year. Dumbledore, Snape and <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</a> quickly overpowered the Death Eater. It was in that moment that Harry realised exactly why Dumbledore was the only wizard that Voldemort ever feared. Barty then truthfully revealed the entirety of Voldemort's plot and his participation in it under the influence of <a href="/wiki/Veritaserum" title="Veritaserum">Veritaserum</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_38-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/78/B4C36M1_Snape_Dark_Mark_reveal.png/revision/latest?cb=20180423221722" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="102" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="B4C36M1 Snape Dark Mark reveal.png" data-image-key="B4C36M1_Snape_Dark_Mark_reveal.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/78/B4C36M1_Snape_Dark_Mark_reveal.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180423221722" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/78/B4C36M1_Snape_Dark_Mark_reveal.png/revision/latest?cb=20180423221722" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/78/B4C36M1_Snape_Dark_Mark_reveal.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180423221722" decoding="async" width="250" height="102" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="B4C36M1 Snape Dark Mark reveal.png" data-image-key="B4C36M1_Snape_Dark_Mark_reveal.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/78/B4C36M1_Snape_Dark_Mark_reveal.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180423221722" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:B4C36M1_Snape_Dark_Mark_reveal.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore telling a disbelieving Fudge of Voldemort's return</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Despite all evidence to the contrary, Minister for Magic <a href="/wiki/Cornelius_Fudge" title="Cornelius Fudge">Cornelius Fudge</a> refused to believe that Lord Voldemort had returned to power and had Crouch subjected to the <a href="/wiki/Dementor%27s_Kiss" title="Dementor&#39;s Kiss">Dementor's Kiss</a> before he could be forced to stand trial before the <a href="/wiki/Wizengamot" title="Wizengamot">Wizengamot</a>. Despite this, Dumbledore knew that Voldemort's return was real and, in response to Fudge's failure to act, reformed the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a>, an alliance brought together during the <a href="/wiki/First_Wizarding_War" title="First Wizarding War">First Wizarding War</a> to fight against Voldemort and his followers. Dumbledore chose to reform the Order as he feared that the start of the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a> was lingering and inevitable to happen.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_38-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Again, Dumbledore was reminded of Harry's exceptional skill and knew that he would surely have to be told of the prophecy soon, but again he chose not to, out of a desire to spare Harry an additional burden.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_41-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="Second_Wizarding_War_(1995–1997)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Second_Wizarding_War_.281995.E2.80.931997.29">Second Wizarding War <span class="template-c">(1995–1997)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=43" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Second Wizarding War (1995–1997)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=43" title="Edit section: Second Wizarding War (1995–1997)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Evading_Cornelius_Fudge">Evading Cornelius Fudge</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=44" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Evading Cornelius Fudge">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=44" title="Edit section: Evading Cornelius Fudge"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Campaign_to_discredit_Albus_Dumbledore_and_Harry_Potter" title="Campaign to discredit Albus Dumbledore and Harry Potter">Campaign to discredit Albus Dumbledore and Harry Potter</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>They're trying to discredit him. Didn't you see the </i>Daily Prophet<i> last week? They reported that he'd been voted out of the <a href="/wiki/International_Confederation_of_Wizards" title="International Confederation of Wizards">International Confederation of Wizards</a> because he's getting old and losing his grip, but it's not true; he was voted out by Ministry wizards after he made a speech announcing Voldemort's return. They've demoted him from Chief Warlock on the Wizengamot, and they're thinking of removing his <a href="/wiki/Order_of_Merlin" title="Order of Merlin">Order of Merlin</a>, First Class too.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Dumbledore's discredit at the hands of the Ministry<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/78/Campaign_to_discredit_Albus_Dumbledore_and_Harry_Potter.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140530154139" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="396" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Campaign to discredit Albus Dumbledore and Harry Potter.jpg" data-image-key="Campaign_to_discredit_Albus_Dumbledore_and_Harry_Potter.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/78/Campaign_to_discredit_Albus_Dumbledore_and_Harry_Potter.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140530154139" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/78/Campaign_to_discredit_Albus_Dumbledore_and_Harry_Potter.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140530154139" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/78/Campaign_to_discredit_Albus_Dumbledore_and_Harry_Potter.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140530154139" decoding="async" width="250" height="396" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Campaign to discredit Albus Dumbledore and Harry Potter.jpg" data-image-key="Campaign_to_discredit_Albus_Dumbledore_and_Harry_Potter.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/78/Campaign_to_discredit_Albus_Dumbledore_and_Harry_Potter.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140530154139" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Campaign_to_discredit_Albus_Dumbledore_and_Harry_Potter.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Campaign to discredit Albus Dumbledore and Harry Potter</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The Ministry immediately began to deny Dumbledore and Harry's claims that the Dark Lord had returned, starting a smear campaign designed to slander and vilify them; in particular, Dumbledore was removed from his positions as <a href="/wiki/Chief_Warlock" title="Chief Warlock">Chief Warlock</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Wizengamot" title="Wizengamot">Wizengamot</a> and <a href="/wiki/Supreme_Mugwump" title="Supreme Mugwump">Supreme Mugwump</a> of the <a href="/wiki/International_Confederation_of_Wizards" title="International Confederation of Wizards">International Confederation of Wizards</a> as punishment for his refusal to stay in line with Ministry propaganda. However, Dumbledore professed not to care, so long as the Ministry did not eliminate him from <a href="/wiki/Chocolate_Frog_Card" title="Chocolate Frog Card">Chocolate Frog Cards</a>. He confessed that he believed that Fudge's persecution of him was of his own free will and not due to the <a href="/wiki/Imperius_Curse" title="Imperius Curse">Imperius Curse</a>, though this was small comfort.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_41-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Before the beginning of the school year, Dumbledore was made <a href="/wiki/Secret-Keeper" class="mw-redirect" title="Secret-Keeper">Secret-Keeper</a> of the headquarters of the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a>, and ensured that Harry Potter's friends did not divulge any information about the Order to him, as he did not want the Order to be compromised in anyway.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_41-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Dumbledore attended Harry's trial at the ministry, arriving three hours early at five a.m by a handy mistake. He presented <a href="/wiki/Arabella_Figg" title="Arabella Figg">Arabella Figg</a> for Harry's defence and offered to call <a href="/wiki/Dobby" title="Dobby">Dobby</a> to testify that Harry had not used a Hover Charm in 1992, and reminded Fudge that he himself had pardoned Harry's accidental inflation of <a href="/wiki/Marjorie_Dursley" title="Marjorie Dursley">Marjorie Dursley</a>. He also commented the unusual behaviour of the court holding a full criminal hearing for a simple case of underage magic. After the Wizengamot had ruled in Harry's favour Dumbledore left without having so much as spoken to Harry or looked at him.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_41-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When the time came to choose the <a href="/wiki/Prefect" title="Prefect">Prefects</a> from the fifth year Dumbledore considered Harry, but out of sympathy for the ordeals he had faced and the ones still to come, he chose to spare him the added responsibility and passed it on to <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a>. This decision confused some people who had assumed Harry would naturally receive it, and would have shown solidarity with the young wizard.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_41-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/08/Umbridge_speech.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160609132202" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="109" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Umbridge speech.jpg" data-image-key="Umbridge_speech.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/08/Umbridge_speech.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160609132202" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/08/Umbridge_speech.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160609132202" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/08/Umbridge_speech.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160609132202" decoding="async" width="250" height="109" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Umbridge speech.jpg" data-image-key="Umbridge_speech.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/08/Umbridge_speech.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160609132202" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Umbridge_speech.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a>, the new DADA professor interrupting Dumbledore</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Dumbledore had come to fear the connection that existed between the Dark Lord and Harry, and purposely avoided him throughout the school year. When signs of this connection became increasingly obvious, Dumbledore had <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a> attempt to teach Harry the art of <a href="/wiki/Occlumency" title="Occlumency">Occlumency</a>, rather than himself, as he feared that Voldemort may have been able to peer into his mind through his connection to Harry. The Ministry also began to interfere heavily at Hogwarts. They appointed Fudge's Senior Undersecretary (Dolores Umbridge) to the post of <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> professor.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_41-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Umbridge started her reign at Hogwarts by rudely interrupting Dumbldore's Start-of-Term Feast. Things got progressively worse from there. Umbridge and Fudge slowly passed rules and regulations that syphoned the powers of the Headmaster, while increasing those of Umbridge herself. Until finally Umbridge was granted the new position of <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_High_Inquisitor" title="Hogwarts High Inquisitor">High Inquisitor</a> of Hogwarts. In response to Umbridge and the Ministry's refusal to teach practical defensive magic, Harry Potter, <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a>, and Ron Weasley created a group of students that met secretly to learn defence against the <a href="/wiki/Dark_Arts" title="Dark Arts">Dark Arts</a>. With Harry acting as the leader and teacher, this organisation was known as Dumbledore's Army, in order to frighten the Ministry.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_41-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/B5C27M3_Dumbledore%27s_escape.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180423215252" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="98" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="B5C27M3 Dumbledore&#39;s escape.jpg" data-image-key="B5C27M3_Dumbledore&#39;s_escape.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/B5C27M3_Dumbledore%27s_escape.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180423215252" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/B5C27M3_Dumbledore%27s_escape.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180423215252" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/B5C27M3_Dumbledore%27s_escape.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180423215252" decoding="async" width="250" height="98" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="B5C27M3 Dumbledore&#39;s escape.jpg" data-image-key="B5C27M3_Dumbledore&#39;s_escape.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/B5C27M3_Dumbledore%27s_escape.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180423215252" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:B5C27M3_Dumbledore%27s_escape.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore escapes the Ministry workers: Fudge, Umbridge, Dawlish and Shacklebolt</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When this illegal society was uncovered, Dumbledore willingly took the blame; pointing out that it was named "<i><a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a>, not Potter's Army.</i>" While Fudge ordered his arrest, Dumbledore stated that he would not come quietly and easily overpowered his would-be captors with a single spell, and went underground; working to aid the Order full-time. In Dumbledore's stead, Umbridge was named Headmistress of <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a> and took full advantage of her position and authority over students and staff alike.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_41-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Duel_with_Lord_Voldemort">Duel with Lord Voldemort</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=45" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Duel with Lord Voldemort">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=45" title="Edit section: Duel with Lord Voldemort"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix"><b>Albus Dumbledore</b>: "<i>It was foolish to come here tonight, Tom. The Aurors are on their way —</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Voldemort</b>: "<i>By which time I shall be gone, and you dead!</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Dumbledore and Voldemort preparing to duel<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<p>Unfortunately, as Dumbledore had feared, Voldemort finally acted to use the connection between himself and Harry Potter. Using <a href="/wiki/Legilimency" title="Legilimency">Legilimency</a>, Voldemort created a vision that indicated that his beloved godfather, Sirius Black, had been captured by Voldemort personally and was being tortured by him within the <a href="/wiki/Department_of_Mysteries" title="Department of Mysteries">Department of Mysteries</a>. Harry, Ron, Hermione, <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny Weasley</a>, <a href="/wiki/Luna_Lovegood" title="Luna Lovegood">Luna Lovegood</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a> all rushed to the Ministry in the hopes of saving Sirius. However, the six students were ambushed by a group of Death Eaters, who hoped to force Harry to recover the record of the prophecy made about him and the Dark Lord. Voldemort perceived that it was too dangerous to enter the heart of the Ministry of Magic himself. Fortunately, Severus Snape was able to alert the Order to this and several members arrived in the Ministry where they battled with the Death Eaters.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_41-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d1/Dumbledore_and_Voldemort_duel.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190324225454" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="141" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dumbledore and Voldemort duel.gif" data-image-key="Dumbledore_and_Voldemort_duel.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d1/Dumbledore_and_Voldemort_duel.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190324225454" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d1/Dumbledore_and_Voldemort_duel.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190324225454" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d1/Dumbledore_and_Voldemort_duel.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190324225454" decoding="async" width="250" height="141" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dumbledore and Voldemort duel.gif" data-image-key="Dumbledore_and_Voldemort_duel.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d1/Dumbledore_and_Voldemort_duel.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190324225454" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dumbledore_and_Voldemort_duel.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore duels Voldemort</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Near the end of the battle, Dumbledore himself arrived and swiftly captured all the Death Eaters personally; except <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a>, who murdered Sirius and evaded a spell cast at her by the revered wizard. After binding the Death Eaters with an <a href="/wiki/Anti-Disapparition_Jinx" title="Anti-Disapparition Jinx">Anti-Disapparition Jinx</a>, Dumbledore went to the atrium of the Ministry where Lestrange had been joined by Voldemort himself, who attempted to kill Harry.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_41-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Voldemort's curse, however, was prevented; Dumbledore quickly animated a golden statue to cover Harry and shield him from the curse. He <a href="/wiki/Piertotum_Locomotor" title="Piertotum Locomotor">animated</a> the other statues from the <a href="/wiki/Fountain_of_Magical_Brethren" title="Fountain of Magical Brethren">Fountain of Magical Brethren</a> to immobilise Bellatrix and alert Ministry officials. With Voldemort having arrived in the Ministry, Dumbledore took this chance to give undeniable evidence to Fudge that the Dark Lord truly had returned and fought him both to protect Harry and hold him at bay. Dumbledore displayed his extraordinary magical capabilities as he calmly countered or dodged Voldemort‘s attacks and returned with his own assault that steadily forced Voldemort to go on the defensive, yet Dumbledore was not fighting to kill, a fact which surprised Voldemort. Soon enough, Dumbledore managed to trap the Dark Lord within an orb of water just after having been saved by Fawkes, who intercepted a killing curse Voldemort has shot at Dumbledore while the latter was countering the strike of a fiery serpent that Voldemort had conjured. Though Dumbledore had failed to capture or defeat Voldemort, the Dark Lord realised himself that he could not overpower his former teacher, and so abandoned his effort and disapparated.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_41-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/da/Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-14891.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170718223647" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="114" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-14891.jpg" data-image-key="Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-14891.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/da/Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-14891.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170718223647" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/da/Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-14891.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170718223647" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/da/Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-14891.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170718223647" decoding="async" width="250" height="114" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-14891.jpg" data-image-key="Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-14891.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/da/Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-14891.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170718223647" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-14891.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore telling Harry the whole prophecy in its entirety</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Before Voldemort fled the Ministry however, he briefly possessed Harry, hoping that Dumbledore would sacrifice the teenager in an attempt to kill him. However, Dumbledore did not take the bait as he cared for Harry too much to do it. Fortunately, Dumbledore did not have to resort to whatever means he would’ve needed to remove Voldemort from Harry himself, as the tremendous power of Harry's love, dwelt on his grief for his late godfather, inflicted great pain upon Voldemort and the Dark Lord was forced to remove himself and block his connection. With his failure to retrieve the prophecy and his attempt on Harry’s life foiled, Voldemort fled the Ministry with Bellatrix, but not before he was seen by Ministry officials, including Minister for Magic <a href="/wiki/Cornelius_Fudge" title="Cornelius Fudge">Cornelius Fudge</a>. With Dumbledore's credibility realised once more, Fudge's was permanently lost. Henceforth, Dumbledore successfully ensured that Fudge removed Umbridge, pardoned Hagrid so he could return to Hogwarts and he himself would be reinstated as headmaster.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_41-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Once he was back at Hogwarts, Dumbledore consulted with a distraught Harry, explaining the meaning of his connection with Voldemort and asserting the meaning of the prophecy. Before the end of the year, he also had the <a href="/wiki/Inquisitorial_Squad" title="Inquisitorial Squad">Inquisitorial Squad</a> disbanded and reverted any damage they did.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_41-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Training_Harry_Potter">Training Harry Potter</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=46" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Training Harry Potter">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=46" title="Edit section: Training Harry Potter"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_Albus_Dumbledore%27s_private_lessons" title="Harry Potter and Albus Dumbledore&#39;s private lessons">Harry Potter and Albus Dumbledore's private lessons</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">"<i>I have been hoping for this piece of evidence for a very long time. It confirms the theory on which I have been working, it tells me that I am right, and also how very far there is still to go.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Dumbledore having witnessed the memory of <a href="/wiki/Horace_Slughorn" title="Horace Slughorn">Horace Slughorn</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/49/Albus_Dumbledore_wearing_Marvolo_Gaunt%27s_Ring.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180811020304" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Albus Dumbledore wearing Marvolo Gaunt&#39;s Ring.jpg" data-image-key="Albus_Dumbledore_wearing_Marvolo_Gaunt&#39;s_Ring.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/49/Albus_Dumbledore_wearing_Marvolo_Gaunt%27s_Ring.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180811020304" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/49/Albus_Dumbledore_wearing_Marvolo_Gaunt%27s_Ring.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180811020304" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/49/Albus_Dumbledore_wearing_Marvolo_Gaunt%27s_Ring.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180811020304" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Albus Dumbledore wearing Marvolo Gaunt&#39;s Ring.jpg" data-image-key="Albus_Dumbledore_wearing_Marvolo_Gaunt&#39;s_Ring.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/49/Albus_Dumbledore_wearing_Marvolo_Gaunt%27s_Ring.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180811020304" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Albus_Dumbledore_wearing_Marvolo_Gaunt%27s_Ring.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore trying on Marvolo Gaunt's ring activating a nasty curse</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>During the summer of 1996, Dumbledore tracked one of Voldemort's Horcruxes to the house of the <a href="/wiki/House_of_Gaunt" title="House of Gaunt">Gaunts</a>. Dumbledore journeyed to <a href="/wiki/Little_Hangleton" title="Little Hangleton">Little Hangleton</a>, where he found the remains of the shack hidden behind weeds and bush. Voldemort had placed many powerful enchantments around the former home of his ancestors; however, Dumbledore proved skilful enough to pass through them unharmed. When he found the Horcrux, a ring formerly owned by <a href="/wiki/Marvolo_Gaunt" title="Marvolo Gaunt">Marvolo Gaunt</a>, he saw that the stone in the ring was one of the <a href="/wiki/Deathly_Hallows" title="Deathly Hallows">Deathly Hallows</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Resurrection_Stone" title="Resurrection Stone">Resurrection Stone</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_30-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>This stone, according to legend, had the power to revive the dead (but in reality, a spiritual form of the person was brought back instead, much like an echo). His desire to see his family overrode his common sense for just a moment and he placed the ring on his finger, forgetting that the ring had been cursed by Voldemort. The curse quickly spread, and were it not for his own prodigious talents, he would have died within moments. Despite this injury, Dumbledore proceeded to destroy the ring, and with it, a piece of Voldemort's <a href="/wiki/Soul" title="Soul">soul</a>, bringing Voldemort that much closer to defeat.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_30-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6b/Snape_and_Dumledore_curse.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161011235602" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="120" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Snape and Dumledore curse.jpg" data-image-key="Snape_and_Dumledore_curse.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6b/Snape_and_Dumledore_curse.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161011235602" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6b/Snape_and_Dumledore_curse.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161011235602" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6b/Snape_and_Dumledore_curse.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161011235602" decoding="async" width="250" height="120" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Snape and Dumledore curse.jpg" data-image-key="Snape_and_Dumledore_curse.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6b/Snape_and_Dumledore_curse.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161011235602" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Snape_and_Dumledore_curse.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape's skills manage to trap the curse on the ring in Dumbledore's hand</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Dumbledore quickly returned to <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>, where the skills of <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a> managed to trap the curse in Dumbledore's hand. However, both Snape and Dumbledore knew that it would eventually spread to the rest of his body. Knowing that the curse would kill him, Dumbledore asked Snape, that when the time came, that he be the one to end Dumbledore's life, rather than <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a>. Malfoy had been given the task of assassinating the headmaster, in order to spare Draco's <a href="/wiki/Soul" title="Soul">soul</a> from being torn Snape had to be the one to do it. Snape later objected to the plan, but was reminded by Dumbledore that it was the only way to spare him from great suffering. During this time, Dumbledore also shared his insights on Voldemort with Harry by showing him the various memories he had collected, giving Harry a greater knowledge of Voldemort's psychology that would help him in his future conflicts.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_30-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5c/Lesson_on_Horcruxes.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141224014816" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="106" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Lesson on Horcruxes.jpg" data-image-key="Lesson_on_Horcruxes.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5c/Lesson_on_Horcruxes.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20141224014816" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5c/Lesson_on_Horcruxes.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141224014816" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5c/Lesson_on_Horcruxes.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20141224014816" decoding="async" width="250" height="106" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Lesson on Horcruxes.jpg" data-image-key="Lesson_on_Horcruxes.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5c/Lesson_on_Horcruxes.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20141224014816" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Lesson_on_Horcruxes.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Harry and Dumbledore discuss memories of Tom Riddle</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Throughout the 1996–1997 school year, Dumbledore passed on certain pieces of information to <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> that would be important for the boy in his quest to destroy the Dark Lord. Dumbledore held private lessons with Harry, revealing in them much of what he had learnt about Voldemort's past, life and <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcruxes</a>. Dumbledore revealed to Harry that he made it his business to try and find out about <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>'s past. He did this by questioning people who had known him as a child and a teenager, and obtained Voldemort-related memories from them.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_30-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He collected memories from <a href="/wiki/Bob_Ogden" title="Bob Ogden">Bob Ogden</a>, <a href="/wiki/Morfin_Gaunt" title="Morfin Gaunt">Morfin Gaunt</a>, Horace Slughorn, and the house-elf Hokey. Using these memories, along with some of his own, he discovered that Voldemort had created six Horcruxes, an unheard of event, been guilty of murders that he framed others for, and also figured out what the Horcruxes could be based on Voldemort's ego and his long interest in Hogwarts: <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle%27s_Diary" class="mw-redirect" title="Tom Riddle&#39;s Diary">Tom Riddle's Diary</a>, <a href="/wiki/Marvolo_Gaunt%27s_Ring" title="Marvolo Gaunt&#39;s Ring">Gaunt's Ring</a>,<a href="/wiki/Helga_Hufflepuff%27s_Cup" class="mw-redirect" title="Helga Hufflepuff&#39;s Cup"> Hufflepuff's Cup</a>, <a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin%27s_Locket" class="mw-redirect" title="Salazar Slytherin&#39;s Locket">Slytherin's Locket</a>, <a href="/wiki/Nagini" title="Nagini">Nagini</a>, and an object of <a href="/wiki/Rowena_Ravenclaw" title="Rowena Ravenclaw">Rowena Ravenclaw</a>'s (later revealed to be her lost <a href="/wiki/Ravenclaw%27s_Diadem" title="Ravenclaw&#39;s Diadem">diadem</a>). They dismissed the idea of a Gryffindor artefact as unlikely as only the Sorting Hat and the <a href="/wiki/Sword_of_Gryffindor" title="Sword of Gryffindor">Sword of Gryffindor</a> remained as items from Gryffindor himself and Voldemort did not have access to them.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_30-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Hunting_for_Horcruxes">Hunting for Horcruxes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=47" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Hunting for Horcruxes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=47" title="Edit section: Hunting for Horcruxes"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">"<i>I would like you to wear your Cloak, please. Very good. Shall we go?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Dumbledore to Harry, before their journey to the cave<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Second_skirmish_at_the_Cave" title="Second skirmish at the Cave">Second skirmish at the Cave</a></i></div></dd>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/be/Halfblood-03561.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141227174834" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="107" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Halfblood-03561.jpg" data-image-key="Halfblood-03561.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/be/Halfblood-03561.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20141227174834" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/be/Halfblood-03561.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141227174834" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/be/Halfblood-03561.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20141227174834" decoding="async" width="250" height="107" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Halfblood-03561.jpg" data-image-key="Halfblood-03561.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/be/Halfblood-03561.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20141227174834" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Halfblood-03561.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore and Harry Potter in the <a href="/wiki/The_Cave" title="The Cave">Crystal Cave</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After much searching, Dumbledore eventually tracked another of Voldemort's Horcruxes to a cave that as a young orphan, he had once visited. As he had promised, Dumbledore allowed Harry Potter to accompany him to the cave and help destroy the Horcrux.
