Setting off from Hogwarts on an evening in early June 1997,<sup id="cite_ref-deathdate_5-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-deathdate-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> he and Harry <a href="/wiki/Apparition" title="Apparition">Apparated</a> to just outside the cave, being unable to enter directly due to its protective enchantments. Once inside, Dumbledore located the Horcrux's second line of defence; a hidden doorway which only opened when it received an offering of blood.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_30-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>They next found themselves in a vast chamber containing an underground lake, with a solitary island at its centre from which a faint green light was visible. After a failed attempt by Harry at <a href="/wiki/Summoning_Charm" title="Summoning Charm">Summoning</a> the Horcrux, Dumbledore located a carefully concealed boat that would allow them safe passage across the lake. During the crossing, Harry learned of the Horcrux's third line of defence; the lake was filled with <a href="/wiki/Inferius" title="Inferius">Inferi</a>, which would attack anyone who touched the lake's water. Dumbledore instructed Harry on the use of fire as the weapon of choice against the Inferi, should it become necessary.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_30-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Arriving at the small island, they found a basin filled with <a href="/wiki/Emerald_Potion" title="Emerald Potion">glowing green potion</a>. This last defence could not be removed by <a href="/wiki/Vanishing_Spell" title="Vanishing Spell">Vanishing</a> or being scooped out; someone would have to drink it to get to the Horcrux that lay within. Dumbledore ordered Harry to help him drink all of the potion, no matter what effects it caused, even if Harry had to force it down Dumbledore's throat.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_30-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Albus_Dumbledore_to_drink_Emerald_Potion.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140813154241" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="113" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Albus Dumbledore to drink Emerald Potion.jpg" data-image-key="Albus_Dumbledore_to_drink_Emerald_Potion.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Albus_Dumbledore_to_drink_Emerald_Potion.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140813154241" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Albus_Dumbledore_to_drink_Emerald_Potion.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140813154241" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Albus_Dumbledore_to_drink_Emerald_Potion.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140813154241" decoding="async" width="250" height="113" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Albus Dumbledore to drink Emerald Potion.jpg" data-image-key="Albus_Dumbledore_to_drink_Emerald_Potion.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Albus_Dumbledore_to_drink_Emerald_Potion.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140813154241" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Albus_Dumbledore_to_drink_Emerald_Potion.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore preparing to drink the <a href="/wiki/Emerald_Potion" title="Emerald Potion">Emerald Potion</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Dumbledore drank and he saw a vision of the duel between him, <a href="/wiki/Gellert_Grindelwald" title="Gellert Grindelwald">Gellert Grindelwald</a> and <a href="/wiki/Aberforth_Dumbledore" title="Aberforth Dumbledore">Aberforth Dumbledore</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ariana_Dumbledore" title="Ariana Dumbledore">Ariana</a>'s death. The drink also was weakening him and made him extremely thirsty as well and caused him great pain (the whole purpose of the potion). He couldn't bear it, but Harry succeeded at getting it down this throat, by telling him it would be over soon. On his last drink he fell unconscious. After a failed attempt by Harry to revive him with <a href="/wiki/Reviving_Spell" title="Reviving Spell">Rennervate</a>, Dumbledore woke up after his period of unconsciousness wanting water.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_30-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b2/Dumbledore-fire.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20080810070750" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="107" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dumbledore-fire.JPG" data-image-key="Dumbledore-fire.JPG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b2/Dumbledore-fire.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20080810070750" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b2/Dumbledore-fire.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20080810070750" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b2/Dumbledore-fire.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20080810070750" decoding="async" width="250" height="107" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dumbledore-fire.JPG" data-image-key="Dumbledore-fire.JPG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b2/Dumbledore-fire.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20080810070750" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dumbledore-fire.JPG" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Albus creating a fire storm to ward off the attacking Inferi</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Harry then attempted to summon water for Dumbledore with the <a href="/wiki/Water-Making_Spell" title="Water-Making Spell">Water-Making Spell</a>, but this proved ineffective as the <a href="/wiki/Water" title="Water">water</a>, for some reason, was scoop-resistant. In desperation, Harry filled a cup with water from the lake. After Dumbledore drank it, the Inferi climbed up from the lake and attempted to kill them. Harry panicked and attempted to fight back with a multitude of spells and curses, including the <a href="/wiki/Impediment_Jinx" title="Impediment Jinx">Impediment Jinx</a> and <i><a href="/wiki/Sectumsempra" title="Sectumsempra">Sectumsempra</a></i> <a href="/wiki/Curse" title="Curse">curse</a>, but none of them worked since the Inferi were too numerous and did not feel pain. Dumbledore, having regained consciousness, <a href="/wiki/Firestorm" title="Firestorm">created a ring of fire</a> around them that repelled the Inferi, driving them back into the lake while he and Harry escaped in the boat with the Horcrux. Harry used a small cut on his arm to reopen the hidden doorway, and once outside the cave they Disapparated back to <a href="/wiki/Hogsmeade" title="Hogsmeade">Hogsmeade</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_30-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=48" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Battle of the Astronomy Tower">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=48" title="Edit section: Battle of the Astronomy Tower"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">"<i>A jet of green light shot from the end of Snape’s wand and hit Dumbledore squarely in the chest. Harry’s scream of horror never left him; silent and unmoving, he was forced to watch as Dumbledore was blasted into the air: for a split second he seemed to hang suspended beneath the shining skull, and then he fell slowly backwards, like a great rag doll, over the battlements and out of sight.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Description of Dumbledore's death<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a></i></div></dd>
<p>They would find no rest there, however, as the Battle of the Astronomy Tower had already begun. Harry and Dumbledore took brooms from behind <a href="/wiki/Rosmerta" title="Rosmerta">Madam Rosmerta</a>'s bar and flew to the Astronomy Tower. Once at the <a href="/wiki/Astronomy_Tower" title="Astronomy Tower">Astronomy Tower</a>, Dumbledore and an invisibility-cloaked Harry were confronted by <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a>. Before Harry could reveal himself, Dumbledore immobilised him with a silent <a href="/wiki/Full_Body-Bind_Curse" title="Full Body-Bind Curse">Full Body-Bind Curse</a>, making it so he could only watch the upcoming event.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_30-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 222px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/20/Draco_disarms_dumbledore.gif/revision/latest?cb=20161007223528" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="220" height="98" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Draco disarms dumbledore.gif" data-image-key="Draco_disarms_dumbledore.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/20/Draco_disarms_dumbledore.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20161007223528" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/20/Draco_disarms_dumbledore.gif/revision/latest?cb=20161007223528" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/20/Draco_disarms_dumbledore.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20161007223528" decoding="async" width="220" height="98" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Draco disarms dumbledore.gif" data-image-key="Draco_disarms_dumbledore.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/20/Draco_disarms_dumbledore.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20161007223528" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Draco_disarms_dumbledore.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore being disarmed by Malfoy</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Malfoy disarmed Dumbledore, and admitted that he, Draco, was behind the series of attacks on Hogwarts students, and that Voldemort had ordered him to kill Dumbledore. Dumbledore revealed that he knew of Draco's mission and of the attempts on his life with the <a href="/wiki/Opal_Necklace" title="Opal Necklace">Opal Necklace</a> and poisoned mead, but allowed him to remain in Hogwarts for knowing Voldemort would kill him if he was exposed and expelled. Dumbledore offered Draco protection, and promised to hide Draco and his mother where Voldemort would never find them. Draco ultimately could not bring himself to kill the Headmaster, even after the arrival and encouragement of several Death Eaters, who were smuggled into the castle by Draco.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_30-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a7/Dumbledore_dies.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140813154818" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="150" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dumbledore dies.gif" data-image-key="Dumbledore_dies.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a7/Dumbledore_dies.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140813154818" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a7/Dumbledore_dies.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140813154818" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a7/Dumbledore_dies.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140813154818" decoding="async" width="245" height="150" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dumbledore dies.gif" data-image-key="Dumbledore_dies.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a7/Dumbledore_dies.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140813154818" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dumbledore_dies.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore's <a href="/wiki/Death" title="Death">death</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>However, Snape — who had been called by <a href="/wiki/Filius_Flitwick" title="Filius Flitwick">Filius Flitwick</a> to assist the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a>, sometime previously — arrived into the Tower and, after Dumbledore pleaded with him, in a way that did not expose Snape's true intentions, <a href="/wiki/Killing_Curse" title="Killing Curse">killed</a> the Headmaster, blasting his body off the tower and falling to the ground below.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_30-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>After all, to the well-organised mind, death is but the next great adventure.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Albus Dumbledore regarding the afterlife<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f7/HBP_Dumbledore%27s_Death_-_Exclusive_%40_Olumencia.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100131025336" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="227" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="HBP Dumbledore&#39;s Death - Exclusive @ Olumencia.jpg" data-image-key="HBP_Dumbledore&#39;s_Death_-_Exclusive_@_Olumencia.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f7/HBP_Dumbledore%27s_Death_-_Exclusive_%40_Olumencia.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20100131025336" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f7/HBP_Dumbledore%27s_Death_-_Exclusive_%40_Olumencia.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100131025336" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f7/HBP_Dumbledore%27s_Death_-_Exclusive_%40_Olumencia.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20100131025336" decoding="async" width="250" height="227" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="HBP Dumbledore&#39;s Death - Exclusive @ Olumencia.jpg" data-image-key="HBP_Dumbledore&#39;s_Death_-_Exclusive_@_Olumencia.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f7/HBP_Dumbledore%27s_Death_-_Exclusive_%40_Olumencia.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20100131025336" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:HBP_Dumbledore%27s_Death_-_Exclusive_@_Olumencia.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Harry kneeling over Dumbledore's body</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>A while later after the battle was over, Harry found Dumbledore’s body lying dead on the ground in front of hundreds of staring people, his body broken from the fall. Harry found the locket and read a letter written by <a href="/wiki/Regulus_Black" title="Regulus Black">R.A.B.</a> and realised that it was not a Horcrux, meaning the locket was a fake. Harry neither knew nor cared what this message meant and he felt that he and Dumbledore had accomplished nothing that night and that the latter had weakened himself by drinking the potion for nothing. Harry started crying over Dumbledore’s corpse as well as straightening his half-moon spectacles upon his crooked nose and Harry wiping a trickle of blood from the dead Headmaster’s mouth with his (Harry’s) own sleeve.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_30-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png/revision/latest?cb=20161209004341" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="98" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="B6C30M1 funeral of Albus Dumbledore.png" data-image-key="B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161209004341" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png/revision/latest?cb=20161209004341" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161209004341" decoding="async" width="250" height="98" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="B6C30M1 funeral of Albus Dumbledore.png" data-image-key="B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161209004341" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore's funeral</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Sometime in early July, a funeral was held for him, attended by Hogwarts students and staff, Ministry of Magic officials (including <a href="/wiki/Cornelius_Fudge" title="Cornelius Fudge">Cornelius Fudge</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rufus_Scrimgeour" title="Rufus Scrimgeour">Rufus Scrimgeour</a>, <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a> and <a href="/wiki/Percy_Weasley" title="Percy Weasley">Percy Weasley</a>), centaurs, members of the Order of the Phoenix (except Severus Snape, due to his covert status, and Mundungus Fletcher, due to his imprisonment in Azkaban), Hogsmeade residents including Dumbledore’s brother <a href="/wiki/Aberforth_Dumbledore" title="Aberforth Dumbledore">Aberforth</a>, <a href="/wiki/Fawkes" title="Fawkes">Fawkes</a>, Hagrid’s half-brother Grawp, Merpeople, <a href="/wiki/Tom" title="Tom">Tom</a> the landlord of the <a href="/wiki/Leaky_Cauldron" title="Leaky Cauldron">Leaky Cauldron</a>, <a href="/wiki/Olympe_Maxime" title="Olympe Maxime">Madame Maxime</a> from <a href="/wiki/Beauxbatons_Academy_of_Magic" title="Beauxbatons Academy of Magic">Beauxbatons Academy of Magic</a>, Bass player of the <a href="/wiki/Weird_Sisters" title="Weird Sisters">Weird Sisters</a> <a href="/wiki/Donaghan_Tremlett" title="Donaghan Tremlett">Donaghan Tremlett</a>, driver of the <a href="/wiki/Knight_Bus" title="Knight Bus">Knight Bus</a> <a href="/wiki/Ernest_Prang" title="Ernest Prang">Ernie Prang</a>, <a href="/wiki/Malkin" title="Malkin">Madam Malkin</a> of the robe shop in <a href="/wiki/Diagon_Alley" title="Diagon Alley">Diagon Alley</a>, the lady who pushed the trolley on the Hogwarts Express, as well as many other witches and wizards.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_30-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Post-mortem_and_legacy">Post-mortem and legacy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=49" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Post-mortem and legacy">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=49" title="Edit section: Post-mortem and legacy"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1997"><a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=50" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: 1997">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=50" title="Edit section: 1997"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/85/The_Life_and_Lies_of_Albus_Dumbledore_-_Mina_Lima_cover.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200420191232" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="370" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="The Life and Lies of Albus Dumbledore - Mina Lima cover.jpg" data-image-key="The_Life_and_Lies_of_Albus_Dumbledore_-_Mina_Lima_cover.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/85/The_Life_and_Lies_of_Albus_Dumbledore_-_Mina_Lima_cover.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200420191232" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/85/The_Life_and_Lies_of_Albus_Dumbledore_-_Mina_Lima_cover.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200420191232" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/85/The_Life_and_Lies_of_Albus_Dumbledore_-_Mina_Lima_cover.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200420191232" decoding="async" width="250" height="370" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="The Life and Lies of Albus Dumbledore - Mina Lima cover.jpg" data-image-key="The_Life_and_Lies_of_Albus_Dumbledore_-_Mina_Lima_cover.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/85/The_Life_and_Lies_of_Albus_Dumbledore_-_Mina_Lima_cover.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200420191232" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:The_Life_and_Lies_of_Albus_Dumbledore_-_Mina_Lima_cover.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><i><a href="/wiki/The_Life_and_Lies_of_Albus_Dumbledore" title="The Life and Lies of Albus Dumbledore">The Life and Lies of Albus Dumbledore</a></i></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After his death, Dumbledore's reputation was smeared somewhat by <a href="/wiki/Rita_Skeeter" title="Rita Skeeter">Rita Skeeter</a>, who wrote an insulting biography called <i>The Life and Lies of Albus Dumbledore</i>. This depicted him in a highly unfavourable light, including suggesting that he delayed his attack on <a href="/wiki/Gellert_Grindelwald" title="Gellert Grindelwald">Gellert Grindelwald</a> because he still held lingering affection for him.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_22-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1998"><a href="/wiki/1998" title="1998">1998</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=51" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: 1998">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=51" title="Edit section: 1998"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f7/Normal_face2face-pg-horizontal.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141122213433" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="149" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Normal face2face-pg-horizontal.jpg" data-image-key="Normal_face2face-pg-horizontal.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f7/Normal_face2face-pg-horizontal.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20141122213433" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f7/Normal_face2face-pg-horizontal.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141122213433" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f7/Normal_face2face-pg-horizontal.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20141122213433" decoding="async" width="250" height="149" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Normal face2face-pg-horizontal.jpg" data-image-key="Normal_face2face-pg-horizontal.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f7/Normal_face2face-pg-horizontal.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20141122213433" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Normal_face2face-pg-horizontal.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Voldemort breaks into Dumbledore's tomb</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In 1998, shortly prior to the start of the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, Lord Voldemort attempted to force the whereabouts of the <a href="/wiki/Elder_Wand" title="Elder Wand">Elder Wand</a> out of its previous owner, the same Gellert Grindelwald. Despite Grindelwald's refusal to disclose its location, Voldemort deduced that it would have been won by Dumbledore after he defeated Grindelwald in the <a href="/wiki/1940s" title="1940s">1940s</a>. He broke into the <a href="/wiki/White_Tomb" title="White Tomb">White Tomb</a> and stole the Wand in hopes of gaining access to its full power.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_22-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>As it turned out, the night of Dumbledore's death was not the last time Harry saw him. After finding out he was one of <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a>'s Horcruxes (Voldemort having accidentally made him one the night he tried to kill him), Harry bravely walked into Voldemort's camp to be killed, just as Dumbledore had (reluctantly) planned. But Voldemort's <a href="/wiki/Killing_Curse" title="Killing Curse">Killing Curse</a> once again failed to kill Harry. Instead, Harry entered a limbo state, where he spoke with Dumbledore's spirit. Dumbledore explained to Harry everything he had not told him when he was alive: the nature of the <a href="/wiki/Deathly_Hallows" title="Deathly Hallows">Deathly Hallows</a>, his friendship with <a href="/wiki/Gellert_Grindelwald" title="Gellert Grindelwald">Gellert Grindelwald</a> and a number of other things.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_22-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Most significantly, he revealed that Harry was not dead because, when Voldemort had used Harry's blood to restore his body, he had unintentionally linked Harry's life to his own, with the result that Voldemort's curse had 'killed' only the fragment of his <a href="/wiki/Soul" title="Soul">soul</a> that had remained in Harry all these years. Harry also attempted to console Dumbledore when his old teacher asked if he had been any better than Voldemort in his quest for power; Harry pointed out that Dumbledore had never killed if he could avoid it, and argued that Dumbledore's search for the Hallows, as opposed to any attempts to create <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcruxes</a>, made him completely different from Voldemort.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_22-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/61/DumbledoreHarryLimbo.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190326005857" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="DumbledoreHarryLimbo.gif" data-image-key="DumbledoreHarryLimbo.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/61/DumbledoreHarryLimbo.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190326005857" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/61/DumbledoreHarryLimbo.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190326005857" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/61/DumbledoreHarryLimbo.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190326005857" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="DumbledoreHarryLimbo.gif" data-image-key="DumbledoreHarryLimbo.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/61/DumbledoreHarryLimbo.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190326005857" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:DumbledoreHarryLimbo.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Harry Potter speaking with Albus Dumbledore in <a href="/wiki/Limbo" title="Limbo">Limbo</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After he had finished his talk, Dumbledore and Harry parted ways: Harry returned to the mortal world and Dumbledore moved, as he would put it, "on." He was the only Headmaster to be laid to rest on the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a> grounds, after Hagrid argued that no other Headmaster had ever given as much to the school as Dumbledore had. His <a href="/wiki/Headmaster_portraits" title="Headmaster portraits">portrait</a> also remained at Hogwarts. After Voldemort's death and Harry revealing that he was the true master of the Elder Wand, he said to <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore%27s_portrait" title="Albus Dumbledore&#39;s portrait">Dumbledore's portrait</a> that he was going to return the wand to his tomb where it would remain until he died and should he be undefeated, he would be the wand's last master which would break its power. He only used the wand for one feat: to repair his own wand which had been broken earlier.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_22-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Harry and <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny Potter</a>'s second son was named <a href="/wiki/Albus_Potter" title="Albus Potter">Albus Severus Potter</a>, after Dumbledore and Severus Snape.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_22-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2020–2021_school_year"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2020.E2.80.932021_school_year"><a href="/wiki/2020%E2%80%932021_school_year" title="2020–2021 school year">2020–2021 school year</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=52" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: 2020–2021 school year">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=52" title="Edit section: 2020–2021 school year"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/82/Albus_Dumbledore%27s_Portrait.gif/revision/latest?cb=20170428141922" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="217" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Albus Dumbledore&#39;s Portrait.gif" data-image-key="Albus_Dumbledore&#39;s_Portrait.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/82/Albus_Dumbledore%27s_Portrait.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170428141922" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/82/Albus_Dumbledore%27s_Portrait.gif/revision/latest?cb=20170428141922" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/82/Albus_Dumbledore%27s_Portrait.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170428141922" decoding="async" width="180" height="217" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Albus Dumbledore&#39;s Portrait.gif" data-image-key="Albus_Dumbledore&#39;s_Portrait.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/82/Albus_Dumbledore%27s_Portrait.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170428141922" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Albus_Dumbledore%27s_Portrait.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore's moving portrait, featuring Fawkes</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After his son, Albus Potter, got injured due to using a prototype <a href="/wiki/Time-Turner" title="Time-Turner">Time-Turner</a> to save Cedric Diggory, Harry visited the portrait of Dumbledore. He gave Harry advice of trying to see his son the way he is rather than make him be something he cannot be and later departed.<sup id="cite_ref-CC_88-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CC-88">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Harry approached him again after hearing Albus and <a href="/wiki/Scorpius_Malfoy" title="Scorpius Malfoy">Scorpius Malfoy</a>, the son of <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a>, are kidnapped by <a href="/wiki/Delphini" title="Delphini">Delphini</a>, the daughter of Lord Voldemort, where he asked Harry what he was doing and answered Harry's questions. Feeling like he was left "cleaning after the messes" Dumbledore left after he died, Harry asked him to leave. In response, Dumbledore tried to justify his actions. He stated that he wanted to fight Voldemort on his behalf but he "felt like he loved Harry too much to not realise that he should had trusted Harry more". He later gave Harry advice and left his portrait once more.<sup id="cite_ref-CC_88-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CC-88">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Dumbledore's reputation was so significant that even years after his death, the only reason Albus and Scorpius avoided contacting him for help when they found themselves stuck in 1981 was because they were concerned that even the knowledge of their existence would taint Dumbledore's future plans, as it was agreed that he had always known enough to know what to do or not to do and awareness of details such as Harry's future son might impact his plans.<sup id="cite_ref-CC_88-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CC-88">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Physical_appearance">Physical appearance</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=53" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Physical appearance">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=53" title="Edit section: Physical appearance"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>He was tall, thin, and very old, judging by the silver of his hair and beard, which were both long enough to tuck into his belt. He was wearing long robes, a purple cloak that swept the ground, and high-heeled, buckled boots. His blue eyes were light, bright, and sparkling behind half-moon spectacles and his nose was very long and crooked, as though it had been broken at least twice.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Dumbledore's physical appearance<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>Albus Dumbledore was tall and thin, with silver hair and beard (auburn in his youth) so long that they could be tucked into his belt. He had a very long and crooked nose that looked as if it had been broken at least twice. (It appears and is implied that his <a href="/wiki/Aberforth_Dumbledore" title="Aberforth Dumbledore">brother</a>'s punch during their <a href="/wiki/Ariana_Dumbledore" title="Ariana Dumbledore">sister</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Muggle_duelling" title="Muggle duelling">funeral</a> played a role in shaping his nose.) He was also said to have long and skilful fingers. His eyes were described to be a brilliant, soul-piercing shade of blue, and usually twinkled with kindness and mischief.
</p><p>When he became genuinely angry, however, Dumbledore would transform from a benign-looking, bright-eyed old man into a wizard even more terrifying than Lord Voldemort himself, with a face that was a classic portrait of cold fury and an aura of power that made him seem as if he was giving off burning heat. Indeed, Harry had — after witnessing a rare moment of Dumbledore's furious rage — confessed to fully understanding why people always said that Dumbledore was the only wizard Voldemort had ever feared.
</p><p>Dumbledore wore half-moon spectacles and a colourful array of robes, ranging from purple to crimson-red. He once claimed to have a scar above his left knee in the precise shape of a map of the London Underground, but whether or not he actually did is unknown. His demeanour was often — if not always — serene and ethereal, and he usually spoke in a calm, pleasant voice even when Harry thought that he was actually furious.
</p><p>During the last year of his life, Dumbledore's right hand was scarred when he donned the cursed Marvolo Gaunt's Ring. Had Severus Snape not intervened with a counter-curse, Dumbledore would have died within minutes. Regardless, the curse left his hand blackened and dead-looking and no amount of healing could repair the appearance. According to Snape, the curse would eventually spread itself from the contained hand and Dumbledore was doomed to die in no more than one year's time. Whether this means the blackening dead-look appearance would spread throughout the entire body is unknown. Death, however, served to restore him to full health and strength: his spirit was described as walking sprightly and upright, with hands that were both whole and white and undamaged, and looking exactly how Harry remembered him to be.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personality_and_traits">Personality and traits</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=54" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Personality and traits">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=54" title="Edit section: Personality and traits"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone"><b>Albus Dumbledore</b>: "<i>Welcome! Welcome to a new year at Hogwarts! Before we begin our banquet, I would like to say a few words. And here they are: Nitwit! Blubber! Oddment! Tweak! Thank you!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>Is he — a bit mad?</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Percy Weasley</b>: "<i>Mad? He's a genius! Best wizard in the world! But he is a bit mad, yes.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> and <a href="/wiki/Percy_Weasley" title="Percy Weasley">Percy Weasley</a> about Albus Dumbledore<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8c/Albus_Dumbledore_-_Richard_Harris_profile.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180510170158" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="353" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Albus Dumbledore - Richard Harris profile.jpg" data-image-key="Albus_Dumbledore_-_Richard_Harris_profile.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8c/Albus_Dumbledore_-_Richard_Harris_profile.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180510170158" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8c/Albus_Dumbledore_-_Richard_Harris_profile.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180510170158" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8c/Albus_Dumbledore_-_Richard_Harris_profile.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180510170158" decoding="async" width="250" height="353" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Albus Dumbledore - Richard Harris profile.jpg" data-image-key="Albus_Dumbledore_-_Richard_Harris_profile.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8c/Albus_Dumbledore_-_Richard_Harris_profile.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180510170158" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Albus_Dumbledore_-_Richard_Harris_profile.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore's flamboyant attire</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure><p>Considered by many to be the most powerful <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">wizard</a> of all time, Dumbledore was benevolent and wise, a great wizard in the vein of <a href="/wiki/Merlin" title="Merlin">Merlin</a>. He had an almost unearthly calm and relaxed demeanour and almost constantly gave off an aura of serenity and composure, rarely displaying intense emotions of anger or fear. He was known for typically speaking in a calm, collected voice, and being firm, but reasonable and kind. He was always courteous, even to people who he found rude or in the case of Fenrir Greyback, disgusting. However, despite his benign nature, it is said that Dumbledore was the only wizard <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> ever truly feared.
</p><p>Dumbledore was notably eccentric. He was quite fond of knitting patterns and frequently wore flamboyant clothing (at one point, he is seen wearing a flowered <a href="/wiki/Bonnet" title="Bonnet">bonnet</a> that he received from a <a href="/wiki/Wizard_Cracker" title="Wizard Cracker">Wizard Cracker</a>). In particular, he had a somewhat odd taste in sweets: he enjoyed Muggle sweets relatively unknown in the wizarding world (particularly <a href="/wiki/Sherbet_lemon" title="Sherbet lemon">sherbet lemons</a>) and the password to his office, supposedly that of his current favourite sweet, was often peculiar choices such as <a href="/wiki/Acid_Pops" title="Acid Pops">Acid Pops</a> and <a href="/wiki/Cockroach_Clusters" title="Cockroach Clusters">Cockroach Clusters</a>. In addition, he had a liking for <a href="/wiki/Chamber_music" title="Chamber music">chamber music</a> as well as <a href="/wiki/Ten-pin_bowling" title="Ten-pin bowling">ten-pin bowling</a>. He often used humour to make people feel comfortable in his presence. Dumbledore has been known to be quite philosophical; often, very few people have the understanding (or patience) to comprehend his philosophies.
</p><p>As a supremely talented wizard, Dumbledore showed numerous examples of extraordinary abilities. His capabilities as a <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">wizard</a> were combined with his extraordinary intellect and extremely cunning and subtle mind that allowed him to comprehend human nature and turn the better aspects of humanity (trust, <a href="/wiki/Love" title="Love">love</a> and friendship) to Voldemort's disadvantage in particular. Due to this, Dumbledore wielded extraordinary powers of deduction that allowed him to be completely unfooled by any charades who could fool even the entire wizarding world and recognise instantly any deception that may have initially fooled him at the slightest of slip ups, as shown repeatedly when he quickly figured out Quirell was distracting him with a letter he faked was from the Minister of Magic, was never fooled by Lockhart's books due to having knew what he truly was and quickly realised the truth, and deduced that Moody was actually Crouch Jnr the moment he asked Harry to be brought to his office. During his Hogwarts career, especially as headmaster Dumbledore always maintained his composure, even in situations that would terrify others. Being attacked by Ministry officials, the opening/re-opening of the Chamber of Secrets, having Dementors at the school, being surrounded by a plethora of Inferi and soon thereafter, staring death in the face (although they may have made him uneasy for the safety of others) did not frighten him. This was shown best at his duel with Voldemort, when he engaged in small talk with him in a calm, almost sardonically humorous way, despite Voldemort's tremondous duelling prowess and his attempts to murder him. Dumbledore was verbally and utterly unafraid of death and was obviously never scared of Voldemort himself, but rather what he may/could do to those he cared for and he was also not afraid of being exposed to great torment. An example of this was in <a href="/wiki/The_Cave" title="The Cave">The Cave</a>, when knowing that the <a href="/wiki/Emerald_Potion" title="Emerald Potion">Potion</a> would cause him severe pain and distress without knowing exactly what would happen to him, Dumbledore did not hesitate to drink it. Despite this, Dumbledore was capable of fear and feared, above all else, that he had actually cast the spell that ended his sister <a href="/wiki/Ariana_Dumbledore" title="Ariana Dumbledore">Ariana</a>'s life. However, he was capable of facing his fears, as shown by how he indirectly confessed his guilt to <a href="/wiki/Leta_Lestrange" title="Leta Lestrange">Leta Lestrange</a>, and by how he later ultimately mustered the strength to confront Grindelwald and end the <a href="/wiki/Global_wizarding_war" title="Global wizarding war">Global wizarding war</a> after years of watching Grindelwald's rampage. Therefore, Dumbledore's Boggart is said to be his sister's corpse.<sup id="cite_ref-JKR_12-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-JKR-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>While Dumbledore (at least in his later years) never displayed arrogance or conceit, he had no use for false modesty either, and if a situation warranted it, was perfectly willing to acknowledge his virtually peerless intelligence and power. He once told Harry that he was fairly confident in his ability to defeat Gellert Grindelwald despite the latter's own great skill and possession of the <a href="/wiki/Elder_Wand" title="Elder Wand">Elder Wand</a>. Dumbledore's portrait also professed to Harry that he had considered personally fighting Voldemort for Harry, further showing Dumbledore's self-confidence. However, Dumbledore also understood that he had his weaknesses and blind spots just as any other man, and worked hard to keep them in check.
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">"<i>As I have already proven to you, I make mistakes like the next man. In fact, being — forgive me — rather cleverer than most men, my mistakes tend to be correspondingly huger.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Dumbledore talks to Harry about his Horcrux theory, and the possibility of his making a mistake<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8d/Tom_and_Dumbledore.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20081012184300" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="107" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Tom and Dumbledore.jpg" data-image-key="Tom_and_Dumbledore.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8d/Tom_and_Dumbledore.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20081012184300" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8d/Tom_and_Dumbledore.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20081012184300" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8d/Tom_and_Dumbledore.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20081012184300" decoding="async" width="250" height="107" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Tom and Dumbledore.jpg" data-image-key="Tom_and_Dumbledore.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8d/Tom_and_Dumbledore.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20081012184300" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Tom_and_Dumbledore.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Albus Dumbledore proving to a young <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Tom Riddle</a> that the Headmaster is a wizard</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>More than anything else, Dumbledore was motivated by his belief in the power of the human spirit. He also had a deep capacity for love, frequently reminding Harry that love was the greatest magic of all. Dumbledore believed in the good in everyone and insisted on giving second chances. He notably argued strongly against the expulsions of <a href="/wiki/Newton_Scamander" title="Newton Scamander">Newton Scamander</a>, and later <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Rubeus Hagrid</a>, as well as refraining from expelling <a href="/wiki/Jacob%27s_sibling" title="Jacob&#39;s sibling">Jacob's sibling</a>, despite the latter repeatedly breaking school rules. Dumbledore also allowed <a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin" title="Remus Lupin">Remus Lupin</a> to be a pupil at his school and later a professor, despite the fact that Remus was a werewolf. He had a great friendship with Hagrid, despite many not trusting the half-Giant. The greatest example of this, however, is Dumbledore's relationship with <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>, in whom Dumbledore was willing to hold a considerable amount of faith after Severus had shown remorse. Dumbledore even saw a possibility for good in <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Tom Riddle</a> as a child, and was open to giving him a second chance, despite the fact that Tom had already revealed himself to be a cruel sociopath and bully even at a young age, though he kept a careful eye on Tom Riddle during his Hogwarts career rather than simply hoping for the best. Although he was devoted to Riddle's defeat after he became Voldemort, Dumbledore was genuinely regretful on how the days he could have easily intimidated Riddle into admitting his wrongdoings and taking responsibility for them were long gone, proving he felt a level of remorse for never managing to do anything significiant to change Riddle. In addition, Dumbledore also believed the rumours of Grindelwald showing remorse for his crimes during his time in prison and showed a level of respect and gratitude for Grindelwald's concealment of the true location of the Elder Wand for a shred of redemption even if it was in vain.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/04/Albus_Dumbledore_%28HBP_promo%29_1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20090817194206" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="334" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Albus Dumbledore (HBP promo) 1.jpg" data-image-key="Albus_Dumbledore_(HBP_promo)_1.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/04/Albus_Dumbledore_%28HBP_promo%29_1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20090817194206" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/04/Albus_Dumbledore_%28HBP_promo%29_1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20090817194206" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/04/Albus_Dumbledore_%28HBP_promo%29_1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20090817194206" decoding="async" width="250" height="334" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Albus Dumbledore (HBP promo) 1.jpg" data-image-key="Albus_Dumbledore_(HBP_promo)_1.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/04/Albus_Dumbledore_%28HBP_promo%29_1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20090817194206" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Albus_Dumbledore_(HBP_promo)_1.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Albus Dumbledore in thought</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Dumbledore was highly perceptive and emotionally intelligent; his knowledge of people's true personality went beyond being simply a good judge of character. This is never more apparent than in his complex insights into Voldemort's psyche, which he pieced together with Harry to deduce where the Horcruxes were hidden. However, this insight also made him extraordinarily good at manipulating people, which he was perfectly willing to do if he thought it necessary. Perhaps the most blatant example of this was with regard to Severus Snape, as he used Snape's love for the late Lilly Evans to manipulate him into helping him protect Harry Potter, her son, despite all the risks it entailed and despite Snape's bitterness and hatred towards Harry's father. Another note worth mentioning in this area, is Dumbledore conjured a bottle of gin to help ease <a href="/wiki/Cole" title="Cole">Mrs Cole</a> during their conversation. He did not offer her a glass, but simply produced it, knowing she would drink it. A lesser note of his emotional insight was with Gilderoy Lockhart: despite Lockhart having fooled every inhabitants in the wizarding world with his books, Dumbledore, having knew what he truly was, was completely unable to be tricked by Lockhart and he was able to effortlessly manipulate Lockhart into taking the job of DADA Professor by slyly hinting Harry Potter was in Hogwarts attending his second year so he can expose him.
</p><p>In spite of Dumbledore's many extraordinary qualities, he was also a somewhat Machiavellian figure.<sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89">&#91;89&#93;</a></sup> He could be stoically pragmatic and was extremely prone to secrecy. He spent a short portion of his youth concocting plans with <a href="/wiki/Gellert_Grindelwald" title="Gellert Grindelwald">Gellert Grindelwald</a> for global domination over <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggles</a>, in the process treating his ill sister with neglect. Whilst Dumbledore was never a deliberately cruel man, at times, he was too far-sighted, making choices that he believed to be for the benefit of humanity even if it deeply hurt some of the people around him. For example, he placed Harry Potter with the Dursley family despite knowing that they would be unlikely to treat him well, as pointed out by Professor McGonagall, all for the sake of keeping him alive.
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>I knew my brother, Potter. He learned secrecy at our mother's knee. Secrets and lies, that's how we grew up, and Albus... he was a natural... How can you be sure, Potter, that my brother wasn't more interested in the greater good than in you? How can you be sure you aren't dispensable, just like my little sister?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Aberforth Dumbledore bitterly describes his brother's inner nature<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>Dumbledore's greatest personality flaw, which he explained to <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a> in 1998,<sup id="cite_ref-DH_22-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> was his desire for power. Particularly in his younger days, he acknowledged that he had been quite selfish and that because of his extraordinary abilities, he had wanted fame, power, and glory for himself. When he and <a href="/wiki/Gellert_Grindelwald" title="Gellert Grindelwald">Gellert Grindelwald</a> were in school, they made plans to enslave Muggles and re-establish wizards as the natural rulers of the world. However, when his sister <a href="/wiki/Ariana_Dumbledore" title="Ariana Dumbledore">Ariana Dumbledore</a> was killed during a duel between himself, <a href="/wiki/Aberforth_Dumbledore" title="Aberforth Dumbledore">Aberforth Dumbledore</a>, and Grindelwald, any desire to accomplish this goal left him. The incident led to him declining any attempts by others to offer him positions of great political authority, and he refused to take the post of Minister of Magic at least three times.
</p><p>Dumbledore, while often kind and calm, did have a very serious side of himself and was capable of a terrifying wrath. This was rarely seen, but appears to be well known and combined with his exceptional magical abilities, made very few of his allies willing to cross him and almost all of his enemies feared him, to the point that even <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> and <a href="/wiki/Gellert_Grindelwald" title="Gellert Grindelwald">Gellert Grindelwald</a> were known for fearing him, despite their own incredible magical powers, wrath and status as the two most dangerous dark wizards in history. Even a slight exertion of Dumbledore's serious side and anger could intimidate the likes of <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, and even the Minister of Magic <a href="/wiki/Cornelius_Fudge" title="Cornelius Fudge">Cornelius Fudge</a>, evidenced when they both were shocked when Dumbledore made it clear quite firmly that Hagrid did not open the Chamber of Secrets, despite Dumbledore not openly showing anger. Additionally, rather than shouting when Harry entered Hogwarts with the <a href="/wiki/Flying_Ford_Anglia" title="Flying Ford Anglia">Ford Anglia</a>, and when Harry failed to get <a href="/wiki/Horace_Slughorn" title="Horace Slughorn">Slughorn</a>'s memory, just an expression of calm disappointment on both occasions was enough to make Harry feel ashamed to the point that he found it preferable if Dumbledore shouted at him. At the apex of Dumbledore's wrath, which happened extremely rarely, such as when he apprehended <a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">Barty Crouch Jnr</a>, who impersonated Moody and almost killed Harry, Dumbledore was described as "being struck with cold, ancient fury". In fact, during this rare moment of intense anger (caused by Dumbledore's realisation that, not only had Voldemort been resurrected, but also that he had been expertly deceived for an entire year), Dumbledore was so terrifying, that even <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</a> and <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>, both extremely powerful and stern wizards who rarely displayed emotions, were clearly uneasy. Harry himself (who was also slightly terrified of his reaction) fully understood then why Dumbledore was the only wizard that Voldemort ever feared. In addition to being completely unintimidated but rather saddened by Harry's profound bursts of rage regarding Sirius, in all the other times Harry unleashed his anger, Dumbledore proved himself capable of quelling even Harry's anger with just a slight exertion of his dark side, as he silenced Harry's questions regarding his judgement of Draco and Snape and even silenced Harry's anger with just indicating he had crossed the line, showing even Harry's rage could not match the seriousness and fury the old but extraordinarily powerful wizard was capable of.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d6/Harry-potter-half-blood-movie-screencaps.com-14905.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150720182901" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="138" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry-potter-half-blood-movie-screencaps.com-14905.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter-half-blood-movie-screencaps.com-14905.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d6/Harry-potter-half-blood-movie-screencaps.com-14905.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150720182901" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d6/Harry-potter-half-blood-movie-screencaps.com-14905.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150720182901" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d6/Harry-potter-half-blood-movie-screencaps.com-14905.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150720182901" decoding="async" width="250" height="138" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry-potter-half-blood-movie-screencaps.com-14905.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter-half-blood-movie-screencaps.com-14905.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d6/Harry-potter-half-blood-movie-screencaps.com-14905.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150720182901" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter-half-blood-movie-screencaps.com-14905.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore's grief</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Fantastic Beasts: The Crimes of Grindelwald - The Original Screenplay">"<i>Regret is my constant companion. Do not let it become yours.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Albus Dumbledore on the nature of regret<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Fantastic_Beasts:_The_Crimes_of_Grindelwald_-_The_Original_Screenplay" title="Fantastic Beasts: The Crimes of Grindelwald - The Original Screenplay">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>Dumbledore was haunted by his traumatic family history. In particular, he was riddled with guilt over the circumstances surrounding the death of his sister. He felt enormous remorse for his selfishness and was tortured for the rest of his life by the possibility that he might have been the one who cast the spell that killed his sister, to the point that he delayed facing Grindelwald until there was no other choice, due to him fearing what his former friend might have known about the death of Ariana. However, he had enough sense to realise that he will inevitably have to duel Grindelwald and therefore he took the position as the Professor of DADA to prepare students for the upcoming dark times. Additionally, Dumbledore's own guilt allowed him to comfort <a href="/wiki/Leta_Lestrange" title="Leta Lestrange">Leta Lestrange</a> over her own guilt in the role she had in her brother <a href="/wiki/Corvus_Lestrange_(V)" title="Corvus Lestrange (V)">Corvus</a>' death. Indeed, it was Dumbledore's advice to Leta that induced her to save <a href="/wiki/Credence_Barebone" title="Credence Barebone">Credence Barebone</a> from <a href="/wiki/Yusuf_Kama" title="Yusuf Kama">Yusuf Kama</a>'s revenge.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f8/Albuson.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190404220237" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Albuson.jpg" data-image-key="Albuson.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f8/Albuson.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190404220237" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f8/Albuson.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190404220237" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f8/Albuson.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190404220237" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Albuson.jpg" data-image-key="Albuson.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f8/Albuson.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190404220237" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Albuson.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore's excitement</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Dumbledore wasn't afraid of death as he believed "to the well organised mind, death is but <a href="/wiki/Afterlife" title="Afterlife">"the next great adventure."</a> Even during his short time in Limbo, he expressed his excitment o Harry for what awaits him. At time Dumbledore could feel the pressure of his role in the world acutely, and relied on his Pensieve to deal with them. He kept vials of memories which he could view in his Pensieve, some of which were his own. He often used this to find connections he might have missed before, and also when he felt he had "too many memories".
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Possessions">Possessions</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=55" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Possessions">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=55" title="Edit section: Possessions"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ae/Pensieve2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20090803154714" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="143" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Pensieve2.jpg" data-image-key="Pensieve2.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ae/Pensieve2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20090803154714" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ae/Pensieve2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20090803154714" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ae/Pensieve2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20090803154714" decoding="async" width="250" height="143" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Pensieve2.jpg" data-image-key="Pensieve2.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ae/Pensieve2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20090803154714" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Pensieve2.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore's <a href="/wiki/Pensieve" title="Pensieve">Pensieve</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Dumbledore's office housed "a number of curious... instruments." Among them was a <a href="/wiki/Pensieve" title="Pensieve">Pensieve</a>, a stone receptacle used to store and review memories, which witches and wizards are able to extract from their heads as a type of fluid. Harry first discovered this device to witness Dumbledore's memory of <a href="/wiki/Igor_Karkaroff" title="Igor Karkaroff">Igor Karkaroff</a>'s trial before the <a href="/wiki/Wizengamot" title="Wizengamot">Wizengamot</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_38-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> and also used it to view <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>'s memories of childhood. During the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_Albus_Dumbledore%27s_private_lessons" title="Harry Potter and Albus Dumbledore&#39;s private lessons">private lessons between Harry and Dumbledore</a>, the Pensieve was used to view a variety of memories about <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Tom Riddle</a>'s past.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_30-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Dumbledore was also seen using the <a href="/wiki/Deluminator" title="Deluminator">Deluminator</a>, a device for removing and later returning light, and for use as a homing device.<sup id="cite_ref-PS1_8-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS1-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> It was confirmed when the object was inherited by Ron that the Deluminator was of Dumbledore's own design.<sup id="cite_ref-DH7_90-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH7-90">&#91;90&#93;</a></sup> Dumbledore was the possessor and master of the <a href="/wiki/Elder_Wand" title="Elder Wand">Elder Wand</a>, an extremely powerful <a href="/wiki/Wand" title="Wand">wand</a> known also as the "Wand of Destiny" or the "Deathstick", and one of the <a href="/wiki/Deathly_Hallows" title="Deathly Hallows">Deathly Hallows</a>, until he was disarmed by Draco Malfoy at the top of the Astronomy Tower.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_30-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> The wand's allegiance was then transferred to Harry Potter nearly a year later.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_22-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> Unlike many of the wand's previous owners, Dumbledore kept its identity a closely guarded secret. 
</p><p>He also owned a pet <a href="/wiki/Phoenix" title="Phoenix">phoenix</a> named <a href="/wiki/Fawkes" title="Fawkes">Fawkes</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-COS_31-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COS-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> who left Hogwarts Castle after Dumbledore's death.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_30-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> It was revealed in that two of Fawkes' feathers form the <a href="/wiki/Wand_core" title="Wand core">magical cores</a> of both Harry's and Voldemort's <a href="/wiki/Wand" title="Wand">wands</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_22-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Professor Dumbledore kept a <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore%27s_journal" title="Albus Dumbledore&#39;s journal">journal</a> in which he would have written in regularly. He also kept a <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore%27s_pocket_watch" title="Albus Dumbledore&#39;s pocket watch">pocket watch</a> with twelve hands, but instead of numbers it had little planets moving around the edge.<sup id="cite_ref-PS1_8-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS1-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Magical_abilities_and_skills">Magical abilities and skills</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=56" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Magical abilities and skills">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=56" title="Edit section: Magical abilities and skills"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/52/Firestorm.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140408213652" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="150" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Firestorm.gif" data-image-key="Firestorm.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/52/Firestorm.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140408213652" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/52/Firestorm.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140408213652" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/52/Firestorm.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140408213652" decoding="async" width="245" height="150" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Firestorm.gif" data-image-key="Firestorm.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/52/Firestorm.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140408213652" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Firestorm.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore casting a very powerful <a href="/wiki/Firestorm" title="Firestorm">firestorm</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">"<i>Albus Dumbledore is the greatest sorcerer in the world.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Harry Potter regarding Dumbledore's magical skill<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>Dumbledore was an outstandingly talented wizard, even while still only a student of <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>, excelling in many fields of magic to the point of being recognised as the most brilliant student to ever attend the school, rivalled only by the prodigiously brilliant <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Tom Riddle</a>, and attaining many awards and prizes that required incredible magical capability to obtain. As an adult, Dumbledore had become an extraordinarily powerful and accomplished wizard of nearly unrivalled abilities and powers, to the point that he was admired and feared by even others of outstanding magical talent, considered to be the greatest wizard of all time by many. Indeed, Dumbledore was the only wizard capable of defeating <a href="/wiki/Gellert_Grindelwald" title="Gellert Grindelwald">Gellert Grindelwald</a> and later forcing Lord Voldemort himself on the defensive.
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>Examined him personally in Transfiguration and Charms when he did N.E.W.T.s ... Did things with a wand I’d never seen before ...</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;<a href="/wiki/Griselda_Marchbanks" title="Griselda Marchbanks">Griselda Marchbanks</a> regarding Dumbledore's exceptional magical skills in his youth<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Magic" title="Magic">Magical</a> mastery</b>: After his first year at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>, Dumbledore was already known to be outstandingly talented and prodigiously accomplished in the magical arts, and seen by some as nothing less than the most gifted student the school had ever seen, winning many awards and prizes that required magical capability beyond his age. As an adult, Albus Dumbledore was considered by many to be the greatest <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">wizard</a> in modern history, if not in all of wizarding history, and he lived up to this assessment on many occasions with his exemplary mastery of magic. He returned to the school to teach first <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a>, excelling to the point that he was considered by many of his pupils as the best teacher in Hogwarts. During the earlier stages of <a href="/wiki/Gellert_Grindelwald" title="Gellert Grindelwald">Gellert Grindelwald</a>'s rise to power, even former Head of the Department of Magical Law Enforcement, <a href="/wiki/Torquil_Travers" title="Torquil Travers">Torquil Travers</a>, begrudgingly admitted that he considered Dumbledore the only wizard with the skill and power needed to defeat Grindelwald, despite his own personal dislike of the Professor.
