Indeed, even Grindelwald himself acknowledged that Dumbledore posed a bigger threat to his <a href="/wiki/For_the_Greater_Good" title="For the Greater Good">cause</a> than any other living wizard and believed that only the extremely powerful Obscurial <a href="/wiki/Credence_Barebone" title="Credence Barebone">Credence Barebone</a> could possibly be capable of killing him. Ultimately, it was Dumbledore's own, direct involvement that ultimately ended the <a href="/wiki/Global_wizarding_war" title="Global wizarding war">Global wizarding war</a> when Albus engaged Grindelwald and ultimately prevailed despite Grindelwald's mastery of the Elder Wand, with <a href="/wiki/Duel_between_Albus_Dumbledore_and_Gellert_Grindelwald" title="Duel between Albus Dumbledore and Gellert Grindelwald">their legendary duel</a> being such an amazing display of power and skill that, according to the eyewitnesses, it was as the greatest wizarding battle ever fought between two wizards, with Albus admitting that he had ultimately been a "shade more skillful” than Grindelwald. Later in his teaching career, he taught <a href="/wiki/Transfiguration_(class)" title="Transfiguration (class)">Transfiguration</a>, a notably complex and difficult branch of magic, and soon rose to the position of the <a href="/wiki/Head_of_Transfiguration" title="Head of Transfiguration">Head of Transfiguration</a> of the school. He would eventually become the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Headmaster" title="Hogwarts Headmaster">Headmaster of the highly prestigious wizarding school</a> and soon established a well-deserved reputation as the most capable headmaster to ever lead Hogwarts, with even Tom Riddle acknowledging Dumbledore as being a worthy choice of the title of Headmaster and going so far as to ask why he would not not take the position of the <a href="/wiki/Minister_for_Magic" title="Minister for Magic">Minister for Magic</a>, which he openly admitted Dumbledore to be fully capable of excelling in, with his ability to uphold the defences of the school being such that not even Voldemort could have ever breached the school or even dared to attempt to do so while it was under Dumbledore's protection, as Dumbledore was the only wizard that the Dark Lord ever feared, with Hogwarts being considered the only safe place left in the wizarding world that was safe from the most powerful dark wizard of all time. When they faced each other in magical combat, Dumbledore proved capable of pressuring Voldemort's overwhelming magical skill and powers with his own while, in Voldemort's own admission, not even fighting to kill, forcing Voldemort on the defensive and to eventually disapparate. Dumbledore also expressed full confidence that he could easily break out from the notoriously secure <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a> even if he was imprisoned. When everything was said and done, Dumbledore had such a profound understanding and knowledge of how magic worked, even at his younger days, that he stood above nearly every other wizard alive, and earned the respect of many famously accomplished wizards, such as the magical theoretician <a href="/wiki/Adalbert_Waffling" title="Adalbert Waffling">Adalbert Waffling</a> and the magical historian, <a href="/wiki/Bathilda_Bagshot" title="Bathilda Bagshot">Bathilda Bagshot</a>. and the alchemist, <a href="/wiki/Nicolas_Flamel" title="Nicolas Flamel">Nicholas Flamel</a>. Throughout his life, he greatly contributed to the advancement of magical knowledge in modern times and became a famous contributor to many magical scholarly journals. Dumbledore also proved capable of overcoming the powerful dark wards placed by Voldemort on the hiding place of his Horcruxes, effortlessly bypassing the enchantments he placed on the <a href="/wiki/Gaunt_Shack" title="Gaunt Shack">Gaunt Shack</a> and doing the same to all but the enchantment on the <a href="/wiki/Emerald_Potion" title="Emerald Potion">Potion of Despair</a> in the Horcrux Cave. In the latter, he showed the currently unmatched ability to detect and analyse magic seemingly upon merely touching or laying his hands, which he used to pass through all of Voldemort's defences.</li>
<li><b>Intellectual genius</b>: Dumbledore was not only a great wizard, but also possessed a tremendous intellect, being considered to be among the most brilliant student to ever attend Hogwarts (rivaled only by Tom Riddle), and, as an adult, was regarded by many as being cleverer than almost any other wizard alive. His intelligence was especially evident through his tactical and strategic genius, proving himself capable of devising elaborate master plans to defeat the most powerful <a href="/wiki/Dark_Wizard" title="Dark Wizard">Dark wizards</a> seen for centuries and oppose their seemingly unstoppable ascensions to power. Particularly good at guessing, hypothesising, and predicting, Dumbledore informed his former student <a href="/wiki/Newton_Scamander" title="Newton Scamander">Newt Scamander</a> about where he could find an illegally trafficked <a href="/wiki/Thunderbird" title="Thunderbird">Thunderbird</a>, knowing that Newt would make haste to save it and take it to <a href="/wiki/United_States_of_America" title="United States of America">America</a> to set it free once it was nursed back to health, and, aware of Grindelwald's intention of infiltrating <a href="/wiki/Magical_Congress_of_the_United_States_of_America" title="Magical Congress of the United States of America">MACUSA</a> while looking for the Obscurial in New York, hoping his former student would find a way to thwart him. The results of this ploy ultimately culminated in the capture of <a href="/wiki/Gellert_Grindelwald" title="Gellert Grindelwald">Gellert Grindelwald</a> and the nine months-delay<sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup> in Grindelwald getting his hand on <a href="/wiki/Credence_Barebone" title="Credence Barebone">Credence Barebone</a>, and the prevention of the exposure of wizardkind to the non-magical world following the <a href="/wiki/Obscurial_attack_on_New_York" title="Obscurial attack on New York">Obscurial attack on New York</a> of <a href="/wiki/1926" title="1926">1926</a>. Following this, he was also able to follow Grindelwald's train of thought in regards to how he would go about recruiting his followers, and guessed correctly that his old friend would set up the <a href="/wiki/International_Statute_of_Wizarding_Secrecy" title="International Statute of Wizarding Secrecy">International Statute of Wizarding Secrecy</a> to be this tool of suppression and offer people freedom from it. Despite his <a href="/wiki/Blood_pact" title="Blood pact">Blood pact</a> with Grindelwald limiting Dumbledore's ability to get directly involved, as well as the constant Ministry surveillance of him, Dumbledore's tactical advice to then Head of the <a href="/wiki/Auror_Office" title="Auror Office">Auror Office</a>, <a href="/wiki/Theseus_Scamander" title="Theseus Scamander">Theseus Scamander</a>, that if he and his men resorted to excessive force to deal with Grindelwald and his followers during the latter's <a href="/wiki/Gellert_Grindelwald%27s_Paris_rally" title="Gellert Grindelwald&#39;s Paris rally">rally</a>, it would only serve to reinforce the point Grindelwald was making about the supposed totalitarian regime of the <a href="/wiki/International_Confederation_of_Wizards" title="International Confederation of Wizards">International Confederation of Wizards</a> and the magical governments that supported it in the minds of those who chose to follow him. Dumbledore continued to play an important, if indirect, role throughout the <a href="/wiki/Global_wizarding_war" title="Global wizarding war">Global wizarding war</a>, with his tactical expertise granting the wizarding world the ability to hold against Grindelwald for sixteen years, buying him enough time to destroy the <a href="/wiki/Blood_Pact" class="mw-redirect" title="Blood Pact">Blood Pact</a> and finally defeat Grindelwald. When <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> rose to power one generation later, Dumbledore's strategic brilliance successfully lead the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> against <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>'s forces for eleven years during the <a href="/wiki/First_Wizarding_War" title="First Wizarding War">First Wizarding War</a>. This was seen quite predominantly again during the events surrounding the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a>, when Dumbledore, through various strategical plans and an almost Machiavellian manipulation of key persons (such as <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a> and <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>) before his death, was able to set the path for <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> to locate Lord Voldemort's <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcruxes</a>, and defeat the Dark Lord. Dumbledore's intellect, his strategic thinking in particular, is one of his key talents. A lesser but still very remarkable testament to his strategical aptitude was his ability to come up with a master plan to save Sirius immediately after learning of his innocence by giving subtle hints to Hermione Granger regarding the Time Turner and later effectively avoid capture from the Ministry while doing jobs for the Order. His genius was also noticeable even after his death, through his will. Dumbledore displayed himself to be immensely foresightful, as he was able to accurately predict the possibility of <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a> initially walking out on the <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore_and_Harry_Potter%27s_Horcrux_Hunt" title="Albus Dumbledore and Harry Potter&#39;s Horcrux Hunt">Horcrux hunt</a> and understand that he would be just as likely to return to it and gave him his <a href="/wiki/Deluminator" title="Deluminator">Deluminator</a> to help him find his way back to Harry and Hermione and use <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a>'s thirst for knowledge to lead her to becoming curious about the symbol of the Deathly Hallows by drawing it in the copy of that he left her, which ultimately led to Harry not only learning of the <a href="/wiki/Deathly_Hallows" title="Deathly Hallows">Deathly Hallows</a> and finally having inserted the <a href="/wiki/Resurrection_Stone" title="Resurrection Stone">Resurrection Stone</a> into the <a href="/wiki/Golden_Snitch" title="Golden Snitch">Golden Snitch</a> that Harry first caught, learned on how to remove it, thus giving Harry the emotional support he needed to sacrifice himself to the Dark Lord. Dumbledore also possessed an exceptional amount of emotional intelligence, deductive abilities and immense intellectual perception, as he was able to completely see through Voldemort's charismatic mask of being a model student and had a considerable understanding of Voldemort's nature, something that allowed him to accurately deduce the location of his Horcruxes. In addition, he was intelligent enough to keep such a watchful eye over Riddle ever since his first opening of the Chamber of Secrets that he effectively kept the Heir of Slytherin from opening the Chamber the second time. He was also the only wizard who was not fooled by <a href="/wiki/Gilderoy_Lockhart" title="Gilderoy Lockhart">Gilderoy Lockhart</a>'s tall tales and was able to easily work out that Lockhart was a fraud from his personal knowledge of him and of two wizards whose memories had been modified by Lockhart. Dumbledore was also not fooled by <a href="/wiki/Quirinus_Quirrell" title="Quirinus Quirrell">Quirinus Quirrell</a>'s timid guise, correctly deducing that he had been working for Voldemort ever since he finished his journey, and although he was initially fooled by Quirell's false letter that said the Ministry needed him, Dumbledore was able to quickly figure it out and return to Hogwarts in time to save Harry. He managed to eventually see through <a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">Bartemius Crouch Junior</a>'s disguise as <a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">Alastor Moody</a> when he took Harry from him, which he said the real Moody never would have done, whereas Snape and McGonagall couldn't see through the disguise, and only followed Dumbledore when he ordered it, coming up with a clever plan to overpower the latter's <a href="/wiki/Occlumency" title="Occlumency">Occlumency</a> by first heavily weakening him with his Stunning Spell before having him exposed to <a href="/wiki/Veritaserum" title="Veritaserum">Veritaserum</a> and also swiftly deducing the pieces of the simple but brilliant plan Crouch used to disguise himself by keeping Moody alive but Imperiused and very weakened in order to ensure he couldn't overpower him and also insert the Polyjuice Potion inside his flask to drink without suspicion. He could easily identify whatever form <a href="/wiki/Jacob%27s_sibling" title="Jacob&#39;s sibling">Jacob's sibling</a> took using the <a href="/wiki/Polyjuice_Potion" title="Polyjuice Potion">Polyjuice Potion</a>, even if said disguise could fool the likes of McGonagall and Snape, and was able to easily help them get away unpunished by slyly revealing his knowledge of their disguise and even rewarding as well as warning them without any suspicion. He was also able to easily outwit the notoriously famous hack journalist <a href="/wiki/Rita_Skeeter" title="Rita Skeeter">Rita Skeeter</a>, having easily caught up with all her escapades at Hogwarts and quickly luring her into a position where he could have easily had her arrested by revealing his knowledge of her Animagus power, therefore leaving Rita effectively at his mercy and preventing her from writing anything directly antagonising towards him, doing so much faster than the also highly intelligent Hermione Granger. Additionally, even <a href="/wiki/Cornelius_Fudge" title="Cornelius Fudge">Cornelius Fudge</a> admired Dumbledore's genius, and thus bombarded Dumbledore with letters asking for advice early into his Minister of Magic career.</li>
<li><b>Charisma</b>: While not famous for his abilities as a manipulator, due to Dumbledore's exceptional amount of emotional intelligence, he was nevertheless exceptionally adept at manipulating others, which he was perfectly willing to do for the greater good, and displayed an immense amount of charisma, able to effectively use a person's characteristics to his advantage to get them to do what must be done and inspire loyalty in others. Unlike <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a>, Dumbledore always sought and used the best within people to get them to do his good-intended bidding and used his charisma to get many to the side of good instead of evil. He was able to effortlessly manipulate <a href="/wiki/Newton_Scamander" title="Newton Scamander">Newton Scamander</a> into believing his intentions when telling him about the illegally trafficked <a href="/wiki/Thunderbird" title="Thunderbird">Thunderbird</a> were purely to just safe the poor creature while actually he was also intending for Newt to stop <a href="/wiki/Gellert_Grindelwald" title="Gellert Grindelwald">Grindelwald</a> from discovering the <a href="/wiki/Obscurial" title="Obscurial">Obscurial</a>'s identity. He could also successfully convince the people he met to tell him about Voldemort and his time outside school despite the fear Voldemort inflicted upon them. The most notable display of his masterful manipulating abilities was when he was able to effectively manipulate <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a> into agreeing to protect <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> and act as a spy in Voldemort's ranks for Dumbledore despite Snape's bitterness and hatred towards Harry's father and full knowledge of the risks his job had by using Snape's love for <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily Evans</a>. Another display of his consummate manipulation skills was when he effortlessly manipulated <a href="/wiki/Gilderoy_Lockhart" title="Gilderoy Lockhart">Gilderoy Lockhart</a> into becoming a teacher at Hogwarts by just slyly hinting that Harry Potter was a second-year student at the school, and being a teacher to the "famous Harry" would propel Lockhart's fame into the stratosphere, notably taking advantage of Lockhart's hunger for more fame and ego to get him to agree to take the job so he could expose him, despite Lockhart not being eager to take the job due to being more interested in his career as an author. Dumbledore's charisma garnered him so much respect and loyalty from his allies that most of them still proved loyal to Dumbledore even after his death and valiantly fought in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a> for him. Indeed, Dumbledore was able to quickly befriend Harry Potter and inspired so much loyalty from his protégé that he was able to successfully get him to continue the hunt for <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcruxes</a>, despite Harry's resentment of Dumbledore's secrecy, and even eventually sacrifice himself as Dumbledore had planned.</li>
<li><b>Teaching skills</b>: Having apparently always been highly interested in teaching, from a young age, Dumbledore already displayed the ability to be a good mentor-like figure and model to his fellow student friends, as noted by <a href="/wiki/Elphias_Doge" title="Elphias Doge">Elphias Doge</a>, and as an adult, Dumbledore's teaching talents coupled with his extraordinary magical capabilities made him fully capable of managing the position of the Professor of <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> and of <a href="/wiki/Transfiguration" title="Transfiguration">Transfiguration</a> at Hogwarts so well as to be considered the greatest teacher at Hogwarts during his time as an instructor. Indeed, his status on the staff was such that he even earned the confidence of his predecessor as Headmaster, Professor <a href="/wiki/Armando_Dippet" title="Armando Dippet">Armando Dippet</a>, and was able to persuade him to allow <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Rubeus Hagrid</a> to stay at Hogwarts as an assistant to the Mr <a href="/wiki/Ogg" title="Ogg">Ogg</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Keeper_of_Keys_and_Grounds" title="Keeper of Keys and Grounds">Groundskeeper</a> of the day, thus henceforth earning the undying respect and loyalty of his former student. Dumbledore also successfully guided <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</a> into becoming an <a href="/wiki/Animagus" title="Animagus">Animagus</a>, which was known to be very difficult to do, by the age of 17. He also noted that he was fully confident that had he been the one who taught <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> <a href="/wiki/Occlumency" title="Occlumency">Occlumency</a>, he would have been able to mould Harry into a successful enough of an Occlumens to resist <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a>. Hermione and Ron were also sure that when Dumbledore gave Harry private lessons, he wanted to teach Harry the most advanced martial magic and was confident that Harry would have learned enough from Dumbledore to be capable of fulfilling the Prophecy. Due to his emotional wisdom and ability to show compassion to all, Dumbledore was also highly adept at offering emotional guidance and also teaching certain people how to perceive the emotional state of others to the point of making even some of the most reclusive students opening up to him, as displayed by his ability to get <a href="/wiki/Leta_Lestrange" title="Leta Lestrange">Leta Lestrange</a> to open up about her brother's death by revealing his own mistakes of not loving <a href="/wiki/Ariana_Dumbledore" title="Ariana Dumbledore">Ariana</a> enough, which ultimately allowed Leta to save <a href="/wiki/Credence_Barebone" title="Credence Barebone">Credence Barebone</a> from <a href="/wiki/Yusuf_Kama" title="Yusuf Kama">Yusuf Kama</a>'s revenge, and gave her the mental fortitude to resist <a href="/wiki/Gellert_Grindelwald" title="Gellert Grindelwald">Gellert Grindelwald</a>'s persuasive speech, and also effectively teach Harry into understanding Voldemort from their private lessons together, which was undoubtedly helpful in Harry's victory over the Dark Lord, as well as grant him the fortitude needed to remain steadfast against Voldemort no matter what happened. As <a href="/wiki/Headmaster" title="Headmaster">Headmaster</a>, Dumbledore even agreed to admit <a href="/wiki/Werewolf" title="Werewolf">werewolf</a> <a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin" title="Remus Lupin">Remus Lupin</a> to Hogwarts, taking the necessary precautions to avoid Remus' monthly transformations from endangering the other students, and forbidding <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a> to reveal Remus' secret, which made Remus fully loyal and highly respectful to him. Dumbledore was also partly responsible (along with some other Hogwarts staff) for teaching and training Lord Voldemort himself, who, while at Hogwarts was considered the most brilliant student to ever attend the school (by Dumbledore) and who later, despite his evil, grew up to be the most powerful dark wizard of all time, and was considered to be the one of the most powerful wizards in history, rivalled only by Dumbledore himself.</li>
<li><b>Leadership skills</b>: Even during his youth, Dumbledore was already an excellent leader, having been good enough to be appointed the <a href="/wiki/British_Youth_Representative_to_the_Wizengamot" title="British Youth Representative to the Wizengamot">British Youth Representative to the Wizengamot</a> and he and Grindelwald were confident they would be fully capable of quickly starting the <a href="/wiki/For_the_Greater_Good" title="For the Greater Good">For the Greater Good</a> revolution to conquer the wizarding world and put down the Muggles. However, he quickly learned his lesson from this mistake and while he had acquired the understanding of what being a leader truly was, he still acknowledged the potential of <a href="/wiki/Newton_Scamander" title="Newton Scamander">Newton Scamander</a> and Harry Potter as being greater than his, as they quickly proved themselves to be more qualified from the beginning due to their lack of lust for power and their willingness to accept any responsibility given to them no matter how large. Nevertheless, the lessons he had learned from his youthful mistakes made him an extraordinarily skilful leader indeed and he was well-respected and feared by many and with his uncanny ability to quickly get his followers to trust him, to the point his skills as a leader was held in such a high regard that he was even offered the position of <a href="/wiki/Minister_for_Magic" title="Minister for Magic">Minister for Magic</a> many times and would have most definitely greatly excelled, with Harry adamantly acknowledging that Dumbledore would have been a far better Minister than <a href="/wiki/Cornelius_Fudge" title="Cornelius Fudge">Cornelius Fudge</a> and <a href="/wiki/Rufus_Scrimgeour" title="Rufus Scrimgeour">Rufus Scrimgeour</a> without hesitation, despite his great anger at Dumbledore at the time, therefore acknowledging his inferiority to Dumbledore as a leader despite Dumbledore's own acknowledgment of Harry being more gifted than he was. Fudge himself held Dumbledore's leadership brilliance in such a high regard to the point that he would often ask for his advice. During the <a href="/wiki/Global_wizarding_war" title="Global wizarding war">Global wizarding war</a>, Dumbledore was able to give useful leadership advice to both <a href="/wiki/Auror_Office" title="Auror Office">Head Auror</a> <a href="/wiki/Theseus_Scamander" title="Theseus Scamander">Theseus Scamander</a>, and Head of <a href="/wiki/Department_of_Magical_Law_Enforcement" title="Department of Magical Law Enforcement">Magical Law Enforcement</a> <a href="/wiki/Torquil_Travers" title="Torquil Travers">Torquil Travers</a> concerning how to best combat <a href="/wiki/Gellert_Grindelwald" title="Gellert Grindelwald">Gellert Grindelwald</a>, though Travers would disregard it but his advice allowed Theseus and most of his allies to survive unscathed Grindelwald's rally in Paris and it was his leadership expertise giving advice to the wizarding authorities that allowed the wizarding world to be not conquered by Grindelwald long enough for Dumbledore to abolish the Blood Pact and defeat Grindelwald personally. It was around this time that Dumbledore also personally taught the prodigious young Tom Riddle, who would ironically grow up to be the most powerful dark wizard of all time, and Dumbledore‘s greatest rival. After Dumbledore's promotion to <a href="/wiki/Headmaster" title="Headmaster">Headmaster</a> of <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a>, he lead the school so effectively, that many considered him the greatest headmaster Hogwarts would ever see. Dumbledore's leadership expertise also allowed him to handle the responsibilities of the <a href="/wiki/Chief_Warlock" title="Chief Warlock">Chief Warlock</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Wizengamot" title="Wizengamot">Wizengamot</a> and <a href="/wiki/Supreme_Mugwump" title="Supreme Mugwump">Supreme Mugwump</a> of the <a href="/wiki/International_Confederation_of_Wizards" title="International Confederation of Wizards">International Confederation of Wizards</a> with such effectiveness as to be well-respected for it by many, according to his friend Elphias Doge. Later on, a more experienced Dumbledore was able to found and effectively lead the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> against <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> and the latter's <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> in both the <a href="/wiki/First_Wizarding_War" title="First Wizarding War">First</a> and <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding Wars</a>, in secret. His leadership allowed Dumbledore to stand against the overwhelming forces of darkness at both the First and Second Wizarding War, despite also having to avoid the <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Magic" title="Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a>'s eyes, inspiring enough loyalty into his allies to make them be fearless and determined that the cause they were fighting for was right even with the massive losses of their loved ones. Due to Dumbledore's leadership skills, many high-ranking Ministry officials, such as <a href="/wiki/Torquil_Travers" title="Torquil Travers">Torquil Travers</a>, <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Cornelius_Fudge" title="Cornelius Fudge">Cornelius Fudge</a>, were shown to fear what would happen if Dumbledore was plotting to overthrow the Ministry, implying that had Dumbledore wanted to, he could easily have overthrown the British Ministry of Magic but he never had any intention of doing so.</li></ul>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>Dumbledore flicked his own wand. The force of the spell that emanated from it was such that Harry, though shielded by his stone guard, felt his hair stand on end as it passed, and this time Voldemort was forced to conjure a shining silver shield out of thin air to deflect it. The spell, whatever it was, caused no visible damage to the shield, though a deep, gonglike note reverberated from it, an oddly chilling sound....</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Dumbledore duelling Lord Voldemort<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6c/DumbVold.gif/revision/latest?cb=20170501083534" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="141" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="DumbVold.gif" data-image-key="DumbVold.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6c/DumbVold.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170501083534" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6c/DumbVold.gif/revision/latest?cb=20170501083534" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6c/DumbVold.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170501083534" decoding="async" width="250" height="141" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="DumbVold.gif" data-image-key="DumbVold.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6c/DumbVold.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170501083534" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:DumbVold.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore pushing back <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> in a clash of magical power</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Duelling" title="Duelling">Duelling</a></b>: Albus Dumbledore was a duellist of extraordinary, almost unrivalled skill. Even at a young age, Dumbledore was already a highly proficient duellist, as he held his own against <a href="/wiki/Gellert_Grindelwald" title="Gellert Grindelwald">Grindelwald</a> and <a href="/wiki/Aberforth_Dumbledore" title="Aberforth Dumbledore">Aberforth</a> in their <a href="/wiki/Duel_at_Godric%27s_Hollow" title="Duel at Godric&#39;s Hollow">three-way duel</a>. As an adult, in addition to having achieved great success in teaching the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a> students in the art of <a href="/wiki/Martial_magic" title="Martial magic">martial magic</a> during his time as the <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> professor, as displayed by the level of ability shown by his students Newt, Theseus and Leta, all of whom became seasoned Ministry magical combatants during the <a href="/wiki/Global_Wizarding_War" class="mw-redirect" title="Global Wizarding War">Global Wizarding War</a>, Dumbledore was acknowledged by even the abrasive <a href="/wiki/Torquil_Travers" title="Torquil Travers">Torquil Travers</a> to be the only one skilful enough to fight and bring Grindelwald in. Even Grindelwald himself acknowledged Dumbledore would be easily capable of overpowering any of his followers, which made him a threat to his revolution even though at the time they could not fight each other directly due to their <a href="/wiki/Blood_pact" title="Blood pact">blood pact</a>, and noted that only <a href="/wiki/Credence_Barebone" title="Credence Barebone">Credence Barebone</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Obscurus" title="Obscurus">Obscurus</a> form would be capable of slaying Dumbledore in magical combat. Even at the height of Grindelwald's power, where the Dark Wizard had killed so many, the whole wizarding world still acknowledged Dumbledore could defeat him and indeed, despite Grindelwald's mastery of the Elder Wand, Albus ultimately proved capable of beating him in what many considered to be the greatest duel ever to be fought, with him describing himself as being a "shade more skillful" than Grindelwald. Prior to his <a href="/wiki/Curse_on_Marvolo_Gaunt%27s_ring" title="Curse on Marvolo Gaunt&#39;s ring">injury</a> and consuming the <a href="/wiki/Emerald_Potion" title="Emerald Potion">Drink of Despair</a> in <a href="/wiki/1996" title="1996">1996</a>, it remained a fact that any witch or wizard would, regardless of skill, would be no match for him,<sup id="cite_ref-92" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-92">&#91;92&#93;</a></sup> to the point that even the extraordinarily powerful <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> strongly preferred to refrain from a face to face confrontation with Dumbledore: Even when the latter was extremely angry over Dumbledore's rejection of his proposal to become DATDA'S Professor, despite coming close to, he refrained from drawing his wand and attacking Dumbledore. During the <a href="/wiki/First_Wizarding_War" title="First Wizarding War">First Wizarding War</a>, when confronting <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>, who was a very accomplished wizard even then, over the Prophecy, Dumbledore instantly disarmed and grounded him before his adversary could react. During the time when <a href="/wiki/Patricia_Rakepick" title="Patricia Rakepick">Patricia Rakepick</a> was present in Hogwarts, Snape noted that Dumbledore was the only one who could certainly defeat the extremely deadly curse-breaker and even Rakepick appeared to be unwilling to confront Dumbledore directly. <a href="/wiki/Jacob%27s_sibling" title="Jacob&#39;s sibling">Jacob's sibling</a>, perhaps the best student duellist, noted that it would tantamount to suicide to try to infiltrate his office. He swiftly dealt with five werewolves that attacked Hagrid's hut during <a href="/wiki/Fenrir_Greyback%27s_attack_on_Hogwarts" title="Fenrir Greyback&#39;s attack on Hogwarts">Fenrir Greyback's attack on Hogwarts</a> without a single scratch. Following the <a href="/wiki/Return_of_Lord_Voldemort" title="Return of Lord Voldemort">Return of Lord Voldemort</a>, upon discovering that one of the teaching staff were in fact a <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a> impersonating ex-Auror <a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">Alastor Moody</a>, Dumbledore quickly blindsided and subdued <a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">Bartemius Crouch Junior</a> with a single <a href="/wiki/Stunning_Spell" title="Stunning Spell">Stunning Spell</a> of such power that it blasted apart the magically sealed door to the <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts_Professor%27s_office" class="mw-redirect" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts Professor&#39;s office">Defence Against the Dark Arts Professor's office</a> and immediately floored said Azkaban escapee, knocking him unconscious. During his attempted arrest by the Ministry of Magic during the <a href="/wiki/1995%E2%80%931996_school_year" title="1995–1996 school year">1995–1996 school year</a>, Dumbledore, with a single spell, instantly defeated <a href="/wiki/Cornelius_Fudge" title="Cornelius Fudge">Cornelius Fudge</a>, <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kingsley_Shacklebolt" title="Kingsley Shacklebolt">Kingsley Shacklebolt</a>, and <a href="/wiki/John_Dawlish" title="John Dawlish">John Dawlish</a> when they attempted to arrest him (though Kingsley was secretly on Dumbledore's side) and escaped. During the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a>, Dumbledore soundly rounded up all of the <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> who had earlier managed to avoid capture from the other Order members just before the following <a href="/wiki/Duel_in_the_Ministry_Atrium" title="Duel in the Ministry Atrium">Duel in the Ministry Atrium</a> took place, during which he swiftly incapacitated the extremely powerful Bellatrix Lestrange, one of Lord Voldemort's most dangerous followers. He subsequently calmly duelled Voldemort himself, countering his attacks and responding with such powerful assault as to force the Dark Lord into constant defence before eventually trapping him in an orb or water, forcing him to disapparate and to try and possess Harry to get Dumbledore to mercy kill the boy. Even with his wand hand irreparably injured, he still remained an extremely skilful duelist, as he noted he was fully confident he could repel any attack attempted on him and Harry by Voldemort‘s followers in case it happened while they travelled to find Slughorn and escort Harry to the Burrow and effortlessly defeated Dawlish again, showing he still could overpower even a seasoned <a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">Auror</a> in his weakened condition rather easily. Dumbledore's duelling style was extremely versatile and dexterous, effortlessly capable of flawlessly adapting to the situation shown during the Battle of the Department of Mysteries, where while fighting the lesser threats posed by the Death Eaters, Dumbledore would simply immediately use powerful magic to incapacitate them, but when fighting the tremendously powerful Dark Lord himself, Dumbledore not only used some of his most powerful spells but also manipulated the environment into securing Bellatrix was out of the fight and Harry was safe, used Fawkes by taking advantage of the latter's immortality to block Voldemort's Killing Curse, and apparating at times to dodge Voldemort's spells before swiftly counter-attacking, a method of duelling that proved considerably efficient when used against the Dark Lord.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a></b>: With the subject apparently being his most prominent expertise out of his many magical abilities, Albus Dumbledore held the position of <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> Professor at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a> for more than twenty years and excelled to the point of being deemed the best teacher in the whole school during his time teaching the subject, showcasing his expertise in fending off <a href="/wiki/Dark_Arts" title="Dark Arts">Dark Forces</a>, up until Torquil Travers banned Dumbledore from teaching the subject. The full extent of Dumbledore's abilities in this field were perhaps best shown during the uprisings of <a href="/wiki/Gellert_Grindelwald" title="Gellert Grindelwald">Gellert Grindelwald</a> and <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>, who were both regarded at the time of their respective rebellions as the most dangerous <a href="/wiki/Dark_Wizard" title="Dark Wizard">Dark Wizard</a> of all time, during which not only did popular opinion quickly grow during both conflicts that Albus Dumbledore would be the only one who could possibly put an end to their respective and seemingly unstoppable reigns of terror, but also that both of the aforementioned dark wizards feared Dumbledore and were unwilling to challenge him directly, with those who opposed said dangerous criminals often being quick to rally at his side. His knowledge and ability where <a href="/wiki/Protective_enchantment" title="Protective enchantment">protective enchantments</a> was concerned was perhaps best shown during his time as <a href="/wiki/Headmaster" title="Headmaster">Headmaster</a> of Hogwarts, when he was personally responsible for upholding the magical protections around the school, and many felt that there was no safer place in the world than Hogwarts Castle, which was even said to be more secure than <a href="/wiki/Gringotts_Wizarding_Bank" title="Gringotts Wizarding Bank">Gringotts Wizarding Bank</a>, as the castle's defences were of a standard the likes of which, most likely, no other previous Headmaster had achieved. Indeed, Dumbledore's <a href="/wiki/Defensive_Charm" title="Defensive Charm">defensive spellwork</a> was so powerful and sophisticated that not even Voldemort himself could find a way through them. In addition, Dumbledore was apparently the primary leader of the staff's efforts in containing the damage unleashed by the opening of the <a href="/wiki/Cursed_Vaults" title="Cursed Vaults">Cursed Vaults</a> and the staff noted repeatedly that had Dumbledore not been absent, he could have succeeded, where they had trouble, easily. Dumbledore was also highly accomplished and knowledgeable in fending off Dark creatures, as shown by him successfully mentoring his students, including the unique <a href="/wiki/Newton_Scamander" title="Newton Scamander">Newt Scamander</a>, on how to overcome a <a href="/wiki/Boggart" title="Boggart">Boggart</a>, only failing with <a href="/wiki/Leta_Lestrange" title="Leta Lestrange">Leta Lestrange</a> due to the tremendous guilt she had over her brother's death, and later by his ability to produce an extremely powerful <a href="/wiki/Patronus_Charm" title="Patronus Charm">Patronus Charm</a> capable of single-handedly chasing away all of the <a href="/wiki/Dementor" title="Dementor">Dementors</a> that <a href="/wiki/Cornelius_Fudge" title="Cornelius Fudge">Cornelius Fudge</a> had ordered stationed around Hogwarts without it even being a corporeal one. Dumbledore was also highly familiar with the concept of <a href="/wiki/Inferius" title="Inferius">Inferi</a> and how to defend against them using fire and in addition to thoroughly explaining to Harry Potter how they were created by Voldemort, he was able to swiftly force off the large army of Inferi in the Horcrux Cave with a single Firestorm. Dumbledore was also aware that an <a href="/wiki/Obscurus" title="Obscurus">Obscurus</a> can be potentially healed by replacing the feelings that made that person an <a href="/wiki/Obscurial" title="Obscurial">Obscurial</a> with a sense of love and belonging, hence he gave such advice to <a href="/wiki/Newton_Scamander" title="Newton Scamander">Newt Scamander</a> concerning <a href="/wiki/Credence_Barebone" title="Credence Barebone">Credence</a>. Dumbledore's knowledge and ability to counter the effects of various spells of dark origin was exceptional, to the point where even <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>, a long-serving <a href="/wiki/Potions_Master" title="Potions Master">Potions Master</a>, eventual successor in the post of <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> instructor and former <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a> with a profound understanding for Dark Magic, repeatedly admitted that Dumbledore's expertise exceeded his own. One such example was when he and Professor McGonagall had to free <a href="/wiki/Ben_Copper" title="Ben Copper">Ben Copper</a> from the <a href="/wiki/Cursed_ice" title="Cursed ice">Cursed ice</a> that resulted from someone tampering with the fabled <a href="/wiki/Cursed_Vaults" title="Cursed Vaults">Cursed Vaults</a> and noted that Dumbledore would have been able to solve the problem far easier than themselves had he been present, and again four years later when he failed to break the curses put on a collection of dark artefacts belonging to <a href="/wiki/Patricia_Rakepick" title="Patricia Rakepick">Patricia Rakepick</a> and handed them over to Dumbledore; whom he judged to be the only wizard capable of properly handling them.<sup id="cite_ref-93" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-93">&#91;93&#93;</a></sup> Years later, he was quick to recognise the attack of <a href="/wiki/Mrs_Norris" title="Mrs Norris">Mrs Norris</a> as a case of <a href="/wiki/Petrification" title="Petrification">petrification</a> rather than <a href="/wiki/Transmogrifian_Torture" title="Transmogrifian Torture">murder</a> after a quick examination of the cat, and knew the only way to undo the attack was to use a Mandrake Restorative Draught after trying to undo it with a spell that should have normally reversed petrification, as well as to quickly identify that the real Moody was under the Imperius Curse and lifted it from him after discovering Crouch had been disguising himself as the seasoned Auror. He also knew that the Killing Curse cannot pass through solid objects, nor truly destroy a Phoenix, and therefore used the Fountain of Magical Brethren's statues and Fawkes to effectively shield himself from Voldemort's Killing Curses during their only known duel. He was also quickly capable of identifying the exceptionally powerful <a href="/wiki/Curse_on_Marvolo_Gaunt%27s_ring" title="Curse on Marvolo Gaunt&#39;s ring">curse on Marvolo Gaunt's ring</a> and effectively suppress its effects long enough to return from the village of <a href="/wiki/Little_Hangleton" title="Little Hangleton">Little Hangleton</a> in <a href="/wiki/Yorkshire" title="Yorkshire">Yorkshire</a> to Hogwarts, in spite of his injuries, for further treatment from <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>, with him having previously managed to successfully penetrate the many powerful dark defences set up by Voldemort around the Gaunt Cottage without being harmed and doing the same to all but the enchantment on the Potion of Despair when he invaded the Cave. Uniquely, Dumbledore was even capable of ripping out the piece of Voldemort's soul from the ring in order to destroy it without destroying the Resurrection Stone. His understanding of human nature also allowed him to understand and effectively take advantage of the functions of ancient magic that wards from any treat that few witches and wizards even knew about: taking advantage of the magical protection that lingered over Harry due to <a href="/wiki/Sacrificial_protection" title="Sacrificial protection">his mother's sacrifice</a>, Dumbledore was even able to effectively ensure that for the next sixteen years he would be safe from both Voldemort and his followers as long as he lived where a blood relative of his mother resided, highlighting his knowledge and proficiency in the subject. To further exemplify Dumbledore's exceptionally skill with the understanding and repelling of dark creatures, he was very skilful in dealing with <a href="/wiki/Werewolf" title="Werewolf">werewolves</a>, as he effortlessly dispatched five werewolves in <a href="/wiki/Hagrid%27s_Hut" title="Hagrid&#39;s Hut">Hagrid's Hut</a>, and simply arriving to <a href="/wiki/Jacob%27s_sibling" title="Jacob&#39;s sibling">Jacob's sibling</a>'s aid sent the notoriously powerful <a href="/wiki/Fenrir_Greyback" title="Fenrir Greyback">Fenrir Greyback</a> running from Hogwarts. Nevertheless of his resentment of dark creatures such as <a href="/wiki/Dementor" title="Dementor">Dementors</a> due to their untrustworthy nature, Dumbledore was still extremely knowledgeable and skilful in their nature and how to deal with them, as he thoroughly explained to Jacob's sibling on Boggarts and why they cannot be destroyed and can only be banished by <a href="/wiki/Boggart-Banishing_Spell" title="Boggart-Banishing Spell">Boggart-Banishing Spell</a>.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Dark_Arts" title="Dark Arts">Dark Arts</a></b>: While not an active practitioner of the Dark Arts, and seldom ever known to have used dark spells of any kind, Dumbledore was nevertheless exceptionally talented in the field of magic, with <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</a>, a long-time colleague of Dumbledore who knew him for most of her life, even insinuating at one point that Dumbledore was fully capable of utilising the same destructive dark powers that <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> wielded, but that he chose not to do so, being "too noble to use them". Dumbledore's extensive knowledge on the topic of Dark Magic allowed him to fully understand the scarcely known and extremely advanced magic used to create <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcruxes</a>, and he was able to quickly identify that Mrs Norris had been <a href="/wiki/Petrification" title="Petrification">petrified</a> upon a brief inspection, whereas others incorrectly believed the cat to be dead when they found her lifeless body. Even while limited by his good nature, Dumbledore still proved to be quite capable of casting powerful hexes and jinxes, as shown when he swiftly incapacitated <a href="/wiki/Cornelius_Fudge" title="Cornelius Fudge">Fudge</a>, <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Umbridge</a>, <a href="/wiki/John_Dawlish" title="John Dawlish">Dawlish</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Kingsley_Shacklebolt" title="Kingsley Shacklebolt">Kingsley</a> with a powerful hex that emitted a streak of silver light, and was described as having the force of a gunshot, and caused the floor to tremble when they tried to arrest him and later easily jinxed Dawlish once again when tailed by him. He seemed to have the capability to perform the <a href="/wiki/Killing_Curse" title="Killing Curse">Killing Curse</a>, as <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a> feared Dumbledore was going to kill him after he had been disarmed and brought to his knees by the headmaster when straying too close to the school during his time as a <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a>.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Occlumency" title="Occlumency">Occlumency</a> and <a href="/wiki/Legilimency" title="Legilimency">Legilimency</a></b>: Dumbledore was also impeccably adept in both <a href="/wiki/Occlumency" title="Occlumency">Occlumency</a> and <a href="/wiki/Legilimency" title="Legilimency">Legilimency</a>. Capable of using Legilimency without needing to use his wand or speak the incantation, many people, particularly Harry Potter, often noted that Dumbledore sometimes seemed to see right into their mind and correctly decipher what they were thinking.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_41-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> However, some of Lord Voldemort's followers, such as Barty Crouch Jnr, and his staff members, such as Horace Slughorn, proved to be excellent Occlumens capable of effectively hiding their thoughts from him. His skill in Legilimency was great enough that he was capable of extracting the true version of modified memories even if it was powerfully done, coaxing out from <a href="/wiki/Morfin_Gaunt" title="Morfin Gaunt">Morfin Gaunt</a> and later <a href="/wiki/Hokey" title="Hokey">Hokey</a> the true version of the memories that Voldemort used powerful magic to falsify, something which he said needed a "great deal of skilled Legilimency" to accomplish, although he did admit that he was not able to do so without difficulty. He also trained <a href="/wiki/Jacob_(Hogwarts_student)" title="Jacob (Hogwarts student)">Jacob</a>, a natural Legilimens, in the art. Dumbledore's skill in Occlumency was so great that he was among the very few (together with <a href="/wiki/Gellert_Grindelwald" title="Gellert Grindelwald">Gellert Grindelwald</a> and <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>) skilled enough in the art to conceal thoughts from Voldemort himself, who was the most powerful Legillimens of all time. At one point, he noted to Harry that he was confident that he was capable enough in Occlumency to train him to successfully to resist Voldemort but due to his fear of Voldemort's reaction to their closeness, he made the ill-fated decision of appointing Snape to train Harry. He could also lower his staunch mind defence enough to allow a lesser Legilimens to enter his mind but still limiting what they could see, enabling <a href="/wiki/Jacob%27s_sibling" title="Jacob&#39;s sibling">Jacob's sibling</a> to enter his mind but preventing them from seeing too much.</li></ul>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/46/PS_House_Cup_winner_updated.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140718153211" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="99" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="PS House Cup winner updated.gif" data-image-key="PS_House_Cup_winner_updated.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/46/PS_House_Cup_winner_updated.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140718153211" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/46/PS_House_Cup_winner_updated.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140718153211" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/46/PS_House_Cup_winner_updated.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140718153211" decoding="async" width="180" height="99" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="PS House Cup winner updated.gif" data-image-key="PS_House_Cup_winner_updated.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/46/PS_House_Cup_winner_updated.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140718153211" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:PS_House_Cup_winner_updated.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore non-verbally and wandlessly changing the colours of the house banners in the Great Hall</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>He clapped his hands. In an instant, the green hangings became scarlet and the silver became gold; the huge Slytherin serpent vanished and a towering Gryffindor lion took its place.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Dumbledore nonverablly and wandlessly changing the colours of Hogwarts house banners<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Wandless_magic" title="Wandless magic">Wandless</a> and <a href="/wiki/Nonverbal_spell" title="Nonverbal spell">non-verbal</a> magic</b>: Albus was highly proficient at both non-verbal and wandless magic, both of which were highly advanced and difficult to perform; his prowess was great enough for him to be fully capable of using both simultaneously.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_7-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> While some people, such as <a href="/wiki/Antonin_Dolohov" title="Antonin Dolohov">Antonin Dolohov</a>, as seen during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_41-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> seemed to produce lesser magic when using it non-verbally, Dumbledore was capable of extraordinary feats such as <a href="/wiki/Sleeping_bag_conjuring_spell" title="Sleeping bag conjuring spell">conjuring</a> hundreds of squishy purple sleeping bags to accommodate the students of Hogwarts, without saying a word.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_36-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> During the Ending Feast in 1992, he only had to clap his hands to transform the banners of the Great Hall from Slytherin to Gryffindor. In addition, during the Welcome Feast in 1993, he extinguished and lit a candle with a mere wave of his hand. While in <a href="/wiki/The_Cave" title="The Cave">The Cave</a>, Dumbledore easily foiled the defences set up by Lord Voldemort using only wandless and nonverbal magic. He later cast the Freezing Charm nonverbally to keep Harry unable to intervene in his death. He could cast the <a href="/wiki/Human-presence-revealing_Spell" title="Human-presence-revealing Spell">Human-presence-revealing Spell</a> wandlessly and nonverbally. He also duelled Voldemort and defeated the Death Eaters during the Battle of the Department of Mysteries without ever uttering any incantation.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_41-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> He was also able to dim the Great Hall's light sources and summon the names of the Champions of the <a href="/wiki/Triwizard_Tournament" title="Triwizard Tournament">Triwizard Tournament</a> to his hand. He even set Riddle's Wardrobe to fire without bothering to look. With sheer will, while having his Admonitors vanished by Theseus, Dumbledore kept the blood pact vial levitated without even having to look or wave his hand.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Spell_creation" title="Spell creation">Spell creation</a></b>: Dumbledore was known for his ability to create unique magical spells and devices and modify already existing spells. He was the inventor of the <a href="/wiki/Deluminator" title="Deluminator">Deluminator</a>, which was considered to be unique. Not only could it remove light sources from the Deluminator's immediate surroundings, as well as bestow them, after it had been bequeathed to Ron Weasley, he discovered that he could sometimes hear Harry and Hermione's voices through it, and that it also allowed him to Apparate to their location, a function that Dumbledore likely added before his death. He also developed a method to communicate using <a href="/wiki/Patronus_Charm" title="Patronus Charm">Patronus Charms</a>, which he taught to the members of the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a>.</li></ul>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">"<i>Dumbledore was on his feet again, pale as any of the surrounding Inferi, but taller than any too, the fire dancing in his eyes; his wand was raised like a torch and from its tip emanated the flames, like a vast lasso, encircling them all with warmth. The Inferi bumped into each other, attempting, blindly, to escape the fire in which they were enclosed...</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Dumbledore fighting the Inferi with a firestorm<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f2/DumbledoreHBPInferi.PNG/revision/latest?cb=20170113003654" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="140" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="DumbledoreHBPInferi.PNG" data-image-key="DumbledoreHBPInferi.PNG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f2/DumbledoreHBPInferi.PNG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170113003654" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f2/DumbledoreHBPInferi.PNG/revision/latest?cb=20170113003654" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f2/DumbledoreHBPInferi.PNG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170113003654" decoding="async" width="250" height="140" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="DumbledoreHBPInferi.PNG" data-image-key="DumbledoreHBPInferi.PNG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f2/DumbledoreHBPInferi.PNG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170113003654" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:DumbledoreHBPInferi.PNG" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore conjuring a <a href="/wiki/Firestorm" title="Firestorm">firestorm</a> to ward off the Inferi and protect Harry Potter</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li><b>Elemental magic mastery</b>: Dumbledore was extremely capable in using magic to manipulate the elements, especially fire, water and wind, although he seemed to prefer the former, for both combative and supplementary purposes, as it seems that when straying away from more conventional combative spellwork, Dumbledore would skilfully use the power of the elements to attack his adversary. In order to converse secretly with Newt Scamander, Dumbledore combined both water and wind to form a thick mist and easily dispersed it after he had finished. He displayed particularly incredible skill in controlling fire, as shown when he easily set ablaze Riddle's wardrobe <a href="/wiki/Flame-Freezing_Charm" title="Flame-Freezing Charm">without actually burning anything</a> in order to display his wizarding powers to him and was able to generate a ring of fire to hold off a throng of <a href="/wiki/Inferius" title="Inferius">Inferi</a> in the Horcrux Cave, which was potent enough to remain unquenchable by the vast ocean that surrounded them.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_30-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> He was also capable of conjuring the everlasting <a href="/wiki/Gubraithian_Fire" title="Gubraithian Fire">Gubraithian Fire</a>, an incredibly advanced piece of magic that extreme few could accomplish, greatly impressing <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a>. In his duel against Voldemort, he used a <a href="/wiki/Fire_rope" title="Fire rope">fiery rope</a> that managed to overshadow the silver shield Voldemort had conjured, forcing him to transfigure it in order to repel the attack, and <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore%27s_hydro-kinetic_spell" title="Albus Dumbledore&#39;s hydro-kinetic spell">easily manipulated</a> the considerable amount of water contained inside the <a href="/wiki/Fountain_of_Magical_Brethren" title="Fountain of Magical Brethren">Fountain of Magical Brethren</a> to rise up and cover Voldemort "like a cocoon of molten glass".<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_41-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b>Magical multilingualism</b>: Dumbledore had an uncanny expertise in mastering many foreign magical languages, as not only could he speak <a href="/wiki/Mermish" title="Mermish">Mermish</a><sup id="cite_ref-GOF_38-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Gobbledegook" title="Gobbledegook">Gobbledegook</a>, but he was even among the very few able to recognise and understand <a href="/wiki/Parseltongue" title="Parseltongue">Parseltongue</a>, the language of snakes, as while he and Harry were inside Bob Ogden's stored memory, he instantly recognised that Marvolo was speaking Parseltongue whereas Harry didn't even realise until Dumbledore pointed it out; he was able to quote verbatim a Parseltongue phrase uttered by Morfin Gaunt in a later stored memory, implying at least a level of ability to speak it.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_30-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>Dumbledore brandished his wand in one, long, fluid movement — the snake, which had been an instant from sinking its fangs into him, flew high into the air and vanished in a wisp of dark smoke.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Dumbledore performing the <a href="/wiki/Snake-Vanishing_Spell" title="Snake-Vanishing Spell">Snake-Vanishing Spell</a> during the <a href="/wiki/Duel_in_the_Ministry_Atrium" title="Duel in the Ministry Atrium">Duel in the Ministry Atrium</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Transfiguration" title="Transfiguration">Transfiguration</a></b>: Dumbledore was known to be highly accomplished and knowledgeable in the incredibly complex art of Transfiguration even before graduating, as his knowledge and proficiency on the subject was already sufficient for him to be allowed to submit some papers to the <a href="/wiki/Transfiguration_Today" title="Transfiguration Today">Transfiguration Today</a>, all of which, particularly his pages on <a href="/wiki/Trans-Species_Transformation" title="Trans-Species Transformation">Trans-Species Transformation</a>, were of a remarkably high standard, to the point that <a href="/wiki/Bathilda_Bagshot" title="Bathilda Bagshot">Bathilda Bagshot</a> was impressed enough to contact him and his N.E.W.T. Examinor <a href="/wiki/Griselda_Marchbanks" title="Griselda Marchbanks">Professor Marchbanks</a> was so impressed by his display during his Transfiguration N.E.W.T. Exam, that she would note that Dumbledore had performed transfiguration magic that "[she] had never seen before." As an adult, Transfiguration had became one of Dumbledore's most prominent areas of expertise, as ever since he was banned from teaching <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> by <a href="/wiki/Torquil_Travers" title="Torquil Travers">Torquil Travers</a>, Dumbledore chose Transfiguration as his next subject to teach and did so magnificently enough to quickly be promoted to the <a href="/wiki/Head_of_Transfiguration" title="Head of Transfiguration">Head of Transfiguration</a> department of the school, holding the position up for many years to come until his ascending to the position of Headmaster of the School. He was seemingly deemed the greatest teacher of the field in Hogwarts's history, as Harry Potter stated Dumbledore had been the best while only aware of Dumbledore's career as Professor of Transfiguration, and having also trained the especially talented Minerva McGonagall into becoming an excellent master of the field and his successor later on. In addition, Dumbledore had been a famously regular and successful columnist to the Transfiguration Today to the point his contribution was deemed good enough to be published among the news of <a href="/wiki/Daily_Prophet" title="Daily Prophet">Daily Prophet</a>. He was quite knowledgeable in the field of Animagus Transformation, having successfully guided Minerva McGonagall into becoming one at the age of seventeen, despite the notorious difficulty and known dangers of that ability. Dumbledore was particularly proficient in <a href="/wiki/Conjuration" title="Conjuration">Conjuration</a> and also accomplished in <a href="/wiki/Vanishment" title="Vanishment">Vanishment</a>, as he could effortlessly and non-verbally conjure a stretcher to transport the unconscious Harry, several hats for the charmed skeletons he enchanted for Hallowe'en Feast Entertainment that he easily vanished upon finishing, hundreds of squishy purple bags to accommodate the Gryffindor students in the <a href="/wiki/Great_Hall" title="Great Hall">Great Hall</a> when <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black%27s_break-in_of_Hogwarts_Castle_(1993)" title="Sirius Black&#39;s break-in of Hogwarts Castle (1993)">Sirius Black broke into the Castle</a>, two armchairs for <a href="/wiki/Arabella_Figg" title="Arabella Figg">Mrs Figg</a> and himself to sit on during <a href="/wiki/Disciplinary_hearing_of_Harry_Potter" title="Disciplinary hearing of Harry Potter">Harry's disciplinary hearing</a>, at one instance quickly vanishing the container of the <a href="/wiki/Goblet_of_Fire" title="Goblet of Fire">Goblet of Fire</a>, a tea tray when the trio came to visit Hagrid, several glasses and a bottle containing Rosmerta's mead, which he later on easily vanished, a bottle of gin and several glasses to accommodate Cole, and a goblet to drink the <a href="/wiki/Emerald_Potion" title="Emerald Potion">Emerald Potion</a>. His mastery of Transfiguration allowed him to make very good use of it in combat, as shown when Dumbledore seamlessly cast the <a href="/wiki/Piertotum_Locomotor" title="Piertotum Locomotor">Piertotum Locomotor</a> spell to animate the statues of the Fountain of Magical Brethren to subdue Bellatrix, protect Harry and repel Voldemort's curses and conjured a large rope of fire that Voldemort had to transfigure into a snake to repel the attack, which Dumbledore easily vanished, during <a href="/wiki/Duel_in_the_Ministry_Atrium" title="Duel in the Ministry Atrium">his duel with the Dark Lord</a>. He also effortlessly transformed the banners of the Great Hall from representing <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin</a> to <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a> with a mere clap of his hands. Dumbledore also had an uncanny knack for immediately figuring out and countering Transfiguration spells done by others, as shown by how he quickly deduced <a href="/wiki/Horace_Slughorn" title="Horace Slughorn">Horace Slughorn</a> had turned himself into a chair and easily undid it with a simple jab of his wand and later on casually figured out the beetle watching over him and Jacob's Sibling as being <a href="/wiki/Rita_Skeeter" title="Rita Skeeter">Rita Skeeter</a> using her Animagus power and called her out on it to make her revert back to her true form. He presumably also undid the transfiguration spell that McGonagall used on the <a href="/wiki/Chessboard_Chamber" title="Chessboard Chamber">Chessboard Chamber</a> to quickly pass through them and get to Harry on time. In order to sing the school song, Dumbledore conjured and animated a ribbon that he twisted to form the lyrics into the air.</li></ul>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">"<i>He raised his wand into the air and pointed it in the direction of Hagrid’s cabin. Harry saw something silvery dart out of it and streak away through the trees like a ghostly bird.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Dumbledore conjuring his Phoenix Patronus<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5a/Dumbledores_phoenix_patronus.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170108235142" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="160" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dumbledores phoenix patronus.jpg" data-image-key="Dumbledores_phoenix_patronus.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5a/Dumbledores_phoenix_patronus.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170108235142" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5a/Dumbledores_phoenix_patronus.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170108235142" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5a/Dumbledores_phoenix_patronus.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170108235142" decoding="async" width="180" height="160" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dumbledores phoenix patronus.jpg" data-image-key="Dumbledores_phoenix_patronus.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5a/Dumbledores_phoenix_patronus.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170108235142" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dumbledores_phoenix_patronus.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Albus' Patronus in the shape of the Phoenix</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Charm" title="Charm">Charms</a></b>: Albus was known to be extremely accomplished in <a href="/wiki/Charm" title="Charm">Charms</a> even as a young man as articles that he wrote about the branch of magic were published in the scholarly journal <i><a href="/wiki/Challenges_in_Charming" title="Challenges in Charming">Challenges in Charming</a></i> and his N.E.W.T examiners Professor Marchbanks was so impressed by his display during his Charms N.E.W.T Exam that he said that Dumbledore "did things with a wand that [she] had never seen before". He also earned the <a href="/wiki/Barnabus_Finkley_Prize_for_Exceptional_Spell-Casting" title="Barnabus Finkley Prize for Exceptional Spell-Casting">Barnabus Finkley Prize for Exceptional Spell-Casting</a> and could already cast such a strong <a href="/wiki/Disillusionment_Charm" title="Disillusionment Charm">Disillusionment Charm</a> that he was effectively able to render himself invisible without needing an Invisibility Cloak, which was a tremendous feat.<sup id="cite_ref-TOBTB_94-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TOBTB-94">&#91;94&#93;</a></sup> As an adult, Dumbledore's mastery of Charms was sufficient to earn him the illustrious title of <a href="/wiki/Grand_Sorcerer" title="Grand Sorcerer">Grand Sorcerer</a>. His proficiency in the incredibly complex Patronus Charm was so advanced that he was able to devise new uses for this charm, allowing it to be used as a form of communication (with the caster speaking with their own voice through the Patronus).<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_38-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> Dumbledore was also capable of effectively performing the extremely complex <a href="/wiki/Fidelius_Charm" title="Fidelius Charm">Fidelius Charm</a>, acting as the Secret Keeper to <a href="/wiki/12_Grimmauld_Place" title="12 Grimmauld Place">12 Grimmauld Place</a> after it was made the Headquarters of the Order of Phoenix. He was even capable of performing the extremely powerful and ancient <a href="/wiki/Bond_of_blood_charm" title="Bond of blood charm">bond of blood charm</a> to further ensure Harry's protection from Voldemort for 17 years while he lived with his aunt, <a href="/wiki/Petunia_Dursley" title="Petunia Dursley">Petunia Dursley</a>. He could easily perform the <a href="/wiki/Portus" title="Portus">Portus</a> Charm successfully to create Portkeys, using it to turn a black kettle in his office to a Portkey that sent Harry and the Weasley children to Grimmauld Place and later the head of the golden wizard statue into a Portkey that took Harry back to Hogwarts. Even without the Deluminator, Dumbledore could easily put out light sources with an unknown charm, which he could do twice while in his office and also while announcing the Triwizard Champions with a mere gesture, and seemed to have been the one who enchanted the device with such ability. He also was responsible for the additional charm cast on the Deluminator that allowed it to guide Ron back to Harry and Hermione after he left. He could cast a variety of powerful and unique enchantments, shown when he enchanted the <a href="/wiki/Mirror_of_Erised" title="Mirror of Erised">Mirror of Erised</a> to only give the <a href="/wiki/Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Philosopher&#39;s Stone">Philosopher's Stone</a> to a person who wished to find it but not to use it, which held firm even against Quirell when he had both the knowledge of Voldemort and his own experience, which had allowed him to easily bypass the other enchantments put in place to protect the artefact, manifested a hand to Newt's location capable of taking Newt to Dumbledore's location and conjured a thick mist capable of hiding him and Newt from magical detection in order to prevent the Ministry from locating them. Dumbledore's mastery and knowledge of all forms of defensive charms was unparalleled, as while he was Headmaster of Hogwarts, Dumbledore was in charge of controlling the protective measures of the castle and the standard of his magic was so strong that not even Voldemort could breach them, with Hogwarts thus being considered the safest it had ever been with Dumbledore in charge. He could easily lift and recast them, evidenced when he temporarily lifted the <a href="/wiki/Anti-Apparition_Charm" title="Anti-Apparition Charm">Anti-Apparition Charm</a> to allow the students to learn how to <a href="/wiki/Apparition" title="Apparition">Apparate</a>. He was also capable of locking doors to prevent them from being opened by seemingly any means apart from Dumbledore himself undoing the enchantment, as he did to further made it look like Harry and Hermione had not done anything to help Sirius escape and Hermione feared the idea of Dumbledore locking the doors of the Hospital Wing before they could get there after succeeding, with Snape and Fudge only able to access the door, despite Snape's rage and Fudge's exasperation, when Dumbledore calmly let them in, and later enchanting the entrance door to Hogwarts to be impenetrable to the <a href="/wiki/Unlocking_Charm" title="Unlocking Charm">Unlocking Charm</a> and making the walls reject any attempt of anyone to climb up. He also was able to cast a powerful <a href="/wiki/Age_Line" title="Age Line">Age Line</a> around the <a href="/wiki/Goblet_of_Fire" title="Goblet of Fire">Goblet of Fire</a> to ensure no one under the age of 17 could cross, with it being such a flawless enchantment that in addition to being humorously enchanted to both repel Ageing Potions and cause those who had used them to cross the line to grow beards, McGonagall adamantly defended that the Age Line Dumbledore had put had no flaws in it when the under-aged Harry Potter became Hogwarts's second champion, with Barty Crouch, while disguised as Moody, therefore being forced to risk exposure by putting Harry's name into the Goblet of Fire personally. He also understood the nature of the Goblet of Fire perfectly, acknowledging that there was no way for them to prevent Harry from competing after he had been chosen, and was able to easily unlock the chest containing the magical object by tapping it three times. Even while not yet Headmaster, Dumbledore was still apparently in charge of the school's protective spells, which proved sufficient to keep out <a href="/wiki/Gellert_Grindelwald" title="Gellert Grindelwald">Gellert Grindelwald</a>, and could undo the protection around the school multiple times at whim - allowing <a href="/wiki/Torquil_Travers" title="Torquil Travers">Torquil Travers</a> and <a href="/wiki/Theseus_Scamander" title="Theseus Scamander">Theseus Scamander</a> to arrive to question him, allowing <a href="/wiki/Newton_Scamander" title="Newton Scamander">Newton Scamander</a>, <a href="/wiki/Porpentina_Goldstein" title="Porpentina Goldstein">Tina Goldstein</a>, and their allies to arrive for advice after <a href="/wiki/Gellert_Grindelwald" title="Gellert Grindelwald">Grindelwald</a>'s Paris rally, and years later allowing <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> to breach the perimeter on a broomstick. Indeed, Dumbledore was even able to make the usually <a href="/wiki/Unplottability" title="Unplottability">Unplottable</a> <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Castle" title="Hogwarts Castle">Hogwarts Castle</a> temporarily Plottable, so as to allow the No-Maj <a href="/wiki/Jacob_Kowalski" title="Jacob Kowalski">Jacob Kowalski</a> to join Newt in visiting the castle for advice. Dumbledore often extracted his memories and put them inside his Pensieve and was able to project the image of his memory regarding the Prophecy of the Chosen One from it for Harry to see.
