In order to entrance the sharp Mrs Cole, Dumbledore non-verbally cast the very complex <a href="/wiki/Confundus_Charm" title="Confundus Charm">Confundus Charm</a> with ease to successfully confound her into believing the blank paper was sufficient to allow a talk between them, a noteworthy feat as even the very skilled and powerful <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a> had trouble using the advanced charm. He also was capable of inserting the Resurrection Stone into the Snitch he gave Harry and enchanting it to only reveal itself when Harry was about to make the ultimate sacrifice, preventing any attempt from Harry to open it. His mastery of the <a href="/wiki/Human-presence-revealing_Spell" title="Human-presence-revealing Spell">Human-presence-revealing Spell</a> was very potent, having been the only wizard seen thus far capable of penetrating the powerful magic of the <a href="/wiki/Cloak_of_Invisibility" title="Cloak of Invisibility">Cloak of Invisibility</a>, henceforth successfully sensing the presence of Harry Potter and Ron Weasley while they had the Cloak on. He was proficient enough in the <a href="/wiki/Slowing_Charm" title="Slowing Charm">Slowing Charm</a> to perform it quickly and without his wand to slow down Harry Potter's swift descent after he was knocked off his broom by the Dementors effectively enough to make him land without any injuries, not even breaking his glass, which Harry's friends commented on, and was able to levitate and carry the stretcher holding Harry's unconscious body all the way back to school without strain for further treatment from Madam Pomfrey. He also effortlessly summoned the names of the Champions of the Triwizard Tournament with a simple gesture, showing he could easily cast simple charms without needing his wand but preferred to do so with it. This was also shown years before, where Dumbledore levitated the vial containing the blood pact between him and Gellert without even needing to gesture, simply through sheer will. In addition, Dumbledore swiftly summoned the sofa in the house of the Dursleys in order to force them to sit on it, enchanted the glasses he filled with Rosmerta's mead to stay suspended in mid-air and repeatedly knock over the Dursleys, and transported the belongings of Harry Potter to the Burrow with ease. In the film, Dumbledore unleashed such a powerful <a href="/wiki/Disarming_Charm" title="Disarming Charm">Disarming Charm</a> to blast down the door to Crouch's office while he was disguised as Moody and send the fake Moody flying a considerable distance away, the impact of him hitting the nearby chair being enough to make the chair stumble backwards and stun him long enough for Dumbledore to breach the distance between them. He simultaneously disarmed and grounded Severus Snape when meeting with him with a single Disarming Charm. He was also able to cast an unknown charm that effortlessly pulled back a fleeing Death Eater during the Battle of the Department of Mysteries. Dumbledore could cast a seemingly modified version of the <a href="/wiki/Silencing_Charm" title="Silencing Charm">Silencing Charm</a> that instead of silencing a target, made the surrounding environment's natural events happen without causing any sound and seemingly rendered any sound coming from the area unable to be heard by all but the ones standing in said place, as he did to ensure he and Severus Snape were not disturbed when they conversed about Snape relying the Prophecy to Voldemort. In addition to making normal use of the <a href="/wiki/Wand-Lighting_Charm" title="Wand-Lighting Charm">Wand-Lighting Charm</a> for light in the dark areas of the Horcrux Cave and Forbidden Forest, Dumbledore was also able to throw the light created by the charm at the centre of the ocean to light the whole cave up. Dumbledore was also very accomplished with the <i><a href="/wiki/Piertotum_Locomotor" title="Piertotum Locomotor">Piertotum Locomotor</a></i> Charm, as he was able to do so seamlessly and in an instant with ease to animate and manipulate the statues of the Fountain of Magical Brethren during his duel with Voldemort. Dumbledore was also able to skilfully perform the <a href="/wiki/Reviving_Spell" title="Reviving Spell">Reviving Spell</a>, as he instantly un-stunned Viktor Krum after Barty Crouch Jnr knocked him out and even managed to partially revive the latter from an extremely powerful Stunning Spell he had unleashed while taking care to not revive him enough to allow Crouch any chance to resist. He warmed up Harry and dried his clothes upon noticing the latter was shivering with a single spell. When playing the <a href="/wiki/Hoggy_Warty_Hogwarts" title="Hoggy Warty Hogwarts">Hoggy Warty Hogwarts</a> song, Dumbledore was capable of simultaneously making the entire school rumble.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Potion" title="Potion">Potions</a></b>: Dumbledore was also considerably knowledgeable and accomplished in Potions, even while still young, as while still a student, he published good papers in <i><a href="/wiki/The_Practical_Potioneer" title="The Practical Potioneer">The Practical Potioneer</a></i>, an academic journal regarding Potions, according to <a href="/wiki/Elphias_Doge" title="Elphias Doge">Elphias Doge</a>. He showed thorough knowledge and understanding of the properties of Love Potion, as he understood that Love Potion merely brought upon the sensation of obsessive love rather than true love, and also the Mandrake Restorative Draught's potent healing properties, which allowed him to have Sprout and Snape begin producing it as the only way to reverse the Petrification caused by the Basilisik inside the Chamber of Secrets. He instantly recognised the drink inside Moody's hip-flask that Crouch used to drink unsuspected as the Polyjuice Potion and knew about <a href="/wiki/Veritaserum" title="Veritaserum">Veritaserum</a>'s inability to overcome the defences of expert Occlumens, thus first stunning Barty Crouch Jnr before having him exposed to the Truth Potion in order to ensure he could not resist it, with Dumbledore notably requesting the strongest batch of Veritaserum in order to further maximise Crouch's inability to overcome it. Dumbledore expressed confidence he could brew the Truth Potion for himself if he desired to use it against Horace Slughorn to make him confess the real memory but Horace's Occlumency and ability to make an antidote for it made it null. He also was able to easily recognise the <a href="/wiki/Ageing_Potion" title="Ageing Potion">Ageing Potion</a> as being the primary method under-aged students would use to submit their names to the <a href="/wiki/Goblet_of_Fire" title="Goblet of Fire">Goblet of Fire</a> by physically ageing themselves to overcome his <a href="/wiki/Age_Line" title="Age Line">Age Line</a> and therefore seamlessly created counters to it to seemingly increase the potion's effects to the point of ageing youngsters enough to make their hair white and give them magnificent beards. In addition, it was quite likely that Dumbledore was the one who instructed Minerva McGonagall on how to brew the complex <a href="/wiki/Animagus_potion" title="Animagus potion">Animagus potion</a> that was needed to become an Animagi and may have even been the one who brewed it for her. He also quickly measured the quality of the <a href="/wiki/Wit-Sharpening_Potion" title="Wit-Sharpening Potion">Wit-Sharpening Potion</a> Merula presented before him and Snape as being the best one he had ever seen and should <a href="/wiki/Jacob%27s_sibling" title="Jacob&#39;s sibling">Jacob's sibling</a> disguise himself as Potion Master Snape to expose Merula's lies as it was actually Penny Haywood who made the potion, Dumbledore would calmly level with them regarding the Potions curriculum and could detect that by the time they had exposed Merula's lies, the Potion had began to wear off and thus allow them to leave before they could be caught for it. It was likely that when he went to the <a href="/wiki/Underground_Chambers" title="Underground Chambers">Underground Chambers</a>, he had no trouble figuring out which one was the <a href="/wiki/Fire_Protection_Potion" title="Fire Protection Potion">Fire Protection Potion</a> needed to pass through the <a href="/wiki/Black_flames" title="Black flames">Black flames</a> Snape had conjured up unharmed and save Harry.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Alchemy" title="Alchemy">Alchemy</a></b>: Apparently having always been highly gifted in the ancient magical science art of Alchemy since his youth, as a student, Dumbledore was already capable enough to earn the interest of <a href="/wiki/Nicolas_Flamel" title="Nicolas Flamel">Nicolas Flamel</a>, who was considered to be the greatest Alchemist in history, being henceforth famous for his correspondence with the famous Alchemist while still a student, and having also won the <a href="/wiki/Gold_Medal_for_Ground-Breaking_Contribution_to_the_International_Alchemical_Conference" title="Gold Medal for Ground-Breaking Contribution to the International Alchemical Conference">Gold Medal for Ground-Breaking Contribution to the International Alchemical Conference</a> during his participation of the event in Cairo. By the time he was an adult, Alchemy was one of Dumbledore's most famous areas of expertise and he contributed considerably to the advancement of the subject alongside his old friend Flamel.</li>
<li><b>Magical chemistry</b>: Dumbledore also had a great deal of knowledge on magical substances, particularly the substance of <a href="/wiki/Dragon%27s_blood" class="mw-redirect" title="Dragon&#39;s blood">Dragon's blood</a>, as he was considered the foremost expert of it and managed to discover twelve ways to use it practically, among them as a spot remover, as an oven cleaner, and for a potion ingredient. His knowledge and experience in the study of Dragon Blood also allowed him to easily distinguish it from <a href="/wiki/Human" title="Human">human</a> <a href="/wiki/Blood" title="Blood">blood</a> by tasting a small amount of it.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Magical_Law" title="Magical Law">Magical Law</a> expertise</b>: Dumbledore displayed outstanding knowledge of the laws of the wizarding world, owning several books in his office concerning it. His expertise in the law allowed him to successfully clear <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> of all charges during his trial for underaged magic when he used a Patronus to defend himself. He also managed to give a convincing enough defence of <a href="/wiki/Morfin_Gaunt" title="Morfin Gaunt">Morfin Gaunt</a>'s innocence in the murder of <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle_Senior" title="Tom Riddle Senior">Tom Riddle Senior</a> and the rest of the <a href="/wiki/Riddle_family" title="Riddle family">Riddle family</a> after acquiring the memory that proved it that he would have successfully convinced the Ministry into letting out Morfin had Morfin not died first in Azkaban. He also displayed his knowledge when taking Harry with him to persuade Slughorn in which he showed full confidence his permission would be enough to allow Harry to use underage magic should there be an attack and lectured Harry on how they could not just apparate to his old friend's house due to the laws banning it.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Care_of_Magical_Creatures" title="Care of Magical Creatures">Care of Magical Creatures</a></b>: Dumbledore's knowledge and understanding of many magical creatures were exceptional, even being sufficient to be comparable to outstanding masters of the subject of the level of <a href="/wiki/Newton_Scamander" title="Newton Scamander">Newton Scamander</a> and <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Rubeus Hagrid</a>. This was shown when he was aware of the old <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore_family" title="Dumbledore family">Dumbledore family</a> legend of a <a href="/wiki/Phoenix" title="Phoenix">Phoenix</a> coming to any one of them in desperate need being true, and quickly understood how Newt's pet <a href="/wiki/Niffler" title="Niffler">Niffler</a> had stolen the <a href="/wiki/Blood_pact" title="Blood pact">Blood pact</a> vial from <a href="/wiki/Gellert_Grindelwald" title="Gellert Grindelwald">Grindelwald</a> as well as being the only one alongside Hagrid aware of how to get past Fluffy something that not even <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a> or <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>, both highly intelligent and knowledgeable wizards, knew about, with <a href="/wiki/Quirinus_Quirrell" title="Quirinus Quirrell">Quirinus Quirrell</a>, who had knowledge and experience in handling dangerous magical creatures, having to get it from the drunk Hagrid under Voldemort's orders, with Dumbledore seemingly easily subduing the dog with either music or other means to get to Harry on time. Dumbledore was also extremely adept at handling all sorts of magical creatures, such as <a href="/wiki/Phoenix" title="Phoenix">Pheonixes</a>, <a href="/wiki/Thestral" title="Thestral">Thestrals</a>, <a href="/wiki/Merpeople" title="Merpeople">Merpeople</a>, <a href="/wiki/Centaur" title="Centaur">Centaurs</a>, and possibly considering his ability to speak their language, <a href="/wiki/Goblin" title="Goblin">Goblins</a>, as shown by how his pet Phoenix <a href="/wiki/Fawkes" title="Fawkes">Fawkes</a> was completely loyal to the point it only remained in the school due to him and after singing a lament upon Dumbledore's death, flew away and never returned and using it in combat at one point to thwart Voldemort's killing curse by having him take the attack and Dumbledore employed Thestrals at times effectively as a mode of transport when not Apparating, successfully communicated with the Merpeople of the Black Lake to learn the progress of the Second Task of the Triwizard Tournament and was one of the few wizards that <a href="/wiki/Forbidden_Forest_Centaur_colony" title="Forbidden Forest Centaur colony">Hogwarts's Centaurs</a> respected and trusted, enough that Dumbledore was able to convince them to return Umbridge safely without any harm done to him; the Centaurs and the Merpeople later payed their respects during Dumbledore's funeral. Dumbledore also was a famous contributor to the defence of <a href="/wiki/Giant" title="Giant">Giants</a> from wizarding violence, with his reputation being enough to make <a href="/wiki/Karkus" title="Karkus">Karkus</a> consider aiding the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> and his ability to give Hagrid the gifts and instruction necessary to steadily convince the giant colony, up until <a href="/wiki/Golgomath" title="Golgomath">Golgomath</a> killed Karkus, with his advice still managing to convince the surviving giants who didn't join Golgomath to not join the Death Eaters, show he was also highly competent in handling Giants. He also was one of the few wizards and witches who interacted with <a href="/wiki/House-elf" title="House-elf">house-elves</a> with kindness and compassion, giving <a href="/wiki/Dobby" title="Dobby">Dobby</a> and <a href="/wiki/Winky" title="Winky">Winky</a> jobs at Hogwarts and encouraging Harry to treat <a href="/wiki/Kreacher" title="Kreacher">Kreacher</a> more kindly. When Hagrid and Kettleburn unleashed a large amount of creatures upon Hogwarts, Dumbledore easily dealt with the many <a href="/wiki/Bowtruckle" title="Bowtruckle">Bowtruckles</a> in the faculty seats of the Great Hall, showing overall, he was exceptionally skilled with handling almost all kinds of magical creatures.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/History_of_Magic" title="History of Magic">History of Magic</a></b>: Dumbledore had excellent knowledge of magical history and lore, having been well-known for his correspondence with the famous historian <a href="/wiki/Bathilda_Bagshot" title="Bathilda Bagshot">Bathilda Bagshot</a> while still young, with particular specialisation in the portions of it that pertained to powerful magical artefacts, such as the <a href="/wiki/Deathly_Hallows" title="Deathly Hallows">Deathly Hallows</a>, from his time studying them with <a href="/wiki/Gellert_Grindelwald" title="Gellert Grindelwald">Gellert Grindelwald</a> due to their shared obsession of the Hallows. As such, Dumbledore was able to identify <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_I" title="James Potter I">James Potter</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Invisibility_cloak" title="Invisibility cloak">Invisibility cloak</a> as the legendary <a href="/wiki/Cloak_of_Invisibility" title="Cloak of Invisibility">Cloak of Invisibility</a> of the Hallows and could see that the Gaunt Ring was the Resurrection Stone. In addition, Dumbledore was able to easily correctly recite the contents of the historical divination poetic book <i><a href="/wiki/The_Predictions_of_Tycho_Dodonus" title="The Predictions of Tycho Dodonus">The Predictions of Tycho Dodonus</a></i>, when questioned by <a href="/wiki/Torquil_Travers" title="Torquil Travers">Torquil Travers</a>. He also had thorough knowledge of the history of the <a href="/wiki/Triwizard_Tournament" title="Triwizard Tournament">Triwizard Tournament</a>, henceforth effectively explaining the reason why it was initially decided the Tournament would no longer be held. Having been one of the few to ever acquire the first-edition copy of <i><a href="/wiki/The_Tales_of_Beedle_the_Bard" title="The Tales of Beedle the Bard">The Tales of Beedle the Bard </a></i> and also having translated and red it's runic contents, Dumbledore was fully aware of the real stories out of the many changed tales in the world-wide famous Wizarding Storybook and the historical background behind it, therefore publishing notes regarding said topic.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Astronomy_(class)" title="Astronomy (class)">Astronomy</a></b>: Dumbledore appeared to be quite knowledgeable and adept in Astronomy, as he owned a <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore%27s_pocket_watch" title="Albus Dumbledore&#39;s pocket watch">special pocket watch</a> that contained moving planets around the edge of seemingly unique astronomy composition, with which he could apparently translate the meaning off to know the current time.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Divination" title="Divination">Divination</a></b>: Although not having taken the subject and admitting to disliking it, Dumbledore displayed decent knowledge of Divination, as he was shown to be fully familiar with <i><a href="/wiki/The_Predictions_of_Tycho_Dodonus" title="The Predictions of Tycho Dodonus">The Predictions of Tycho Dodonus</a></i>, a Divination book, correctly answering all of Travers's questions regarding the book. His knowledge of the subject also allowed him to effortlessly identify the difference between real and false Seers as well as quickly recognise the usage of the gift, as he was not fooled by Sybill's attempts to impress him as it didn't truly contain any trace of the gift, whereas apart from Hermione Granger, Ron Weasley and Harry Potter, most of the students believed her prophecies were real, but immediately saw her as a genuine Seer once Sybil delivered the Chosen One Prophecy. He was also capable of somehow accurately deciphering the contents of Prophecies, having successfully figured out that the <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney%27s_first_prophecy" title="Sybill Trelawney&#39;s first prophecy">Chosen One prophecy</a> about one with the power to defeat <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a> was about <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, not <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a>, despite both being born almost on the same day, and also that the unique Chosen One power Harry possessed was love. He apparently had a level of skill in the practical aspect of the subject, owning at least a single silver device containing the ability to tell him of events happening elsewhere, which he used to recognise Arthur Weasley had truly been attacked by Nagini and his wounds were severe.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Muggle_Studies" title="Muggle Studies">Muggle Studies</a></b>: Dumbledore's knowledge regarding Muggles and ability to interact with them was considerable, with him often employing many Muggle sweets as passwords for the Headmaster's office and at one point managing to effectively interact with the Muggles controlling <a href="/wiki/Wool%27s_Orphanage" title="Wool&#39;s Orphanage">Wool's Orphanage</a> to successfully go to the young <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Tom Riddle</a>, quickly convincing one of the employers into calling the matron <a href="/wiki/Cole" title="Cole">Mrs Cole</a>, who he calmly levelled with and convinced to trust him, needing little aid of his magic against the admittedly sharp woman. He was also well-known for his great contribution to the support of Muggles of wizardkind.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Healing_magic" title="Healing magic">Healing magic</a></b>: Dumbledore was accomplished in healing magic as he managed to temporarily control the immensely powerful curse on <a href="/wiki/Marvolo_Gaunt%27s_ring" class="mw-redirect" title="Marvolo Gaunt&#39;s ring">Marvolo Gaunt's ring</a> long enough to destroy it and return to Hogwarts to receive further treatment from <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>, and easily healed his wound with a <a href="/wiki/Healing_spell" title="Healing spell">healing spell</a> after using his blood to open the passageway in <a href="/wiki/The_Cave" title="The Cave">The Cave</a> when searching for <a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin%27s_Locket" class="mw-redirect" title="Salazar Slytherin&#39;s Locket">Salazar Slytherin's Locket</a>. He also appeared to be accomplished in treating magical creatures, as <a href="/wiki/Cecil_Lee" title="Cecil Lee">Cecil Lee</a> took <a href="/wiki/Chiara_Lobosca" title="Chiara Lobosca">Chiara Lobosca</a> in her wolf form to his office for treatment after she was wounded by Greyback and he appeared to have succeeded in treating her.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Apparition" title="Apparition">Apparition</a></b>: Dumbledore was extremely skilled in Apparition, as he was the only known wizard apart from Lord Voldemort capable of Apparating silently.<sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95">&#91;95&#93;</a></sup> He could transport himself from one place to another with pin-point precision, even when locked in combat, as shown by how he dodged some of Voldemort's spells during <a href="/wiki/Duel_in_the_Ministry_Atrium" title="Duel in the Ministry Atrium">their duel</a> by teleporting away before quickly counter-attacking.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Flight" title="Flight">Flying</a></b>: Dumbledore was an excellent broomstick flyer, as, despite being considerably weakened from having drunk the <a href="/wiki/Emerald_Potion" title="Emerald Potion">Emerald Potion</a>, he was able to fly from <a href="/wiki/Hogsmeade" title="Hogsmeade">Hogsmeade</a> to the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Castle" title="Hogwarts Castle">Hogwarts</a> <a href="/wiki/Astronomy_Tower" title="Astronomy Tower">Astronomy Tower</a> at great speed and was even able to cast a spell while en route to undo the protections around the Castle. He also managed to fly back from "mid-way" to the British Ministry of Magic to Hogwarts fast enough to still have the time needed to save Harry from Quirell. In addition, he apparently effortlessly managed to capture the right key out of the <a href="/wiki/Winged_Keys" title="Winged Keys">Winged Keys</a> to unlock the door to McGonagall's real Wizard Chess obstacle.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Love" title="Love">Love</a></b>: Dumbledore was extremely learned and knowledgeable in the nature of love along with the magic associated with it, and showed a remarkably powerful capability to feel true love. This was shown when Dumbledore advised <a href="/wiki/Newton_Scamander" title="Newton Scamander">Newt Scamander</a> on how to potentially heal the <a href="/wiki/Obscurial" title="Obscurial">Obscurial</a> <a href="/wiki/Credence_Barebone" title="Credence Barebone">Credence</a> of the latter's <a href="/wiki/Obscurus" title="Obscurus">Obscurus</a> - by replacing the feelings that made Credence an Obscurial with a sense of love and belonging. Later, he also advised <a href="/wiki/Leta_Lestrange" title="Leta Lestrange">Leta Lestrange</a> to not torture herself over her brother's death, since he himself had not loved his own late sister <a href="/wiki/Ariana_Dumbledore" title="Ariana Dumbledore">Ariana</a> enough. Furthermore, Dumbledore was able to understand the true magical power behind a <a href="/wiki/Sacrificial_protection" title="Sacrificial protection">loving sacrifice</a>, telling <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> about the magical protection the latter had inherited when his mother sacrificed herself to protect him from Voldemort, and was also able to inform Harry that his own ability to love allowed him to close the connection between him and Voldemort and repel Voldemort's attempted possession of Harry by focusing on grief when he was unable to perform <a href="/wiki/Occlumency" title="Occlumency">Occlumency</a>. Due to this, he was also the only person who understood that Voldemort's act in using Harry's blood to help in restoring him to full power actually strengthened the magical protection within Harry to the point that Voldemort could not kill Harry while he himself was still alive.<sup id="cite_ref-DH35_96-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH35-96">&#91;96&#93;</a></sup> Dumbledore's understanding of love and sacrificial protection also made him cast the <a href="/wiki/Bond_of_blood_charm" title="Bond of blood charm">bond of blood charm</a> upon Harry to ensure he had further protection from Voldemort for 17 years alongside his mother's sacrifice while living with his aunt, <a href="/wiki/Petunia_Dursley" title="Petunia Dursley">Petunia Dursley</a>. Dumbledore was also able to distinguish between pure, unconditional love which most people felt for each other, and the obsession which was caused by Love Potions. While Dumbledore became "quite asexual" in his older years, after the disaster following his romantic interest in teenage friend <a href="/wiki/Gellert_Grindelwald" title="Gellert Grindelwald">Gellert Grindelwald</a>, he evidently cared greatly about his family, close friends, students, allies and the wizarding community. His ability to love gave him the strength to overcome his selfishness and obsession for power, and stand up to Grindelwald in order to protect his brother Aberforth when Grindelwald attacked him. His ability to love also allowed Dumbledore to eventually overcome his fear of learning who really killed Ariana and duel Grindelwald again at the heights of the latter's power and defeat him when Grindelwald was threatening to take over both wizarding and Muggle worlds. Dumbledore's ability to love was his most redeeming quality, as it allowed him to become a far better person by protecting many people he cared about, especially when Voldemort rose to power. His ability to love also made him concerned about Harry Potter's safety, to the point that he kept <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney%27s_first_prophecy" title="Sybill Trelawney&#39;s first prophecy">the Prophecy</a> a secret from him earlier on, and distanced himself from Harry during the latter's fifth year, hoping it would reduce the connection between Harry and Voldemort, along with protecting Harry several times.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Study_of_Ancient_Runes" title="Study of Ancient Runes">Study of Ancient Runes</a></b>: Dumbledore was also proficient in Ancient Runes, as he was able to perfectly understand the contents of his first-edition copy of <i><a href="/wiki/The_Tales_of_Beedle_the_Bard" title="The Tales of Beedle the Bard">The Tales of Beedle the Bard </a></i>, which were written completely in Runes. His ability to read and understand the runic language the book was shown by the fact that he had written a series of extensive notes on the book's various stories, providing his own interpretations of the stories' events, as well as recording significant historical background to how the stories had been changed or adapted over the years from this first edition.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Herbology" title="Herbology">Herbology</a></b>: Dumbledore had a fair share of knowledge on magical plants and their properties, as he knew of the healing properties of <a href="/wiki/Mandrake" title="Mandrake">Mandrakes</a> and therefore began the production of the <a href="/wiki/Mandrake_Restorative_Draught" title="Mandrake Restorative Draught">Mandrake Restorative Draught</a> to cure the petrification done when the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a> was opened. Although he was never shown directly handling magical plants, he had no problem bypassing the Devil Snare of the Philosopher Stone Chambers to reach Harry in time, showing he was at least adequately skilled in the field.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Wandlore" title="Wandlore">Wandlore</a></b>: From his correspondence with <a href="/wiki/Gellert_Grindelwald" title="Gellert Grindelwald">Gellert Grindelwald</a> in their youth over the <a href="/wiki/Elder_Wand" title="Elder Wand">Elder Wand</a> as it was one of the three fabled <a href="/wiki/Deathly_Hallows" title="Deathly Hallows">Deathly Hallows</a>, Dumbledore became highly knowledgeable of wandlore. Henceforth, he was not only able to easily recognise that the effect that happened during <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Duel_in_Little_Hangleton" title="Duel in Little Hangleton">confrontation</a> with <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a> was <a href="/wiki/Reverse_Spell" title="Reverse Spell">Reverse Spell</a> and explain the reason behind its occurrence to Harry, but he was also capable of understanding the reason of the unique effect <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter%27s_wand" title="Harry Potter&#39;s wand">Harry's wand</a> had when confronted by Voldemort and its activation only happening when around Voldemort so as to explain to Harry the reason why he was able to break <a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy" title="Lucius Malfoy">Lucius</a>'s wand but <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione</a> could break his wand. Finally, Dumbledore was aware that should the master of the Elder Wand die a natural death, he would remain undefeated and the wand's powers will be destroyed, henceforth attempting to do so by having <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a> kill him with the <a href="/wiki/Killing_Curse" title="Killing Curse">Killing Curse</a>, although it failed due to Draco <a href="/wiki/Disarming_Charm" title="Disarming Charm">Disarming</a> him first.</li>
<li><b>Indomitable willpower</b>: Dumbledore, in true <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a> fashion, had tremendously strong willpower, most prominently shown by his ability to overcome strong emotional attachments and desires and recover from horrendous losses from a young age, and become even stronger from the experience, as shown by Dumbledore immediately standing up to <a href="/wiki/Gellert_Grindelwald" title="Gellert Grindelwald">Grindelwald</a>, despite his crush for the latter and desire to complete the <i><a href="/wiki/For_the_Greater_Good" title="For the Greater Good">For the Greater Good</a></i> revolution they planned when Grindelwald attacked <a href="/wiki/Aberforth_Dumbledore" title="Aberforth Dumbledore">Aberfoth</a>, later showing determination to find a way to terminate the <a href="/wiki/Blood_pact" title="Blood pact">Blood pact</a> he had made with Grindelwald, and later still, after the blood pact was somehow overcome, mustering up the willpower to confront Grindelwald when the latter was at the height of his power in the <a href="/wiki/Global_wizarding_war" title="Global wizarding war">Global wizarding war</a>, despite his strong fear of Grindelwald knowing who had really killed <a href="/wiki/Ariana_Dumbledore" title="Ariana Dumbledore">Ariana</a>, all of which instead of breaking Dumbledore, made him the benevolent wizard respected by most of the Wizarding World. Dumbledore was also confident that he would be able to resist the effect of the <a href="/wiki/Dementor" title="Dementor">Dementors</a> long enough to easily escape <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a> and was known for having entered Azkaban at least once to recover <a href="/wiki/Morfin_Gaunt" title="Morfin Gaunt">Morfin Gaunt</a>'s memory and left without any effect on him. Additionally, Dumbledore was never intimidated when questioned by high-ranking <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Magic" title="Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a> officials, such as <a href="/wiki/Torquil_Travers" title="Torquil Travers">Torquil Travers</a>, <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cornelius_Fudge" title="Cornelius Fudge">Cornelius Fudge</a>, or <a href="/wiki/Rufus_Scrimgeour" title="Rufus Scrimgeour">Rufus Scrimgeour</a>, even when Travers forced him to wear two <a href="/wiki/Admonitor" title="Admonitor">admonitors</a>, or when Fudge tried to send him to Azkaban, nor was he ever intimidated by Voldemort, not only willing to speak the name his former student had used to terrorise the wizarding Britain but he would even casually refer to Voldemort as Tom in direct confrontation. A lesser display of Dumbledore's extreme willpower was his complete mastery of <a href="/wiki/Occlumency" title="Occlumency">Occlumency</a> and non-verbal magic, both of which required high amounts of mental strength. Additionally, Dumbledore's encouragement aided his allies in developing a similar willpower, with <a href="/wiki/Leta_Lestrange" title="Leta Lestrange">Leta Lestrange</a> and <a href="/wiki/Theseus_Scamander" title="Theseus Scamander">Theseus Scamander</a> notably resisting <a href="/wiki/Gellert_Grindelwald" title="Gellert Grindelwald">Grindelwald</a>'s persuasive speech, and <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> being encouraged by Dumbledore's example to be steadfast against <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> numerous times.</li>
<li><b>Intimidation master</b>: Despite Dumbledore's benevolent personality and famous standing as a well-meaning and good man, he proved himself to be an extraordinarily effective intimidator if necessary. With his unmatched magical power and skills as well as his well-concealed and barely unleashed dark side, Dumbledore was capable of striking fear even into the heart of the extremely powerful <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> and <a href="/wiki/Gellert_Grindelwald" title="Gellert Grindelwald">Gellert Grindelwald</a>, despite them being, perhaps, the closest individuals to matching him in power and skill, to the point that it was a widely known fact that both feared Dumbledore and refrained from attacking Hogwarts while he was there. Dumbledore's mere presence was so overwhelmingly intimidating that a group of <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> outright ran from him when he arrived during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a>, with even the intensely sadistic and extremely powerful <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a> fleeing as soon as she was able to from him. In addition, <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a> was quick to plead with Dumbledore not to kill him out of fear of what Dumbledore could do to him despite his own tremendous skills and powers and concern for <a href="/wiki/Lily" title="Lily">Lily</a> driving him to contact Dumbledore and <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a> noted that Dumbledore was more intimidating than <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</a>, a notably strict individual. Dumbledore's experience in intimidation tactics was such that he could effectively intimidate others while remaining calm with just a single sentence, as shown when he not only visibly unnerved <a href="/wiki/Cornelius_Fudge" title="Cornelius Fudge">Cornelius Fudge</a> and Harry Potter, despite Fudge's standing as the Minister for Magic and Harry's bravery, while just seriously defending <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Hagrid</a> and not outright angry but he even silenced Harry's own anger at him for trusting Snape despite Harry's tremendous rage over Snape's involvement in his parents death while only indicating Harry had crossed the line and still remaining calm. Additionally, just an expression of calm disappointment was enough to make Harry feel ashamed of his attempt to enter Hogwarts with the <a href="/wiki/Flying_Ford_Anglia" title="Flying Ford Anglia">Ford Anglia</a>, and his failure to get <a href="/wiki/Horace_Slughorn" title="Horace Slughorn">Slughorn</a>'s memory, with Harry on both occasions finding it preferable if Dumbledore shouted at him. At the peak of Dumbledore's wrath, when he was furiously interrogating <a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">Barty Crouch Jnr</a>, Dumbledore was capable of exerting such a massively fearsome appearance that Snape and McGonagall were visibly wary of the Headmaster and left Harry visibly terrified and he even described Dumbledore as being more fearsome than Voldemort, acknowledging he knew why Voldemort feared the old but still extraordinarily powerful wizard.</li>
<li><b>Conducting</b>: Dumbledore was fully capable of single-handedly leading the singing of the <a href="/wiki/Hoggy_Warty_Hogwarts" title="Hoggy Warty Hogwarts">Hoggy Warty Hogwarts</a> song, showing he had apt musical abilities.</li>
<li><b>Social networking</b>: Due to his vast reputation, Dumbledore had a vast network of followers and international contacts around the whole Wizarding World, to the point that he was known for knowing all that happens. Indeed, even the abrasive <a href="/wiki/Department_of_Magical_Law_Enforcement" title="Department of Magical Law Enforcement">Department of Magical Law Enforcement</a> Head <a href="/wiki/Torquil_Travers" title="Torquil Travers">Torquil Travers</a> showed begrudging admiration of Dumbledore's international contacts network while questioning the <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> professor. Later, during his job application meeting with Dumbledore, even <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> himself was impressed by how well-informed the new Hogwarts Headmaster was. This was what allowed Dumbledore to be aware of his old friend <a href="/wiki/Gellert_Grindelwald" title="Gellert Grindelwald">Gellert Grindelwald</a> being disguised as <a href="/wiki/Percival_Graves" title="Percival Graves">Percival Graves</a> and his search of the Obscurial that terrorised <a href="/wiki/New_York" title="New York">New York</a>, of <a href="/wiki/Credence_Barebone" title="Credence Barebone">Credence Barebone</a> being considered by many to be the long-lost <a href="/wiki/Corvus_Lestrange_(V)" title="Corvus Lestrange (V)">Corvus Lestrange</a>, of the feud between the <a href="/wiki/Kama_family" title="Kama family">Kama family</a> and <a href="/wiki/Lestrange_family" title="Lestrange family">Lestrange family</a>, of <a href="/wiki/Nicolas_Flamel" title="Nicolas Flamel">Nicolas Flamel</a> being urgently needed at <a href="/wiki/Gellert_Grindelwald" title="Gellert Grindelwald">Grindelwald</a>'s rally in Paris (communicating with Nicolas via the latter's <a href="/wiki/Nicolas_Flamel%27s_phoenix-embossed_book" title="Nicolas Flamel&#39;s phoenix-embossed book">phoenix-embossed book</a>), of <a href="/wiki/Leta_Lestrange" title="Leta Lestrange">Leta Lestrange</a>'s death at Grindelwald's rally, of several <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> being at Hogsmade waiting for Voldemort's return, of <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> hiding in Albania, of <a href="/wiki/Frank_Bryce" title="Frank Bryce">Frank Bryce</a>'s disappearance (from Muggle newspapers), of <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>'s arrival at the Burrow, and, thanks to <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>, of the majority of Voldemort's plans in the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a>. Additionally, Dumbledore's contacts allowed him to provide safe-houses for his allies, such as <a href="/wiki/Nicolas_Flamel" title="Nicolas Flamel">Nicolas Flamel</a>'s house for <a href="/wiki/Newton_Scamander" title="Newton Scamander">Newt Scamander</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Potter_cottage" title="Potter cottage">Potter cottage</a> for the endangered <a href="/wiki/Potter_family" title="Potter family">Potter family</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a>'s <a href="/wiki/12_Grimmauld_Place" title="12 Grimmauld Place">12 Grimmauld Place</a> house for the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a>'s headquarters. He was somehow aware of <a href="/wiki/Rita_Skeeter" title="Rita Skeeter">Rita Skeeter</a>'s Animagus ability too. However, while this did usually made Dumbledore well-informed, his contacts network was not always a perfect source of information, since in 1927 he was unaware that his relative <a href="/wiki/Credence_Barebone" title="Credence Barebone">Aurelius Dumbledore</a> had allegedly survived a shipwreck and was now called "<a href="/wiki/Credence_Barebone" title="Credence Barebone">Credence Barebone</a>", in 1981 he was unaware of <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a>'s innocence, and in 1995 he was unaware of <a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">Bartemius Crouch Junior</a>'s infiltration of his school in the guise of <a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">Alastor Moody</a>.</li>
<li><b>Physical aptitude</b>: Despite his advanced age and rather skinny build, Dumbledore was in superbly good physical condition, as he has been seen to be capable of physically performing feats that should be far beyond someone of his age and body, rivalling that of a much younger, fit man: his strength was great enough to raise <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> forcibly off the ground away from <a href="/wiki/Cedric_Diggory" title="Cedric Diggory">Cedric Diggory</a>'s body with one hand, which shocked Harry. Dumbledore was also astonishingly fast and agile for someone his age, as shown during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a>, describing as having sped past Harry and Neville when they blinked away from his arrival, and he displayed sufficient swimming ability to quickly swim with a "perfect breaststroke" and speed surpassing Harry, in the churning sea to reach <a href="/wiki/The_Cave" title="The Cave">The Cave</a>, with a considerably large tolerance to climate weathers to be entirely unfazed from the coldness of the waters, whereas Harry was left shivering upon emerging to the grounds of the cave. He also effortlessly jumped to the seventh trunk of Moody, which was used by Crouch to hold the real Moody while disguised as him, and landed gracefully on his feet, with his landing being only of light impact, before climbing back up with Moody on hand without issue. He also was capable of overpowering the weakened and injured <a href="/wiki/Quirinus_Quirrell" title="Quirinus Quirrell">Quirinus Quirrell</a> to forcibly and quickly remove him from his struggle with Harry. Dumbledore also displayed considerable endurance and stamina, as after only a brief moment of rest from being incapacitated by the <a href="/wiki/Emerald_Potion" title="Emerald Potion">Emerald Potion</a>, he was able to cast a <a href="/wiki/Firestorm" title="Firestorm">firestorm</a> to fend off the Inferi in <a href="/wiki/The_Cave" title="The Cave">The Cave</a>, and quickly afterwards fly from Hogsmeade to Hogwarts. In addition, he had a strong tolerance for pain, as shown when slicing his hand with a knife to use his blood to unlock the Cave, he did not even flinch and went as far as to soberly say the reason why to the shocked Harry.</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Career_accomplishments">Career accomplishments</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=57" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Career accomplishments">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=57" title="Edit section: Career accomplishments"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>In a long career, Albus Dumbledore served as teacher of at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a>, first as its <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> instructor and later as a <a href="/wiki/Transfiguration" title="Transfiguration">Transfiguration</a> Professor, (and eventual promotion to Head of the <a href="/wiki/Transfiguration_department_(academic_department)" title="Transfiguration department (academic department)">Transfiguration department</a>), making contributions to such learned, scholarly publications as <a href="/wiki/Transfiguration_Today" title="Transfiguration Today">Transfiguration Today</a>, <a href="/wiki/Challenges_in_Charming" title="Challenges in Charming">Challenges in Charming</a>, and <a href="/wiki/The_Practical_Potioneer" title="The Practical Potioneer">The Practical Potioneer</a>, ultimately rounding his career off by becoming arguably the finest and most revered <a href="/wiki/Headmaster" title="Headmaster">Headmaster</a> the school had ever seen. He was also a famous alchemist who worked with <a href="/wiki/Nicolas_Flamel" title="Nicolas Flamel">Nicolas Flamel</a>, the only known maker of the <a href="/wiki/Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Philosopher&#39;s Stone">Philosopher's Stone</a>, and was credited with discovering the twelve uses of <a href="/wiki/Dragon" title="Dragon">dragon</a>'s blood.
</p><p>Dumbledore became the <a href="/wiki/Chief_Warlock" title="Chief Warlock">Chief Warlock</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Wizengamot" title="Wizengamot">Wizengamot</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Supreme_Mugwump" title="Supreme Mugwump">Supreme Mugwump</a> of the <a href="/wiki/International_Confederation_of_Wizards" title="International Confederation of Wizards">International Confederation of Wizards</a>. He was removed from these posts during his conflict with the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a> under <a href="/wiki/Minister_for_Magic" title="Minister for Magic">Minister for Magic</a> <a href="/wiki/Cornelius_Fudge" title="Cornelius Fudge">Cornelius Fudge</a>, but was reinstated when the Ministry was forced to acknowledge that he had correctly warned that Voldemort had returned. He held the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_Merlin" title="Order of Merlin">Order of Merlin</a>, First Class, for Grand Sorcery.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Relationships">Relationships</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=58" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Relationships">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=58" title="Edit section: Relationships"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Family">Family</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=59" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Family">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=59" title="Edit section: Family"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Parents">Parents</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=60" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Parents">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=60" title="Edit section: Parents"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>Do not misunderstand me. I loved them. I loved my parents, I loved my brother and my sister, but I was selfish</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Albus Dumbledore<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div><figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c8/Percival_Dumbledore.png/revision/latest?cb=20110406190748" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="299" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Percival Dumbledore.png" data-image-key="Percival_Dumbledore.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c8/Percival_Dumbledore.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20110406190748" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c8/Percival_Dumbledore.png/revision/latest?cb=20110406190748" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c8/Percival_Dumbledore.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20110406190748" decoding="async" width="180" height="299" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Percival Dumbledore.png" data-image-key="Percival_Dumbledore.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c8/Percival_Dumbledore.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20110406190748" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Percival_Dumbledore.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Albus' father, <a href="/wiki/Percival_Dumbledore" title="Percival Dumbledore">Percival</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Albus' relationship with his parents was not very clear. However, it can be theorised that he most likely did not hold his <a href="/wiki/Percival_Dumbledore" title="Percival Dumbledore">father</a> in high regard, as he was imprisoned in <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a> for magically attacking three <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggle</a> boys who had inflicted permanent psychological damage on Ariana. According to <a href="/wiki/Aberforth_Dumbledore" title="Aberforth Dumbledore">Aberforth</a>, their mother taught Albus secrecy. Given that she read stories to him, it can be assumed that Albus had a good relationship with her, or at least a better one than the one she had with Aberfoth. Her death made Albus feel angry and bitter, as it left him with the responsibility of a damaged sister and a wayward brother, and he thought himself trapped and wasted.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7c/Kendra_Dumbledore.png/revision/latest?cb=20110406191633" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="263" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kendra Dumbledore.png" data-image-key="Kendra_Dumbledore.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7c/Kendra_Dumbledore.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20110406191633" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7c/Kendra_Dumbledore.png/revision/latest?cb=20110406191633" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7c/Kendra_Dumbledore.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20110406191633" decoding="async" width="180" height="263" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kendra Dumbledore.png" data-image-key="Kendra_Dumbledore.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7c/Kendra_Dumbledore.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20110406191633" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kendra_Dumbledore.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Albus' mother, <a href="/wiki/Kendra_Dumbledore" title="Kendra Dumbledore">Kendra</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Later on, during his conversation with Harry in limbo, he confessed that he truly loved each and every one of his family, but was blinded by his ambition and his madness. He had originally intended to use the <a href="/wiki/Resurrection_Stone" title="Resurrection Stone">Resurrection Stone</a> to bring back his parents, so that the heavy responsibility on his shoulders would be lifted. After Ariana's tragic and unexpected death, he planned, instead, to use the stone (if he ever found it, that is) to bring back his parents and his sister to apologise to them. This desire, however, ultimately caused his death: the Resurrection Stone had become part of a ring whose curse infected him the instant he put in on, and slowly killed him.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Ariana_Dumbledore">Ariana Dumbledore</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=61" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Ariana Dumbledore">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=61" title="Edit section: Ariana Dumbledore"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Fantastic Beasts: The Crimes of Grindelwald - The Original Screenplay">"<i>Not as well as I should have done.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Albus Dumbledore to <a href="/wiki/Leta_Lestrange" title="Leta Lestrange">Leta Lestrange</a> when asked if he had loved Ariana.<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Fantastic_Beasts:_The_Crimes_of_Grindelwald_-_The_Original_Screenplay" title="Fantastic Beasts: The Crimes of Grindelwald - The Original Screenplay">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/0e/Ariana_Dumbledore_Hog%27s_Head.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120108013927" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="237" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Ariana Dumbledore Hog&#39;s Head.jpg" data-image-key="Ariana_Dumbledore_Hog&#39;s_Head.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/0e/Ariana_Dumbledore_Hog%27s_Head.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120108013927" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/0e/Ariana_Dumbledore_Hog%27s_Head.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120108013927" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/0e/Ariana_Dumbledore_Hog%27s_Head.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120108013927" decoding="async" width="180" height="237" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Ariana Dumbledore Hog&#39;s Head.jpg" data-image-key="Ariana_Dumbledore_Hog&#39;s_Head.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/0e/Ariana_Dumbledore_Hog%27s_Head.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120108013927" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ariana_Dumbledore_Hog%27s_Head.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Ariana_Dumbledore" title="Ariana Dumbledore">Ariana Dumbledore</a>, his younger sister</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Albus Dumbledore was Ariana Dumbledore's eldest brother, and was not nearly as close to his younger siblings as they were to each other. Although he loved his younger sister, Albus was resentful when he had to take responsibility for her after their <a href="/wiki/Kendra_Dumbledore" title="Kendra Dumbledore">mother</a>'s death, which forced him to stay at home, and thus abandon his ambitious plans. When he and <a href="/wiki/Gellert_Grindelwald" title="Gellert Grindelwald">Gellert Grindelwald</a> made plans to subjugate <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggles</a> and take power in the <a href="/wiki/Wizarding_world" title="Wizarding world">wizarding world</a>, Albus planned to bring Ariana with them, but Aberforth pointed out that she was in no state to go. This launched a three-way duel between the brothers and Grindelwald, and Ariana was accidentally killed in the fray. Albus was devastated by his sister's death and for the rest of his life, Albus never forgave himself for the part he played in her death and always felt tremendous guilt and remorse over it. While he hardly ever spoke of this guilt to anyone, Dumbledore admitted it to <a href="/wiki/Leta_Lestrange" title="Leta Lestrange">Leta Lestrange</a> in an effort to get her to open up about her own guilt, and admitted that he had not loved Ariana enough during her life. Dumbledore was also haunted with the fear that it had been him to kill Ariana, to the point that he delayed facing Grindelwald for years.<sup id="cite_ref-DH35_96-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH35-96">&#91;96&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>From then on, Albus' <a href="/wiki/Boggart" title="Boggart">Boggart</a> would be Ariana's corpse.<sup id="cite_ref-JKR_12-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-JKR-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Aberforth_Dumbledore">Aberforth Dumbledore</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=62" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Aberforth Dumbledore">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=62" title="Edit section: Aberforth Dumbledore"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>They were not alike: Aberforth was never bookish and, unlike Albus, preferred to settle arguments by <a href="/wiki/Duelling" title="Duelling">duelling</a> rather than through reasoned discussion... In fairness to Aberforth, it must be admitted that living in Albus' shadow cannot have been an altogether comfortable experience.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Description of the Dumbledore brothers<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/40/Aberforth_Dumbledore.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170911160033" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="209" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Aberforth Dumbledore.jpg" data-image-key="Aberforth_Dumbledore.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/40/Aberforth_Dumbledore.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170911160033" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/40/Aberforth_Dumbledore.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170911160033" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/40/Aberforth_Dumbledore.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170911160033" decoding="async" width="180" height="209" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Aberforth Dumbledore.jpg" data-image-key="Aberforth_Dumbledore.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/40/Aberforth_Dumbledore.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170911160033" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Aberforth_Dumbledore.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Aberforth_Dumbledore" title="Aberforth Dumbledore">Aberforth Dumbledore</a>, his younger brother</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Aberforth Dumbledore was Albus' younger brother. Although Albus loved him, the two brothers were not close to each other, as they were very different persons in both personality, with Aberfoth resenting being in Albus's shadow. Despite not being close, it cannot be doubted that Albus loved and cared for him dearly, evidenced by the fact that even though he resented having to stay at home, Albus still refused to allow Aberfoth to stop his education out of concern of his brother's future. While Albus likely alienated him, along with Ariana, during his obsession with Gellert Grindelwald, when Grindelwald attacked Aberforth, Albus immediately came to his brother‘s aid and fought against his lover, clearly displaying that even at the height of his worst years, Albus still cared for Aberforth’s well-being immensely. After Ariana's death, Albus and Aberfoth's relationship became very estranged, as Aberfoth blamed Albus for the death of the sister he and his mother spent so much time caring for. Although they eventually established a cordial relationship with each other, with Aberfoth joining the Order of Phoenix when Albus founded it and attending Albus's funeral, Aberfoth and Albus still remained distant as Aberfoth was not able to forgive Albus. Albus himself made no attempts to change his brother's opinion about him, apparently acknowledging that he deserved it and accepting it as his punishment for their tragic family past, which Albus had a hand in. However, Albus was nevertheless saddened that he and Aberfoth never could reconcile and he did had a strong desire to make peace with him, as whenever he looked into the Mirror of Erised later in his life, Albus would see himself and Aberfoth reconciled and all of his family returned to him. Albus also came to believe that Aberforth was a better person than he was due to his much greater devotion to Ariana, which <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> disagreed with. Aberfoth himself however, eventually changed his opinions of his brother when Harry Potter helped him realise what Albus' intention really was and had forgiven him, as he chose to participate in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, helping the students and faculty of Hogwarts and the Hogsmeade residents to protect the school where Albus served as Headmaster for almost half of his lifetime, from Lord Voldemort, as well as to allow Harry time to find what he thought to be the last <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcrux</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Gellert_Grindelwald">Gellert Grindelwald</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=63" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Gellert Grindelwald">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=63" title="Edit section: Gellert Grindelwald"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>Did I know, in my heart of hearts, what Gellert Grindelwald was? I think I did, but I closed my eyes.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Albus Dumbledore to Harry Potter, about his friendship with Gellert Grindelwald<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/70/Grindelwald_Profile.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170425165236" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="198" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Grindelwald Profile.jpg" data-image-key="Grindelwald_Profile.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/70/Grindelwald_Profile.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170425165236" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/70/Grindelwald_Profile.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170425165236" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/70/Grindelwald_Profile.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170425165236" decoding="async" width="180" height="198" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Grindelwald Profile.jpg" data-image-key="Grindelwald_Profile.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/70/Grindelwald_Profile.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170425165236" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Grindelwald_Profile.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Gellert_Grindelwald" title="Gellert Grindelwald">Gellert Grindelwald</a>, his former lover and great enemy</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Dumbledore first met Gellert Grindelwald when he was seventeen. They were introduced by Grindelwald's great aunt, <a href="/wiki/Bathilda_Bagshot" title="Bathilda Bagshot">Bathilda Bagshot</a>. They got along almost instantly, according to Bagshot. They were ultimately united by their desire to have the <a href="/wiki/Deathly_Hallows" title="Deathly Hallows">Deathly Hallows</a>. They also made a <a href="/wiki/Blood_pact" title="Blood pact">blood pact</a> and they swore an oath never to fight each other. It is also known that the two were romantically involved. It is said that their relationship was intense and passionate. This was so much so that Dumbledore would, for a time, see Grindelwald in the Mirror of Erised as his greatest desire. 
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>Gellert — <br /> Your point about Wizard dominance being </i>For the <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggle</a>'s own good<i> — this, I think, is the crucial point. Yes, we have been given power and yes, that power gives us the right to rule, but it also gives us responsibilities over the ruled. We must stress this point, it will be the foundation stone upon which we build. Where we are opposed, as we surely will be, this must be the basis of all our counterarguments. We seize control </i><a href="/wiki/For_the_Greater_Good" title="For the Greater Good">for the greater good</a><i>. And from this it follows that where we meet resistance, we must use only the force that is necessary and no more. (This was your mistake at <a href="/wiki/Durmstrang_Institute" title="Durmstrang Institute">Durmstrang</a>! But I do not complain, because if you had not been expelled, we would never have met.)<br />Albus</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;One of Albus Dumbledore's letters to Grindelwald in their school years as they plotted Muggle domination<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>They got along for two months until Aberforth, Dumbledore's brother, confronted them over the neglect of Ariana Dumbledore. Grindelwald lost control during the argument and attacked Aberforth. Dumbledore rushed forward to defend his brother, and during the duel his sister, Ariana was killed. Grindelwald fled and Dumbledore ended their friendship, although his romantic desires did not subside.
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Fantastic Beasts: The Crimes of Grindelwald - The Original Screenplay">"<i>Oh we were closer than brothers.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Albus Dumbledore to Torquil Travers, about his bond with Gellert Grindelwald<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Fantastic_Beasts:_The_Crimes_of_Grindelwald_-_The_Original_Screenplay" title="Fantastic Beasts: The Crimes of Grindelwald - The Original Screenplay">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a2/Dumbledore_Mirror_of_Erised.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190209142936" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="138" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dumbledore Mirror of Erised.gif" data-image-key="Dumbledore_Mirror_of_Erised.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a2/Dumbledore_Mirror_of_Erised.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190209142936" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a2/Dumbledore_Mirror_of_Erised.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190209142936" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a2/Dumbledore_Mirror_of_Erised.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190209142936" decoding="async" width="250" height="138" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dumbledore Mirror of Erised.gif" data-image-key="Dumbledore_Mirror_of_Erised.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a2/Dumbledore_Mirror_of_Erised.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190209142936" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dumbledore_Mirror_of_Erised.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">For a long and tumultuous time in his life, Albus's greatest and most desperate desire was his former best friend and lover, Gellert Grindelwald</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Grindelwald spent a number of years gaining power in Europe while Dumbledore spent his time teaching young wizards at Hogwarts. While Grindelwald and his army terrorised Europe, Dumbledore remained in Britain and refused adamantly to face Grindelwald. While this was partially due to the Blood Pact, which also kept Britain safe as Grindelwald couldn't attempt an attack as it would mean a duel with Albus, which would violate the Pact, Dumbledore showed he still had lingering affection for Grindelwald, as when he looked at the Mirror of Erised at this time in his life, he saw Grindelwald. Nevertheless, Dumbledore tried to indirectly participate in Grindelwald's defeat and he used Newt to do it by sending him to America with the injured Thunderbird Frank, knowing somehow Grindelwald had infiltrated America in search for the Obscurial there, which Dumbledore knew he intended to use against him. However, after the death of Leta Lestrange, Dumbledore put aside whatever affection he had for Grindelwald and was determined to break the Blood Pact.
</p><p>While not having the vial destroyed, he made sure that the wizarding world would survive Grindelwald's reign of terror by providing whatever intellectual and possibly magical assistance he could. After finally succeeding, Dumbledore directly tracked down Grindelwald. Upon finding each other, Dumbledore and Grindelwald initiated a legendary duel of 1945, unleashing all of their extraordinary magical capabilities on each other, the display being so amazing that it remains among the greatest magical battles ever in history. Dumbledore eventually triumphed in the end, despite Grindelwald's mastery of the <a href="/wiki/Elder_Wand" title="Elder Wand">Elder Wand</a>, becoming the wand's new master and he then brought in Grindelwald to the authorities of the magical world, who imprisoned him in his own prison <a href="/wiki/Nurmengard_Castle" title="Nurmengard Castle">Nurmengard</a>.
</p><p>Years later in <a href="/wiki/1998" title="1998">1998</a>, Grindelwald refused to give any information to <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> about the Elder Wand despite the fact that he was imprisoned, wandless and face-to-face with the only Dark Wizard ever considered greater and more powerful than himself. This seems to indicate that Grindelwald no longer held the views of those who practised the Dark Arts and had contemplated and felt remorse over his actions and that his lie was a last act to repent for his sins, something which Dumbledore acknowledged to be true, implying despite Grindelwald's crimes, Dumbledore still retained some fondness for him and believed that he truly had felt remorse over his crimes during his imprisonment in Nurmengard. It was speculated by <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> that Grindelwald had given his life to prevent Voldemort from desecrating Dumbledore's tomb, possibly indicating Grindelwald still respected and cared for Dumbledore despite all that happened.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Newt_Scamander">Newt Scamander</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=64" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Newt Scamander">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=64" title="Edit section: Newt Scamander"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Fantastic Beasts: The Crimes of Grindelwald - The Original Screenplay">"<i>Do you know why I admire you, Newt? More perhaps than any men I know. You do not seek power. Or popularity. You simply ask, is the thing right in itself? If it is, you do it, no matter the cost.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Albus Dumbledore to Newt when they met in <a href="/wiki/London" title="London">London</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Fantastic_Beasts:_The_Crimes_of_Grindelwald_-_The_Original_Screenplay" title="Fantastic Beasts: The Crimes of Grindelwald - The Original Screenplay">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/15/Newt_New_York.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20181123165118" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="180" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Newt New York.jpg" data-image-key="Newt_New_York.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/15/Newt_New_York.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20181123165118" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/15/Newt_New_York.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20181123165118" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/15/Newt_New_York.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20181123165118" decoding="async" width="180" height="180" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Newt New York.jpg" data-image-key="Newt_New_York.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/15/Newt_New_York.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20181123165118" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Newt_New_York.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Newton_Scamander" title="Newton Scamander">Newt Scamander</a>, his former student and friend</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Dumbledore's relationship with famous <a href="/wiki/Magizoologist" title="Magizoologist">magizoologist</a> was very close. During Newt's time at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>, Dumbledore was his <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> Professor. When one of <a href="/wiki/Leta_Lestrange" title="Leta Lestrange">Leta Lestrange</a>'s experiments involving a magical beast went too far, endangering the life of another student. Newt did not want to see a friend thrown out of school, so he took the blame for Leta's actions, and was thus sentenced to be expelled from Hogwarts in her place. Albus developed unending trust and loyalty to him after he argued strongly against his expulsion. It is unclear whether the expulsion was enforced or not, or if it was temporary or permanent. However, Newt was allowed to keep his wand. After school Newt probably was in a regular contact with his teacher. Newt respected his mentor enough to do tasks for him.
