Dumbledore told him where to find one ill-bred <a href="/wiki/Thunderbird" title="Thunderbird">Thunderbird</a> and later sent his former student to <a href="/wiki/New_York" title="New York">New York</a> to release this beast, whose natural environment was <a href="/wiki/Arizona" title="Arizona">Arizona</a>. At this time Newt helped capture <a href="/wiki/Gellert_Grindelwald" title="Gellert Grindelwald">Gellert Grindelwald</a>, who was trying to convince <a href="/wiki/Obscurial" title="Obscurial">Obscurial</a> <a href="/wiki/Credence_Barebone" title="Credence Barebone">Credence Barebone</a> to join his ranks. Newt was extremely loyal to Dumbledore, because when he appealed to his travel ban, he lied to the committee members that he had gone to the <a href="/wiki/United_States_of_America" title="United States of America">United States</a> on his orders. When Grindelwald managed to escape, Albus felt that he would not be able to fight the dark wizard, so he asked Scamander for help. Dumbledore admired him, because he didn't care about power or popularity, which is quite ironic as Dumbledore once craved at least one of these things. He sent Newt to <a href="/wiki/Paris" title="Paris">Paris</a> to rescue Credence, who survived battle in New York, but Newt was reluctant, nevertheless he was willing to accept the address of a <a href="/wiki/Nicolas_Flamel" title="Nicolas Flamel">safe-house</a>. The rumours of Newton's potential travel to <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">France</a> reached the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">British Ministry of Magic</a>, and a delegation, including Newt's brother <a href="/wiki/Theseus_Scamander" title="Theseus Scamander">Theseus Scamander</a>, Leta Lestrange and <a href="/wiki/Torquil_Travers" title="Torquil Travers">Torquil Travers</a>, was sent to Hogwarts Castle to question Dumbledore. Albus only pretended that he did not know anything about it and said that Newt is not a great follower of orders. During the <a href="/wiki/Gellert_Grindelwald%27s_Paris_rally" title="Gellert Grindelwald&#39;s Paris rally">Battle in Lestrange family Mausoleum</a>, vial of Dumbledore's and Grindelwald's <a href="/wiki/Blood_pact" title="Blood pact">blood pact</a> was stolen from Grindelwald, however, without his knowledge by a <a href="/wiki/Niffler" title="Niffler">Niffler</a> belonging to Newt Scamander. Shortly thereafter Scamander brought it to Dumbledore at Hogwarts. Dumbledore expressed regret at Leta's death in mausoleum. Newt in turn did not ask Dumbledore why he would form a blood pact with Grindelwald but simply asked him to destroy it, showing respect for his privacy. Although it apparently took years, Dumbledore clearly managed to abolish the blood pact, allowing him to finally defeat Grindelwald in a legendary duel.
</p>
<h3><span id="Tom_Riddle_(Lord_Voldemort)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Tom_Riddle_.28Lord_Voldemort.29">Tom Riddle (Lord Voldemort)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=65" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Tom Riddle (Lord Voldemort)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=65" title="Edit section: Tom Riddle (Lord Voldemort)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix"><b>Voldemort</b>: "<i>You do not seek to kill me, Dumbledore? Above such brutality, are you?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Dumbledore</b>: "<i>We both know there are other ways of destroying a man, Tom. Merely taking your life would not satisfy me, I admit.</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Voldemort</b>: "<i>There is nothing worse than death, Dumbledore!</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Dumbledore</b>: "<i>You are quite wrong. Indeed your failure to understand that there are things much worse than death has always been your greatest weakness.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Lord Voldemort and Dumbledore during their <a href="/wiki/Duel_in_the_Ministry_Atrium" title="Duel in the Ministry Atrium">Duel in the Ministry Atrium</a>, as part of the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/78/Lord_Voldemort.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150829033655" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="223" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Lord Voldemort.jpg" data-image-key="Lord_Voldemort.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/78/Lord_Voldemort.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150829033655" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/78/Lord_Voldemort.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150829033655" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/78/Lord_Voldemort.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150829033655" decoding="async" width="180" height="223" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Lord Voldemort.jpg" data-image-key="Lord_Voldemort.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/78/Lord_Voldemort.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150829033655" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Lord_Voldemort.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a>, his former student and greatest enemy</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Dumbledore personally approached <a href="/wiki/Cole" title="Cole">Mrs Cole</a>, the caretaker of the orphanage in which <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Tom Riddle</a> resided to enrol the latter in Hogwarts. Dumbledore met Tom Riddle for the first time there and was unaware at the time that he had just met the person who would become most powerful and dangerous Dark Wizard of all time. He was however intrigued by Tom Riddle as his powers were surprisingly well-developed by such a young wizard who had begun to use them consciously. Dumbledore was also disturbed by the fact that Tom was a <a href="/wiki/Parseltongue" title="Parseltongue">Parselmouth</a>, a rare ability supposedly connected with the Dark Arts, although not as much as the fact that Tom had obvious instincts for cruelty, secrecy and domination which was proved by the fact that Tom had used his magic to hurt the other children in the orphanage. Dumbledore then returned to Hogwarts intending to keep an eye upon Tom Riddle, as he was alone and friendless, a dangerous situation, but at that point Dumbledore, ever the man who staunchly believed in second chances and redemption, still considered Riddle as being not a lost cause and could repent
</p><p>When then-headmaster <a href="/wiki/Armando_Dippet" title="Armando Dippet">Armando Dippet</a> confided in Dumbledore about Tom Riddle approaching him about staying on after graduation to teach <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> — which he only refused due to Tom's age, suggesting he ask again in a few years — Dumbledore advised him against it. Though he explained none of his reasons to Professor Dippet, for the headmaster was just as charmed by Tom as the other professors, Dumbledore felt uneasy about the request and did not want Riddle back at Hogwarts in a position of power.
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">"<i>The time is long gone when I could frighten you with a burning wardrobe and force you to make repayment for your crimes. But I wish I could, Tom, I wish I could...</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Albus Dumbledore<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>While Dumbledore was aware of <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Tom Riddle</a>'s transformation and rise to power, he still maintained contact with the latter, even allowing him to visit <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">the school</a> for a supposed job interview. When Tom, or Lord Voldemort as he began calling himself, visited the school, Dumbledore was courteous. However Dumbledore suspected that Voldemort wanted more than a job, likely wanting to raise an army. He was troubled at some of the rumours about Tom, these were true of course. When Dumbledore turned down Voldemort's request, this sealed the deep resentment Voldemort would continue to feel towards him and he cursed the Defence Against the Dark Arts post out of spite.
</p><p>It was clear that while many who followed Dumbledore's cause both feared and despised Voldemort greatly, Dumbledore did not share such views as he had known Tom Riddle personally, and although he was committed to defeating him, Dumbledore held no personal resentment nor fear towards the Dark Lord and continued to see him as his former student worthy of being pitied for his childhood and complete inability to understand love, as he had never received any. He even appeared to feel some deep-rooted guilt and remorse over his inability to change Riddle, as he noted with great sadness in his face and tone that he sincerely wished he could have forced Voldemort to repent for his sins in a peaceful manner. Dumbledore understood the evil in Riddle as a result from a string of unfortunate events and performed intensive research on him, eventually discovering his Horcruxes. After Riddle's transformation into Lord Voldemort, contrary to the rest of the wizarding community's fear of saying the Dark Lord's name, Dumbledore, as the only person Voldemort (secretly) feared, refused to be intimidated by the Dark Lord, referring to him as "Voldemort" to others and as "Tom" in conversation with Voldemort himself, a subtle but steadfast refusal to allow Lord Voldemort to dictate the terms of their relationship and a trait that would later be inherited by Harry Potter.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/08/Movie-duel.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170103051228" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Movie-duel.jpg" data-image-key="Movie-duel.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/08/Movie-duel.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170103051228" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/08/Movie-duel.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170103051228" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/08/Movie-duel.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170103051228" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Movie-duel.jpg" data-image-key="Movie-duel.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/08/Movie-duel.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170103051228" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Movie-duel.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Albus Dumbledore locked in combat with <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/1996" title="1996">1996</a>, Dumbledore and Voldemort met face to face in the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a>. Voldemort started a dangerous <a href="/wiki/Duelling" title="Duelling">duel</a> during which he used all of his tremendous magical capabilities in an attempt to murder Harry Potter along with his former teacher. Fortunately for Dumbledore, he proved himself to be worthy of his title as the only wizard who was ever feared by Voldemort and maintained The offensive in the battle, eventually forcing Voldemort to flee. A short while later, Dumbledore became aware of Voldemort's plan to use <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a> to kill him, possibly as Voldemort realised from their previous altercation that he would lose a duel with Dumbledore head on and thus used Dumbledore's empathy for Draco to give Draco a greater chance to kill him. Dumbledore requested to <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Snape</a> that he should be the one to kill him instead of Malfoy. Despite dying to Snape in <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a>, Dumbledore's legacy allowed Harry Potter to defeat Voldemort once and for all in <a href="/wiki/1998" title="1998">1998</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Patricia_Rakepick">Patricia Rakepick</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=66" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Patricia Rakepick">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=66" title="Edit section: Patricia Rakepick"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/Patricia_Rakepick_-_Hogwarts_Mystery.png/revision/latest?cb=20180827165324" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="276" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Patricia Rakepick - Hogwarts Mystery.png" data-image-key="Patricia_Rakepick_-_Hogwarts_Mystery.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/Patricia_Rakepick_-_Hogwarts_Mystery.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180827165324" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/Patricia_Rakepick_-_Hogwarts_Mystery.png/revision/latest?cb=20180827165324" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/Patricia_Rakepick_-_Hogwarts_Mystery.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180827165324" decoding="async" width="180" height="276" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Patricia Rakepick - Hogwarts Mystery.png" data-image-key="Patricia_Rakepick_-_Hogwarts_Mystery.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/Patricia_Rakepick_-_Hogwarts_Mystery.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180827165324" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Patricia_Rakepick_-_Hogwarts_Mystery.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Patricia_Rakepick" title="Patricia Rakepick">Patricia Rakepick</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Albus Dumbledore was, at the time of <a href="/wiki/Patricia_Rakepick" title="Patricia Rakepick">Patricia Rakepick</a>'s arrival at Hogwarts, the school's <a href="/wiki/Head_of_Transfiguration" title="Head of Transfiguration">Head of Transfiguration</a> under then <a href="/wiki/Headmaster" title="Headmaster">Headmaster</a> <a href="/wiki/Armando_Dippet" title="Armando Dippet">Armando Dippet</a>, until he eventually succeeded the latter in said post at some point during her magical education. Unlike all of the other staff members, Dumbledore did not let her rebellious streak, a trait for which, seen as it went beyond mere mischief-making, many of his colleagues came to distrust and dislike her for, cloud the fact that she was an exceptional student and spoke highly of her abilities even after her graduation. He welcomed her warmly back to Hogwarts upon inviting her back to the castle to help the staff in their efforts to put a stop to the threat posed to the security of the school and those who dwelled therein by the fabled <a href="/wiki/Cursed_Vaults" title="Cursed Vaults">Cursed Vaults</a>, though it is unknown if he shared <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>'s suspicions about her ulterior motives, the latter of whom believed, quite correctly, that Dumbledore trusted her.
</p><p>After Rakepick revealed herself to be a traitor working for <a href="/wiki/R" title="R">R</a>, Dumbledore did not seem too surprised, showing that he did suspect her but just didn't took it to extreme levels. Regardless, Dumbledore didn't seem to resent her too much for having ruthlessly tortured <a href="/wiki/Merula_Snyde" title="Merula Snyde">Merula Snyde</a>, as although he considered it a major priority to neutralise her, Dumbledore openly suggested against <a href="/wiki/Merula_Snyde" title="Merula Snyde">Merula Snyde</a> being too focused to kill her.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Harry_Potter">Harry Potter</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=67" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Harry Potter">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=67" title="Edit section: Harry Potter"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>I cared about you too much. I cared more for your happiness than your knowing the truth, more for your peace of mind than my plan, more for your life than the lives that might be lost if the plan failed. In other words, I acted exactly as Voldemort expects we fools who love to act.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Dumbledore explaining his feelings for Harry<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3c/Harry_Potter_movies_hbp_promostills_6.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180528175859" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="245" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry Potter movies hbp promostills 6.jpg" data-image-key="Harry_Potter_movies_hbp_promostills_6.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3c/Harry_Potter_movies_hbp_promostills_6.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180528175859" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3c/Harry_Potter_movies_hbp_promostills_6.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180528175859" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3c/Harry_Potter_movies_hbp_promostills_6.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180528175859" decoding="async" width="180" height="245" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry Potter movies hbp promostills 6.jpg" data-image-key="Harry_Potter_movies_hbp_promostills_6.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3c/Harry_Potter_movies_hbp_promostills_6.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180528175859" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry_Potter_movies_hbp_promostills_6.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, his favourite student</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Dumbledore was well known for the care and steadfast championing of Harry Potter. It was Dumbledore who planned and wanted the infant Harry to be taken from the cottage at <a href="/wiki/Godric%27s_Hollow" title="Godric&#39;s Hollow">Godric's Hollow</a> where Harry's parents had been murdered, taking him away from his godfather and rightful guardian. He then left Harry in the care of Harry's <a href="/wiki/Petunia_Dursley" title="Petunia Dursley">Aunt Petunia</a> and <a href="/wiki/Vernon_Dursley" title="Vernon Dursley">Uncle Vernon</a> in Surrey, Little Whinging, placing Harry on the doorstep of their home, despite them not being named guardians in the event of James and Lily's death. Despite being aware of the criminal abuse Harry had suffered while living with the Dursley family through a contact, <a href="/wiki/Arabella_Figg" title="Arabella Figg">Arabella Figg</a>, he did not step in to prevent the abuse Harry suffered as a child, leaving him to suffer with his magical hating Aunt and Uncle and bullying cousin <a href="/wiki/Dudley" title="Dudley">Dudley</a>. Throughout Harry's years at Hogwarts, Dumbledore provided him with protection and guidance, and supplemented Harry's schooling with additional information about Lord Voldemort.
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">"<i>You are protected, in short, by your ability to love! The only protection that can possibly work against the lure of power like Voldemort’s! In spite of all the temptation you have endured, all the suffering, you remain pure of heart, just as pure as you were at the age of eleven, when you stared into a mirror that reflected your heart’s desire, and it showed you only the way to thwart Lord Voldemort, and not immortality or riches. Harry, have you any idea how few wizards could have seen what you saw in that mirror? Voldemort should have known then what he was dealing with, but he did not!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Dumbledore telling Harry about his uncommon nature as a wizard<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>After the <a href="/wiki/Return_of_Lord_Voldemort" title="Return of Lord Voldemort">Rebirth of Lord Voldemort</a>, Dumbledore, in an effort to prevent Voldemort from learning certain details through his link to Harry, refused to disclose certain details to Harry. This caused some friction between the two. When Dumbledore explained to Harry that he had done so because he cared a great deal for him and wished to avoid Voldemort learning the true nature of their relationship, Harry was still angry but was more understanding.
</p><p>By <a href="/wiki/1996%E2%80%931997_school_year" title="1996–1997 school year">Harry's sixth year</a>, Albus Dumbledore took on the role of providing Harry with additional insights into the origins of <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>, as Voldemort's power was growing enormously stronger. He did this largely through the use of the <a href="/wiki/Pensieve" title="Pensieve">Pensieve</a>. He entrusted Harry with the task of getting a final, crucial memory from <a href="/wiki/Horace_Slughorn" title="Horace Slughorn">Horace Slughorn</a> regarding Voldemort's knowledge of <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcruxes</a>. When Dumbledore was killed, Harry was devastated.
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">"<i>You are talented, famous, and powerful — everything Horace values.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Albus Dumbledore's opinion of  Harry Potter<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fb/Harry_Dumbledore_limbo.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141122220457" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="134" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry Dumbledore limbo.jpg" data-image-key="Harry_Dumbledore_limbo.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fb/Harry_Dumbledore_limbo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20141122220457" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fb/Harry_Dumbledore_limbo.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141122220457" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fb/Harry_Dumbledore_limbo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20141122220457" decoding="async" width="180" height="134" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry Dumbledore limbo.jpg" data-image-key="Harry_Dumbledore_limbo.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fb/Harry_Dumbledore_limbo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20141122220457" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry_Dumbledore_limbo.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Harry Potter speaking with Albus Dumbledore in Limbo</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Harry and Dumbledore forged a strong Student <i>—</i> Headmaster bond, comparable to that between two close family members (most likely case of a great-grandfather <i>—</i> grandson), in spite of the century in age difference. Harry felt comfortable enough around the impressive, intimidating figure of Dumbledore to shout at him in frustration, cry out of grief, admit to his fears, and entrust him with his life. Dumbledore in return considered Harry to be a talented and powerful <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">wizard</a> who had inherited his parents' best qualities, noting that Harry was a leader of superior quality to himself, as Harry led because others looked to him to lead them rather than because he had ever sought power or authority for himself. He also had great faith in Harry as shown when Dumbledore was in a weakened state and Harry, who had never Apparated beyond a few feet, had to <a href="/wiki/Apparition" title="Apparition">Apparate</a> them both back. Dumbledore told Harry that he wasn't worried because he was with Harry.
</p><p>Before the final event of the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, after Harry sacrificed himself and was struck by Voldemort's Killing Curse and nearly died back in the <a href="/wiki/Forbidden_Forest" title="Forbidden Forest">Forbidden Forest</a>, his soul went to a place resembling <a href="/wiki/King%27s_Cross_Station" title="King&#39;s Cross Station">King's Cross Station</a>, where Dumbledore was waiting to speak with him. The fact that Dumbledore himself was there to meet Harry in a place between life and death attests to the bond of fellowship between them. After the war, Harry also named his <a href="/wiki/Albus_Potter" title="Albus Potter">second son</a> after Dumbledore.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Rubeus_Hagrid">Rubeus Hagrid</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=68" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Rubeus Hagrid">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=68" title="Edit section: Rubeus Hagrid"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>I would trust Hagrid with my life.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Albus Dumbledore's trust in Hagrid<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cd/Rubeus_Hagrid.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160121163026" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="247" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Rubeus Hagrid.jpg" data-image-key="Rubeus_Hagrid.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cd/Rubeus_Hagrid.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160121163026" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cd/Rubeus_Hagrid.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160121163026" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cd/Rubeus_Hagrid.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160121163026" decoding="async" width="180" height="247" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Rubeus Hagrid.jpg" data-image-key="Rubeus_Hagrid.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cd/Rubeus_Hagrid.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160121163026" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Rubeus_Hagrid.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Rubeus Hagrid</a>: his friend, colleague, and former student</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Dumbledore displayed an innate trust of Rubeus Hagrid in every situation starting from when Hagrid attended Hogwarts. Dumbledore believed that Hagrid did not open the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a> and asked the former Headmaster <a href="/wiki/Armando_Dippet" title="Armando Dippet">Armando Dippet</a> to train Hagrid as the gamekeeper so he could stay. Since that time Dumbledore has shown many examples of his faith in Hagrid. For example, Hagrid is the one tasked to protect <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> as he is brought to live with the Dursleys, in addition he is asked to bring the <a href="/wiki/Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Philosopher&#39;s Stone">Philosopher's Stone</a> back from Gringotts. Dumbledore also sent Hagrid on other important missions, such as attempting to persuade the <a href="/wiki/Giant" title="Giant">giants</a> to join the side of the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a>. Dumbledore additionally was the only one who supported Hagrid's decision to bring his giant half-brother <a href="/wiki/Grawp" title="Grawp">Grawp</a> with him back to Hogwarts after his mission to recruit the giants failed, allowing Grawp to stay in the Forbidden Forest and later having him sent to the mountains near Hogsmeade. Hagrid was also devastated by Dumbledore's death in 1997. He was also right about telling Harry that Snape was on Dumbledore's side. Hagrid in return greatly admired and trusted Dumbledore, and took extreme offence to anyone who dared insult the Headmaster.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Minerva_McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=69" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Minerva McGonagall">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=69" title="Edit section: Minerva McGonagall"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone"><b>Minerva McGonagall</b>: "<i>Professor Dumbledore is a very great wizard, Potter, he has many demands on his time —</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>But this is important.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Minerva McGonagall regarding Dumbledore's feelings towards Harry<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/84/Mcgonagall.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150810172040" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="255" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Mcgonagall.jpg" data-image-key="Mcgonagall.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/84/Mcgonagall.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150810172040" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/84/Mcgonagall.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150810172040" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/84/Mcgonagall.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150810172040" decoding="async" width="180" height="255" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Mcgonagall.jpg" data-image-key="Mcgonagall.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/84/Mcgonagall.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150810172040" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Mcgonagall.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</a>: his friend, colleague, and former student</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Minerva McGonagall knew Dumbledore for the majority of her life. She attended <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a> as a student during Dumbledore's time as the <a href="/wiki/Transfiguration_(class)" title="Transfiguration (class)">Transfiguration</a> <a href="/wiki/Professor" title="Professor">Professor</a> and later went on to replace him when he took the position of <a href="/wiki/Headmaster" title="Headmaster">Head</a> of the school. She served for many years as his Deputy Headmistress, standing in for him and even replacing him as standing Headmistress on several occasions.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_30-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-COS_31-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COS-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Minerva had great faith in Dumbledore, placing great stock in the differences between him and <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_7-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> However, she did not hesitate to disagree with him when she felt the need to do so. She was extremely opposed to his decision to place <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> with his narrow-minded <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggle</a> <a href="/wiki/Petunia_Dursley" title="Petunia Dursley">aunt</a> and <a href="/wiki/Vernon_Dursley" title="Vernon Dursley">uncle</a>, saying that "<i>You couldn’t find two people who are less like us</i>."<sup id="cite_ref-PS1_8-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS1-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> She also served more than once to bring Dumbledore back on track when he became distracted from the matter currently at hand.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_38-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Dumbledore discovered Minerva in tears in her classroom late one evening, after she found out about the marriage of a <a href="/wiki/Dougal_McGregor" title="Dougal McGregor">young love</a> to another woman. She confessed the whole story to him and Albus Dumbledore offered both comfort and wisdom; telling Minerva some of his own family history, previously unknown to her. The confidences exchanged that night between two intensely private and reserved characters were to form the basis of a lasting mutual esteem and friendship.
</p><p>Minerva had no qualms about displaying her loyalty to Dumbledore. When <a href="/wiki/Cornelius_Fudge" title="Cornelius Fudge">Cornelius Fudge</a> brought <a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">Aurors</a> to arrest Dumbledore in <a href="/wiki/1996" title="1996">1996</a>, she boldly stepped forward and announced her intention to fight the Aurors on his behalf. She only stepped back at Dumbledore's insistence when he reminded her that Hogwarts and her students would need her in his absence.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_41-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Minerva was devastated when Dumbledore was killed in <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a> during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a>, and attended his funeral.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_30-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> A year later, when <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> returned to Hogwarts on a mission given to him by Dumbledore she did not question the decision of her dead friend, but immediately sought to provide whatever assistance she could.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_22-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Severus_Snape">Severus Snape</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=70" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Severus Snape">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=70" title="Edit section: Severus Snape"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows"><b>Albus Dumbledore</b>: "<i>I prefer not to put all my secrets in one basket, particularly not a basket that spends so much time dangling on the arm of Lord Voldemort.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Severus Snape</b>: "<i>Which I do on your orders!</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Albus Dumbledore</b>: "<i>And you do it extremely well. Do not think that I underestimate the constant danger in which you place yourself, Severus. To give Voldemort what appears to be valuable information while withholding the essentials is a job I would entrust to nobody but you.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Dumbledore and Snape on the latter's espionage<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/35/Severus_Snape_OOTP.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141122220746" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="245" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Severus Snape OOTP.jpg" data-image-key="Severus_Snape_OOTP.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/35/Severus_Snape_OOTP.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20141122220746" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/35/Severus_Snape_OOTP.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141122220746" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/35/Severus_Snape_OOTP.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20141122220746" decoding="async" width="180" height="245" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Severus Snape OOTP.jpg" data-image-key="Severus_Snape_OOTP.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/35/Severus_Snape_OOTP.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20141122220746" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Severus_Snape_OOTP.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>, a trusted ally, colleague, and former student</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Snape's relationship with Dumbledore was one of close, but not indefinite trust. After indirectly and accidentally sending Voldemort after <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily</a>, Snape turned to Dumbledore to keep her safe. Dumbledore chose to capitalise on Snape's remorse and initiated him into the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> as a double agent.
</p><p>As a spy for the Order, Snape silently kept his place within the ranks of the <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>, while informing Dumbledore about their movements. He also adopted the role of secret agent for Voldemort, and supplied him with strategic scraps of information about the Order. The content of these reports was often dictated by Dumbledore. It is implied that Snape withheld little, if any, information from Dumbledore that was relevant to the Order's success, while Snape deliberately did the opposite for Voldemort.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/26/Snape_and_Dumbledore.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160819104925" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="270" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Snape and Dumbledore.jpg" data-image-key="Snape_and_Dumbledore.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/26/Snape_and_Dumbledore.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160819104925" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/26/Snape_and_Dumbledore.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160819104925" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/26/Snape_and_Dumbledore.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160819104925" decoding="async" width="180" height="270" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Snape and Dumbledore.jpg" data-image-key="Snape_and_Dumbledore.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/26/Snape_and_Dumbledore.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160819104925" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Snape_and_Dumbledore.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><i>"I am fortunate, extremely fortunate, that I have you, Severus..."</i></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince"><b>Albus Dumbledore</b>: "<i>Severus... please...</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Severus Snape</b>: "<i>Avada Kedavra!</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Dumbledore asking Snape to end his life<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<p>It is notable that Dumbledore did not confide completely in Snape, thereby minimising the potential damage that might occur if Snape was compromised. Snape resented Dumbledore's secrecy, and was offended by this lack of faith in his abilities. However, when Snape discovered that he had been used as a pawn in <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a>'s own destruction, he was horrified, seeing it as a calculated betrayal of Lily's memory.
</p><p>Dumbledore clearly underestimated Snape's capacity for <a href="/wiki/Love" title="Love">love</a>, and years later was very surprised to learn that Snape still maintained his devotion. Furthermore, he complimented Snape's bravery, stating he was far braver than Igor Karkaroff and that sometimes they sorted too soon, leaving Snape dumbstruck. But in contrast to this, Dumbledore overestimated Snape´s feelings to get over "old grudges" and therefore assigned him to tutor Harry in Occlumency, which ended badly between the two parties. 
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>I am fortunate, extremely fortunate, that I have you, Severus.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Dumbledore's gratitude towards Snape<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/1996" title="1996">1996</a>, Dumbledore was cursed by putting on <a href="/wiki/Marvolo_Gaunt%27s_Ring" title="Marvolo Gaunt&#39;s Ring">Marvolo Gaunt's Ring</a>, which was a <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcrux</a> (he put it on when he was distracted by finding out that it was the Resurrection Stone, hoping to talk to his dead family). He managed to contact Severus who was able to contain the <a href="/wiki/Curse" title="Curse">curse</a> in his right hand. However, Snape knew and told Dumbledore that the curse would get stronger and stronger and eventually kill him painfully, giving him a prognosis of about a year. By this time, Dumbledore was aware of Voldemort's plan to kill him through assigning <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a> by threatening to kill his parents. Knowing that he was going to die in a year and to save Draco Malfoy's safety and his soul, he ordered Snape to give him a quick and painless death when the time came. Snape, although resistant at first to killing Dumbledore, carried it out at the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a>, when Draco Malfoy had managed to bring <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> into Hogwarts. Dumbledore also entrusted Snape with protecting the students once Hogwarts fell into Voldemort's control.
</p><p>It is notable that despite trusting Snape had reformed, Dumbledore never allowed him his coveted position of professor of <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a>, ostensibly under the concern that it would cause him to revert to "old habits". However, it is more likely that he did it out of a desire to protect Snape from the <a href="/wiki/Jinx" title="Jinx">jinx</a> he believed Lord Voldemort had put on the job after failing to acquire the position himself. This same jinx prevented any teacher from lasting more than twelve months at the post, sometimes with fatal results. After being cursed by Marvolo Gaunt's ring and ordering Snape to kill him, Dumbledore finally granted him the Defence Against the Dark Arts post, knowing that if Snape were to kill him he would be vilified by the wizarding public and forced to abandon the post.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Elphias_Doge">Elphias Doge</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=71" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Elphias Doge">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=71" title="Edit section: Elphias Doge"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>Thought the sun shone out of my brother's every orifice, he did.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Aberforth Dumbledore on Elphias Doge<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4e/Elphias_Doge_2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110610163841" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="245" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Elphias Doge 2.jpg" data-image-key="Elphias_Doge_2.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4e/Elphias_Doge_2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20110610163841" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4e/Elphias_Doge_2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110610163841" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4e/Elphias_Doge_2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20110610163841" decoding="async" width="180" height="245" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Elphias Doge 2.jpg" data-image-key="Elphias_Doge_2.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4e/Elphias_Doge_2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20110610163841" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Elphias_Doge_2.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Elphias_Doge" title="Elphias Doge">Elphias Doge</a>, his friend for many years</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Elphias Doge became a close friend of Dumbledore's during their first day at Hogwarts. Elphias suffered from <a href="/wiki/Dragon_Pox" title="Dragon Pox">Dragon Pox</a>, and everybody avoided him. Elphias thought Dumbledore was a very great <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">wizard</a>, and a very great person, and believed that his many early losses endowed him with great humanity and strong sympathy, as he stated in an obituary he wrote for Albus Dumbledore, after his <a href="/wiki/Death" title="Death">death</a>.
</p><p>Elphias pitied Dumbledore about his <a href="/wiki/Percival_Dumbledore" title="Percival Dumbledore">father</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kendra_Dumbledore" title="Kendra Dumbledore">mother</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Ariana_Dumbledore" title="Ariana Dumbledore">sister</a>, and had a highly opinion of him. Elphias soon became a member of the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a>, an organisation that Dumbledore had led. He also attended Albus Dumbledore's funeral.
</p><p>Elphias also told Harry to never believe <a href="/wiki/Rita_Skeeter" title="Rita Skeeter">Rita Skeeter</a> and <a href="/wiki/Muriel" title="Muriel">Muriel</a>'s slanders about Albus Dumbledore's family life, including that Ariana was a <a href="/wiki/Squib" title="Squib">Squib</a>. It is possible that Elphias Doge fought in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Ron_Weasley_and_Hermione_Granger">Ron Weasley and Hermione Granger</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=72" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Ron Weasley and Hermione Granger">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=72" title="Edit section: Ron Weasley and Hermione Granger"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">"<i>Headmaster, you've got to stop them. They've got the wrong man.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Hermione Granger and Ron Weasley regarding <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/17/The-trio-Harry-Potter-and-the-chamber-of-secrets-potterhead-29266030-365-400.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20191008170323" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:The-trio-Harry-Potter-and-the-chamber-of-secrets-potterhead-29266030-365-400.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" <p>Ron Weasley and Hermione Granger were <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>'s best friends and, like Harry, they thought Dumbledore was a great <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">wizard</a>. Dumbledore liked them too, despite that he wasn't as close to them as he was to Harry. 
</p><p>After his <a href="/wiki/Death" title="Death">death</a>, he left Ron his <a href="/wiki/Deluminator" title="Deluminator">Deluminator</a> (a unique artefact created by Dumbledore himself) and Hermione his copy of <i><a href="/wiki/The_Tales_of_Beedle_the_Bard" title="The Tales of Beedle the Bard">The Tales of Beedle the Bard </a></i>. These gifts were proven very useful, as Ron abandoned Harry and Hermione formerly to find his family, and, when he wanted to come back to Harry and Hermione, the Deluminator showed him the way. The trio also read the <i>Tales of Beedle the Bard</i>, and learned about the <a href="/wiki/Deathly_Hallows" title="Deathly Hallows">Deathly Hallows</a>. Harry, Ron and Hermione also visited Dumbledore's <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore%27s_portrait" title="Albus Dumbledore&#39;s portrait">portrait</a>, after the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Weasley_family">Weasley family</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=73" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Weasley family">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=73" title="Edit section: Weasley family"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/Weasley_family.png/revision/latest?cb=20200417054614" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="145" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Weasley family.png" data-image-key="Weasley_family.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/Weasley_family.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200417054614" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/Weasley_family.png/revision/latest?cb=20200417054614" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/Weasley_family.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200417054614" decoding="async" width="250" height="145" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Weasley family.png" data-image-key="Weasley_family.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/Weasley_family.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200417054614" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Weasley_family.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The <a href="/wiki/Weasley_family" title="Weasley family">Weasley family</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Apart from Ron, Dumbledore was respected greatly by the rest of the Weasley family. They considered him as the greatest wizard of all time and supported him through everything (except Percy who disbelieved him about Voldemort's return) and was even the Hogwarts Headmaster during the times in which all the Weasleys attended Hogwarts.
</p><p>Arthur and Molly Weasley always respected Dumbledore and were very loyal to him. Arthur, like Dumbledore, believed in the equality of all witches, wizards and Muggles while Molly considered him a great wizard who doesn't make mistakes. When the Ministry of Magic began to disbelieve Dumbledore and Harry, they supported the two famous wizards rather than the Ministry and became members of the second Order of the Phoenix.
</p><p>Dumbledore's relationship with Bill happened to be a friendly one since they were both Gryffindors and liked each other. It is very likely that he also had a good relationship with Charlie.
</p><p>Percy also thought of Dumbledore as a great wizard, but sometimes odd. In <a href="/wiki/1995" title="1995">1995</a>, Percy's relationship with Dumbledore became antagonistic when he and Harry claimed that Voldemort had returned, Percy was loyal to the Ministry and participated in discrediting Harry and Dumbledore altogether. When the truth was revealed, Percy learned he had made a mistake and in 1997, attended Dumbledore's funeral.
</p><p>Fred and George appeared to respect Dumbledore very much. Dumbledore also appeared to like the twins, despite their mischief-making, but knew they were good people at heart. They even joined the second Order of the Phoenix and even <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a>.
</p><p>Ginny Weasley admired Dumbledore a lot and became his student in 1992. Dumbledore comforted and reassured Ginny after she was possessed by a fragment of Voldemort's soul and manipulated into opening the Chamber of Secrets during the 1992–1993 school year. Ginny was one of the first people to learn about Dumbledore's death, and the only one able to console Harry afterwards. Ginny also named her younger son, Albus Severus Potter after Dumbledore.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="James_and_Lily_Potter">James and Lily Potter</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=74" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: James and Lily Potter">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=74" title="Edit section: James and Lily Potter"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>James had showed it to me just few days previously. It explained much of his undetected wrongdoing at school</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Albus Dumbledore to Harry Potter<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 202px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/81/Lily_and_James_Potter.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20090727171514" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="200" height="150" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Lily and James Potter.jpg" data-image-key="Lily_and_James_Potter.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/81/Lily_and_James_Potter.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20090727171514" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/81/Lily_and_James_Potter.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20090727171514" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/81/Lily_and_James_Potter.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20090727171514" decoding="async" width="200" height="150" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Lily and James Potter.jpg" data-image-key="Lily_and_James_Potter.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/81/Lily_and_James_Potter.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20090727171514" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Lily_and_James_Potter.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/James_Potter_I" title="James Potter I">James</a> and <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily Potter</a>, his friends and former students</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Dumbledore first met James Potter and Lily Evans during their first year at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>, where he was the Headmaster. Dumbledore had a good relationship with both of them, knowing them both to be pure souls. James had lent Dumbledore his <a href="/wiki/Cloak_of_Invisibility" title="Cloak of Invisibility">Invisibility Cloak</a> one of the three <a href="/wiki/Deathly_Hallows" title="Deathly Hallows">Deathly Hallows</a>. After James's <a href="/wiki/Death" title="Death">death</a> Dumbledore returned the cloak to James's son, <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a>.
</p><p>When the Potters became Voldemort's targets due to a prophecy made about their son and the Dark Lord, Dumbledore attempted to protect them by casting the <a href="/wiki/Fidelius_Charm" title="Fidelius Charm">Fidelius Charm</a> and offering to be their Secret Keeper, but the role of <a href="/wiki/Secret_Keeper" title="Secret Keeper">Secret Keeper</a> went instead to <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Peter Pettigrew</a>, which turned out to be a fatal mistake, as Peter turned out to be a spy, and he betrayed Lily and James to Voldemort, who killed them. Dumbledore was very saddened by their deaths and dedicated the rest of his life to protecting their son, Harry without giving him any happiness in his childhood. He often told Harry about the great goodness of his parents, and repeatedly consoled him with the assurance that his parents would never ever truly leave him because of their love for him. Dumbledore also believed that Harry's love for his parents was his greatest power.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Dursley_family">Dursley family</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=75" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Dursley family">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=75" title="Edit section: Dursley family"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>Remember my last, Petunia</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Albus Dumbledore's Howler to Petunia Dursley, reminding her of the protection that she gave Harry<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/72/Dursley_Family.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170310050024" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="184" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dursley Family.jpg" data-image-key="Dursley_Family.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/72/Dursley_Family.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170310050024" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/72/Dursley_Family.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170310050024" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/72/Dursley_Family.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170310050024" decoding="async" width="250" height="184" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dursley Family.jpg" data-image-key="Dursley_Family.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/72/Dursley_Family.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170310050024" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dursley_Family.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The Dursleys, whom he entrusted Harry Potter to</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Dumbledore had been known to have at least some correspondence with the Dursley family before the birth of <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">their nephew</a>. In <a href="/wiki/1971" title="1971">1971</a>, <a href="/wiki/Petunia_Dursley" title="Petunia Dursley">Petunia Evans</a> wrote a letter to Dumbledore asking if she could attend <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a> along with <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">her sister</a>. Dumbledore kindly rejected her request due to her being a <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggle</a>, which had likely contributed to Petunia's already growing hatred of magic. Ten years later, Dumbledore illegally dropped Petunia's <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">nephew</a> at her doorstep shortly after the <a href="/wiki/Attack_at_Godric%27s_Hollow_(1981)" title="Attack at Godric&#39;s Hollow (1981)">murders</a> of <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">her sister</a> and <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_I" title="James Potter I">brother-in-law</a>, despite the fact they were not named guardian candidates of Harry in the events of James and Lily's death. Dumbledore had hoped that doing so would ensure an <a href="/wiki/Sacrificial_protection" title="Sacrificial protection">ancient form of magic</a> that Lily's wilful loving sacrifice for her son had created. However, Petunia and her <a href="/wiki/Vernon_Dursley" title="Vernon Dursley">own husband</a> both resented Harry's presence for the next ten years.
</p><p>After Harry had received his letter from <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Rubeus Hagrid</a>, Vernon had denounced Dumbledore as a "<i>crackpot old fool</i>" and refused to pay for Harry's school funds. In response to this irreverent outburst, Hagrid gave a pig's tail to Vernon's son, <a href="/wiki/Dudley_Dursley" title="Dudley Dursley">Dudley Dursley</a>. In the summer of <a href="/wiki/1995" title="1995">1995</a>, Vernon was about to throw Harry out of the <a href="/wiki/4_Privet_Drive" title="4 Privet Drive">house</a> when Petunia received a <a href="/wiki/Howler" title="Howler">Howler</a> from Dumbledore simply stating "<i>Remember my last, Petunia</i>." Less than a year later, Harry and Dumbledore were talking about why the former had to stay at the Dursley house despite his miserable existence he endured there.
</p><p>A couple of months later, Dumbledore met with the Dursleys for the final time in his life. During his visit to their house, Dumbledore went over the protection that the Dursleys were affording Harry, Harry's inheritance of <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a>'s possessions, and current updates in the <a href="/wiki/Wizarding_world" title="Wizarding world">wizarding world</a>. In addition, Dumbledore chastised the Dursleys for their indulgence of their son, Dudley. Vernon and Petunia were likely indignant at Dumbledore's remarks.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Sirius_Black">Sirius Black</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=76" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Sirius Black">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=76" title="Edit section: Sirius Black"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i><a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius</a> was a brave, clever, and energetic man, and such men are not usually content to sit at home in hiding while they believe others to be in danger.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Albus Dumbledore's opinion of Sirius<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bc/OOTP_promo_front_closeup_Sirius_Black.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150918055024" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="269" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="OOTP promo front closeup Sirius Black.jpg" data-image-key="OOTP_promo_front_closeup_Sirius_Black.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bc/OOTP_promo_front_closeup_Sirius_Black.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150918055024" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bc/OOTP_promo_front_closeup_Sirius_Black.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150918055024" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bc/OOTP_promo_front_closeup_Sirius_Black.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150918055024" decoding="async" width="180" height="269" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="OOTP promo front closeup Sirius Black.jpg" data-image-key="OOTP_promo_front_closeup_Sirius_Black.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bc/OOTP_promo_front_closeup_Sirius_Black.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150918055024" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:OOTP_promo_front_closeup_Sirius_Black.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a>, his friend and former student</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Dumbledore had also a good relationship with Sirius Black, <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_I" title="James Potter I">James Potter</a>'s best friend and <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>'s godfather, as well as a member of the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a>, an organisation that Dumbledore led to oppose Voldemort and his followers. Like the rest of the wizarding world, Dumbledore initially believed that Sirius was the one who betrayed Lily and James to <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> (and helped to condemn him in Azkaban with unproven statements and lack of evidence about his supposed betrayal), but, in 1994, he learned that it was actually <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Peter Pettigrew</a>. As he had no way to prove Sirius' innocence, despite being Chief Warlock and having the power to give him a trial, Dumbledore compensated by helping Hermione and Harry save Sirius from the <a href="/wiki/Dementor%27s_Kiss" title="Dementor&#39;s Kiss">Dementor's Kiss</a>, and to escape from his Ministry captors, by means of a <a href="/wiki/Time-Turner" title="Time-Turner">Time-Turner</a> and <a href="/wiki/Buckbeak" title="Buckbeak">Buckbeak</a>.
</p><p>The two resumed their friendship, and Sirius helped Dumbledore to recall the Order of the Phoenix an hour after Voldemort returned. However, their relationship was soon strained: Dumbledore forced Sirius to stay at <a href="/wiki/12_Grimmauld_Place" title="12 Grimmauld Place">12 Grimmauld Place</a> on account of his being a wanted convict, and because he had a tendency to act rashly, which could lead him to put himself in great danger. Though his intentions were noble, Sirius could not bring himself to appreciate Dumbledore's thoughtfulness, as he utterly despised the home which brought him many bitter, unhappy memories, and the fact that he was to be alone in the house most of the time made it all the more intolerable. Nevertheless, he still trusted Dumbledore enough to confide in him about how Harry felt Voldemort awaking inside him the night that <a href="/wiki/Arthur_Weasley" title="Arthur Weasley">Mr Weasley</a> was attacked. Dumbledore was devastated when Sirius died, believing that it was mostly his fault and comforted Harry to the best of his ability, and expressed his belief that Sirius was a lively man of wit and courage, with a deep and genuine concern for his <a href="/wiki/Love" title="Love">loved</a> ones, and would not hesitate to come to their rescue even if it meant putting himself in danger. Sirius' death was also a factor that led to Dumbledore confessing to Harry several things that had been kept secret from him, mainly about the true power of his mother's sacrificial protection, and <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney%27s_first_prophecy" title="Sybill Trelawney&#39;s first prophecy">the prophecy</a> about him and Voldemort.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Remus_Lupin">Remus Lupin</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=77" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Remus Lupin">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=77" title="Edit section: Remus Lupin"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">"<i>On a happier note, I am pleased to welcome two new teachers to our ranks <a href="/wiki/1993%E2%80%931994_school_year" title="1993–1994 school year">this year</a>. Firstly, <a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin" title="Remus Lupin">Professor Lupin</a> who had kindly consented to fill the post of <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> teacher</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Albus Dumbledore introducing Remus<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e2/Remus_Lupin_Deathly_Hallows_promo_image.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161119235913" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="240" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Remus Lupin Deathly Hallows promo image.jpg" data-image-key="Remus_Lupin_Deathly_Hallows_promo_image.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e2/Remus_Lupin_Deathly_Hallows_promo_image.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161119235913" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e2/Remus_Lupin_Deathly_Hallows_promo_image.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161119235913" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e2/Remus_Lupin_Deathly_Hallows_promo_image.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161119235913" decoding="async" width="180" height="240" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Remus Lupin Deathly Hallows promo image.jpg" data-image-key="Remus_Lupin_Deathly_Hallows_promo_image.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e2/Remus_Lupin_Deathly_Hallows_promo_image.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161119235913" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Remus_Lupin_Deathly_Hallows_promo_image.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin" title="Remus Lupin">Remus Lupin</a>: his friend, former student, and former colleague</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Another good friend of Dumbledore was Remus Lupin, one of <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_I" title="James Potter I">James</a>'s and <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius</a>'s dearest friends, and a <a href="/wiki/Werewolf" title="Werewolf">werewolf</a>. It was Dumbledore who, by several special precautions, ensured that Remus was able to come to Hogwarts to receive a proper magical education despite his werewolf status. He became a member of the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> after his graduation. Later on, in <a href="/wiki/1993" title="1993">1993</a>, Dumbledore gave him the post of teaching <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a>, a decision some considered questionable.
