He even helped Remus control his werewolf-side by having Snape brew the <a href="/wiki/Wolfsbane_Potion" title="Wolfsbane Potion">Wolfsbane Potion</a> for him on a regular basis. On his part, Remus confessed that Dumbledore's trust and exceptional kindness towards him meant everything to him, given that the vast majority of the wizarding world shunned him because of the deep prejudice towards werewolves, and Remus felt guilty for betraying this kindness by allowing his three Marauder friends illegally become Animagi and roaming wild during their schooling years. Despite this, after learning of Sirius's innocence, Dumbledore forgave Remus for his supposed betrayal, understanding his Marauder friends only became Animagi to help Remus in his werewolf form and considered it an extraordinary achievement. He rejoined the Order of the Phoenix when Dumbledore re-instated it in <a href="/wiki/1995" title="1995">1995</a>, and they both fought in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a>, where Remus suffered a devastating loss: Sirius died in the hands of <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a>. Later on, upon overhearing a conversation about Harry's misgivings of Snape, he told Harry that to doubt Snape would be to doubt Dumbledore. In 1997, Remus was devastated by Dumbledore's <a href="/wiki/Death" title="Death">death</a> after the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a>, and later demonstrated his faith and loyalty to Dumbledore by fighting in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Alastor_Moody">Alastor Moody</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=78" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Alastor Moody">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=78" title="Edit section: Alastor Moody"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">"<i>That is not Alastor Moody. You have never known Alastor Moody. The real Alastor would never remove <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">you</a> from my side, after <a href="/wiki/Duel_in_Little_Hangleton" title="Duel in Little Hangleton">what had happened</a>...</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Dumbledore, talking about <a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">Barty Crouch Jnr</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a1/Alastor_Moody_Profile.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20081103144159" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="280" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Alastor Moody Profile.jpg" data-image-key="Alastor_Moody_Profile.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a1/Alastor_Moody_Profile.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20081103144159" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a1/Alastor_Moody_Profile.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20081103144159" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a1/Alastor_Moody_Profile.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20081103144159" decoding="async" width="180" height="280" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Alastor Moody Profile.jpg" data-image-key="Alastor_Moody_Profile.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a1/Alastor_Moody_Profile.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20081103144159" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Alastor_Moody_Profile.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">Alastor Moody</a>, his friend</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure> 
<p><a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">Alastor Moody</a> was a prominent <a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">Auror</a> and Dumbledore's close friend. They fought together in many battles, and the intimacy of their friendship can be demonstrated by an instance where the usually formidable, no-nonsense Moody actually teased Dumbledore for his hatred of the <a href="/wiki/Dementor" title="Dementor">Dementors</a>. In <a href="/wiki/1994" title="1994">1994</a>, Moody accepted Dumbledore's offer to teach <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a>, but was captured and imprisoned by <a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">Barty Crouch Jnr</a>, who impersonated him during the 1994-1995 school year, in order to send <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> to <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>.
</p><p>Dumbledore and Moody fought along in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a>, where they suffered a devastating loss: <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius</a>, one of their dear friends, was killed by <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a>. Moody turned out to be the next member of the Order to die after Dumbledore.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Fawkes">Fawkes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=79" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Fawkes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=79" title="Edit section: Fawkes"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f8/Fawkes_WB_F2_FawkesCloseUpIllustration_Illust_100615_Port.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20151218225509" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="243" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Fawkes WB F2 FawkesCloseUpIllustration Illust 100615 Port.jpg" data-image-key="Fawkes_WB_F2_FawkesCloseUpIllustration_Illust_100615_Port.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f8/Fawkes_WB_F2_FawkesCloseUpIllustration_Illust_100615_Port.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20151218225509" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f8/Fawkes_WB_F2_FawkesCloseUpIllustration_Illust_100615_Port.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20151218225509" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f8/Fawkes_WB_F2_FawkesCloseUpIllustration_Illust_100615_Port.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20151218225509" decoding="async" width="180" height="243" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Fawkes WB F2 FawkesCloseUpIllustration Illust 100615 Port.jpg" data-image-key="Fawkes_WB_F2_FawkesCloseUpIllustration_Illust_100615_Port.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f8/Fawkes_WB_F2_FawkesCloseUpIllustration_Illust_100615_Port.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20151218225509" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Fawkes_WB_F2_FawkesCloseUpIllustration_Illust_100615_Port.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Fawkes, his loyal pet Phoenix</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets"><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>Professor. Your bird — I couldn’t do anything — he just caught fire</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Albus Dumbledore</b>: "<i>About time, too. He’s been looking dreadful for days; I’ve been telling him to get a move on.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Dumbledore regarding Fawkes to Harry Potter<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<p>Albus Dumbledore had a very strong bond with <a href="/wiki/Fawkes" title="Fawkes">Fawkes</a>, his pet <a href="/wiki/Phoenix" title="Phoenix">phoenix</a>, who served as a messenger and close companion. Dumbledore always looked after Fawkes when he was reborn after his countless deaths and in return Fawkes was extremely loyal to him. Fawkes was willing to take a Killing Curse in order to protect Dumbledore, and did so in order to defend him from Lord Voldemort. He also helped Albus escape from several members of the Ministry of Magic when they tried to arrest him. When Dumbledore died Fawkes mourned him by singing a lament and then left Hogwarts and was apparently never seen again.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Order_of_the_Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=80" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Order of the Phoenix">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=80" title="Edit section: Order of the Phoenix"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince"><b>Draco Malfoy</b>: "<i>I was supposed to meet you here, but your phoenix lot got in the way!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Dumbledore</b>: "<i>Yes, they do that.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco</a> to Dumbledore during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d0/Order_of_the_Phoenix_%E2%80%93_first_generation.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150206155602" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="102" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Order of the Phoenix – first generation.jpg" data-image-key="Order_of_the_Phoenix_–_first_generation.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d0/Order_of_the_Phoenix_%E2%80%93_first_generation.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150206155602" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d0/Order_of_the_Phoenix_%E2%80%93_first_generation.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150206155602" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d0/Order_of_the_Phoenix_%E2%80%93_first_generation.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150206155602" decoding="async" width="250" height="102" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Order of the Phoenix – first generation.jpg" data-image-key="Order_of_the_Phoenix_–_first_generation.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d0/Order_of_the_Phoenix_%E2%80%93_first_generation.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150206155602" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Order_of_the_Phoenix_%E2%80%93_first_generation.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The original <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a>, his allies</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The Order of the Phoenix was an organisation Dumbledore formed to oppose Voldemort and his forces. He had good relationships with most of the members, such as his brother <a href="/wiki/Aberforth_Dumbledore" title="Aberforth Dumbledore">Aberforth</a>, <a href="/wiki/Elphias_Doge" title="Elphias Doge">Elphias Doge</a>, <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Rubeus Hagrid</a>, <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>, <a href="/wiki/James_and_Lily_Potter" title="James and Lily Potter">James and Lily Potter</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a>, <a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin" title="Remus Lupin">Remus Lupin</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">Alastor Moody</a>.
</p><p>He was also friends with <a href="/wiki/Kingsley_Shacklebolt" title="Kingsley Shacklebolt">Kingsley Shacklebolt</a>, who believed in equality and fairness for all <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">wizards and witches</a> and <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggles</a>; <a href="/wiki/Arabella_Figg" title="Arabella Figg">Arabella Figg</a>, whom he trusted to watch Harry Potter during his years at the Dursley's house (and heard about the abuse Harry suffered while doing nothing); <a href="/wiki/Nymphadora_Tonks" title="Nymphadora Tonks">Nymphadora Tonks</a>, an Auror; <a href="/wiki/Dedalus_Diggle" title="Dedalus Diggle">Dedalus Diggle</a>; <a href="/wiki/Hestia_Jones" title="Hestia Jones">Hestia Jones</a>; <a href="/wiki/Emmeline_Vance" title="Emmeline Vance">Emmeline Vance</a>; <a href="/wiki/Sturgis_Podmore" title="Sturgis Podmore">Sturgis Podmore</a>; <a href="/wiki/Mundungus_Fletcher" title="Mundungus Fletcher">Mundungus Fletcher</a>; and the <a href="/wiki/Weasley_family" title="Weasley family">Weasley family</a>. Emmeline Vance was killed by <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> during the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a>.
</p><p>Other possible Dumbledore's friends who were killed or seriously injured during the <a href="/wiki/First_Wizarding_War" title="First Wizarding War">First Wizarding War</a> were <a href="/wiki/Edgar_Bones" title="Edgar Bones">Edgar Bones</a>, <a href="/wiki/Caradoc_Dearborn" title="Caradoc Dearborn">Caradoc Dearborn</a>, <a href="/wiki/Benjy_Fenwick" title="Benjy Fenwick">Benjy Fenwick</a>, <a href="/wiki/Marlene_McKinnon" title="Marlene McKinnon">Marlene McKinnon</a>, <a href="/wiki/Dorcas_Meadowes" title="Dorcas Meadowes">Dorcas Meadowes</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Fabian_Prewett" title="Fabian Prewett">Fabian</a> and <a href="/wiki/Gideon_Prewett" title="Gideon Prewett">Gideon Prewett</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Alice_Longbottom" title="Alice Longbottom">Alice</a> and <a href="/wiki/Frank_Longbottom" title="Frank Longbottom">Frank Longbottom</a>, who were tortured into insanity by <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a> and <a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">Barty Crouch Jnr</a>
</p><p>Dumbledore was also friend of many allies of the Order, including <a href="/wiki/Olympe_Maxime" title="Olympe Maxime">Olympe Maxime</a>, the headmistress of <a href="/wiki/Beauxbatons_Academy_of_Magic" title="Beauxbatons Academy of Magic">Beauxbatons Academy of Magic</a>, whom he met during the <a href="/wiki/Triwizard_Tournament" title="Triwizard Tournament">Triwizard Tournament</a>, his co-workers <a href="/wiki/Filius_Flitwick" title="Filius Flitwick">Filius Flitwick</a>, <a href="/wiki/Pomona_Sprout" title="Pomona Sprout">Pomona Sprout</a> and <a href="/wiki/Horace_Slughorn" title="Horace Slughorn">Horace Slughorn</a>, <a href="/wiki/Augusta_Longbottom" title="Augusta Longbottom">Augusta Longbottom</a>, <a href="/wiki/Edward_Tonks" title="Edward Tonks">Ted</a> and <a href="/wiki/Andromeda_Tonks" title="Andromeda Tonks">Andromeda Tonks</a>. Other allies of the Order were Dumbledore's students, <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny Weasley</a>, <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a>, <a href="/wiki/Luna_Lovegood" title="Luna Lovegood">Luna Lovegood</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lee_Jordan" title="Lee Jordan">Lee Jordan</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Percy_Weasley" title="Percy Weasley">Percy Weasley</a>. He also liked the <a href="/wiki/House-elf" title="House-elf">house-elf</a> <a href="/wiki/Dobby" title="Dobby">Dobby</a>, and pitied the house-elf <a href="/wiki/Kreacher" title="Kreacher">Kreacher</a>, asking them to work at Hogwarts kitchens.
</p><p>It is possible that all the members and allies of the Order who were neither killed nor imprisoned, fought in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a> (except Arabella Figg, who was a <a href="/wiki/Squib" title="Squib">Squib</a>, and couldn't fight. However, she might have helped in another way.)
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Hogwarts_staff">Hogwarts staff</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=81" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Hogwarts staff">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=81" title="Edit section: Hogwarts staff"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8e/MM_AD_AS.png/revision/latest?cb=20110715192105" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="115" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="MM AD AS.png" data-image-key="MM_AD_AS.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8e/MM_AD_AS.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20110715192105" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8e/MM_AD_AS.png/revision/latest?cb=20110715192105" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8e/MM_AD_AS.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20110715192105" decoding="async" width="250" height="115" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="MM AD AS.png" data-image-key="MM_AD_AS.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8e/MM_AD_AS.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20110715192105" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:MM_AD_AS.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore in-between <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Professors McGonagall</a> and <a href="/wiki/Aurora_Sinistra" title="Aurora Sinistra">Sinistra</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Except the already mentioned Minerva McGonagall, <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Rubeus Hagrid</a>, <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>, <a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin" title="Remus Lupin">Remus Lupin</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">Alastor Moody</a>, Dumbledore had many co-workers during his career at Hogwarts. Some of his earliest co-workers were: <a href="/wiki/Armando_Dippet" title="Armando Dippet">Armando Dippet</a>, the previous Headmaster, Dumbledore being notably among the very few Dippet trusted apparently due to his teaching efficiency; <a href="/wiki/Herbert_Beery" title="Herbert Beery">Herbert Beery</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Herbology" title="Herbology">Herbology</a> Professor, who later resigned his teaching post at Hogwarts to go teaching at the <a href="/wiki/Wizarding_Academy_of_Dramatic_Arts" title="Wizarding Academy of Dramatic Arts">Wizarding Academy of Dramatic Arts</a>, who Dumbledore was apparently on good terms with as despite Herbert being such an enthusiast, he trusted Dumbledore enough to confide in him the personal fact that his first act made all his other performances ruined; <a href="/wiki/Galatea_Merrythought" title="Galatea Merrythought">Galatea Merrythought</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> Professor, who retired before Dippet's death; <a href="/wiki/Silvanus_Kettleburn" title="Silvanus Kettleburn">Silvanus Kettleburn</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Care_of_Magical_Creatures" title="Care of Magical Creatures">Care of Magical Creatures</a> Professor; and <a href="/wiki/Horace_Slughorn" title="Horace Slughorn">Horace Slughorn</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Potions_(class)" title="Potions (class)">Potions master</a>, who was hired twice, and gave Harry Potter his memory, helping him and Dumbledore find and destroy Voldemort's Horcruxes.
</p><p>After Dippet's death, he became the new <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a> headmaster. He also had a friendship with <a href="/wiki/Filius_Flitwick" title="Filius Flitwick">Filius Flitwick</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Charms_(class)" title="Charms (class)">Charms</a> Professor and <a href="/wiki/Head_of_Ravenclaw_House" title="Head of Ravenclaw House">Head of Ravenclaw House</a>, <a href="/wiki/Pomona_Sprout" title="Pomona Sprout">Pomona Sprout</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Herbology" title="Herbology">Herbology</a> Professor and <a href="/wiki/Head_of_Hufflepuff_House" title="Head of Hufflepuff House">Head of Hufflepuff House</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Poppy_Pomfrey" title="Poppy Pomfrey">Poppy Pomfrey</a>, the nurse.
</p><p>Every Hogwarts staff member, with the exception of <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a>, both respected and held a high opinion of Dumbledore. Other staff were <a href="/wiki/Argus_Filch" title="Argus Filch">Argus Filch</a>, the caretaker; <a href="/wiki/Wilhelmina_Grubbly-Plank" title="Wilhelmina Grubbly-Plank">Wilhelmina Grubbly-Plank</a>, the Care of Magical Creatures Substitute Professor; <a href="/wiki/Firenze" title="Firenze">Firenze</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Centaur" title="Centaur">centaur</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Divination" title="Divination">Divination</a> Professor; <a href="/wiki/Rolanda_Hooch" title="Rolanda Hooch">Rolanda Hooch</a>, the Flying Instructor; Aurora Sinistra, the <a href="/wiki/Astronomy_(class)" title="Astronomy (class)">Astronomy</a> Professor; <a href="/wiki/Bathsheda_Babbling" title="Bathsheda Babbling">Bathsheda Babbling</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Study_of_Ancient_Runes" title="Study of Ancient Runes">Study of Ancient Runes</a> Professor; <a href="/wiki/Septima_Vector" title="Septima Vector">Septima Vector</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Arithmancy" title="Arithmancy">Arithmancy</a> Professor; <a href="/wiki/Irma_Pince" title="Irma Pince">Irma Pince</a>, the librarian; <a href="/wiki/Cuthbert_Binns" title="Cuthbert Binns">Cuthbert Binns</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Ghost" title="Ghost">ghost</a> and the <a href="/wiki/History_of_Magic" title="History of Magic">History of Magic</a> Professor; <a href="/wiki/Charity_Burbage" title="Charity Burbage">Charity Burbage</a> the <a href="/wiki/Muggle_Studies" title="Muggle Studies">Muggle Studies</a> Professor. 
</p><p>Dumbledore knew <a href="/wiki/Gilderoy_Lockhart" title="Gilderoy Lockhart">Gilderoy Lockhart</a>, the Defence Against the Dark Arts Professor (<a href="/wiki/1992%E2%80%931993_school_year" title="1992–1993 school year">1992-1993</a>), when he was still a student. It's unknown how Dumbledore viewed him but he apparently found Lockhart's antics to be amusing instead of irritating rather than the other professors, as he kindly denied Lockhart's proposal of starting a school newspaper rather than punishing him as many, if not all, of the other staff members have been known to do out of dislike of Lockhart's vanity seeking. Due to his optimistic personality and tendency to see the good in people in order to try to give them another chances, it can be assumed that he may have once thought that Lockhart can overcome his love for vanity and become a great wizard due to his talents. However, upon Lockhart modifying the memories of two wizards that Dumbledore knew, Dumbledore, having never been fooled by Lockhart's tall tales, easily found out the truth and immediately decided to appoint him as a Hogwarts professor to expose Lockhart's fraudulence, and because Lockhart at the time was the only person willing to apply for the cursed Defence against the Dark Arts post. Despite Dumbledore's evident dislike of Lockhart's deeds, he nevertheless did not seem to truly hate Lockhart, as he was cordial and polite to him whenever they interacted and after the Memory Charm completely wiped out Lockhart's memories, Dumbledore was compassionate enough that he decided to leave Lockhart in peace and did not expose his crimes, likely as he pitied Lockhart and saw that having completely lost all of his popularity and with the remnants of his magical brilliance now lost to him and his cunning now harmless, to condemn him to being eternally despised by the wizarding community would be unnecessarily cruel, not to say that if he did reveal what Lockhart had did, he would likely be either sentenced to Azkaban or heavily secured in St Mungo, both fates that he seemingly deemed too cruel of a punishment for what Lockhart did.
</p><p>Another Professor was <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney" title="Sybill Trelawney">Sybill Trelawney</a>, who taught Divination. Dumbledore planned on discontinuing Divination but went to her job interview out of politeness, by the end of the interview however, he has summed her up as a fraud. When he heard her conceiving <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney%27s_first_prophecy" title="Sybill Trelawney&#39;s first prophecy">Sybill Trelawney's first prophecy</a>, he hired Trelawney to protect her from the <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>. In 1995, when <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a> sacked Trelawney and tried to banish her from Hogwarts, it was Dumbledore who stepped in and told Umbridge he wished that Trelawney remain at Hogwarts.
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Quirinus_Quirrell" title="Quirinus Quirrell">Quirinus Quirrell</a> was the Muggle Studies Professor, before he started to teach Defence Against the Dark Arts. It was unknown of Dumbledore's feelings towards him at the time but he likely saw Quirrell as being a gifted wizard from his academical performances during his time as a student, considering that he had been the Headmaster by the time Quirrell came to Hogwarts and appointed him in first Muggle Studies before having him teach Defence Against the Dark Arts. It was unknown how he felt about Quirrell's delicateness or if he knew of Quirrell's bitterness over his bullying making him desire to be noticed, but it was likely that although he was concerned about it, ever the optimist, he had hoped that Quirrell could overcome this with time. However, when Quirrell met Voldemort when he travelled around the world, and shared his body with him and since then, he served him faithfully, trying to steal the <a href="/wiki/Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Philosopher&#39;s Stone">Philosopher's Stone</a> and kill Harry Potter, Dumbledore quickly saw through Quirrell and after he was killed by Harry Potter in 1992, being burned by Harry's touching, Dumbledore openly noted that Quirrell's fate was well-deserved, noting on how Quirrell's hunger for power, hatred and ambitions made him allow Voldemort to possess him and incapable of understanding love, fell victim to it, showing his disgust at his former professor.
</p><p>In 1995, <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a> was appointed the Defence Against the Dark Arts Professor by the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a>. She was a sadistic woman who enjoyed punishing students. Umbridge became High Inquisitor of Hogwarts, and later Headmistress. In the end of the year, she was chased by centaurs, and left Hogwarts.
</p><p>Every member of the Hogwarts staff was devastated by Dumbledore's <a href="/wiki/Death" title="Death">death</a>, and it is more than likely that every member fought in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>.
</p>
<h3><span id="Dumbledore's_Army"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Dumbledore.27s_Army">Dumbledore's Army</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=82" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Dumbledore&#039;s Army">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=82" title="Edit section: Dumbledore&#039;s Army"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix"><b>Albus Dumbledore</b>: "<i>Well, the game is up. Would you like a written confession from me, Cornelius — or will a statement before these witnesses suffice?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Cornelius Fudge</b>: "<i>Statement? What — I don't —?</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Albus Dumbledore</b>: "<i>Dumbledore's Army, Cornelius. Not Potter's Army. Dumbledore's Army</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Albus Dumbledore and Cornelius Fudge discussing Dumbledore's Army<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Dumbledore%27s_Army.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161123060553" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="166" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dumbledore&#39;s Army.jpg" data-image-key="Dumbledore&#39;s_Army.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Dumbledore%27s_Army.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161123060553" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Dumbledore%27s_Army.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161123060553" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Dumbledore%27s_Army.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161123060553" decoding="async" width="250" height="166" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dumbledore&#39;s Army.jpg" data-image-key="Dumbledore&#39;s_Army.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Dumbledore%27s_Army.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161123060553" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dumbledore%27s_Army.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Some members of Dumbledore's Army</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p><a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a> was an organisation formed and led by <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, in order to protect the students of Hogwarts from <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>.
</p><p>Its members were <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny Weasley</a>, <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a>, <a href="/wiki/Luna_Lovegood" title="Luna Lovegood">Luna Lovegood</a>, <a href="/wiki/Fred_and_George_Weasley" title="Fred and George Weasley">Fred and George Weasley</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cho_Chang" title="Cho Chang">Cho Chang</a>, <a href="/wiki/Dean_Thomas" title="Dean Thomas">Dean Thomas</a>, <a href="/wiki/Seamus_Finnigan" title="Seamus Finnigan">Seamus Finnigan</a>, <a href="/wiki/Padma_and_Parvati_Patil" title="Padma and Parvati Patil">Parvati and Padma Patil</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lavender_Brown" title="Lavender Brown">Lavender Brown</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hannah_Abbott" title="Hannah Abbott">Hannah Abbott</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ernest_Macmillan" title="Ernest Macmillan">Ernie Macmillan</a>, <a href="/wiki/Susan_Bones" title="Susan Bones">Susan Bones</a>, <a href="/wiki/Justin_Finch-Fletchley" title="Justin Finch-Fletchley">Justin Finch-Fletchley</a>, <a href="/wiki/Michael_Corner" title="Michael Corner">Michael Corner</a>, <a href="/wiki/Terry_Boot" title="Terry Boot">Terry Boot</a>, <a href="/wiki/Anthony_Goldstein" title="Anthony Goldstein">Anthony Goldstein</a>, <a href="/wiki/Katie_Bell" title="Katie Bell">Katie Bell</a>, <a href="/wiki/Alicia_Spinnet" title="Alicia Spinnet">Alicia Spinnet</a>, <a href="/wiki/Angelina_Johnson" title="Angelina Johnson">Angelina Johnson</a>, <a href="/wiki/Colin_and_Dennis_Creevey" title="Colin and Dennis Creevey">Colin and Dennis Creevey</a>, <a href="/wiki/Zacharias_Smith" title="Zacharias Smith">Zacharias Smith</a> and <a href="/wiki/Marietta_Edgecombe" title="Marietta Edgecombe">Marietta Edgecombe</a>.
</p><p>All of the members of Dumbledore's Army were devastated by Dumbledore's death, and it is possible that all of them fought in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>. Three of the members were killed: <a href="/wiki/Fred_Weasley" title="Fred Weasley">Fred Weasley</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lavender_Brown" title="Lavender Brown">Lavender Brown</a> and <a href="/wiki/Colin_Creevey" title="Colin Creevey">Colin Creevey</a>. The two defectors, <a href="/wiki/Marietta_Edgecombe" title="Marietta Edgecombe">Marietta Edgecombe</a> and <a href="/wiki/Zacharias_Smith" title="Zacharias Smith">Zacharias Smith</a>, are the ones who did not believe in Dumbledore from the beginning, and did not participate in the final battle.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Other_friendships">Other friendships</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=83" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Other friendships">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=83" title="Edit section: Other friendships"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>During his life, Dumbledore became friend of many famous wizards and witches, such as <a href="/wiki/Nicolas_Flamel" title="Nicolas Flamel">Nicolas Flamel</a> and his wife, <a href="/wiki/Perenelle_Flamel" title="Perenelle Flamel">Perenelle</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bathilda_Bagshot" title="Bathilda Bagshot">Bathilda Bagshot</a> and <a href="/wiki/Griselda_Marchbanks" title="Griselda Marchbanks">Griselda Marchbanks</a>. Nicolas Flamel and Perenelle were over 650 years of age, when they agreed to destroy the Philosopher's Stone to thwart <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>'s return. Bathilda Bagshot died a few months after Dumbledore, being killed by Voldemort.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Death_Eaters">Death Eaters</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=84" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Death Eaters">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=84" title="Edit section: Death Eaters"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bellatrix_Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=85" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Bellatrix Lestrange">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=85" title="Edit section: Bellatrix Lestrange"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>...or dear Bellatrix, who likes to play with her food before she eats it...</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Dumbledore regarding Bellatrix Lestrange's sadistic personality<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/Bella2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140623202746" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="270" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Bella2.jpg" data-image-key="Bella2.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/Bella2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140623202746" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/Bella2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140623202746" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/Bella2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140623202746" decoding="async" width="180" height="270" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Bella2.jpg" data-image-key="Bella2.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/Bella2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140623202746" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Bella2.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a>, his former student</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Bellatrix Lestrange was a <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a> who fought in both Wizarding Wars. She was fanatically loyal to Lord Voldemort who was her only true love and so, although reluctantly acknowledging Dumbledore as a very powerful wizard, considered her master as the superior wizard. Bellatrix was among the few people who knew of the <a href="/wiki/Plot_to_assassinate_Albus_Dumbledore" title="Plot to assassinate Albus Dumbledore">plan to assassinate Dumbledore</a>, and that <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a> had been assigned the task of murdering him. Bellatrix did not live to discover that her initial suspicions of Snape's loyalty had been correct, dying during a ferocious duel with <a href="/wiki/Molly_Weasley" title="Molly Weasley">Molly Weasley</a>. Dumbledore recognised Bellatrix as an incredibly dangerous and sadistic <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a>, commenting to <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a> that, given the choice, he would prefer to die a quick and clean death rather than fall prey to Bellatrix who tended to "play with her food". Bellatrix also killed many of Dumbledore's friends, such as <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a>, <a href="/wiki/Dobby" title="Dobby">Dobby</a> the <a href="/wiki/House-elf" title="House-elf">house-elf</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Nymphadora_Tonks" title="Nymphadora Tonks">Nymphadora Tonks</a>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Lucius_Malfoy">Lucius Malfoy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=86" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Lucius Malfoy">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=86" title="Edit section: Lucius Malfoy"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">"<i>On the other hand, I would advise you, Lucius, not to go giving out any more of Lord Voldemort’s old school things. If any more of them find their way into innocent hands, I think Arthur Weasley, for one, will make sure they are traced back to you...</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Albus Dumbledore dismissing Lucius Malfoy<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/54/Lucius_Malfoy_Profile.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190115061220" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="266" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Lucius Malfoy Profile.jpg" data-image-key="Lucius_Malfoy_Profile.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/54/Lucius_Malfoy_Profile.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190115061220" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/54/Lucius_Malfoy_Profile.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190115061220" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/54/Lucius_Malfoy_Profile.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190115061220" decoding="async" width="180" height="266" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Lucius Malfoy Profile.jpg" data-image-key="Lucius_Malfoy_Profile.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/54/Lucius_Malfoy_Profile.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190115061220" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Lucius_Malfoy_Profile.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy" title="Lucius Malfoy">Lucius Malfoy</a>, his former student</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p><a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy" title="Lucius Malfoy">Lucius Malfoy</a> was a prefect during Dumbledore's early years as Hogwarts Headmaster, and was among the Death Eaters who avoided Azkaban after <a href="/wiki/First_Wizarding_War" title="First Wizarding War">First Wizarding War</a>. In 1991, Lucius's son, <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco</a>, started attending Hogwarts. The Malfoys had a strong dislike of Dumbledore due to his love and acceptance of Muggle-borns and belief in Muggle rights. In 1992, Lucius manipulated <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny Weasley</a> into re-opening the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a> by giving her <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle%27s_Diary" class="mw-redirect" title="Tom Riddle&#39;s Diary">Tom Riddle's Diary</a> in order to stigmatise her father <a href="/wiki/Arthur_Weasley" title="Arthur Weasley">Arthur</a> and kick Dumbledore out of <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>. This failed because Dumbledore was able to guess the truth, when Harry Potter saved Ginny from the <a href="/wiki/Serpent_of_Slytherin" title="Serpent of Slytherin">Basilisk.</a> Dumbledore thus let Harry decide Lucius' punishment, which was giving the Malfoy <a href="/wiki/House-elf" title="House-elf">house-elf</a> <a href="/wiki/Dobby" title="Dobby">Dobby</a> his freedom as a reward and let Lucius himself get stripped from his position on the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Board_of_Governors" title="Hogwarts Board of Governors">Hogwarts Board of Governors</a>. In 1996, Dumbledore and Lucius fought in the Battle of the Department of Mysteries. Lucius was stunned and imprisoned in Azkaban, failing to give Voldemort the Prophecy about the Chosen one, so Voldemort became angry and made Draco a Death Eater and ordered him to kill Dumbledore, otherwise he would kill his family. During a discussion about Horcruxes, Dumbledore expressed to Harry a certain sympathy to Lucius, as he believed that Lucius was secretly glad to be imprison for accidentally getting rid of his master's Horcrux diary and the debacle of the prophecy retrieval. Draco attempted to kill Dumbledore, on Voldemort's orders, telling him that the Dark Lord would kill him, if he didn't so. Dumbledore showed kindness and sympathy to Draco's plight, sensing he wasn't capable of murder and suggested him to abandon Voldemort, and that he and his <a href="/wiki/Narcissa_Malfoy" title="Narcissa Malfoy">mother</a> would be hidden by the Order of the Phoenix. Draco would most likely have accepted, but was interrupted by Death Eaters. A year later, the Malfoy family changed sides.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Peter_Pettigrew">Peter Pettigrew</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=87" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Peter Pettigrew">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=87" title="Edit section: Peter Pettigrew"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">"<i>You saved his life, <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a>... <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">he</a> owes you a life-debt...</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Albus Dumbledore regarding Pettigrew<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7f/Wormtail_DH1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140602041920" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="267" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Wormtail DH1.jpg" data-image-key="Wormtail_DH1.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7f/Wormtail_DH1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140602041920" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7f/Wormtail_DH1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140602041920" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7f/Wormtail_DH1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140602041920" decoding="async" width="180" height="267" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Wormtail DH1.jpg" data-image-key="Wormtail_DH1.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7f/Wormtail_DH1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140602041920" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Wormtail_DH1.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Peter Pettigrew</a>, his former student</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p><a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Peter Pettigrew</a> was a member of the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> and another close friend of James Potter. It is possible that he was a friend of Dumbledore. However, in 1981, Pettigrew betrayed <a href="/wiki/James_and_Lily_Potter" title="James and Lily Potter">James and Lily</a> to <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a> in his role as their family <a href="/wiki/Secret-Keeper" class="mw-redirect" title="Secret-Keeper">Secret-Keeper</a> and faked his own death by cutting off his finger in a crowded London street which he blew up with the <a href="/wiki/Blasting_Curse" title="Blasting Curse">Blasting Curse</a> in order to frame <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a>. Like the rest of the wizarding world, Dumbledore initially believed that it was Sirius who was behind the Potters' betrayal, and that Pettigrew died confronting him about their deaths. He learned the truth in <a href="/wiki/1994" title="1994">1994</a>, when Harry Potter saved Pettigrew's life from Sirius' and Remus Lupin's attempt to extinguish it for his crime. After Harry saved Sirius from the <a href="/wiki/Dementor" title="Dementor">Dementors</a>, Dumbledore congratulated him by saying that as long as Pettigrew was a Death Eater in a <a href="/wiki/Life_debt" title="Life debt">life-debt</a> with the last Potter, he would requite. Dumbledore's observation was proven true: Pettigrew attempted to strangle Harry during the <a href="/wiki/Skirmish_at_Malfoy_Manor" title="Skirmish at Malfoy Manor">Skirmish at Malfoy Manor</a>, but he hesitated when Harry reminded him of the debt, causing the <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew%27s_silver_hand" title="Peter Pettigrew&#39;s silver hand">silver hand</a> that was given to him by Voldemort to strangle and kill him.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Igor_Karkaroff">Igor Karkaroff</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=88" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Igor Karkaroff">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=88" title="Edit section: Igor Karkaroff"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1b/Igor_Karkaroff_GoF.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100724115703" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="273" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Igor Karkaroff GoF.jpg" data-image-key="Igor_Karkaroff_GoF.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1b/Igor_Karkaroff_GoF.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100724115703" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1b/Igor_Karkaroff_GoF.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100724115703" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1b/Igor_Karkaroff_GoF.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100724115703" decoding="async" width="180" height="273" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Igor Karkaroff GoF.jpg" data-image-key="Igor_Karkaroff_GoF.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1b/Igor_Karkaroff_GoF.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100724115703" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Igor_Karkaroff_GoF.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Igor Karkaroff</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p><a href="/wiki/Igor_Karkaroff" title="Igor Karkaroff">Igor Karkaroff</a> was a Death Eater in the First Wizarding War. Dumbledore participated in his trial, and saw him betraying many Death Eaters to avoid imprisonment in Azkaban. After his release, he abandoned Voldemort and became the Headmaster of <a href="/wiki/Durmstrang_Institute" title="Durmstrang Institute">Durmstrang Institute</a>. He met Dumbledore in 1994, when he visited Hogwarts during the <a href="/wiki/Triwizard_Tournament" title="Triwizard Tournament">Triwizard Tournament</a>. At first, the two headmasters greeted each other as old friends, seemingly showing no animosity. However Karkaroff would later denounce  Dumbledore as a fraud who put Harry Potter's name in the <a href="/wiki/Goblet_of_Fire" title="Goblet of Fire">Goblet of Fire</a>, and was even more angry to learn about <a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Senior" title="Bartemius Crouch Senior">Barty Crouch Snr</a>'s attack on Durmstrang champion <a href="/wiki/Viktor_Krum" title="Viktor Krum">Viktor Krum</a>, suggesting that the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">British Ministry of Magic</a> was tainted with corruption. He left Hogwarts after Voldemort's rebirth, and was killed by Death Eaters in 1995. Despite public appearances, Dumbledore thought Karkaroff was a coward.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Barty_Crouch_Junior">Barty Crouch Junior</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=89" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Barty Crouch Junior">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=89" title="Edit section: Barty Crouch Junior"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f4/Barty_Crouch_Junior.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161221034115" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="282" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Barty Crouch Junior.jpg" data-image-key="Barty_Crouch_Junior.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f4/Barty_Crouch_Junior.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161221034115" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f4/Barty_Crouch_Junior.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161221034115" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f4/Barty_Crouch_Junior.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161221034115" decoding="async" width="180" height="282" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Barty Crouch Junior.jpg" data-image-key="Barty_Crouch_Junior.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f4/Barty_Crouch_Junior.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161221034115" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Barty_Crouch_Junior.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Barty Crouch Jnr, his former student</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Another very loyal Death Eater was <a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">Barty Crouch Jnr</a>, who was imprisoned in Azkaban by his <a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Senior" title="Bartemius Crouch Senior">father</a>, but escaped with the help of his <a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Jnr%27s_mother" class="mw-redirect" title="Bartemius Crouch Jnr&#39;s mother">mother</a>. Crouch played a key-role in Voldemort's rebirth, after he captured and imprisoned <a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">Alastor Moody</a>, and took his form, to teach at Hogwarts, while Dumbledore thought he was dead. Crouch put Harry's name in the Goblet of Fire, and helped him with the tasks of the Triwizard Tournament, sending him to Voldemort. When Harry escaped, Crouch attempted to kill him, but was stopped by Dumbledore. Barty Crouch was given the <a href="/wiki/Dementor" title="Dementor">Dementor</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Dementor%27s_Kiss" title="Dementor&#39;s Kiss">Kiss</a> in 1995. Dumbledore showed cold fury and disgust at Crouch Jnr's actions but was still disappointed and revolted when Cornelius Fudge sentenced him to Dementor's Kiss as it both meant that Voldemort's return could no longer be testified and that the Crouch family blood line had permanantly ended. This show that despite his disgust of Crouch Jnr's actions, he still had some pity for what Crouch Jnr became.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Fenrir_Greyback">Fenrir Greyback</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=90" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Fenrir Greyback">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=90" title="Edit section: Fenrir Greyback"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b2/Greybackthewerewolf.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100721162120" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="248" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Greybackthewerewolf.jpg" data-image-key="Greybackthewerewolf.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b2/Greybackthewerewolf.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100721162120" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b2/Greybackthewerewolf.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100721162120" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b2/Greybackthewerewolf.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100721162120" decoding="async" width="180" height="248" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Greybackthewerewolf.jpg" data-image-key="Greybackthewerewolf.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b2/Greybackthewerewolf.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100721162120" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Greybackthewerewolf.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Fenrir Greyback</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p><a href="/wiki/Fenrir_Greyback" title="Fenrir Greyback">Fenrir Greyback</a> was a savage <a href="/wiki/Werewolf" title="Werewolf">werewolf</a> who seemed to have had dealings with Dumbledore in the past, as Dumbledore was shocked that he, of all people, had come to Hogwarts the night that the Death Eaters entered the <a href="/wiki/Astronomy_Tower" title="Astronomy Tower">Astronomy Tower</a>. He was also disgusted that Greyback had started to attack outside the full moon and enjoyed the taste of human flesh. Greyback offered to 'do Dumbledore for afters', indicating that he would, possibly, maul him to death after attacking children within the castle. In fact, Dumbledore seemed somewhat disappointed when he incorrectly believed that Draco would invite Greyback into the castle.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Other_Death_Eaters">Other Death Eaters</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=91" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Other Death Eaters">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=91" title="Edit section: Other Death Eaters"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>It is likely that Dumbledore knew and fought other Death Eaters during the Wars and attended their trials if caught. It is certain that the Death Eaters both hated and yet feared Dumbledore.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=92" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=92" title="Edit section: Etymology"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Dumbledore's given names could be interpreted as representing the four primary divisions of the British Isles:
</p>
<ul><li><i>Albus</i> may be the masculine form of "Alba", the Gaelic name for Scotland or an Italian word meaning "sunrise", possibly alluding to the rebirth symbols associated with him (see <a href="/wiki/Phoenix" title="Phoenix">Phoenix</a>). It is also a Latin word for white, and thus could be meant to invoke Good as traditionally associated with white, or merely to refer to his long white hair and beard.</li>
<li><i>Percival</i> is a legendary Arthurian knight from Wales involved in the Grail quest. In <i>Le morte d'Arthur</i> by Thomas Mallory, Percival is both hero of the quest for the Grail and narrator of the tale, as is the case for Dumbledore in parts of the story. It is a name which presumably comes from his <a href="/wiki/Percival_Dumbledore" title="Percival Dumbledore">father</a>.</li>
<li>Clodius Albinus was a Roman usurper proclaimed emperor by the legions in Britain and Hispania upon the murder of Pertinax in 193. After Pertinax was assassinated, the praetorian prefect Aemilius Laetus and his men, who had arranged the murder, "sold" the imperial throne to wealthy senator Didius Julianus, effectively crowning him emperor, but a string of mutinies from the troops in the provinces meant the next emperor was far from decided. Immediately afterwards, Pescennius Niger (possibly <a href="/wiki/Phineas_Nigellus_Black" title="Phineas Nigellus Black">Phineas Nigellus Black</a>) was proclaimed emperor by the legions in Syria; Septimius Severus (<a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>) by the troops in Illyricum and Pannonia; and Albinus by the armies in Britain and Gaul.</li>
<li><i>Wulfric</i> is an Anglo-Saxon name found in the <i>Anglo-Saxon Chronicle</i> and could be representative of England. Wulfric translates literally as "wolf-power", and is reminiscent of another similar name, Beowulf, which means "powerful wolf-bear". The legendary hero Beowulf slew the monster Grendel as a youth, a name similar to <a href="/wiki/Gellert_Grindelwald" title="Gellert Grindelwald">Gellert Grindelwald</a>, the dark wizard Dumbledore defeated in his own youth. Beowulf was fatally wounded by a dragon in a sea cave, and the only one who would help him was his squire, an orphaned son of some loyal followers. Dumbledore was also severelly wounded by the <a href="/wiki/Emerald_Potion" title="Emerald Potion">potion</a> in <a href="/wiki/The_Cave" title="The Cave">The Cave</a> and the orphaned follower is obviously Harry.</li>
<li><i>Brian</i> is the name of the legendary Irish high-king and hero Brian Boru who defeated the Vikings at the Battle of Clontarf near Dublin. Dumbledore himself was a veteran of many wizarding battles against Dark wizards.. However, this name was probably chosen because of its comic mundanity compared to his other four names.</li>
<li><i>Dumbledore</i> is an old 18th century English word for 'bumblebee'. It is still used in Newfoundland, Canada, to refer to a bumblebee. Rowling stated she imagined him flitting about the castle humming to himself.</li>
<li>"Albus Dumbledore" may be inspired from JK Rowling's old school headmaster, Alfred Dunn.</li>
<li>The name Albus can also come from Latin origins and means pure or white. Albus can also be associated with the Greek Goddess Aphrodite (the Goddess of Love) and viewed as having been "graced" by her. According to Rowling herself, the first names of Albus Dumbledore and <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Rubeus Hagrid</a> were chosen based on "the white" and "the red", which were considered essential mystical components of <a href="/wiki/Alchemy" title="Alchemy">alchemy</a>. Dumbledore was given the white for asceticism, "a spiritual theoretician, brilliant, idealised, and somewhat detached".<sup id="cite_ref-pottermorecolours_97-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pottermorecolours-97">&#91;97&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
