<ul><li>Dumbledore is portrayed by the late <a href="/wiki/Ireland" title="Ireland">Irish</a> actor <a href="/wiki/Richard_Harris" title="Richard Harris">Richard Harris</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_(film_series)" title="Harry Potter (film series)">film adaptations</a> of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone (film)">Harry Potter and the Philosopher's Stone</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets (film)">Chamber of Secrets</a></i>.</li>
<li>When Harris died of Hodgkin's Disease in <a href="/wiki/2002" title="2002">2002</a>, <a href="/wiki/Michael_Gambon" title="Michael Gambon">Michael Gambon</a> was recast as Dumbledore and portrays him in the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_(film_series)" title="Harry Potter (film series)">film adaptations</a> of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban (film)">Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire (film)">Goblet of Fire</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix (film)">Order of the Phoenix</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince (film)">Half-Blood Prince</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_1" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 1">Deathly Hallows: Part 1</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_2" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2">Part 2</a></i>.
<ul><li>Therefore, Dumbledore is one of the 14 characters to appear in all 8 film adaptations.<sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98">&#91;98&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Both actors who have played the elderly Dumbledore have been Irish. In an interview on the DVD of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban (film)">Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban</a></i>, Gambon mentions that his Irish accent is quite pronounced as Dumbledore, but no one asked him to change it. (The Irish tones of Harris' accent are less pronounced.)</li>
<li>A younger Dumbledore (aged around 62) is portrayed by <a href="/wiki/Richard_Harris" title="Richard Harris">Harris</a> in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets (film)">Chamber of Secrets</a></i> and <a href="/wiki/Michael_Gambon" title="Michael Gambon">Gambon</a> portrays an older Dumbledore in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire (film)">Goblet of Fire</a></i> (aged around 100) and <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince (film)">Half-Blood Prince</a></i> (aged around 57).</li>
<li>Michael Gambon also voices Professor Dumbledore in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter:_Hogwarts_Mystery" title="Harry Potter: Hogwarts Mystery">Harry Potter: Hogwarts Mystery</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99">&#91;99&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Prior to Michael Gambon being recast as Dumbledore, the role was offered to Sir Ian McKellen, but he declined.<sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100">&#91;100&#93;</a></sup></li></ul></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Toby_Regbo" title="Toby Regbo">Toby Regbo</a> portrayed an even younger Dumbledore (aged around 18) in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_1" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 1">Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 1</a></i><sup id="cite_ref-101" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-101">&#91;101&#93;</a></sup> and <i><a href="/wiki/Fantastic_Beasts:_The_Crimes_of_Grindelwald" title="Fantastic Beasts: The Crimes of Grindelwald">Fantastic Beasts: The Crimes of Grindelwald</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-Pottermore_102-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Pottermore-102">&#91;102&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jude_Law" title="Jude Law">Jude Law</a> portrays Dumbledore, at the age of around 47, in <i><a href="/wiki/Fantastic_Beasts:_The_Crimes_of_Grindelwald" title="Fantastic Beasts: The Crimes of Grindelwald">Fantastic Beasts: The Crimes of Grindelwald</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103">&#91;103&#93;</a></sup>
<ul><li>Along with <a href="/wiki/Nagini" title="Nagini">Nagini</a>, Minerva McGonagall and <a href="/wiki/Gellert_Grindelwald" title="Gellert Grindelwald">Gellert Grindelwald</a>, Dumbledore is one of four characters who appear in both the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_(film_series)" title="Harry Potter (film series)"><i>Harry Potter</i></a> and <a href="/wiki/Fantastic_Beasts_(film_series)" title="Fantastic Beasts (film series)"><i>Fantastic Beasts</i></a> film series to date.</li></ul></li>
<li>Michael Gambon's portrayal of Dumbledore is noticeably different from both Richard Harris' and from the books'. In the books, Dumbledore is noted to have been very calm and collected in nearly all circumstances. He has also been known to have worn a pointy wizard's cap, long majestic robes, and have a lengthy untethered beard. However, Gambon's Dumbledore is somewhat different in that regard. Though still calm and collected most of the time, he tends to traverse further into the emotional spectrum of his character. This can be seen clearly in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire (film)">Goblet of Fire</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix (film)">Order of the Phoenix</a></i> where he sometimes raises his voice at Harry Potter and the students respectively. This somewhat uncharacteristic behaviour is wholly absent, however, in his portrayals in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban (film)">Prisoner of Azkaban</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince (film)">Half-Blood Prince</a></i>, and <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_2" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2">Deathly Hallows: Part 2</a></i>.</li>
<li>Gambon’s physical portrayal as Dumbledore is also slightly different, opting for a somewhat Bohemian look, including a fez-like tasselled hat, along with long and flowing robes that seem to have subtle Indian/Arabian influences. His beard is also tied with a thread-like chain, the ends of which feature miniature bells. Dumbledore doesn't always wear his spectacles in the films (except the third where he was wearing them during every on-screen appearance in that film, while in the fourth film he wore his spectacles at different times, in the fifth film he wore them only during the Start-of-Term Feast and in the sixth film, he wore them just during the Start-of-Term Feast and for a brief moment in his office examining Tom Riddle’s diary just before Harry entered and sees Dumbledore’s memory of meeting Riddle. Also, just after Harry is seen entering and the next shot of Dumbledore comes, his spectacles have gone which is one of the film’s mistakes). What can also be noted is that Gambon's Dumbledore is far more energetic than Harris' Dumbledore which is more in line with the character from the books. Discounting the special case of Tom Riddle/Voldemort, Dumbledore is, to date, the only major core character in the series to be recast.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/J._K._Rowling" title="J. K. Rowling">J. K. Rowling</a> has stated that Albus Dumbledore is her favourite character in the whole series.<sup id="cite_ref-104" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-104">&#91;104&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Dumbledore does not say Harry Potter's name at all in the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban (film)">film adaptation</a> of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban</a></i>. This is the only film in which this happens, although <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_1" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 1">Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 1</a></i> would not count, due to Dumbledore having died near the end of <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince (film)">the previous film</a> and flashbacks and voices of Dumbledore saying hints and the like.</li>
<li>In the early drafts of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix</a></i>, Dumbledore would not resist arrest by the Ministry of Magic, after the discovery of <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a>, and would've uttered: "<i>Then to Azkaban I must go. I trust I'm allowed a toothbrush?</i>"<sup id="cite_ref-105" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-105">&#91;105&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>In the films, Dumbledore has the distinction of being the first human character to appear in the film series.</li>
<li>In 2007, J.K. Rowling revealed that Dumbledore was gay, and harboured romantic feelings for <a href="/wiki/Gellert_Grindelwald" title="Gellert Grindelwald">Gellert Grindelwald</a>.  Rowling also commented that "this added to Dumbledore's horror when Grindelwald showed himself to be what he was." This love was caused by Dumbledore meeting someone "as brilliant as he was." Only the subtlest of hints can be found in <i>Deathly Hallows</i> relating to this. Reportedly the earliest indication of Dumbledore's orientation came when Rowling vetoed a line of dialogue in one of the recent film scripts that would have referenced a romantic involvement with a woman.<sup id="cite_ref-carnegie_106-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-carnegie-106">&#91;106&#93;</a></sup> Rowling explains this further by elaborating on the motivations behind Dumbledore's flirtation with the idea of wizard domination of Muggles: "He lost his moral compass completely when he fell in love and I think subsequently became very mistrustful of his own judgement in those matters so became quite <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/asexual" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:asexual">asexual</a>. He led a <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Celibacy" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Celibacy">celibate</a> and a bookish life."<sup id="cite_ref-jkrstudent_107-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-jkrstudent-107">&#91;107&#93;</a></sup> Later, in the digital bonus edition of Fantastic Beasts: The Crimes of Grindelwald, Rowling confirmed that Dumbledore and Grindelwald did indeed have a romantic relationship in their youth, and that it was quite intense and passionate.</li>
<li>When asked on twitter why Dumbledore sends other people to deal with the bad guy (in this case Grindelwald) she said he has his reasons and to be patient.<sup id="cite_ref-108" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-108">&#91;108&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>The published version of <i>The Tales of Beedle the Bard</i> reveals that Lucius Malfoy tried to assure Dumbledore would be removed from the post of Headmaster of Hogwarts after he had ensured the inclusion of pro-Muggle tales in the book. Dumbledore, in turn, commented that he worked hard to make Malfoy "Voldemort's least favourite Death Eater".</li>
<li>In <a href="/wiki/J._K._Rowling" title="J. K. Rowling">J. K. Rowling</a>'s website <a href="/wiki/Wizard_of_the_Month" title="Wizard of the Month">Wizard of the Month</a> archive, Albus Dumbledore was the Wizard of the Month before <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, which was the last.<sup id="cite_ref-109" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-109">&#91;109&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ciar%C3%A1n_Hinds" title="Ciarán Hinds">Ciarán Hinds</a>, who played Albus's brother Aberforth, claimed that Dumbledore was 123 years old when he died.<sup id="cite_ref-110" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-110">&#91;110&#93;</a></sup> This would make his year of birth 1874.</li>
<li>According to Rowling in 2018, we will learn more about Grindelwald's and Dumbledore's past in the upcoming films.<sup id="cite_ref-111" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-111">&#91;111&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>In one interview, <a href="/wiki/J._K._Rowling" title="J. K. Rowling">J. K. Rowling</a> said that Dumbledore was a sprightly 150.<sup id="cite_ref-112" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-112">&#91;112&#93;</a></sup> This is possibly referenced in the <i>Half-Blood Prince</i> film, when the trio humorously speculates 150 as his age, before cracking up.</li>
<li>At the end of the first part of the <i>Deathly Hallows</i> film, it is shown that Dumbledore is buried on the island in the <a href="/wiki/Great_Lake" title="Great Lake">Black Lake</a> that Harry and Lupin take a stroll through in the <i>Prisoner of Azkaban</i> film.</li>
<li>Dumbledore is similar in appearance and role to Gandalf from J.R.R. Tolkien's Lord of the Rings trilogy. His resemblance to Gandalf is perhaps strongest in the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince (film)">film adaptation</a> of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince</a></i>, and he also resembles Gandalf the White in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_2" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2">Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2</a></i>. The fire attack he uses to fight the Inferi could also be compared to Gandalf's "Flame of Anor". Many used Gandalf's supposed death (as he survived) to support their theories that Dumbledore survived, but J.K. Rowling said to not expect him to "pull a Gandalf". Ironically, Ian McKellen, the actor who portrayed Gandalf in both the Lord of the Rings and the Hobbit trilogies, was offered the role of Dumbledore after the death of Richard Harris, but refused due to Harris not approving of him.
<ul><li>In addition, Dumbledore's character also has parallels between both Gandalf and even Obi Wan Kenobi from George Lucas' Star Wars original trilogy. All three characters possess magical abilities and serve as principle mentors to the main protagonists of each of the respective stories (Harry Potter, Frodo Baggins, and Luke Skywalker) guiding them on their journey to accomplish their respective tasks each are destined for. All protagonists would later witness their mentor's demise first hand affecting them greatly, but the latter are later able to establish communications again with their mentees, either through visions, or being reborn (in Gandalf's case). Finally in each of the films when facing off against a major antagonists, each mentor is taunted for being weak by being spitefully called "old man." In the Extended Edition of the Return of the King, the Witch-king calls Gandalf that before breaking his staff. In Star Wars Episode IV, Darth Vader taunts Obi Wan "You're powers are weak, old man" before slaying him. Finally, in the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix (film)">fifth Harry Potter film</a>, Voldemort tells Dumbledore "You've lost old man" whilst possessing Harry during the <a href="/wiki/Duel_in_the_Ministry_Atrium" title="Duel in the Ministry Atrium">Duel in the Ministry Atrium</a>.</li>
<li>In appearance and biography, Dumbledore also resembles two characters in Ursula K. Le Guin's <i>Earthsea</i> books. The first of those is the main character, Ged, who is recognised from his childhood as an extremely powerful and talented wizard, but in his pride, ignores warnings about the risks involved, confident his power will protect him. However, after a terrible accident caused by his pride, he is forced to reconsider his views, spends a long time undoing the consequences, and later becomes a respected and well-known hero, as well as the headmaster of his old school. The second character is Archmage Nemmerle, the old headmaster of Ged's school during his studies here, who gives his life to save the young wizard during the aforementioned accident. He has a bird familiar that vanishes without a trace when Nemmerle dies.</li></ul></li>
<li>Dumbledore and Harry Potter are also quite similar in some ways: They were Gryffindor students, they wear glasses (Harry wears full moon and Dumbledore wears half-moon), both are half-bloods, both their mothers were Muggle-born and both were brilliant Hogwarts students. Both also had defeated powerful dark wizards, were talented duelists, had an affinity for magic involving love, and acted as leaders of their own covert organisations. In addition, Harry and Dumbledore both possessed outrageous tempers that when witnessed were great enough to cow and frighten even those closest to them.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Evanna_Lynch" title="Evanna Lynch">Evanna Lynch</a>, who plays <a href="/wiki/Luna_Lovegood" title="Luna Lovegood">Luna Lovegood</a> in the film series, named her cats after Harry Potter characters: she has a cat named Luna and another named Dumbledore.</li>
<li>In the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince (film)">film adaptation</a> of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince</a></i>, Dumbledore tells <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a>: "Years ago I knew a boy who made all the wrong choices." There has been some debate about who he is referring to. Possibilities include <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Tom Riddle</a>, <a href="/wiki/Gellert_Grindelwald" title="Gellert Grindelwald">Gellert Grindelwald</a>, <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a> and himself.</li>
<li>In addition to the portrait of Dumbledore that was hung in his office automatically after his death, a <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore%27s_portrait_(II)" title="Albus Dumbledore&#39;s portrait (II)">second portrait</a> of him was hung in several places in Hogwarts castle and could also been in the Headmaster's office.</li>
<li>J. K. Rowling has said that if she could meet any character in the <i>Harry Potter</i> novels for dinner, it would be Dumbledore, as she feels she would have a lot to discuss with him and she would love his advice.<sup id="cite_ref-infosheet_113-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-infosheet-113">&#91;113&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/LEGO_Harry_Potter" title="LEGO Harry Potter">LEGO</a> version of Albus Dumbledore makes a cameo appearance in the 2014 film <i><a href="https://brickipedia.fandom.com/wiki/The_LEGO_Movie" class="extiw" title="w:c:lego:The LEGO Movie">The LEGO Movie</a></i> alongside other characters from popular LEGO sets. In the film, he is a Master Builder and sits next to Gandalf at a meeting of the other builders. When addressed by <a href="https://brickipedia.fandom.com/wiki/Vitruvius" class="extiw" title="w:c:lego:Vitruvius">Vitruvius</a>, Dumbledore becomes irritated by his inability to pronounce his name properly. He, along with the other Master Builders was captured by the villains and later rescued. He speaks in a high effeminate voice. It is completely unknown if he was killed during the attack of Evil Cop's patrol to Cloud Cuckoo Land and its subsequent destruction.</li>
<li>While the magic used by Dumbledore to detect the traces of magic in the Horcrux cave was unknown to Harry, it may be related to the work of <a href="/wiki/Aurologist" title="Aurologist">Aurologists</a> as mentioned on <a href="/wiki/The_New_York_Ghost" title="The New York Ghost">The New York Ghost</a> in <i><a href="/wiki/Fantastic_Beasts_and_Where_to_Find_Them_(film)" title="Fantastic Beasts and Where to Find Them (film)">Fantastic Beasts and Where to Find Them (film)</a></i>.</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Appearances">Appearances</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?veaction=edit&amp;section=94" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Appearances">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore?action=edit&amp;section=94" title="Edit section: Appearances"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="noprint" style="float: right; clear: right; margin-top: 2px; margin-left: 2px; margin-bottom: 2px; background-color: #D8E9FC; text-align: left; font-size: 90%; width: 250px;"><span class="rtop" style=""><span class="r1" style="background: #D8E9FC"></span><span class="r2" style="background: #D8E9FC"></span><span class="r3" style="background: #D8E9FC"></span><span class="r4" style="background: #D8E9FC"></span></span><div style="float:left; margin-left: 5px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bc/Wiki.png/revision/latest?cb=20091217124448" class="image"><img alt="Wiki.png" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="35" height="21" data-image-name="Wiki.png" data-image-key="Wiki.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bc/Wiki.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/35?cb=20091217124448" class="lazyload" /></a></div><div style="margin-left:50px">The Harry Potter Wiki has 741 images related to <i><b><a href="/wiki/Category:Images_of_Albus_Dumbledore" title="Category:Images of Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a></b></i>.</div><span class="content-bg rbottom" style=""><span class="r4" style="background: #D8E9FC"></span><span class="r3" style="background: #D8E9FC"></span><span class="r2" style="background: #D8E9FC"></span><span class="r1" style="background: #D8E9FC"></span></span></div>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">Harry Potter and the Philosopher's Stone</a></i> <small>(First appearance)</small></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone (film)">Harry Potter and the Philosopher's Stone (film)</a></i></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone_(video_game)" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone (video game)">Harry Potter and the Philosopher's Stone (video game)</a></i></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets</a></i></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets (film)">Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets (film)</a></i></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets_(video_game)" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets (video game)">Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets (video game)</a></i></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban</a></i></li>
